  *MASARAUTA*

      

         *HAKKIN MALLAKA*
*HALIMATU ILYAS KANGIWA.*
      (AuntyHaliloss).

*SHEKARAR RUBUTU*
       *2021*

*GODIYA*

_Tsantsar godiya ga ubangijin talikai wanda ya ke iko akanmu bayinsa,ya kyautar mana da lafiya,ya kyautar mana da iskar shaka,wannan kadai abin godiya ce a gare mu ga ubangijinmu Assamadu._

*HAR KULLUM HAR ABADA*

_Ina jinjina ga iyayenmu,ina rokon Allah ya kara masu lafiya tare da nisan kwana,ya Kara saka mana jinkansu a zukatanmu._

*GAME DA LABARI.*
_Ba cin zarafi ne ga wasu ba,illa iyaka ilmantarwa da kuma nishadantarwa,don haka wanda ya ga wani abu ya kusance shi,to arashi ne._

*SADAUKARWA GA*

_Daukacin masoyana da kuma litattafaina,wanda idan babu ku,to fa Halimatu ba za ta kai labari a fagen Rubutu ba._

*BismillahirRahmanirRahim.*

*BABI NA DAYA*

Tafiya ta ke a hankali,sanye da alkebba a saman wani tsadaddan leshi,da wasu takalma jinin sarauta,hannunta da wuyanta sanye da wasu kayan ado wanda da kun gan su kun san tabbas tsadaddune.

Kuyangu ne bayanta su na take mata baya,sai wata gefenta d'auke da kayan lambu irinsu lemu,inibi,ayaba,tuffa da sauran kayan marmari,acikin wani madaukin kaba.

Gidan ganye suka nufa,wani wajan shak'atawa ne da sarki kan zauna ya huta,sai dai ba kowa ne yake zuwa wajan ba bayan shi sai ko Gimbiya Aymana,domin kuwa itace Yar da yafi ji da ita a cikin jerin yaran nashi.

Wata matace ta fito tare da Jakadiya,Gimbiya Aymana ta d'an tsaya tana dai-daita nutsuwarta tare da d'an rusunawa alamar ban girma zuwa ga mahaifiyarta ta"Ranki ya dad'e Umma."

Matar ta gyara mayafinta tace"Gimbiya ina zaki je a wannan lokacin da muke sauraran shigowar bak'in namu?"

"Za'a iya tararsu ni zanje Gidan ganye in huta"

Jakadiya dake gefen Umma tace"a gafarceni uwar d'akina,rashin ganinki zaisa ran Mai martaba ya sosu,kuma kinga sauran matan gidannan  kowacce zata baiyana da iyalansu ne."

Yamutsa fuska ta yi tana ɗaga baki za ta yi magana,Umma ta ce"lallai kizo tarar bak'in nan da za su zo."

Ta na maganar ta na cigaba da tafiya Gimbiya Aymana,ta d'an tsaya,kuyangar dake gefenta ta ce"Yar sarki jikar sarki,takawarki lafiya,bacin ranki fushin yaranki"

Juya idanuwa ta yi,ta yi hanyar juyawa don komawa cikin gidan,gabad'aya kuyangun suka yi saurin bud'a mata hanya suna komawa bayanta.

Babban b'angaran su ta nufa,ta na d'an sauri don sam bata so aka tsaidata ba,saboda ba ta son haduwa da bak'in.

A falo suka barta ta ida shigewa ta na shiga ɗakin ta fara cire Alk'ebbar jikinta,ta zauna kan wata kujera tana ɗan jan gajeran tsaki.

Wata matashiryar budurwa ta fito daga band'aki ta na tsane jikinta ga dukkan alamu wanka ta fito,yarinyar ta kalli yayar tata"Gimbiya lafiya kuwa,kin fasa fita hutawar ne?"

"Umma ce muka had'u,tace lallai sai na jira bak'in sun zo"

"Ai na fad'i maki,ba za ta bari ba,musamman yadda tasan Mai martaba yana ɗokin zuwan baƙin nan"

Gimbiya ta cire takalmin kafarta"Sam banga amfanin murna akan baƙuncin da masarautar TORO zasu kawo mana ba,Akan me zamu bari mu saki jiki dasu."

juyawa Budurwar tayi tana cigaba da shirinta"Idan har mai martaba zai amince da zancen mu to da tuni ya amince."

Aymana ta miƙe tana barin wajan don yin nata shirin,Kuyangu ne suke shirin binta,hannu kawai ta ɗaga masu alamar bata buƙatar hakan.

****
Acikin gidan kuwa kowane ɓangare na masarautar shiri ake don zuwan baƙin musamman waɗanda suke ganin zuwan yaron sarkin masarautar TORO kamar wani leƙen a shiri ne ga tasu masarautar.

Sai wajan ƙarfe Huɗu baƙin suka iso ɗan sarkin Toro ne da tawagarshi ya zo gaishe da Maimartaba domin haɗaka da kuma dawo da zumincin tsakaninsu.

A wani ƙaton ɗakin baƙi na masarautar BILYAM an kuma ƙayatar da ɗakin da ado irin na sarauta,shigowar baƙin ne ya maido da hankalin mutanan gidan,hakan yasa kowa ya nufi ɗakin don miƙa gaisuwa zuwa ga Babban ɗan sarkin Toro.

Shi kanshi mai martaba da iyalansu basu ɓata lokaci ba wajan zuwa.

Mai martaba ya zauna saman karagar shi tare da ɗan ware ido yana kallon mutanan da suka halarshi ɗakin,yaran shi ne maza manya guda biyu sai matan shi.

Umma ta ɗan juya ita kanta Aymana take dubawa don batason abinda zaisa ta ɓata ran mai martaba.

Yarima Amin ya miƙe tare da gyara jabbar dake jikinshi,yana nufa wajan da Maimartaba ya ke.

Fadawanshi suka miƙe suna mashi kirari tare da kambamawa,A hankalin ya rage tsawon shi gaban Mai martaba tare da rusunawa cikin tsananin Girmamawa.

Sarki yayi Murmushi yana amsa gaisuwar da yake mashi ya miƙa mashi hannu alamar  su gaisa.

Yarima Amin ya cire hular kanshi,don neman albarkar Mai martaba.

Fadawan masarautar suka ɗauka da faɗin"Sarki ya gaishe da sarkin wata rana a masarautar Toro,Sarki ya amshi gaisuwar Yarima Amin."

Mai martaba ya kalli Fuskar Yarima tare da jin daɗin yadda yaga tsananin Girmamawa a tare da Yaron.

Hannu yasa ya ɗagoshi daga durƙuson da yayi tare da alamar ya zauna,Yarima ya zauna sosai Yana faɗin.

"Sarki ya na gaisheka,ya ce a miƙo saƙon ban girma ga zakin Sarki da babu irin shi a nahiyarmu."

Murmushin girma yayi,kasancewar babu wanda yake jinsu hakan yasa babu wani bafadan da ya tofa albarkacin bakinshi,balle su ari bakin sarki wajan ci mashi albasa.

"Na gode sosai Yarima."

Yana maganar yana kallon ɗakin lokacinne yake son gabatar da kowa ga Yarima amma kuma Gimbiya Aymana ba ta nan.

Hakan yasa ranshi ya sosu ya juya yana ƙara gyara zama.Yarima Ya miƙe ya nufi wajan Gimbiyoyin dake wajan wato matan sarki,wanda daka gani bama sai ka tambayi matsayinsu a wannan zama ba.

Gaisuwa ya farayi ɗaya bayan ɗaya cikin Girmamawa kamar yadda ya gaishe da maimartaba.

Sosai sukaji daɗi suna mashi sannu da zuwa DARUL-BILYAM.

Wajan  Sauran Yaran sarki ya nufa babu wani nuna mulki ko isa ya nufi gunsu,sai dai su hannu ya miƙa masu yana murmushi,Yarima Shureim yace"Banyi tunanin ganin ka irin wannan lokacin ba"

Murmushi yayi ya kalli Bilkisu,Bilkisu tace"Barka da zuwa Masarautar Bilyam"

"Yauwa"yace sannan ya juya don komawa wajan mai marta ba,dai-dai lokacin Maimartaba yana bada saƙo don kira mashi Gimbiya Aymana.

Dan aiken bai kaiga tafiya ba sai ga Gimbiya Aymana ta shigo cikin shigar Alfarma,shiga ta ƴaƴan sarauta.cikin taƙama take isowa falon tana nufar wajan Sarki.

Gaba ɗaya aka fara gaishe da ita cikin  falon sai dai sam kamar ba da ita ake ba,Sarki yayi ajiyar zuciya yasaka aranshi ƙila shiri ne ya tsaida ita.

Yarima Amin ya ɗago don ganin mai shigowar da kuma tantance kirarin da yaji ana mata.

yayi mamakin ganin yadda babu annuri a fuskarta,sai ya tuna ba ita ɗaya ce yakula da hakan a tare da itaba.

Ɗan sauri ta ƙarayi tare da rusunawa tana faɗin"Ayi mani Afuwa ina kan shiryawa ne..."

"Aymana ga baƙi nan sunzo"cewar maimartaba.

Bata ɗago ba don kallon su,sai bakinta da ta ɗaga tare da faɗin"Aminci ga baƙin masarautarmu"

Hatta tawagar Yarima Amin da suke kusa sun gane ita ɗin yar sarki ce,kuma tana taƙama da mulki a cikin gidan nasu.hakan yasa suka yi saurin amsa mata,wannan dalilin ne ya hana Yarima Amin yin magana.

Gimbiya Ayma ta ɗago da sauri,tana kallon su,kenan shi ɗan sarki yafi ƙarfin ya buɗe baki ya amsa.

Hakan ya ɗugunzuma ta,tana shirin miƙewa,Mai martaba yace"Ki zauna.Na tura  a duba wajan zaman su har zuwa lokacin da zasu tafi,Sannan kuma na ɗaura nauyin kula da baƙin akanki,ina so abasu kulawa."

Aymana tace"Ban gane ba Mai mar..."

"Ina nufin ke ce zaki kula da cinsu,shansu,da sauran buƙatunsu,Wannan shine Yarima Amin Babban ɗan sarkin a masarautar TORO" yana magana yana nuna Yarima.

kallon shi tayi,ai ko ba a faɗa ba ta gane shine,ko don kayan dake jikin shi.

"InshaAllah ba zasu nemi komai su rasa ba, DARUL-BILYAM za a basu kulawa"

daƙyal Aymana take maganar saboda ba har zuciyarta ne ba,sai don sanin babu wata kalma da ake amfani da ita wajan yiwa mai martaba musu.

Mai martaba ya kalli shi"wannan itace Aymana zata kula daku har ku tafi"

Rusunawa yayi tare da Faɗin"Mun gode Baba"

Aymana tayi mamakin ganin girmamawa da yake yi.

Take aka bada umarnin kaisu masauki tare da basu abinci.

saidai ran Aymana a ɓace yake don sarki yace itace zatayi masu jagoranci.

Bayan fitar baƙin Sarki yabar wajan,hakan yaba kowa damar surutai da kuma maida yadda akayi.

Umma itace mahaifiyar Aymana sai Hajiya wadda itace Babbar matar mai martaba,Mama itace mace ta Ukku.

Ya'yansu suka matso gunsu suka fara magana,akan baƙin.

Umma tace"Kun ga duk yadda muke tunani ba haka bane gashi Yaro mai ladabi da..."

bata ida ba Hajiya tace"Ni nasan mutanan nan,wannan wani kwanton ɓauna ne, ladabin bana gaske bane."

Yarima Sureim yace"Allah hajiya Sarkin Toro baya da nuna ƙasƙanci yana ba iyalanshi tarbiya shima"

"Mudai ko miye ba zamu manta abinda sukayi mana ba,itace masarauta da ba zamu taɓa sakin jiki da suba"cewar Faruk

Bilkisu ta kalli Hajiya tace"bafa zamu saki jiki dasuba"

Jakadiyya ta juyar da kai"Ai suna neman shiri ne bayan sun anshe martabar masarautar mu,dole xamu zama cikin shiri,ta yadda zamu kwato ƴancinmu"

Hajiya tace"Dole ne wannan,daɗina dake ganewa."

Umma ta miƙe"Na barku lafiya"

Mama ta bita da Harara,ita dama ba a zama ayi shawarar kirki da ita,da an fara magana,zata tsame jikinta.

Hajiya tace"umma ta gaida aisha"

       ***
Gimbiya Aymana ta nufi wani gini wanda akayi a masarautar anyi shine don zuwan baƙin,sannan kuma ba ayi shi da tsarin zamani ba,kasancewar masarautun nahiyar suna gine-gine basu yada al'adunsu ba.

Kuyangune ke binta baya sai Yarima Amin da yake tako a hankali ganin yadda ita kanta wacce suke biye ba sauri ne take yi ba.

Fadawanshi suna binshi a baya.

Wata Baiwa tazo bucewa hannunta ɗauke da kaya ga alama cikin gida zata shiga,sam bata kula da su Gimbiya ba,hakan yasa tayi karo da Gimbiya Aymana.

Cikin zafin nama Aymana ta ja baya kaɗan tare da daka mata tsawa tana ɗaga hannu tare da marinta.

"Baki da hankali ko ke..."

kafin ai mana ta ida kuyangu suka fara magana"Hattara dai yarinya"

har lokacin ai mana tana tsaye bata ko motsaba,gaya Baiwar ta zubar da kayan hannunta saboda zafin marin da aka yi mata.

Yarima Amin yaja ya tsaya yana mamakin Aymana,bata fa bige ta ɗin ba,amma harda mari,sam baiji daɗi ba.

Wata kuyanga tace"Ki samu Gimbiya don babu hakuri a Zunubin da kika aikata"

"Don Allah ina neman Afuwa,Allah ya huci zuciyar Uwa a gare mu"

Yarima Amin ya harɗe hannuwanshi a ƙirji yana son su tafi.

Gimbiya Aymana ta cigaba da tafiya su Yarima suna binta a baya,har ƙofar masaukin,anan ta ɗan tsaya tare da juyowa ta kalle shi dai-dai lokacin shima ita yake kallo"Nan ne Masaukin naku,za a kawo maku abinci yanzu,akwai waɗanda zasu kula daku ko da kuna buƙatar wani abun."

Yarima Amin baiyi magana ba,don ta sure mashi a zuciya kuma ya tuna da maganar Maimartaba na cewar itace zata kula dasu ɗin,sai dai yaga halayyarta,shi ba ya son ganin ana wulaƙanta ɗan Adam,Hakan ya sa gabaɗaya masarautar su ake son shi.

Ta gaban Gimbiya Aymana yabi yana tura ƙofar shiga,kallo ta bishi da shi sam tafara ɗugunzuma ganin yadda har akwai wanda yake nuna mata iko da izza,juyawa tayi zata tafi dai-dai lokacin ya juyo"Mun gode sannan zaki zauna ko da muna buƙatar wani abun ki kawo mana."

Chak taja ta tsaya.


ku biyoni.

*SHAFI NA BIYU*

Chak ta ja ta tsaya ta na juyowa domin kallon shi,a lokaci ɗaya su ka haɗa ido,ɗan murmushi ta yi wanda bai kai zuciba,sai dai kuma duk da haka kyawunta ya baiyana,daƙyal ta iya buɗe baki"In sha Allah."

Ba ta kuma magana ba,Yarima ya shige ciki,da kanta ta je wajan da ake haɗa Abinci,zuwanta ya  sa ma'aikatan dagewa wajan harhaɗawa,aka biyota da shi,sai da ta tabbatar an ajiye komai kafin ta bar ɓangaren tana ɗan sauri jin an fara kiran salla.
 
     ****
Dadaddare suna wajan zamansu domin yin fira,duka yaran kowa yana wajan,haka su kan yi lokaci bayan lokaci Musamman yau da suke ganin suna da Zancan tattaunawa.

Bilkisu ta ɗan ja guntun tsaki,Faruk ya kalleta"Tun ɗazu sai wani shan tsamiya kike mana,kin kasa magana."

"Mi ye abin saita furta,bayan kunsan damuwarta"Cewar Yarima shureim.

Aymana ta ɗago"Idan kina da damuwa ki faɗi,nasan dai maganar bata wuce ta Yarima Amin."

"Atunanina zai so da TAKOBIN gidanmu ne,ashe ba abinda ya kawo shi ba kenan."

"Hmmm na faɗa muku,haka nan suke ganin zasu maido alaƙarmu dasu."

Faruk ya kaɗa kai"Sam ni banga wani abin alaƙa dasu ba,Amma Sarki ya dage akan hakan,Martabarmu na hannunsu,sam bamuna wani ƴenci ko martaba a wannan nahiyar kum..."

Bai idaba Aymana ta miƙe"Na barku lafiya,tuna har yau babu wata ma fita da muke da ita don kwato TAKOBI daga hannun masautar Toro."

Tana maganar tana barin wajan,wajan su Yarima ta nufa sai dai Fadawanshi sunce yana ciki ne,Hakan yasa ta juya,domin dama zuwan don tambayar ko sun buƙatar wani abu ne.

        ****

Tsaye ta ke a Falon farko na ɓangaran baƙin,ga kuyangu da kayan karin Yarima Amin,sai dai Aymana ba ta ba su Umarnin ajiyewa ba.

Yarima ya fito daga Cikin ɗakin shigarshi a yau ba kayan Sarauta bane,wani farin yadi ne da aka yiwa ɗinki na zamani ya amshi jikinshi sosai,kanshi babu Hula sai sumar kanshi data kwanta saboda gyara da yake mata.

Agogon Hannu yake ɗorawa,Ƙamshin turaren shi ne yasa Aymana ɗagowa,tana kallon shi,Farine yana da tsayi sai dai baya da kwarin jiki,yana da gyawun fuska.

Kallonsu yayi yana amsa gaisuwar su.Aymana ta yi saurin faɗin"Ga kayan kari har rana tayi kum..."

Bai bi ta kanta ba,ya kalli kuyangun tare da magana"Babu nauyi ne,ba za ku ajiye ku huta ba?"

"Ku Ajiye"cewar Aymana tana masu nuni da wani wajan cikin Abinci"A'a a ƙasa zaku ajiye"

Cikin sauri da ladabinsu suka hau jera Abincin kamar yadda Yarima yace.

Yarima ya maido hankalinshi akan Aymana"Ina kwana."

Sam ita ta manta da maganar gaisuwa sai taji babu daɗi"Fatan ka tashi lafiya"Tana maganar ta maida hankalinta kan kuyangunta.

"Tsayuwar me kuke?"

Cikin sauri su ka yi hanyar fita,sai ɗaya da ko wane lokaci tana tare da ita,hakan yasa bata tafi ba.

Yarima ya matsa yana zama kan kujerar da ke gefen shi"Za ki iya zama."

Ɗan shiru tayi tana kallon Ƙasa don batasan miye dalilin zaman ba,Yarima ya ɗauki wayar shi yayi kira,ba jimawa Fadawanshi suka shigo.

"Na fito ban ganku ba?"

"Ranka ya daɗe bamu san ka gama ba."

Yarima yayi Murmushi"Zaku iya zama ayi ƙari,ina son mu fita gaishe da Baba"

Sai lokacin Aymana ta saci kallon shi,shi kuma yana shirin ɗaukar filet don zuba abinci.

"Kawo a zuba Mai gida" cewar wani dake ƙoƙarin ansar filet ɗin.

"A a zan zuba,kowa ya ɗauki filet ya zuba kar muyi rana wajan fita."

Ya kuma kallon Aymana"Allah yasa Gimbiya ta karya."

Sai lokacin ta tuna da yabata izinin zama,Hakan yasa ta zauna kujerar nesa tana faɗin"A'a ba yanzu ba."

kuyangarta ta zauna ƙasa saman kafet gefen kujerar da take sama.

Yarima ya dawo ƙasa yana ɗan dai-daita zaman shi yana tsakiya fadawan Ukku a gefen dama Ukku a gefen Haggu.

Aymana tayi Mamaki,kenan a tare zasu ci abinci,lokaci ɗaya.

Ita kam bata son rashin girmama sarauta,taya zasu zauna gunshi.

Yarima ya ɗan ja wayarshi yana dannawa.Mahaifinshi ya ke kira sai dai ba'a amsa kuran ba,Ya juya yana kallon wani bafade"Na san Mai Girma yayi fushi tun jiya ban neme su ba."

"Ranka ya daɗe nasan zasuyi tunanin akwai gajiya a tare da kai."

Aymana ta miƙe"Na barku lafiya."

"Muna so ne mu gama mu fita tare don gaida mai Martaba."

"Mai martaba ya fita tun safe." ta bashi amsa tana gyara tsayuwa.

Yarima ya aje cokalin da yake cin abinci"Ashe dai na jima,ban gaishe da Mai martaba ba har ya fita."

Aymana zatayi magana Bilkisu ta shigo tare da Sallama tana gaishe da Yarima"Lafiya lau Bilkisu zance ko Gimbiya Bilkisu."

"Duk gidannan Gimbiya ɗaya ce"Tana magana tana cije leɓo,Aymana ta kalleta"Wato ba zaki daina yiman wannan abin ba,ta juya ta kalli Kuyangar gabanta"Don Allah ku rinƙa ce ma Bilkisu Gimbiya."

Dariya Yarima yayi kenan suna ɗan wasa a tsakaninsu"Wace ni na zama Gimbiya ai sai Mai gida ya horani,kaga ga gaban goshi nan."

Yarima yaji daɗin zuwan Bilkisu ya miƙe tsaye"Ku muje cikin gidan"

Fadawan shi suna shirin miƙewa ya tsaida su don basu gama ba.

Haka suka jera suna tafiya,kamar wasa aka cigaba da fira,amma fa banda Aymana,Bilkisu ce da Yarima,har suna abin ban dariya kamar sun daba.

Kuyanga kuwa sai mamaki take hali irin na Yarima.

Ɓangaren Hajiya sukaje,sai dai basu yi wata fira ba,gaisuwace kawai don ko fuska bata sakar mashi ba.

Bilkisu kuwa dama tana bayan su Hajiya sai dai tana da juriya da kauda kai akan abu.hakan yada bata nunawa Yarima komai ba.

A wajan Mama ne ma har ta bashi ɗan labarin yadda suka ƙagara yazo shi dai murmushi kawai yayi.

Aymana kuwa dama tun a hanya suka rabu,tayi ɓangaren Umma wadda ita ce Mahaifiyarta ita da Bilkisu.

Daga wajan Mama suka wuce gun Umma,Umma tana zaune sukayi sallama ta Amsa masu tana washe baki"Kenan babu gajiya tare dakai tunda har ka iya tashi yanzu."

"Ah Umma rana tayi fa saboda rashin tashina da wuri hakan yada ban gaishe da maimartaba ba."

Bilkisu tace"Gimbiya Aymana ce kawai tasan tafiyar shi don Jakadiya ta kirata lokacin."

Yarima ya kauda maganar ta hanyar sake gaisheta.Yar fira Yarima yayi mata,Umma taji daɗi sosai,Hakan yasa itama ta saki jiki tana tambayar shi mutanan gidansu.

Yarima yaɗan bata labarin gidansu kaɗan daga abinda yake iya baiyanawa.

Bilkisu tace"Kenan a Toro baku da wani hawa da kuke na sarauta."

"Mu kam muke hawa,duk sati ranar Alhamis akwai hawan zamiya da mukeyi musamman idan ina nan,nine ma nake shiryawa."

Umma tace"wato kana son Doki kenan."

"Sosai kuwa."

"Don Allah Yaya Yarima kayi mana anan,kaga gobe ma Alhamis."

"A'a Bilkisu a bari a shirya kafi..."

"Haba Umma wane shiri akwai duk abin buƙata."

Yarima yace"Haka kike da zumuɗi?"


Umma tayi dariya"Ai wannan tafi hakan ma.

Sun jima sosai,har Yarima baisan ya kwashi wannan lokacin a wajan Umma ba,Haka ta matsa mashi akan ya ƙara cin wani abu amma yace baya buƙata yanzu.

Bayan ya fita yaje masallaci yayi salla sai lokacin suka haɗu dasu Yarima Faruk su ka yita fira abinsu.

             ****
Cikin gidan kuwa sai gulmace gulmace ake musamman tsakanin Bayi,Fadawa,kuyangu da sauran ma'aikatan gidan,saboda Kuyangar Aymana takai labarin yadda Yarima Amin ya shaƙu da Fadawanshi dai bai nuna banbanci,har abinci yake ci dasu,suna halin Allah wadai da DARUL-BILYAM domin anan tsantsar Mulki  yake.

Lokacin da ya koma Ɓangaran su acan ya samu Aymana da tawagarta sun kawo mashi abinci,godiya yayi mata tare da faɗin"Zaku iya tafiya saboda zanyi Bacci ne yanzu." sai dai cikin kulawa yake magana.

"Ba damuwa zamu dawo zuwa anjima don tabbatar da baka buƙatar wani abun."

Yarima ya jinjina kai,don bacci ne a tare dashi kasancewar ya saba ɗanyin bacci da rana,gaya yau baiyi ba.

***
Bayan sallar isha Aymana ta na zaune ɗakin Umma ta fara jin maganganu sanarwa akan hawan da Yarima Amin zai yi wato baƙon masarautar su.Mai sanarwa yana sake maimaitawa.

Sosai ta yi Mamaki wane irin hawa zai yi haka,waye ya bashi izinin yin hawa a masarautar su.,kenan yanzu za a rinƙa yin wani abu ba tare da sanin ta ba.

Zunbur ta yi ta miƙe ta na ɗaukar wani mayafi ta na fitowa,don ba zata iya jurewa ba.



*Muje zuwa.*

*SHAFI NA UKKU*

A ƙofa ta haɗu da Hajiya ta na shirin shigowa ɓangaran,Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya Hajiya tace "Yanzu jakadiya ta ke gayamin Hawan Yarima,kenan zamu saka ido ya zama shima ya na da wani tsari a gidannan."

"Sam ba zai yiwu ba,ba zai samu wannan izinin ba."

"Ai idan bai samu ba ba za ki ji Sanarwa ba"

"Kenan Mai martaba ya bada umarni?"cewar Aymana tana zaro ido,don tasan an riga an gama tunda har Maimartaba ya bashi izini.

Hajiya ta har zuƙa"Lallai ba zamu saka ido ba,wai miyasa Maimartaba baya tunanin ko Yaron nan yazo da wani tsafine,baya tunanin ko yazo ƙara mallakar gidan nan."

"Ko ma miye nizan je gun Baba,zanyi magana dashi."Ta yi maganar tana wuce Hajiya.

Aikuwa haka akayi Aymana ta na zuwa duk mutanen ƙofar babu wanda ya tambayeta ko Lafiya za ta shiga wajan Sarki a yanzu,ganin fuskarta a ɗaure hakan ya sa Gaisuwa ce kawai ta haɗa su.

A Zaune ta samu Maimartaba,ta nemi izinin zama tare da Gaishe da shi kamar yadda ta saba,kallonta yayi tare da faɗin

"Fuskar ki babu walwala Allah ya sa ba wani ya taɓa ƴarlelena ba"

Jin yayi salon rarrashinta da bata dama hakan yasa ta samu kwarin guiwa"Akan Hawan zamiya da akace Yariman Toro zaiyi ne"

"Me ya faru da hawanne?"

"Maigirma ina ganin kamar muna sakin jiki,da kuma basu dama data wuce iyaka,ina gudun kar hakan ya..."

Bata ida ba ya katseta"Aymana har yanzu abinda baku gane ba shi zaman lafiya yafi zama ɗan sarki,Ke yafi ma sarkin kan shi,Mu zauna da Masarautun nahiyarmu lafiya shine zai bamu damar kuɓuta daga nauyin da Allah ya bamu"

"Baba amma Takobin gidanmu dake hannun su fa kenan."

"Kar a kumayi man magana akan wani abunmu dake gunsu,Sun riga sun ci gasa,hakan ya basu damar mallakar takobin gidannan."

"Amm.."

kafin ta ida ya katseta"Zaki iya tafiya,Ni da kaina na bada izinin hawa ga Yarima Amin,babu wanda ya isa ya hana,kuma babu canza baki a tare dani."

Wani irin abu Aymana taji hakan yasa ta duƙar dakai tana neman afuwa ganin fusatar da yayi.

Cikin wani irin yana yi tayi ɓangaren Hajiya acan ta samu bata nan sai dai tana ɓangaren Mama,a mamakinta duka yaran gidan suna zaune.

Ko da suka ganta basu tsaya tambaya ba,Aymana bata zaune ba ta dafa wani"Akan wani yau Sarki ya haƙiƙance mani,wannan wane irin abune."

"Me sarkin ya ce?"

"Ya ce babu makawa akan abinda ya ce?"

Ta na maganar fa juya tana fita daga ɓangaran,Sashen Umma ta nufa acan ta samu Bilkisu tana ma Umma tsarin yadda zasuyi.

Aikuwa tasha faɗa agun Aymana,Sai dai Aymana bata samu goyon bayan Umma ba,don Umma bata son wasa haka bata lamunci raini ba.

Aymana ta dafe kai tana zama"Shi kenan Umma kuyi Hakuri"

"Ni ba haƙuri na nemi ku bani ba,kuna ɗauka mutanen gidannan suna son kune komi?dole ne sai kunyi haɗin kai dasu?"

"Ni dai Allah Umma na daina kamar yadda kika buƙata." cewar Bilkisu.


Aymana ta ce"Yanzu Umma akan hakane kike wanann abin?taya zamu bar wasu can su taka masarautarmu?"

Yar dariya Umma tayi"Ga ki Babba amma har yanzu kanki yana maki rawa,ke duk soyayyar da Maimartaba yake maki kina ɗauka mutanen gidannan suna farin ciki ne?"

Aymana ta miƙe tana fitowa,sashen su ta nufa don hutawa,ita sam bata saba da wannan hayaniyar ba.

A ɓangaren yarima kuwa ya ɗan zuba ido zuwan Aymana da mutanen sai dai ankawo mashi abinci banda ita,sannan kuma bai tambayi inda take ba.

           *****
Tun da ta tashi da safe ta fito gidan tsaye take ana mashi shirin abinci,sauri take don tana son zuwa gunshi,saboda ta tambaye shi abinda zaya iya buƙata a wajen hawan.

Kuyangartace ta shigo wajan girka abincin,tana sallama tare da faɗin "Ranki shi daɗe ina da magana."

Aymana ta kalleta tana juyawa"Ku ci gaba kina zuwa."

Wajen farfajiya suka fito"Uwar ɗakina akwai matsala,Naga Hajiya ta aiki Jakadiya ta biyu cikin gari."

"Me hakan ke nufi?"cewar Aymana

"Jiya naji suna faɗar Baƙon nan bazaiyi hawaba,idan ma yayi bazai sauko lafiya ba."

Zaro ido Aymana tayi,ta dafe kai"Maza kira min Bilkisu ina ɓangaren Umma."

Acan suka haɗu Aymana ta gayawa Umma Abinda ya faru,Umma tace"Lallai ku gayawa Yarima Amin kar yayi hawa yau"

Bilkisu tace"Ina gudun suyi mashi yadda sukayiwa sarkin yaki."

Aymana ta miƙe "bamuda lokacin ɓatawa ya zama dole mu dakatar da Yarima"

Fita su kayi da sauri suna nufar ɓangaren yarima Amin,Abisa mamakin su sai suka samu baya nan ance ya shiga cikin gari.

Hakan ya ɗaga hankalinsu sosai,Bilkisu ta kalli Aymana  tana tambayarta yadda zasuyi.

Aymana ta juya tana dafe kai,saika kuyangu sun shigo da kayan abincin Yarima.Wata irin gigitacciyar tsawa ta daka masu tare da korasu,har saida ɗaya cikin su tayi zubar da kayan marmarin dake hannunta.


"Zan kuma komawa don neman alfaramar sarki,wanann lokacin ba zamu bari a cutar da wani ba"

Wata irin kora Maimartaba yayiwa Aymana,don duk tunanin shi bata da wani dalilin da ya wuce gaba,ranshi ya ɓaci sosai akanta.

Umma ta samu tana kuka"Yanzu haka zamu bari ayi Hawannan A cutar da wani."


Umma tace "kuyi tunani?"

"Ba zamu bari Jakadiyya ta biyu ta shigo gidannan ba har sai an gama hawannan,Haka kuma ba kowane zai shigo gidannan ba har sai an gama Hawa."

Bilkisu ta miƙe "taso muje"

Umma tace"Kar kuyi gaggawa,ku bari sai gab za a fara don kar su ankara.
      ****
Aymana da kanta ta shiga filin dake gidan ganye na cikin gidan anan ta sa ana gyrawa za ayi Hawan,kowa yayi mamaki ganin ba anan aka saba yin wani hawan al'adaba a gidan.

komi aka tsarashi cikin tsari na alfarma,acewarta jar yarima ya raina masarautar su yayi tunanin basu da kayan Ado.

Shi kuwa Yarima yaje gun wani abokin shine a cikin gari,don zaman gidan ma yaɗan dame shi.
   
          *****
Ƙarfe Ukku yahau hanyar dawowa a lokacin yana da sauran Awa ɗaya tak wadda zai shirya don yin hawa.

Cikin Mamaki ya ke kallon gidan an gyara anyi kwalliyar sarauta sosai da abubuwan ado,amma ƙofofin gidan rufe yake.

Haka su ka tsaya suna jiran abasu umarnin shiga,Amma basu samu ba.

Sai dai an sanar dasu ta ƙofar bayane zasu iya shiga saboda Aymana ta Hana kowa shiga gidan yanzu.

Bilal abokin Yarima ya kalleshi yace"Dama ana hana shiga masarauta ba tare da sanarwa ba."

Taɓe baki yayi"Ina tunanin su suna yin hakan,amma bakaji wacce aka ce ta hana ba?"

"Wacece Aymana?"

Shiru yayi mashi ganinta a tsaye a ƙofa da kuyangu zagaye da ita.

Hakan ya ɗan ɓata ran yarima a karo na farko,Shi kan shi baisan lokacin da ya haɗe raiba.

Ya kalli Billal"Mu tsaya anan."

Tsaida mota yayi Yarima ya buɗe ya fito cikin kamala da taƙamar sarauta,Aymana ta kalle shi yana ma fadawanshi magana da suka fito a motarsu.

Aymana ta matsa gun Yarima tana wa fadawan magana"Ko zaku iya bamu waje?"

Yarima ya kalleta"Zaki iya magana ba sai sun bar wajan ba"

Aymana yau taga kamakar Sarauta a tare da shi,hakan yasa ta juyar da kai"Muna shirin Hawane naga kamar ka taushe hannu"

"Lokaci zai ishe ni shiryawa an..."

kafin ya ida Aymana ta ɗan ja baya tana ɗaure fuska,Yarima kuwa baisan Aymana tana tsaron lafiyar shi bane.

A ƙafa zasu ida takawa zuwa ciki,sai ga Bilkisu ta fito,a bisa mamakinta sai taga yarima ya sakar mata fuska suna shiga ciki.

Har kofa takaishi,suka shiga shida Bilal fadawanshi kuma suka dakata daga farfajiyar wajan.

Aymana ta ba wa masu aikin Umarnin hana kowa shiga gidan daga lokacin har dare,sai da izininta,wanda ya saɓa kuwa sai haɗu da hukuncinta.

Zuwa tayi ta kwashi kayan da ta tanada domin shirin yarima kama daga Shadda,kayan hawan doki kayan kwalliyar jiki da takalmi,Agogo da rawani komai an haɗa mashi.

Itace gaba zuwa ɓangarran a falon farko ta tsaya ta ga yana waya hakan yasa ta dakata tare da nunawa ma'aikatan su aje akan kujerun ɗakin.

Yarima yayi bankwana tana tsinke wayar tare da mai da hankali kanta"Wannan kayan fa?"

"Sune zakayi amfani dasu wajan Hawan,zaka iya dubawa idan akwai wani abun da kake buƙata"

Ɗan murmushi yayi"Duk na haɗa kayan da zanyi amfani"

"Da wannan ne za ka yi amfani."

Za yayi magana Ai mana ta kalli ma'aikatan zaku iya jirana a ƙofa.fita sukayi.

Bilal ya kallesu duka biyun"Kai ka saka wanda tace tund..."

"Na riga na fidda wanda zan saka"

"Shi kenan zaka iya saka wanda yayi maka,amma kayi komai a hankali,sannan kaji tsoron wasu masarautun da ba naku ba"

Tana maganar tana juyawa,binta yayi da kallo,yana miƙewa tsaye,Bilal zaiyi magana,yarima ya dakatar dashi.

Ƙarfe huɗu kowa na gidan ya halarci Gidan ganye,ma zaunan da aka tana 
da ya gewaye wajan,kowa a wadace,a lokacin harmasu kiɗa da busa sun fara,ga tambura ana dokawa.

Hajiya,Mama da mutanansu suna zaune a nasu ɓangaran.

Yaran sarki su Yarima Shureim duk suna nasu ɓangaran, kuyangu,bayi da fadawa kowane ya samu waje,saidai wasu a zaune wasu a tsaye.

Ya rage Mai martaba ne da Yarima amin ake jira,sai kuwa Gimbiya Aymana wacce take ta shiryawa kamar itace ta shirya Hawan tun farko.

*SHAFI NA HUDU. 4*

*Sadaukarwa ga Mum Sayyed & Noor ina jin daɗin yadda ki ke posting littafin Masarauta.💖💖💖*

Yarima kuwa shiga ya yi irinta yaran sarakan nahiyar,bai saka kayan da Aymana ta bashi ba,tun a ƙofar ɓangaren ya hau dokin shi sai faɗawa dake jan linzami.

Haka suka nufi wajan taron,Dai-dai lokacin Aymana ta na kan zama saman kujerar da aka tanada dominta.Chak taja ta tsaya don kallon shigowar Yarima Amin,ayau yayimata kalar Sarauta sosai shigar ta burgeta duk da taji babu daɗi ganin bai saka nata kayan ba.

Murmushi tayi tasa hannu ta ɗan gyara Alƙebbar jikin ta,Bilkisu ta matso"Kin ga ɗan gayun Yarima ko?"

murmushi ta kumayi mai nuna isa tana riƙo hannun Bilkisu.anan aka sanar da zaman Aymana sannan Yarima Amin.

Sai dai yace yana jiran zuwan maimartaba kamin zaman shi,Yana kan faɗa sai ga Sarki ya shigo da zagagen shi,ana mashi kirari.

Yarima ya sauko yana nufa gun Sarki anan ya kai gaisuwa,Sarki ya miƙa mashi hannu,shi kam yarima baya iya haɗa hannu da Manyan shi hakan yasa ya ƙara sunkuyar da kai.

"Fatan komi ya kammala."

"InshaAllah yanzu za a fara"

"Allah ya bada sa'a"

yana niyar tashi sai ga Aymana ta zube gaban sarki don gaishe shi"Aymana shiri yayi Allah yayi maki Albarka"

"Ameen Baba"

A tare suka miƙe yana nufar tsakiyar filin yayin data koma kan kujerarta,Yarima yana hawa dokin aka faɗi cewar Zai fara zamiyane ga Gimbiya kafin Sarki.

Aymana ta fara kallon mutanan wajan dake kirari suna kiɗe kiɗe.

Can ƙarshen fili ya koma Yarima ya gilgiza linzamin doki yana ƙara daidaita sirdi.

kafin kace mi,dokin ya harzuƙa ya fara sukuwa,ya na sassarfa,dokin ya fara gudu yana gudu idan ka gani zakayi tunanin Yarima zai faɗo,da gudu dokin ya nufi Wajan Aymana,a tunanin kowa Aymana zata razana,amma Sai miƙewa tsaye da tayi tana gangarowa tana tunkarar dokin.

ihu aka saka,Dokin yayi wani irin kuka yana ɗaga hafa kamar zaya haye Aymana.wata irin zamewa sukayi daidai lokacin Yarima ya zare wata wuƙa yana tilli da ita zama.

Ga mamakinsu Dokin ya tsaya wuƙar ta dawo hannun Yarima,kiɗa da busa aka soma,Yarima ya sauko yana miƙa dokin hannun wani bafade.

Haɗa ido sukayi da Aymana.Murmushi tayi hakan shima nashi ɓangaren.

Ya juya yana ɗaga hannuwa sama.yayi tattaki.

Hajiya da Mama suka kalli juna basuyi tunanin Zai sauko kan dokin lafiya ba,Jakadiya ta biƙe haɓa"To ko dai shima da abinda ya taka?"

Shi kuwa Yarima wajan zama ya nufa,ya dan zauna kadan ana gudanar da wasu shagulgulan,ya mike ya nufi cikin gida bai jima ba ya dawo da shigar kayan da Aymana ta kai mashi.

Ya k'ara yin kyau sosai kowa ya san yarima akwai gayu,ba b'ata lokaci ya kumayin zamiya ga Mai martaba.

Kowa abin ya burge shi.

Sai da aka fara kiran sallar magriba aka tashi,hakan yasa kowa ya wuce.

        ***
Washe gari Aymana bata je gun shi ba,saboda tsananin gajiya,mutanan gidan sunji dad'in zuwan yarima koba komai sun samu sauk'i daga bangaran mulki irin na Aymana don yanzu sai su wuni basu ganta ba.

Da marece Yarima ya b'angaren Kaka wato mahaifiyar Maimartaba,fira suke sosai Kaka tace"Gaskiya idan ka tafi zamuyi kewarka"

"Nima haka nake tunani zanyi kewarku fiye da yadda za ku yi"

Za ta yi magana Bilkisu ta shigo"Na yi tunanin kana d'akin Umma naje tace baka Shiga ba."

"Daga wajan Sarki nayo wajan Kaka."

"Ta nan tana maka surutu da tsegumi da fad'a ko."

"Jini da Yarnema,ni ce mai tsegumin,yaushe rabon da in ganki d'akin nan ma."

Yarima yayi dariya"Ki barta so ta ke tayi tsokana shiyasa"

Kaka ta gyara zama"Barta yanzu in korata"

Bilkisu zatayi magana sai ga wata Baiwa ta shigo,ta gaishe su tare da matsawa wajan Kaka,Bilkisu ta ce"Lafiya kuwa?"

"A'a dama Gimbiya ce ta turoni in duba Yariman Toro,ta je ba ya nan."

Yarima ya kalli agogon dake sak'ale hannunshi,Bilkisu tace"Je ki ce gaya nan b'angaran?"

Ta mik'e Aymana ta maida hankali gunshi"K'ila abincinka aka kai?"

"Zai iya yuwwa hakan."

Kaka ta ce"Lallai ka shigo gidan nan da sashen dama,wato Ja'irar yarinyarnan ce take neman ka."

Dariya yayi,Bilkisu zata yi magana sai ga Aymana da mutananta.

"Za ku iya jirana a k'ofa"

Far sun juya Aymana tace"Farida ki kawo mana abin motsa baki,kar ki wuce minti Ukku."

Cikin sauri zata juya yarima yace"Farida ko?"

Kuyangar ta juyo ta maida hankali gunshi"Na ga waje akwai rana,ki ce masu su tafi kawai Gimbiya zata nemesu idan tana buk'atar wani abun."

"To ranka shidad'e."

"Ke kuma kibi a hankali kar kiyi saurin da zai sa ki zubar da abinda kika d'auko"

Anan bata bada Ansa ba don ta san dole tabi Umarnin uwar d'akinta.

Yarima ya juya yana kallon Aymana wanda take fad'in "Sannunku da hutawa?"

Ta matsa wajan Kaka ta durk'usa"Kaka sannu da gida,ina fatan kun wuni lafiya."

"Ki na so kiga na wuni lafiya amma baki zuwa gaishe ni."

Dariya tayi sosai har sauti yana fita,Da sauri yarima ya kalleta tunda yazo sai dai yaga murmushinta amma ba dai Dariya irin haka ba.

"Ai Kinga abin da yake hananu zuwa irin...."

"Tafi can,dama bakiyi niya ba"

"To yanzu dai ayi hak'uri"

"Bani yin hak'urin ga Yarima nan kullum sai ya shigo amma..."

"kaka tunda ta bada hak'uri ayi hak'urin" cewar yarima yana 'yar dariya.

Bilkisu ta ce"Kai kuwa ka barsu,kayi kallo."

Aymana ta juyo kanta"To Kaka kinmaji yarinyar nan so take daga kanmu"

Dariya kaka tayi"Barta ai na fasa fad'an,tana fama da kai kamar na k'adangare"

Gaba d'aya sukayi dariya,Aymana ta mik'e tana komawa kan kujera,ta kalli yarima"Tun d'azo nake duba ka kum..."

"Ina nan."

"To sannu da hutawa,fatan baka buk'atar wani abun?"

Yanzu yarima yad'an fara fahimtar Aymana,ita kawai raini ne bataso daga mutaten gidan,amma idan ita da mai wani muk'amine zata saukar da kanta.

Kallon shi kawai take ganin kamar yana tunani,ganin zai juyo tayi saurin maida hankalinta kan wayar hannunta.

"Ina nan ina  cewa idon yaron nan ya tafi sai munji babu dad'i." Cewar Kaka dake kallon Aymana.

Shiru tayi mata"Ba ki ji na ne?"

"Uhmm haka ne Kaka."

"Ai zamu tambayi Sarki mu ma muje Toro mu..."

Cikin sauri Aymana ta kalli Bilkisu,Yarima kuma ya kalleta"Da naji dad'in zuwanki Bilkisu."

"Ai ko bai barku juwa ba ni zan sa shi ya barku"

Kuyanga ta shigo da kayan lambu akan tire babba ta nufi gun Gimbiya.

"A'a can zaki ajiye,ni Ayaba kawai nake buk'ata"

Ajewa tayi tana d'aukar Ayaba,ta koma kun Aymana,ta na b'are mata bayan Aya.

Aymana ta amsa ta na kaiwa baki.Farida ta kalli Bilkisu tace"Uwar d'akina in b'are maki naki ne"


"A'a zata yi da kanta,ki tafiyar ki kawai."

Farida ta juya kan Aymana"Zan iya tafiya."

"An ba ki umarni kuma sai kin kuma tambayata raini ne wannan komi?"

Tana magana yana d'an tasowa alamar fad'a"Kenan idan nace ki tsaya shi ba zaki bi nashi umarnin ba"tana magana cikin zuciya.

"Ki yi hakuri Gim..."

"Dalla b'ace min da gani."

Mik'ewa tayi,dai-dai lokacin Yarima ya kalli Bilkisu "Idan bance ta barshi ba kema za a b'are makine?"

"A'a"

"Ya fi kyau ki san abinda zaki ci yana da muhimmanci,musamman kayan lambu,baki san me ta tab'a ba kafin shigowarta"

Aymana ta kalli Ayabar hannunta,sai taji bata son ci don ita kanta bata son k'azanta.mik'ewa tayi ta aje kan tire din da babu komai.

Kowa yayi mamaki,Yarima yaso k'ara magana akan abinda tayiwa Farida sai dai kuma baya so taga ya ciki shiga shirginta,hakan yasa ya Barta sai wani lokacin.


****

Zuwan Yarima Amin da yan kwanakin da yayi ya fara sauya komai na gidan musamman agun ma'aikata da wanda suke barori a gidan

Yarima har zama yake dasu yanajin buk'atun su,wani abun zasuce Aymana ce take da ikon kawowa a gidan amma bata kawoba.

Ya fahimci itace take komai,sai dai kuma bata ba Talakawanta damar fad'an muradin su,bata da lokacin zama gunsu.

*SHAFI NA BIYAR. 5*

*SADUKARWA GA Mrs S. Waziri.*

Yau zaman su a fadar mai martaba ne,wata ƙaramar fada da yake zama da mutanen gidanshi,sai dai babu wanda yake magana kowanne da abubuwan da yake tunani,Yarima Amin ya na gefen sarki, Aymana tana nesa dasu,Bilkisu kuwa tana gun Umma suna dan magana jefi-jefi.

Hajiya da Mama kowane yana nazari akan zaman Yarima Amin da maimartaba,gabaɗaya sun kasa fahimtar yadda Maimartaba yake son zama da Yarima a yanzu duk wata kulawar da yake ba yaranshi maza ya koma kan Yarima Amin.

Shi kuwa Mai martaba a bisa zaman da yayi da Amin ya fahimci asalin kyawun hali da ɗabi'u irin na shi musamman akan na ƙasa da shi.

"Zuwa dare ina son ganin ka a ɗakina."

Yarima Amin ya kalle shi cikin ɗan razana don ya san tunda yazo gidan bai taɓa shiga cikin sashen sarki ba balle har ɗaki.

"To in sha Allah Baba."

Mai martaba Ya miƙe yan kallon gimbiya Aymana ita ɗinma shi take kallo,murmushi yayi hakan ya bata damar miƙewa tsaye don yi mashi rakiya.

Sauran mutanen wajen kuwa,sauka lafiya suka yi mashi.

Umma ta miƙe tana barin wajan tare da faɗin "Na barku lafiya." 

Wasu daga cikinsu sun amsa sai dai wasu sun bita da kallon ko in kula.

Yarima Amin kuwa ya tashi zuwa ɓangaren shi,yayin da ya masu bankwana cikin ladabi.

Anan fa suka buɗe babin cigaba da gulmace-gulmace da maganganun nuna tsana akan Yarima.

Hajiya ta ce"Ya zama lalle mu san abin yi tun wuri,don naga wankin hula yan neman kaimu dare."

"Yarima nan yana gab da komawa mafifici a gidannan"cewar Mama da ke gyara zama.

Yarima Shuraim ya ce"Ki bar komai hannu na da kanshi zai tattara ya koma don ba zan laminta,ina mai jiran gado in koma ɗan kallo daga nesa ba."

       ****
Da yamma  Sarki ne zaune da Umma tana zuba mashi shayi a kofi,a duk cikin matan shi Allah ya gani ya fi son Umma,domin Soyayyar ne ya shafi Aymana,saboda sauƙin hali,da ba abu baya,sam ita babu ruwanta da shiga shirgin da ba nata ba.

"Gimbiya ina so muyi wata magana da ke?"

Ta miƙa mashi kofi tana faɗin"Ina jinka rankaya daɗe."

Murmushi yayi tare da tashi zaune daga kishingiɗe da yake"Me kika fahimta kan yaron nan Yariman Toro."

"Wajen me kenan."

"Halaiya da kuma ɗabi'u."

"Yaro ne mai ganin girman mutane ga sanin darajar al'umma, kafin zuwansa banyi tunanin zamu same shi a haka ba..."

"Shi kenan barni nan,dama na saba jin bakinki yana faɗin alkhairan mutane"

Yar dariya tayi"Kenan baka yadda ba,to ka tuhumi fadawa da sauran mutanen gidan Ni dai nasan...

"Ina son ba shi Auren 'yata Aymana na..."

Cikin yar razana ta ɗago"Shi yace maka..."

"Ni ne nake son haɗa auren"

"A gani na idan bashi yayi maganar ba kar mu fara,ganin yadda zamani ya canza" tayi maganar cikin sanyin murya don tasan bata isa sauya ra'ayinsa ba, domin ya bata haƙƙinta ne na mahaifiya.

"Ina son Aymana,ina son ganin ta zauna hannun nagari,Soyayyar da nakewa Aymana wani lokaci na kanji dama Namiji ne da nan da lokaci ƙanƙani zan sauka na bata karagar mulki na."

Umma ta ɗanyi shiru,tare da zurfafa tunani idan bata amince ba waye zai auri Aymana wanda suke ganin zata samu kulawa,dama kyan ɗiyar sarki ta zama matar sarki ko da wata ranane.

"Ya zamu yi da maganganun mutanen gidannan,ina tsoron gabar dake tsakanin mu ta saka rauni..."

"Wai har yanzu kuna ganin akwai gaba a tsakanin mu,Mutanen nan fa gasar shekara suka ci,hakan ya sa aka basu Takobin gidan nan,abun da ya wuce tun shekara da shekaru shi kanshi Babana Labari ya samu balle ni."

"Me Kaka zata ce idan taji zancen nan."

"Ki bar komai a hannuna,ina son fita haƙƙin kine na mahaifiyar yarinyar nan."

"Na amince"

***

Cikin Marece saida Mai martaba yabi ɗakunan manyan gidan irinsu Mahaifiyar sa wanda suke kira da Nene,da kaka ya basu shawara tare da sanar dasu.

Kaka harda Yar rawa"Wallahi abinda nake guri kenan,sai dai bani so ace na cika kawo abinda ba a amince da shi ba,Ai Aminu yaron kirki ne,ga sanin darajar manya."

Sai dai inda aka samu matsala wajen Mahaifiyar Sarki,domin Nene mace ce mai ra'ayin riƙau,duk yadda yayi don fahimtar da ita ya kasa,haka suka tashi shi yana kan ra'ayin shi ita kuma tana kan nata.

***

Ɓangaren Aymana kuwa ba ta san abinda ke faruwa ba,tana cen don haɗa abincin dare na Yarima,babu abinda ya dame ta, gurin ta ayi mashi kalolin abinci don bata son yaga kamar basu da wani abun a gida.

Umma kuwa harta fara shedawa Bilkisu"Umma ko kinsan tun ranar hawan nan,nayi sha'awar ganin Aymana da Yarima Amin,Allah sun dace."

"Ni kaina nayi ra'ayin sai dai ina godiya ga Allah daya kawo abin cikin sauƙin."

"Bari na gaya mata."

"A'a sam karki kuskura."

***

Ƙarfe takwas Aymana ta shiga ɓangaren Yarima ita da kuyangunta,yau ba shi ɗaya bane harda abokinshi Bilal,ta ga ta san fuskar shi,sai da tayi tunanin sannan ta tuna shi ne wanda suka shigo ranar da akayi Hawa.

Bayan amsa sallama Aymana ta ce"Sannun ku da gida."

"Ina wuni Yarima ya bata amsa."

Wannan shi ne karo na biyu da ya gaisheta,azuciyarta ta ce baza a kuma ba,ta ma rasa abin cewa hakan yasa ta ce"Baƙo gare ka ne?"

"Eh."ya bata amsa ta juya tana faɗin"Yau ma sai ance ku ajiye"

Cikin sauri suka hau jera abincin,tare da neman izinin komawa ida kwaso wani.

Bilal ya kalleta yace"Ina jin Gimbiya Aymana ashe da rabon in ganta."

Ɗan tsuke fuska tayi, Yarima ya kalle ta"Ka ga Aymana."

"Uhmm" ta ce ta saka hannu Aljihun doguwar rigarta,ta fiddo wayarta tana fara dannawa.

"Da kin sanar da ba a kawo abincin nan ba,yaufa mutane na sun shiga gari,abincin yayi yawa."

"Idan ka gama sai a mayar."

Bilal ya kalli Yarima"ka ce zaka shiga cikin gida kuma."

"Au ka ganni ko,kiran Maimartaba ne dole in shiga,da ba ka tunamin ba bansan ya kenan ba"

Ya juya yana kallon ta"Kin san me za'ayi?"

Yana maganar yana saka hula tare da takalmin, Tsayawa tayi tana kallon shigar shi,wani farin yadine ɗinkin riga da wando rigar iyakarta guiwa, babu aiki jikin kayan sai wani maɓallai masu launin ja dake jere a tsakiyar gaban rigar zaka iya hangar singileti fara dake ciki,hannun lins ne.
Hular daya aza ta ƙara fiddo asalin kyawun fuskar.

Sauri tayi ta kauda kai "A'a"

"Ko akai abincin a ɗakin Kaka zanje can na ci,Yanzu Maimartaba yake son gani na."

"Abokin ka fa?"

"Zai zauna jirana ai"

Yana maganar yana bi ta gefen ta,akan kujera ya ɗauki wata jar rigar Jabba yana azawa akan kayan,sai ya ida komawa jinin sarauta ko wani baƙon matashin  malamin addinin Muslunci.

Harɗe hannuwa tayi tare da binshi da kallo,Bilal kuma ita yake kallo ganin zata juyo yayi saurin kauda kai.

Aymana ta maya bayan Yarima,sai dai ta bada umarni kamar yadda Yarima ya buƙata,ɗakin ta ta nufa don shirin bacci.

Yarima lokacin da ya isa Maimartaba yana zaune hakan yasa ya gane ya ɗan jima yana sauraren zuwan shi,cikin ladabi ya durkusa,yana gaisuwa.
"Ka zauna Yarima fatan ka wuni lafiya."

"Ina neman afuwar rashin zuwana akan lokaci."

Sarki baiyi magana ba sai dai zama da ya gyara yana faɗin"Aminu na kiraka ne don sanar da kai irin farin cikin zuwan ka da nayi da kuma kyawun halinka, nayi ma mutanen gidan nan sha'awar ace sune suke da hali irin na Masarautar ku."

"Mun gode Baba"

Gyaran murya Sarki ya kuma yii"Saboda hakan na yanke wani hukunci ba tare da sanar da kai ba,ko neman izininka."

Yarima ya ɗan jinjina ki"Kana da ikon Hukunci akan duk wanda yake ƙarƙashin masarautar nan,balle ni Baba,Ina jin ku kamar manyan gidanmu."

"Ina son baka Auren 'yata Aymana Yarima."

Cikin firgici Yarima Amin ya ɗago sam bai taɓa tunanin wannan shi ne abin da zai fito bakin shi ba"Ban saka ka akan dole ba Aminu,amma kana da ikon Zaɓa ko faɗar ra'ayinka akai"

Yarima kuwa tuni ya shiga tunanin halin da ya baro gidansu yadda suke son ganin ya fiddo mata don yin aure,a zaman shi na ƙarshe da mahaifiyar shi sun tashi akan zata zaɓa mashi tunda ba abinda ya sa gaba ba kenan.




*Mu je zuwa*

*Haliloss ɗin ku ce*

*SHAFI NA SHIDDA. 6*

Tunani kawai yake, gyaran muryar da Sarki yayi shi ne sanadiyar dawowar Yarima Amin cikin hankalin sa"Ina jin ka ko kana ganin na baka lokaci don yin nazari akan magana ta?"

"A'a Baba ai wannan hukunci ne ka yanke akaina,wane tunani kuma bayan naka?Na Amince,kuma zan bi umarninka kamar yadda zanbi umarnin Sarkin Toro."

Wani farin ciki ya ziyarci zuciyar Sarki"Naji daɗi Aminu,Allah yayi maka Albarka,zan nemi Babanka na sanar mashi da kaina."

Sunkuyar da kai yayi,sosai ya ƙarajin nauyin Maimartaba yanzu"Za ka iya tafiya,Allah yayi mana jagora."

Yarima ya kuma sunkuyawa cikin ladabi"Na gode Baba"

Murmushi kawai Maimartaba yake yi,shi kuwa da kyal ya iya miƙewa yana ɗan dafe ƙirjin shi dake bugawa da ƙarfi,yana fita ɗakin yayi cikin gidan.

A mamakin shi anan ya fara ganin gungun mutane sosai ranshi ya bashi maganganun da suke akan auren shi ne da Aymana.

Yarima kasa wucewa ɓangaren Kaka yayi don ba shi da wani kuzarin hakan.

Akan kujera ya samu Bilal ya ɗan fara bacci ajiyar zuciyar shi ce ta tashi Bilal ɗin.

"Wai ka dawo ban sani ba?"

Bai bashi ansa ba ya cire rigar Jabbar dake saman kayan,kan kujera ya faɗa yana dafe kai.

"Me ke faruwa naganka kamar a hargitse?"

"Kama ce ma?"

"Na ga ka fita lafiya lau amma ka dawo a haka."

Yarima ya rufe ido yana buɗewa"dole ne,taya zan ɓullowa lamarin auren Aymana a lokacin da mutanan gidan nan..."

Bai jira ya ida ba"Auren Aymana?"

"Maimartaba ne ya ce ya bani  aurenta,tare da zaɓi idan bana ra'ayi na faɗa mashi"

"To me ka ce mashi."

"Kana tunanin zan iya musu da shi,na ce na amince amma wal..."

"Amma me? Ai shi kenan zance ya ƙare sai mu shirya biki domin kuwa..."

"Bilal kasan kuwa mutanen gidan nan yadda suke."

"Mutanen gidanne zaka aura ko Aymana?"

"Ita ɗin ma nasani,kuma nasan ba zata amince ba."

"Ni fa tun zuwanta naga dacewar ku"

Yarima ya kauda kai yana miƙewa tsaye"Matsala ta da kai ana maganar gaske kana sako wasa"yayi maganar yana shigewa ciki.

****

Aymana bata san abinda ke faruwa ba,sai washe gari kuma duk gidan an rasa wanda zai tunkare ta da maganar,har ta gama shirya kayan karin Yarima.

Bata same shi a falon ba sai fadawan shi da sukace ya na shiryawa ne.

Fitowa tayi ta nufi ɗakin Kaka,Kaka ta rangwaɗa guɗa"Na kusa aurar dake in huta da zuwa kwasar min abin..."

"Waye za kiyiwa auren?"

"Ke mana,ba ki da labari?"

"Kaka kenan yau kuma da wannan tsokanar kika tashi,bari inje in dawo mu ida maganar"tana maganar tana yin hanyar fita.

"Kin dai kaima angon naki abinci ko?"

Wani irin juyi Aymana tayi"Me kike ce Kaka?"

"Angon ki Yariman Toro,gaki Gimbiya ga shi Yarima"

Aymana tayi tatttaki zuwa wajen ta"kibari karma yaji don Allah hakan zai zubar da..."

"Ai Maimartaba ma ya faɗi mashi."

Hanyar ƙofa tayi tana sauri,karo sukayi da Hajiya"Gimbiya kinji abinda Sarki yayi?"

"Kar ki ce min da gaske ne Hajiya?"

Hajiya ta dafe kai ta jingina da wani bango"Ai bansan mi Sarki yake shirin yiba,taya zai ba da Auren ki ga Yariman Toro,ashe duk Soyayyar da yake cewa yana maki a baki ne kawai?"

"Haba Hajiya wannan fa ba gaskiya bane?"

"Aymana wallahi duk mutanen gidan nan kowa ya sani kuma..."

Kafin ta ida Kaka ta fito"Kedai bakiji daɗi ba,yanzu hure mata kunnuwa zaki yi don baƙin ciki"

Aymana ta sara kai tayi sashen mahaifiyar ta tun kafin ta shiga take kwalla kiran Umma,Umma ta ce"Wannan wane irin kirane Gimbiya?"

Zama tayi dirshen a gabanta"Wai Baba ya bada aure na ga..."

"Yanzu wannan shi ne dalilin kike min wannan kiran,maganar da tun jiya aka gama ta."

"Haba Umma wai ba ku so na ne ko mi?"

"Soyayyar kenan Aymana,Sarki ya zaɓa maki Aminu a matsayin miji,kuma ni kaina na amince"

Aymana zata miƙa  Umma ta riƙo hannunta"Yarima shi ne muji da ya dace da rayuwar ki,shi ne mutumin da zai kula dake fiye da tunanin ki"

Sai lokacin Aymana taji hawaye na bin kuncinta"Umma don Allah kar ku ce haka"

Rarrashinta Umma ta fara yi cikin kalamai masu daɗi,sai dai sam bata ɗauka don tana ganin ko da za ayi mata auren dole to ba dai da Yarima ba.

Ko da Aymana ta bar wajan Umma ɗakin Maimartaba ta nufa sai dai ance mata yana wajan Nene mahaifiyar shi.

Hakan yasa ya nufi ɗakin cikin dakewar zuciya,chak ta tsaya tana sauraron maganganun sarki.

"Na riga na yanke hukunci,kiyi hakƙuri Nene,amma wata rana da kanku zaku ji daɗin haɗin nan,Ina da tabbacin Aymana ba zata tozarta ba kamar yadda kuke tunani."

"Wai kana ɗauka auren Yariman ne kawai mafita,kenan babu wani mai halin kirki sai shi?"

"Ina so taje inda aka san darajarta"

"Ba fa zan amince ba."

Sarki ya miƙe yasan halinta,bayaso su cika gardama,baiyi mamakin ganin Aymana tana sharar kuka ba.

Kamo hannunta yayi suka koma ɗakin Nene"Naso ace nine na fara gaya maki maganar Auren ki Aymana"

"Don Allah Baba kar ka"

"Ba na so ki saka kanki wahala Aymana, Yarima kamar ya zama mijinki,indai ina da rai"

"Baba ka..."

"Ba ki son shi ne?"

Shiru tayi ta kasa magana"kiyi Addu'a akan samun nasarar lamarin,amma ni dai ina maki sha'awar hakan Aymana,inason ganin ki a farin ciki,ina so na aurer dake inda ba zaki tozarta ba."

"Akwai wanda ya isa tozarta jinin sarki"cewar Nene dake gyara zama.

"Don Allah Nene ki barni nayi magana da ita"

"Kinsan bana magana biyu ki ɗauka anyi angama"

Yana maganar yana miƙewa yabar masu ɗakin wani kuka Aymana ta saka tana fita itama.

Duk wanda ya ganta sai dai ya bata hanya yana ƙara waiwayenta,cikin lokaci kaɗan ta fita hayyacinta.

****

Yana gama karyawa ya ɗauko wayar shi,danna wa yayi yana kiran Ummi wato mahaifiyar shi.

Ƙanwarshi Saratu ta ɗauka"Yaya mutanen Darul-Bilyam"

Murmushi yayi ya miƙe ya koma kan kujera"Ina Ummi"

"Ga ta"tana maganar ta miƙa mata.

Ko gaisuwa baiyi ba ya ce"Ran Ummi ya daɗe,kin kusa zama Ummin gaske."

"Au da ni ta wasa ce"

"Za ki ƙara yawan yara?"

"Me hakan yake nufi?"

"To bandai sani ba,Yarima dai ya samo mata"

Dariya tayi tana faɗin "shiririta,wato don kaga abinda nake magana kenan shi ne kace haka"

"Uhmm Ummi ki shirya tarbar suruka Wallahi"

Da farko tayi tunanin wasa yake,sai da Yarima ya kwashe  komai ya gaya wa Ummi,Ummi ta ce"kai Yarima harka amince,kasan bana son abinda zai taɓa min kai?"

"Ummi yaron ki kika sani,itama anaji da ita fa"anan ya bata labarin Aymana a gidan sai dai ya ɓoye wasu halayya nata shi kanshi bai san dalilin Hakan ba.

"To Aminu Allah ya tabbatar da Alkhairi,agaishe da 'ya ta"

Sun jima suna fira Yarima ya miƙe don fitowa waje,shi kanshi baya son haɗuwa da mutanen gidan.

****

Aymana kuwa gari yayi mata zafi,ko wane ɓangare taje babu daɗi,musamman gun su Mama da Hajiya,domin wasu hujjoji suke bata akan an cutar da ita idan har aka haɗata da Yarima Amin.

Umma da Kaka kuwa suna nuna mata gaskiya akan hakan.

Har dare bata ci komai ba,sai ma ɗaki data shige ta rufe kanta.Haka Bilkisu ta sameta sai dai ta kasa yi mata magana,sai kuka da take yi.

Ita kanta Bilkisu taji babu daɗi kuma ta tausayawa Aymana,amma ita kanta tana son auran.

"Yanzu Gimbiya kuka zaki rinƙa yi?wallahi ina da tabbacin zakiji daɗin zama da Yarima"

"Bilkisu don Allah kada muyi haka bani son Auren haɗin nan,taya zanje gidan su Yarima Amin amatsayin suruka,mutanen da su kansu sun san ba mu ra'ayin su"

"Har yanzu ba kida wata hujja,amma..."

"Kina nufin wannan ba hujja ba ce?"

"Ina so ki fahimci yanzu fa babu inda zakije ayi maki wulaƙanci kefa ƴar sarki ce,yanzu baki yiwa kanki sha'awa zama matar sarki?"

Aymana ta juya kwanciyarta"ki ja min ƙofa idan kin fita bana son ƙara jin baki ki.

Bilkisu bata kuma magana ba,ta fice wajan Yarima Amin ta nufa,sosai yaji daɗin zuwanta fitowa yayi suna zama farfajiyar dake ɓangaren"Maimartaba ya sa na kasa fita ko nan da ƙofa"

"Saboda mi?"

"Ina jin nauyin mutanen gidan,gaya duk yau Gimbiya bata zo ba,hakan ya tabbatar min ta samu labarin hukuncin Baba"

"Kwarai ta samu,don duk yau babu abinda ta saka a cikinta,yanzu haka daga gunta nike"

*SHAFI NA BAKWAI. 7*

Yarima ya kalli Bilkisu"Ta ya ya za a barta babu abinci tsawon wannan lokacin,tun jiya,haba Bilkisu?"

Cikin damuwa yake maganar ita kanta Bilkisu wani irin kallo take mashi don gane gaskiyar abin da yake faɗa"Yanzu fa ta ƙi bani lokacin magana balle na yi mata tayin abinci."

Shi kan shi yasan cewar maganar auren shi da Aymana ta zo mashi a kiɗime,amma yasan dole ne ita ma ta shiga hali,musamman yadda yasan mace tana da rauni akan maganar aure.

"Don Allah Bilkisu ki samu abinci ki kai mata"

Miƙewa tayi tana barin wajan,Yarima ya bi bayanta sai dai cikin dakewa ya isa sashen Umma.

Tana zaune saman kujera,Yarima ya durƙusa gabanta,cikin girmamawa fiye da kowane lokaci,tare da gaida ita.

Umma tana murmushi"Alhamdulillah fatan kana lafiya?"

"Lafiya ƙalau Umma."

Shiru yaɗan bi bayan gaisuwar Umma ce ta daure wajan fara mashi maganar auren"Umma nima haka na samu labarin kuma inshaallah ba zaku sameni da aikata ba dai-dai ba."

Sosai ta ji daɗi"Nasan haka Yarima Allah ya daidaita tsakaninku."

Shiru yayi yana kallon ƙasa"Ita tana can tana kukan da bazai fissheta ba."

"Yanzu na tura Bilkisu ta kai mata abinci."

Murmushi Umma tayi,zata kuma magana Hajiya tayo sallama tare da shigowa,suka ansa.

Yarima yaɗan sunkuya ya gaida ita tare da miƙewa zai basu gu.

Hajiya ta ce"A zo zauna,dama maganar taka ce ta kawo ni"

Umma ta ɗan gyara zama tana kallon fuskar Hajiya sam bataji daɗi kallon da take wa Yarima ba.

"Na je na dubo Gimbiya Aymana,tunda muke da ita a gidan nan bamu taɓa ganinta cikin ƙunci irin wannan ba..."

"Hajiya ai dama zata yi hakan amma a hankali zata koma lafiya."cewar Umma.

Hajiya ta aikawa Umma da wani wawan kallo"Sam ba zamu lamunci ganin 'yarmu cikin ƙunci ba,Aymana ta yi magana da Maimartaba ya ce bazai janye maganar shi ba."

Yarima ya ɗan ɗago yana kallon Hajiya yana son karantar ta,ci gaba tayi da magana"Daga ƙarshe ya tabbatar sai idan kaine ka ce baka amince ba."

Umma ta ce"Haba Hajiya wannan wace irin magana ce,ku fa manya ne bai kamat..."

"Idan ke ba zaki iya magana ba to mu ba zamu yi shiru ba."

Yarima ya kalli Umma"Shi kenan Umma karki damu"

"Zaka janye maganar kenan?"

Yarima ya kalli Hajiya ya gano tsantsan makirci a tare da matar murmushi yayi"Ina jin nauyin Baba ba zan iya kallon idon shi na faɗa mashi ba zan bi umarnin shi ba."

Ajiyar zuciya Umma tayi,Hajiya ta ci gaba"To so kake ayi abinda zai kawo danasani,Aymana dai bata sonka  kuma na san kaima ba sonta kake ba."

Yarima ya kalli Umma data yi tagumi,tana kallon Hajiya,Hajiya tace"To ko kana son ta ne?"

"Ba ni so kuga kamar nayi rashin kunya amma tun farkon zuwana gidan nan naji tsananin soyayyar Aymana a tare dani,kuma...."

Hajiya ta miƙe tana buga cinya"Ƙarya kake wannan makirci ne,dama ba don Allah  kazo gidannan ba kazo ne don wasu manufarku akan mu."

Umma ta kalli Yarima"Ta shi kaje,komi kenan za su nemeka"

Yarima ya sunkuya yana masu bankwana ya kalli Hajiya dake huci ya ce"Na barku lafiya." Ya fice.

Umma ya kalli Hajiya"Haba Hajiya wannan fa tamkar zubar da girma ne ga suruki."

Tafa hannuwa Hajiya tayi"kenan harkin bashi?"

Umma tayi hanyar ƙuryar ɗakinta"Na ba shi"

Anan ta bar Hajiya tana cizon yatsa don ba haka taso ba,babu abinda ta tsana irin ganin ci gaban su,musamman sanin yadda Sarki ya fifita Aymana akan yaranta,hakan yasa ta ke baƙin cikin ganin Aymana zata auri ɗan sarki.

Kwafa tayi tana barin sashen cikin sauri ta nufi ɓangaren Mama.

***

Yarima yana zaune da fadawanshi fira yake dasu sosai har yana dariya,babban  cikin sune ya fara magana "Mu fa kwana biyu kenan bamuga Uwar ɗakinmu ba."

Yarima ya girgiza kai"A tunaninka zaka ganta yanzu ne,ai tun ranar da taji labari ban kuma ganin ta ba."

Zasu ƙara magana Yarima ya ɗaure fuska yana tashi don barin wajan,ya ɗan ja rai irin na yaran sarakai,suna ganin hakan suka kame kansu gudun kar suyi laifi.

Cikin gida ya nufa,yau zaije gun Kaka ne yana tafiya ya ci karo da Bilkisu"Ina za ki je?"

"Zanje neman Gimbiya na shiga ɗakinta bata nan"

Yarima ya ɗan taɓe baki,a zuciyar yace ita shikenan sai ta ƙuntata kanta"Zanje wajan Kaka ki same ni muyi fira."ya faɗa a fili.

"To"ta bashi amsa.

Tsaye ya samu Kaka tana sababi don dama ya ji muryarta tun kafin ya ƙaraso,murmushi yayi shi kanshi ya fahimci faɗan kaka.

"Ja'irar yarinya sai kin shanye Madarar nan,ko yanzu in ɓata ranki"

Aymanace zaune kan kujera da kofi a hannunta,sai dai har lokacin bata ɗaga kofin ba balle ta sha.

Yarima yayi gyaran murya Kaka ta ɗago tana tafiya dudduƙe"Sannu da gida Kaka"

Sai da gaban Aymana ya faɗi jin Muryar shi,ta sa hannu tana gyara wuyan rigarta,tare da yane mayafi,kauda kai yayi ganin rigar babu nauyi zaka iya ganin shacin jikinta.

Kaka tace"Zo zauna don ko baka zo ba zan aika kiranka"

"Me na yi Kaka?"

Zata yi magana Bilkisu ta shigo,tana kallon Aymana.

Kaka ta miƙe "fita zanyi insha Iska amma yarinyar nan ta ƙi cin abincin"

"Kaka je ki sha iska bari zamu bata abincin ni da Yaya Yarima"cewar Bilkisu.

Kaka ta fice tana banbami,Bilkisu ta zauna gefen Yarima,dake bin ƙofar da Kaka ta bi da kallo.

Yayi ajiyar zuciya,Aymana ta ajiye kofin hannunta akan tebur ɗin gefen ta.

Yarima ya tashi ya nufi wajan da take,kofin ya ɗauka tare da zama gefen ta.

Wata irin faɗuwar gaba Aymana taji,sai dai kanta yana ƙasa bata ɗago ba,sanyayyan ƙamshin turaren Yarima ya fara shigar ta,ta ja jikinta kaɗan Yarima ya kalleta.

"Ki sha Madarar nan,kar Yunwa ta kama min mata."

Da sauri ta ɗago ta kalle shi, kenan shi da gaske ya amince da auren ta,rufe ido tayi ta fara tunanin kalaman shi.

Jira Yarima ya ɗaga mata yana sakin murmushi,gabaɗaya Aymana ta rasa abin yi,Hannu ta saka ta ƙarɓi kofin.


Yarima yace"Yauwa ko ke fa."

Baki takai kofin ta fara sha,bisa mamakin su bata ɓata lokaci ba ta shanye Madarar Yarima ya kalleta"A ƙara maki?"

Kai ya kaɗa alamar a'a,Yarima ya ce"Bana ganewa kiyi mani magana"

"Ya ishe ni"

Kallon Bilkisu yayi tana rufe bakinta da hannu dariya take sonyi amma babu dama"Miƙo mata ruwa."

Hannu yasa ya buɗe ruwan da ta bashi,ya miƙa mata,a karo na biyu babu gardama ta sha kaɗan ta ajiye.

Yarima ya miƙe"Bilkisu tashi muje tunda ta sha"

Yana maganar yana nufar ƙofa"Ina zaka je"

"Ina zaka je bamuyi magana ba Yarima abin nan fa da wahala,ta ya za ce na yi auren da bana jin soyayya a cikin sa,ba zan iya ba,ina so ka janye maganar nan Yarima"

Ahankali yake dawowa gunta"Ba zan janye magana ba tunda ba nine na kafa ta ba Aymana"

"Dama da shirin hakan kazo gidanmu,duk abubuwan da akayi a baya bai muku ba sai kunzo da salon yaudara,wai miyasa zaku manta da asalin gabar tsakanin mu?in banda Maimartaba da sanyin hali irin nashi taya zai saki jiki akanku"

Kallon ta kawai yake ya harɗe hannuwanshi a ƙirji yana karantar yanayinta,kalaman ta ba sune a zuciyar ta ba,bakinta ne kawai yake faɗa.a zahiri yasan Aymana bazata iya kalamai irin haka akan shi ba,sanin cewar rashin daraja a iyakar talakawan ta ne,amma tana daraja masu mulki.

"Na riga nace ba zan aureka ba,amma kowa ya juyan baya a gidannan,akanka an wayi gari ni Gimbiya Aymana Babana yana fushi dani."


Kujera Yarima ya nuna mata"ki zauna"

Bilkisu ta na gefen su tana jinsu,saidai batayi magana ba.

Aymana ta zauna Yarima ya koma nesa da ita"Ki ba sarki haƙuri ya janye maga..."

"Ya riga yace sai idan kaine ka faɗa da kanka,me yasa za a bani rashin 'yanci a gidannan?"

"Mi ye mafita,ta ya zamu yi Maimartaba ya janye maganar auren mu?"

A hankali Aymana ta dawo kusa dashi"Hanya ɗaya ce Yarima"

"Faɗa min hanyar,sam ba zan lamunci ganin 'yar sarki mai ji da gayu,mulki,ƙasaita ta koma kamar yadda kike ba a yanzu,dole zamu yi koma miye don ganin Gimbiya ta dawo matsayinta Azuciyar Maimartaba"

Wani sanyi Aymana taji"ka je da kanka ka faɗiwa sarki baka so na,kana so yabar zancen Aure na da kai,hakan ne kawai hanyar da zai sa Sarki ya janye maganar."

*SHAFI NA TAKWAS . 8*

*SADAUKARWA GA Oum Shuraim*

Aymana ta cigaba da Magana"Idan kuma har ba zaka janye maganar Auren nan ba,to akwai sharaɗi na biyu,sharaɗin kuwa shine idan har kana so na aureka Sai ka yarda kaine zaka maido da martabar gidanmu,mulkinmu da kuma muƙamin masarautar mu"

"Me hakan yake nufi"Ya bata amsa yana nazarinta.

"TAKOBIN Gidanmu da take hannunku,dole ya dawo hannunmu,kuma kai ne zaka maido wannan muƙamin da kanka,in har kana so na aureka."


Miƙewa yayi yana jin wata izza tana fuzgar shi jin yau ana bashi umarni,kamar aike haka yake jin  yanayin maganarta,hakan  ya tafarfasa zuciyar Yarima.

Yanzu ne ya tabbatar tana wasa da sarautar shi,tana tunanin shi baya son ɗaukakar tashi masarautar.

Gyaran murya kawai yayi, sakin fuskar da yayi a farko ya kau,Azuciyar shi bai san me Aymana take jin tana taƙama da shi ba,idan mulki ne ya sani a tasu masarautar aka fi mulki da nuna izza amma a masarautar su Aymana ya gama fahimtar itace kawai ta ɗauki kwatankwacin Izza da ya kamata duk ɗan MASARAUTA yayi.

Baiga laifin ta ba hakan ya sa ya ɗaga laɓɓan shi da kyal ya furta"kee!!! ina so ki sani ni ban kasance wanda nake bin umarnin wanin da bai kai nabi umarnin sa ba,kamar yadda na amincewa Sarki ba zan taɓa canzawa ba."


Daga faɗar haka ya fice cikin takon ƙasaita,su duka biyun kallo suka bi shi dashi,Bilkisu ta matso gun Gimbiya Aymana.

Fitar Yarima kuwa ɓangaren Sarki ya nufa,gaishe da shi fadawa suka fara yi,sunyi mamakin ganin fuskar shi babu walwala kamar yadda suka saba.anan ya sanar yana son ganin mai martaba,aka sanar da Sallama,sallama kuwa ya isar da saƙon agun Sarki.

Sarki jin ance Yarima ne hakan yasa ya bada umarni ya shigo.

Yana zaune saman kujera Yarima ya sunkuya ya yi gaisuwa tare da faɗin"Allah ya taimake ka nazo akan maganar auren ne ina son komawa gida cikin 'yan kwana ki,lokuttana ba su da tsayi a yanzu,gaya Maimartaba ya fara damuwa akan rashin komawata."

Tsawon mintuna goma Sarki baiyi magana ba yana nazari akan maganar Yarima,cikin rashin tsammani Sarki yace"Zan ɗaura Aurenka gobe,zan sa asanar da Mutanan TORO."

Yarima bai ji komai ba don yadda ya fara jin izzarshi hakan bazai sa ya nuna damuwa ko razana ba"Ranka shi daɗe,ina godiya sannan ina neman wata alfarmar akan Kar a sanar ma mutanen Toro,zai fi naje da matata don bar ma su abin mamaki kuma hakan zai kawar da tunanin su na son sai an ƙara wani lokaci domin suma su halarci taron.ina mai neman Alfarma."

Yarima ya yi saurin yanke hukunci ne,don sanin idan har wasu daga gidansu suka san zai yi Auren ba lallai ne hakan ya faru ba,don Sarkin TORO ya damu akan rashin Auren Yarima,gaya wasu daga ƙannan shi ko wanne da auren shi,hakan yasa hankalin mahaifiyarshi baya kwance,itama gurin ta yayi auren saboda shine Mai jiran gado.

Haka suka tashi a wannan zama, lokacin daya koma sashen shi anan ya bawa fadawanshi umarnin haɗa nasu kayan don sun kusa wucewa.


Kamar wasa Al'ummar Darul-Bilyam suka tsinkayi maganar ɗaurin auren Aymana da Yarima Amin.

Aranar kuka baya musaltuwa agun Aymana,Durƙushe take gaban mahaifiyarta,baki take bata akan Auren.

"Wannan shi ne asalin darajarki Aymana,kiyi biyayya kiyi aurenki,Ni ina mai alfahari zaki koma cikin Babbar masarautar nahiyarmu,masarautar da babu irinta a duk kusa damu,abin jin daɗin ma wata rana kece matar Maimartaba ga Masarautar TORO masarautar da suke da TAKOBI,ke kanki kinsan yadda masarautun dake kusa damu suke son mallakar wannan Mulki ya koma gunsu."

Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya,ita kanta a zuciyarta bawai bataso bane,domin tana so taga ta ƙara samun daraja,amma kuma tana kishi tare da son mallakar TAKOBI,tana ganin babu wani muƙami daya wuce ta dawo itama taga masarautar mahaifinta ta zama ita ce babbar masarauta kamar TORO.

A take ta tuno maganganun Hajiya da Mama da kuma sauran Yayyenta akan tayi Auren Amma ta je da sharaɗin dawo da TAKOBIN da rashin shi yayi sanadiyar ƙanƙancin masarautar su.

Kaɗa kai Ayama tayi ta kamo hannun Ummanta"Umma tabbas ke uwa ce ta gari,har kullum zanyi alfahari dake,amma ni zan zama matar sarki da take da Izza da mulki,zan je Toro kamar yadda Mai martaba ya umarta,amma wata rana dole zan dawo da martabar mu."

***

A wani ƙaton mazaunin su,Mama,Nene,Hajiya,Yarima Shuraim da Yarima Faruk kowanne ranshi a ɓace yake jin kalamin da akace Yarima yayiwa Gimbiya.

A wannan lokacin ya zama dole su nuna isa akan Umma da Kaka,da suke goyon bayan Auren.

Kowa ya gama bayanin shi da kuma nuni akan darajar Takobin da suke rigima kanta.
"Idan har shi Yarima Amin zai nuna kishi akan masarautar su,Umma taya zaki goya baya Aymana ta aure shi tsakani ga Allah,ya zama dole muyi kishi mu dawo da mulkinmu"cewar Nene dake kallon Umma.

Umma ta girgiza kai"canza ra'ayin Maimartaba ba ƙaramin abu ba ne a garemu,amma zancen Yarima ya firgitani,banyi tunanin zai nuna iko akan Aymana ba."

Taɓe baki Hajiya tayi"Dama ke ce kika ɗauka zai zama kariya a gare ta,amma ni nasan zata zama kamar baiwar da ba zata taɓa samun 'yanci ba a masarautar Toro"

Mama tace"Ni dai kishina akan yaran gidan nan ne,idan har TAKOBI ta dawo hannun mu,to fa babu wanda ya isa ya ja da Darul-Bilyam."

Yarima Shuraim yasan shine namiji mai jiran karagar hakan yasa ya tabbatar kamar shi ake shirin yiwa yaƙi"Dole Aymana ta je gidan kuma ta dawo mana da TAKOBIN mu"

Umma ta kalli Aymana"Na baki Umarnin dawo da masarautarku kamar Zinarin da aka tsuma wanda darajar shi zai linka darajar kowane,ta hanyar dawo da TaKOBI a gidan nan."

Bilkisu ta zaro ido jin Umma ta amince da zancen su"Haba Umma yanzu kin amince Aymana ta je Toro ba don Auren kirki ba sai don wata manufar ku ta...."

Wani wawan mari Umma takai mata"Daga lokacin da bamuda wata daraja,ba zaki taɓa kiran kanki yar sarkin data fito daga babbar masarauta ba."

Kaka ta kalleta"Yanzu marinta kikayi saboda ra'ayinki ya canza.Nice ya kamata na ji haushi,ni da na rasa Ɗana da nafi ji dashi lokacin da TaKOBI ta bar gidannan shine sanadiyar Rasuwar mahaifin Sarkin yanzu,saboda baƙin ciki."

"Amma kaka duk da bakin cikin rasa yaron ki hakan baisa kikaji kina son ganin dawowar Masarautar nan ba"

Kaka ta miƙe tana jan hannun Bilkisu"ki saka masu ido sunyi nisan da ba sa jin kira.

A ƙofa suka yi kiciɓus da Kawunsu Aymana wato ƙanin Maimarta ba,wanda shi ne yake binshi,saidai uba suka haɗa amma kowa da mahaifiyar shi.

Shima Kawu Harun ya so mulkin masarautar Bilyam wanda bayan baiwa Baban Aymana sai da sukayi gaba da shi,don shi yaso ya zama Sarki,kuma ko yanzu yana da ƙudurin zama sarkin hakan yasa yake goyon bayan Aymana ta dawo da TaKOBI,don yayi mulkin babbar masarauta.

Ciki ya shiga yana kallon su"Aymana ki tashi ki koma ciki ki fara shiri kuma ki saka a ranki lokacin ɗaukakar masarautarku yazo,kuma ke zaki ɗaga darajar gidannan."cewar Kawu Harun.

Aymana ta miƙe da ƙasaitacciyar tafiyar ta takon ta zuwa gaban iyayen nata"Na gode da goyon bayan ku in sha Allah nice sanadin farin cikin gidan nan...

      *MASARAUTA.*

       (AuntyHaliloss).

*SHAFI NA TARA. 9*


Maganar Aymana ta faranta ran kowa haka ta miƙe tana barin wajan duk wanda ya haɗu da ita a gidan sai yayi mamakin ganin yadda ƙunci ya yaye daga zuciyarta,sashen Mahaifinta ta nufa babu wata sanarwar zata gana dashi haka aka bata umarnin shiga.

Cikin Mamaki ya kalleta ganin yau babu ƙunci atare da ita"'Yata  zo zauna nan."

Ita kanta tasan ta rasa kulawar mahaifinta na wani lokaci"Baba ina mai tuba a gare ka akan gardama ga umarninka a lokacin farko,yanzu na Amince zan auri Yarima kamar yadda ka umarta."

Yasan wani lokaci tana da sanyin hali kalar na mahaifiyarta,sai dai kuma yasan basu iya juya ma abu baya ba,haka kuma basu da wahalar canza ra'ayi har ƙara Aymana tana da kafiya da jajircewa.

"Shi kenan Aymana,ki je kuyi shiri anjima ƙarfe huɗu ne ɗaurin auren,kuma ya sanar dani gobe ne zaku tafi,ina so abada umarnin shirya mutanen da zasu rakaki,a turomin Jakadiyya."

Sunkuyawa tayi tana faɗin"Saƙon ka ya isa kamar yadda kace."

Fitar Gimbiya Aymana ta yi sashenta, kuyangu ta samu a sashen aiki kawai suke mata,ta tsaya tana kallon Farida"Ayi gaggawar samar min kayan da zan saka nan da mintuna sha biyar"

Cikin bin umarnin ta bar wajan ta shiga ɗakinta,tana shirin shiga wanka taji shigowar Kaka,da wani ƙoƙo ɗauke da magani a ciki.

"karɓi kisha wannan zai maki amfani wata rana."

Aymana ta amsa ta aje gefe"Za ki sha ko ajewa zakiyi?"

"Zan sha" ta bata ansa tana shigewa ciki Kaka tabar ɗakin tana jin haushin yaran zamani.

Lokacin da ta fito ta samu Bilkisu a zaune da kaya akan gadonta,Aymana ta ajiye abun data tsane gashin kanta,ta kalli Farida data shigo da jakunkuna hannunta.

"Ki fitar da kowane"

"To ranki shi daɗe"

"Ga kaya nan na kawo maki fa,zasu yi kyau a wannan muhimmiyar ranar taki Gimbiya"cewar Bilkisu

Ɗaga kayan Aymana tayi"Na gode 'yar uwarta,amma zani barsu sai zamu tafi ina saka."


Bilkisu ta miƙa"Na barki lafiya."

"Ki jira ki taimakawa Farida wajan gyara ni,ina ga kamar aikin zai mata yawa"

Komawa tayi ta zauna tana haɗa kaya,Aymana ta shiga shafa tsadaddun mayuka da turaruka nan take ƙamshi ya game ɗakin.

Kayan suka fara miƙa mata,Bilkisu ta je gun madubin tana ɗaukar kayan kwalliyarta"Zan ɗan gyara maki fuskarki kaɗan."

"Bana buƙatar kwalliyar da zata sa agane akwai koda kwalli a tare dani"

"Ba da yawa zan yi ba"

Shiru tayi Bilkisu tayi mata kwalliya mai haske kaɗan zaka gane tayi kwalliya,wani tsadadden farin leshi ta saka,Bilkisu tana ɗaura mata ɗankwali Farida kuwa takalma take saka mata,tare da wasu sarƙoƙin ƙafa na asalin zinare.

'yan hannu da agogon hannunta masu haske da kyalli,Bilkisu zata miƙo mata Alkyabba Aymana tace"Bani maganin can na sha kar kaka ta kuma harzuƙa."

Aymana tana zaune jiran masu fita da ita,Jakadiya dasu Hajiya sai Mama sune suka zo fita da ita.

Yarima Amin kuwa lokacin yana Babbar fadar mai martaba wanda acanne ake ɗaura auren.

Duk wanda ya halarci ɗaurin Auren ya fahimci kyau da taƙama kalar ta Yarima,kowa yayi sha'awar shi a ranar.

Babu ɓata lokaci aka haɗa mutane da kuma tawagar rakiyar Aymana.

Mutanan farko Bayi ne da kuyangu da wasu dakarun akan dawakai.

Lokacin 'yan uwa da wasu daga cikin iyayen Aymana suka fito da ita.

Ana fitowa da ita aka hau guɗa da kirari gareta,anan Jakadiya ta fito da saurinta da kofi a hannu,Madarar shanu ce a ciki anan ta hau watsawa Aymana madarar a fuska,ta miƙa kofin gefe kafin wata ta miƙo mata lalle aka shafa mata a hannuwanta.

Aymana tasa hannu tana goge Madarar,aka aza mata Alkyabba,tare da fesheta da turaruka.Ƙanwar Mahaifiyar ta ta fiddo turmin Atamfa,turare da goro ta miƙawa Jakadiya, wannan shine al'adar su idan za a kai yar sarki gidanta.

Akan wani keken doki da aka ƙayata da wani jan kyalle,Yarima yana gefe akan kujera a ɗayan gefen ne Aymana ta zauna,sosai suka fito ahalin sarauta kasancewar Yarima kanshi harda rawani.

A kashin ƙarshe na tawagar kuwa,mahaya ne masu yawa duk wanda yaga tafiyar sai yayi sha'awar hakan.

Barde ne a gaba yana basu kariya gudun faruwar wani abun.

Fadawane masu tarin yawa a zagaye da keken dokin da Yarima da Aymana suke.

Haka suka ɗauki hanyar Masarautar TORO,ga makiɗa da masu  busa suna yi.

  *MASARAUTAR TORO*

Daga farkon gini da tsarin bangon masarautar hatimin TAKOBIN masarautar ne sai dai an ƙayatar da bangon da ja da tsanwan launi Babbar masarauta ce da babu kamarta.

Ƙofor masarautar guda ɗaya ne,a hanya ɗaya ne,saɓanin da da take da ƙofofi guda Ukku,harin da wasu masarautu suke kawowa Takobin mulkin hakan yasa aka mayar da ƙofar shiga ɗaya,ya zama kowaye zai shiga to lallai tanan ne zai shiga haka kuma a wajan fita.

Suna isa aka hau murnar dawowar Yarima Amin domin kuwa mutanen gidan sunyi kewarshi sosai,a bisa mamakin su da tunanin su zai dawone kamar yadda ya tafi,kasancewar bai faɗiwa kowa aurenshi ba.

Ba suyi mamakin ganin tawagar data rakoshi ba,kasancewar suna da labarin Sarkin Bilyam zai karrama Yarima Amin.

Dama sun shirya wa Yarima hawan doki da kilisa,haka masu wasa da kura suna yi,wasannin gargajiya sosai.

Wajan wasu Rumfuna aka isa dasu,anan aka sauko da Yarima ana murnar dawowar shi.

Babban hadimin shi yasa"Asanar akwai baƙi da kuma mata a gurin Yarima"

Lokacin duk baƙin sun zauna akan wasu kujeru,Sai lokacin Yarima ya koma gun Aymana da Kuyangarta,sai Kanwar Umma da suke tare,kallon su yayi ya ɗan tsaya yana sauraron masu sanarwai.

Kowa yayo kansu yana kallon,dai dai lokacin Sarki ya fito,zuwa mazaunin shi,haka Ummi mahaifiyar Yarima da sauran abokan zamanta su Hajiya Maigado.

Ƙannan Yarima maza duk suna zaune,kowane rai a murtuke domin sun san dawowar Yarima wani ƙuncine a tare dasu,domin ayanzu sune suke tafiyar da ragamar gidan.

Daga nesa da Matan kuwa 'yaya ne da jikoki,na Masarautar,kowa yasha ado mazansu da matan su.

Kuyangu,Bayi da barorin gidan sun cika wajan sai dai kowanne sanye da wasu kaya,riga ja sai tsanwan wando.

Daga ɗayan gefen Sarki 'yan uwan sarkine masu riƙe da wasu muƙamai irinsu Galadima,Waziri,Baraya,Garkuwa,Maga yaƙi da kuma wasu daga cikin Hakinman garin.

Abin Kallo a Masarautar Toro yawanci duk mutanen gidanne suke riƙe da sarautunsu,wani muƙamin ma ba dole sai ɗan gado zai riƙe ba amma saboda ƙarfin iko da kowa yake ji,sannan kowa yana so ce yana riƙe da muƙamin hakan yasa duk sun gaje Sarautun iya su kansu,babu bare a cikin su.

Sai da Maimartaba ya ɗan girgiza jin Yarima ya dawo da Mata,shi kan shi Yarima yasan hakan,sai dai bai damu ba don yasan hakan shi ne babban burin shi yaga yayi Aure.

Iso aka farayiwa Baƙi, kuyangu da bayi suna nuna masu mazaunan su,Anan aka zaunar da Aymana.

Yarima ya yi Tattaki zuwa wajan mai martaba dake zaune akan wata karaga ta alfarma,sunkuyawa yayi cikin ban girma ya fara magana "Sarkin kowa Sarki mai adalci,Yarima ya dawo sai dai yazo da babban Al'amari tare da tuba akan rashin sanarwar kafin aikata hakan."

Saboda mulki da iko,ko motsi Sarki baiyi ba, tsawon daƙiƙa  goma,Yarima ya ƙara sunkuyawa"Na yi burin saka Mahaifina farin ciki,sai dai na samu tsaɓanin hakan."

Wani bafade dake gefe ya fara magana"Ya shugaba na,Yarima yana tuba,a bisa babban kuskure."

Sarki yasa hannu ya ɗago hannun Yarima yana murmushi"Azo min da Yarinyar."

"Ki tashi muje gun Ummi tana son ganawa dake."

"Dare fa yana yi."

"Sauka lafiya Ummi"

"Na barki Lafiya"

Tana ficewa Aymana ta samu damar ƙarewa ɗakin kallo,duk tsaruwar ɗakunan iyayenta wannan ya wuce su sosai.

Kamar daga sama Aymana taji ana faɗin" Duk wani damanmmaki da muka zartar, wasu shingaye da muka zana domin isa ga zama matar Ɗan sarki ba zama Gimbiyar gida bane,akwai mutanen dake son zama sarakunan masarautar mu,mallakar wannan mulki sai ni da kuma mahaifina,shigowar ki wannan gida tamkar saka ƙafarki a makomar fir'auna ne,nice zan haifi ɗa agurin Yarima kuma Gimbiyar gida."

Cikin mamaki Aymana ta kalli Ayda wacce take tsaye akanta cikin sauri ta miƙe tsaye  murmushi tayi cikin ji da kai, tare da mulkin da yake bin jikinta, kamar ba zata tanka mata ba, sai kuma taga dacewar  tankawar "Sai yaushe mutane zasu daina shiga damuwar wasu?zama ɗan sarki shine tunƙaho ba matar sarki ba, Mahaifin kine zai yi mulki kiyi fahari ba miji ba,ko baka auri Yarima ba indai kai ɗan sarki ne za a kiraka Gimbiya"
