*SHAFI NA SHAƊAYA. 11*


Aymana bata ƙarasa ba ganin Yarima Amin dake tunkarosu,hakan ya ba Ayda damar juyawa tana kallon Yarima,ja tayi da baya kaɗan,don akwai shakkun Yarima sosai agunta,fuskokinsu kawai yake kallo,duk maganganunsu babu wanda bai ji ba.

Sai dai bai yi magana ba yasa hannu ya riƙo hannun Aymana,har sun fara tafiya  sai kuma ya juyo"Ko ki ji,ko ki yarda,ko ki bi koma akasin haka,ba zan lamunci yin abinda ba daidai ba ga matata,ki kiyaye?"

Cigaba da tafiya su ka yi,sai dai Aymana binshi kawai take,har ƙofar ɗakin Hajiya maigado suka tsaya,sai anan ya cire hannun shi daga nata.

Sannan ya fuskanceta"Ayda kenan 'yar gidan Waziri,Yaya a gun Maimartaba,shi ne yaso zama sarki,saboda wasu halayya nashi marasa kyau hakan yasa al'umma suka juya baya a gare shi."

"Har yanzu Waziri yana mai soyuwa ga mulkin mahaifinka..."cewar Aymana da ke kallon shi.

"Ni ne zan maki wannan bayanin"

"Ya zama dole Ayda tabar shirgina,babu ruwana da tana son auren ka,in zata aureka ni ban hana ba,ƙofa a buɗe take agunta,amma na rantse da ƙarfin mulkin mahaifina idan ta cika shiga damuwata ba zata ji ni da daɗi ba,aka ce mata mulkin miji wani mulkin tunƙaho ne?"

Yarima ya harɗe hannuwa"Da ni kike magana ba Ayda ba ki tsabtace kalaman ki"

Juyawa tayi tana shirin shigewa Amin ya ce"Kar naji wani ya fahimci bakyason aure na"

Da karfi ta juyo"Zan yaudari kai na ne?"

Baiyi magana ba ya juya don ya gama faɗan abinda zai faɗa.

Ƙofar ɗakin da aka sauketa ta shiga akan gado ta samu Bilkisu tana jiranta.

Mai martaba ne zaune a cikin turakarshi,Ummi tana gefen shi"Takobin nan itace ƙarfin mulkinmu,haka kuma auren Yarima ya zama wani ginshiƙi a garemu,mallakar mulkin gidannan sai wanda ya shirya ganin mutanen da suke harin karagata,amma nasan yarinyar zata zama kariya sannan zata zamarwa Yarima sulke,saboda tana gadon Takobin,ƙarfin mulkin gidannan duk a ƙarƙashin mulkin su ne."

Ummi tayi ajiyar zuciya,ita kanta tasan akwai aiki babba agaban ɗan nata, soyayyar da Sarki yake mashi hakan ya ƙara saka ƙiyayyar shi a zuciyoyin mutanen gidan"Ina tsoro ina maijin tsoron ranar da za a nemi wanda zai gaji gidannan."

"Ranar tana zuwa,sannan kuma da yardar Ubangijin musulunci Yarima Amin shi ne magajin karagata."

***
Bayan ficewar su Yarima a fusace Ayda ta fice zuwa ɓangaren mahaifinta,a tsaye ta sameshi da mahaifiyarta,su kansu magana suke akan abinda ya faru a gidan.

Durƙushewa Ayda tayi"Kenan na zama ƙasƙantarciya,ni ce za a musalta azabar da za ayi mani da azabar da akewa bayi,Ni ce yau aka kalla aka gorantamin akan rashin mulki ga mahaifina,yau an gaya mani cewar ni ba 'yar sarki bace,sannan kuma ban ɗauki matakiba."

Waziri ya ɗago Ayda"Duk abinda zaije ya dawo sai mahaifinki ya zama Sarki,ko ɗanki ya zama magajin gobe,ko ki zama matar sarki."

"Wa ne irin mulki yarinyar take taƙama dashi?lallai akwai babban lamari a tare da yarinyar"cewar Inna dake kallon Ayda.

"Ki wantar da hankalin ki,lokaci yayi da za a san biri asan gatanshi a gidan nan"

***
Duk zaman Aymana a sashen  Hajiya maigado,abin mamaki so biyu suka ganta,tana ɓangaren yaranta,Yarima Saifu ya kalleta"An sanar dani  tunda har Yarima ya Auri ɗiya daga masarautar Bilyam,ya ƙara samun ƙarfin ikon mallakar gidan nan,miye makomar mu idan bamu mulki gidannan ba."

Hajiya maigado ta yi murmushi"Kaine kaɗai zaka mulki gidan nan hankali ya kwanta,ina mai gantsuwa Amin bazai taɓa samun kwanciyar hankali ba in har ya hau karagar nan."

"Hajiya na fahimci tsantsar farin ciki a tare da Maimartaba ba tun yanzu yake son ganin Amin yayi Aure ba,zai iya yiwa auren nan da masaniyar shi,ya ɓoye wa kowa."

***

Washe gari da safe aka shirya shagalin bikin Yarima da Gimbiya Aymana a gidan,a wajen ne aka gabatar da kuyangi goma,Bayi biyar da zasu zama masu hidima ga Aymana,Maimartaba ya bayar da kyaututtukan girma ga baƙin shi,sannan ya bada tawaga don rakiyar mutanen da suka kawo Aymana.

Daga wajan jikin kai tsaye wani Babban ɓangare aka nufa da Aymana inda aka ce anan ne ɓangaren Yarima da zai zauna da matar shi.

Farfajiyace farko a ɓangaren sai wasu ƙofofi biyu dake sadaka da makeken falo kujeru zagaye dashi anyi mashi adon sarauta daga gefen dama ne ɗakunan Gimbiya sai ɗayan gefen na Yarima,kowane ɗaki da gado da kujeru,da banɗaki a ciki.

Aymana taji daɗin amincewa da barin Farida guyangar dake mata hidima.

Duk sauran kuyangi suna waje Farida ce kawai zata rinƙa samun damar shiga ɗakin Aymana.

Gaba ɗaya hankalin Farida baya a nutse,Aymana ta kula da hakan sai dai ta damu itama da son jin miye damuwarta,hakan yasa ta tambaye ta.

Farida tace"Tun tashina a Darul-Bilyam na saba rayuwa,acan aka haifeni nayi rayuwa yau gani na canza wani gidan kuma a matsayin baiwa,babban tashin hankalina irin ƙalubalen dana fahimci akwai a gidan nan."

"Duk wani abu mun saba dashi,baƙon al'amari bai wuce yadda zamu fahimci kowa na gidan nan ba."cewar Aymana.

"Ranki ya daɗe na fara samun wasu bayanai akan zamantakewar gidan nan,shiyasa nake tausayawa kaina."

"Farida zamu bisu sannu musan komai akansu,duk wani al'amari da kikaji kiyi gaggawar sanar dani komai."

Share hawaye Farida tayi"Dole ne Hakan,ke ce gata ke kika yarda dani har kawowata wannan matsayin"

Aymana tayi murmushi"Zan ƙara samar maki wani gatan Farida, in sha Allah lokaci zai zo da zan gyanta ki,na fitar dake daga ƙasƙantarciyar rayuwa,ki zama mai gyanci kamar ko wane ɗa."

"Na gode ranki ya daɗe".

Sallama suka jiyo Farida ta amsa,Jakadiyyace da Fadima,Aymana ta kallesu tana muskuta zamnta,duka suka rusuna gabanta,Jakadiya babbar macece sosai Fadima kuwa dududu shekarunta bai wuce ishirin da Ukku ba.

Jakadiya tace"Ranki ya daɗe aike ne daga wajan Hajiya Maigado."

"Ina jinki."

"Wannan Fadima ce"tana maganar tana dafa kafaɗar Kuyangar,kafin ta ci gaba

"Cewa tayi wannan ta zama kyauta daga gareta,ta zama cikin masu hidimta maki,ki sakata cikin jerin kuyangin ki"

"Na amsa,sannan inaN godiya,kuma ina gaida ita."

Jakadiya ta miƙe yana faɗin"Na barki lafiya."

***

Sai Dare Aymana ta jiyo shigowar Yarima da Fadawanshi,a ƙofa suka rabu dashi,ya ida shigowa gidan.

Sai da yaje ɗakinshi yayi wanka yayi shirin kwanciya cikin wani farin kayan bacci riga da wando,sai dai wandon iya guiwa yake,gaban rigar da botura.har ya kwanta Aymana ta faɗo mashi arai.

Miƙewa yayi ya ɗauki wasu takalma masu laushi ya saka ya ɗauko wayoyinshi yana shiga sashenta.

Tana kwance ta ɗan rufa da bargo mara nauyi saboda na'urar sanyaya ɗaki dake aiki,tsaye yayi a ƙofa,sam bata ji motsin shiga waya take dannawa.

Sallama yayi ta juyo tana Amsawa da ɗan saurinta,tare da miƙewa zaune,bargon ya sauka,rigar baccinta ta baiyyana,riga ce launin ja,tana da sharara a gaba.

"Sannu da gida."

"Fatan kin wuni lafiya."

Aymana ta zuro ƙafafunta ƙasa ganin Yarima ya zauna saman kujera,hakan ya basu damar fuskantar juna.

Yarima ya ɗan tsaya yana kallon Aymana"Fatan babu baƙunta a tare da ke?"

"Sam ina jin kamar ina gidanmu,saboda kusanci da na ƙarayi da wani mallaki nawa."

Yarima ya girgiza kai,azuciyar shi yayi tunanin ba zata daina maganar mallakar Takobi ba kenan.

"Shi kenan,ki huta lafiya,na zo ganin lafiyar ki ne"yana maganar yana miƙewa don barin ɗakin,Aymana ta bi bayan shi da kallo har ya ɓace kafin ta koma ta kwanta.

****

Ƙarfe goma na safe kuyangi suke kai kawo a harabar ɓangaren,Farida tana binsu da idanuwa,sai maganganun su dake ɗaukar hankalinta,duk akan Yarima Amin ya shiga ɗaki yau,musamman masu shekarun cikinsu,wanda ta fahimci suna jiran umarnin shi don bada shedi ga al'ummar gida.

Ta hanyar nuna zanin gadon da suka ɓata kokuma duba lafiyar Gimbiya Aymana.

An ɗauki lokaci Farida ta shiga ciki a tsaye ta samu Aymana tana kimtsa kanta"Ya ke Uwar ɗakina ina son sanar dake jiran bayyanar wani abu na shirri da mutanen gidan nan suke jira tsakanin ki da Yarima."

Da sauri ta ɗago"Har yanzu suna bayyanar da hakanne?"

"Gaskiya domin jira suke kawai suji."

"Babu wani abun baiyyanarwa,kar in ji ko kalma ɗaya daga bakinki akan mu,ki gyaraman ɗaki ki fice kawai."

"To ranki ya daɗe"

Abin ya daɗe a zuciyar Aymana haka nan kawai ta kauda maganar,don tasan hakan ma bazai faru tsakanin ta da Yarima ba,irin wannan lokacin da Babu wata soyayyar juna a tsakanin su.

****

Ummi ce zaune a ɗakinta,ita kanta son jin sanarwar Yarima ya fasa kwai a gidan take,domin kuwa wannan shine nasarar su,hakan shine tabbacin zasu ɗau hanyar kawo Magaji a gidan.

"Aje a haɗa kayan karin kumallo ga Yarima da Gimbiya."ta ba wata Baiwa dake yi mata tausa umarni.

"An riga anyi komai tun ɗazu,na bar wajan ana shirin kai masu abincin."

Ummi ta kaɗakai alamar gamsuwa.

****

"Nace kije kema ki zama a cikin bayinta,ina son jin duk wani bayani nata,idan kika kuskura naji wani abun da baki sanar dani ba to lallai zaki haɗu da fushina."maganar Ayda kenan ga Kuyangar dake mata hidima.

Ɓangaren Aymana yarinyar ta shiga itama tana son jin komai daga wajan sauran ƴan'uwanta bayi.

Farida ta fito a falon fa samu bayi suna rige wajan shigowa jera abinci hakan ya faru don ganin kwam.

Tsaye tayi tana kallonsu,Hassatu ta zo taja hannun Fadima suka fice."Ke me faru nifa Ayda ce tace nazo naga komai."

"Har yanzu babu wani bayani,nima Hajiya Mai gado ce ta sani jiye mata komai na gidan"

Hassatu ta ja tsaki"Muje kawai"

Sai ƙarfe goma shaɗaya Yarima Amin ya fito anan ya samu Farida zaune,ita da Hassatu,zubewa sukayi gaban shi"Barka da safiya Ranka ya daɗe."

Bai amsaba ya samu waje ya zaune saman kujera,yana kallon abinci da aka jera ya maida hankalin shi kan Farida"Uwar ɗakin ki ta tashi ne?"

"Eh ta tashi Allah ya taimakeka"

Hassatu tace"Ko ayi mata magana ne?"

Kallonta yayi yaga tana ladabi akan su"A sanar da ita Yarima ya tashi."

Farida ya miƙe sai dai kafin me har Hassatu ta rigata tare da cewa"Angama ranka ya daɗe."

Ta shige tana sallama sai dai  ba a amsa mata ba,tsawon lokaci,bin ɗakin tayi da kallo tana karantar komai,zuwa can Aymana ta fito daga wata ƙofa,Hassatu ta zube gaban ta"Barka da fitowa Uwar gida agun Yarima."

Aymana ta kalleta,ta na shirin zama taci gaba"Mai girma ya fito yace a sheda maki ya tashi."

"Me hakan yake nufi?"

"Yana zaune dai a falo"

"Ko yana buƙatar ganina ne?"ta tambaya cikin nuna isa da iko.

Hakan ya sa Hassatu ta ɗago idonta kaɗan ta kalleta"Na fahimci hakan uwar ɗakina."

"Ina fitowa yanzu."

Sunkuyawa Hassatu tayi tana fitowa,ta tsunna gefen da Farida take"Allah ya taimakeka tace asanar dakai tana fitowa yanzu."

Baiyi magana ba ya cigaba da dannawayar hannunshi,Cikin mintuna Ukku Aymana ta fito tafiyarta a hankali,cikin doguwar rigar shadda an ƙayatar da shadda da Aiki abin wuya da abin hannu duk na sinari,ƙafarta akwai sarƙar ƙafa wanda yake ja hankalin su Farida.

Cikin sauri suka fara mata sannu da fitowa,Bayan ta zauna kujerar dake gefen shi Farida ta matsa wajenta"Idan akwai buƙatar wani abu ina waje."

"Zaku iya tafiya."

Waje suka yi sai dai Hassatu bata so hakan ba,taso ace a wajan zasu tsaya,ita kuwa Farida tasan Aymana ba ta san zaman su idan suna tare da manya,ko suna zaune ahalin su,balle yanzu da take tare da mijinta.

Bayan ficewarsu Yarima ya aje wayar saman hannun kujerar,Yana kallon Aymana"Barka da safiya"tace tana kallon shi itama.

"Ya kamata ace kin karya kafin wannan lokacin."

"Idan ina buƙatar hakan zanyi"ta ba shi amsa.

Yarima ya koma saman kafet,ya na faɗin "miƙomin wayata"

"Ba lokacin waya bane yanzu,lokacin abincin ka ne."

Shiru yayi yana jin ƙarar sarƙar ƙafarta,ta zo ta zauna ta yi shiru,Yarima yana jiran Aymana ta haɗa masu abincin.

Ita kuwa ita kanta so take a haɗa mata don sabone su duka,da sauƙi ma Yarima yana ɗaukewa fadawanshi wani aikin,yana yi da kanshi.

Shiru na wani lokaci,Aymana ta ja filat tana fara zubawa,ta ajiye a tsakiya"Ranka ya daɗe zaka iya ci Yanzu"

Murmushi yayi,ta saka cokali biyu tana fara murza nata a ciki,Yarima gyara zama suka fara cin abincin.

Shi kanshi baya da ra'ayin ace zai yi nisa da matar shi koda ace shi ne sarki,hakan da tayi ya ji daɗi sosai.

***
Fitar Hassatu sashen su Ayda ta nufa,Ayda tana kwance Hassatu ta zube gabanta"Banga alama ko wani shedar Yarima ya kusanci matar shi ayau ba."

Ayda ta miƙe zaune"Kar kiyi mani ƙarya,yadda yake kakkayi tare da ikirarin Matar shi."

"Babu ƙarya,duk Kuyangin dake sashen jiran fitowar bayani suke,babu wani bayani sannan nice naje kira mashi Gimbiyar,kwatakwata ma ba a ɗaki ɗaya suka kwana ba."

"Akwai alamar gaskiya a zancen Hassatu,ku ake kira wajan gyaran karen gidan nan ranar farkon su."cewar Ayda

***

Hajiya Mai gado ta kalli Jakadiya"Anya kuwa ba munafunci bane,taya za ace ba a baiyyana zancen nan ba."

"Ranki ya daɗe Fadima kanta tace bataga alamar komai ba"

Kira ta kwalla mata,Fadima ta shigo"Ke ba na turaki don bacci bane a ɓangaren Yarima,dole ki maida hankali kan aikinki."

"Uwar gijiyata iyakar abinda na gani shi na faɗa"

Hajiya Maigado ta yi dariya"Mun ji mun gani."

***

Ummi tana tsaye tana kai kawo a ɗakin hankalinta yaɗan tashi,ta nufi ƙofa don ta ƙagara taga Jakadiya,anan suka ci karo don fitowarta kenan daga wajan Hajiya Maigado.

Cikin sigar munafunci tace"Yau naga zuciyar Uwargidan Maimartaba a dagule."

Ummi ta koma ciki ta zauna kan kujera,Jakadiyya ta bita ta zube ƙasan kafet"Allah ya sanyaya zuciyar uwar ɗakina."

Ajiyar zuciya Ummi tayi"Mi yake faruwa a ɓangaren Yarima?"

"Ummi ba nida wani bayani,banje sashen ba."

Wata gigitacciyar tsawa tayi mata tare da miƙewa"Kina aikin me har baki je ba,ina so maza-maza ki jiyomin abinda ke faruwa."

"Aminci ga zuciyar Ummi,An bi umarninki kamar yadda kika ƙindaya."

Tana maganar tana miƙewa,Ummi ta bita da Harara.

***

Aymana kuwa ko da suka gama karyawa sawa tayi aka fitar da komai,ta koma kan kujera tayi zamanta,shi ɗin ma hakane,zaman baya musu daɗi sai dai Yarima baya son fita don kar ayita maganar yana ango ya fita tun wuri.

Sai wajan ƙarfe ɗaya ya fita Masallaci ita kuma ta shiga ɗaki bayan gama salarta ta fito harabar ɓangaren kuyangi suka zo kanta kowanne yana son tambayar ta ko tana buƙatar wani Abu.

Aymana ta kalli Farida"A ɗauko mani shifiɗa,zan zauna anan ne."

Wani makeken kafet aka aje mata tare da tuntun don kishingiɗawa,Aymana ta na zaune Sai ga Hassatu ta shigo da kayan marmari akan wani mazubin kaba.

Farida ta amsa ta aje gefenta,ta kallesu ɗaya bayan ɗaya"Ina san sanin kowanne daga cikin ku."

Haka suka cigaba da gaya mata sunyensu da suma aikin su a gidan.

Aymana ta kalli wacce shekarunta zasu kai talatin da wani abu tace"Ke fa mi ye sunan ki?"

"Sunana  Aisha"

Aymana ta kalli sauran kuyangin"Za ku iya tafiya"

Har sun miƙa ta kallesu"Aisha Zauna ke da Farida."

Haka suka zauna gefenta,ta ɗauki tuffa tana sha,an ɗauki lokaci Takalli Kuyanga tace"Aisha shekarunki nawa a gidannan?"

"Ranki shi daɗe ni a gidan nan aka haiheni,asalin iyayena Bayi ne a gidannan"

Aymana ta jinjina kai tare da tashi zaune don tasan A'isha tana da masaniya akan komai na gidan"Mi ye asalin halayyar mutanen gidannan da yadda suka ɗauki mulkinsu."

Aisha ta matsa kaɗan don tasan ta samu shiga wajan Gimbiya,ta fara faɗa mata halin Hajiya Maigado da yaranta,da suna ƙudurin su na son mallakar wannan gidan.

"Ɓangaren Ummi fa."

Aisha tace"Ranki ya daɗe ai itace mahaifiyar Yarima."

"Na sani in son jin wani abu dangane da halayyar ta,kamar yadda kika faɗi min na Hajiya Maigado."

Shiru ta ɗan yi"ko kina tsoron wani abu?ba zaki faɗimin mugayen halayyar ta ba don tana mahaifiyar miji na?"

"Wallahi ba haka bane,Allah sarki,Uwar ɗakin kowa kenan,Ummi mace ce mai kirki da son mutanenta,bata nuna ƙyamar kowa,babu ruwanta da munafunci,shine dalilin da yasa kowa yake son ta a gidan nan."

"Miye alaƙar Yarima da Mahaifiyar sa?"

"Wanann kuma wata soyayya ce ta musamman,duk da Ummi tana da kawaici akanshi kasancewar shi ɗan fari."

"Sai Mai martaba fa?"

Aisha tace"Don Allah kiyi mani aikin gafara,kar maganganuna su jamin fushin gidan nan"

Aymana ta gane ta sosai,tace"Kar ki damu"

"Shi dai Mai martaba bashi da wani guri daya wuce ganin Yarima Amin ya zama Sarki a masarautar nan,soyayyar da yake ma Yarima hakanne ya ja mashi."

"Kamarya kenan?"

"Tsana a gurin masu son Mallakar mulkin gidannan.

"'Ya'yan Hajiya Maigado kenan?"

"Ai basu kaɗai ne masu son mulkin ba,akwai  Waziri yafi kowa nuna izza da juya masarauta,kuma shine yake son zama sarki har gobe."

Aymana ta ajiye tuffa data fara ci tace"Ita fa 'yar tashi"

Aisha tace"Ai yana kan abu biyu ne,na farko ya zama Sarki,idan hakan bai samu ba,dama akwai 'yarshi da ke son auren Yarima,idan ya aureta zata haihu,idan ta haihu Kinga kenan mulki zai koma hannunshi,tunda jikan shi ne."

"Saboda Masarautar mu ta kasance babbar masarauta data mallaki TaKOBI,ƙarfin mulkin gidannan ya shafe ƙarfin mulkin masarautun duk nahiyarnan"

Ayaman ta miƙe tsaye ta fara kai kawo,zuciyarta tana ɗugunzuma,da son jin zancen  Takobin su"A ina TAKOBI take a gidannan?"

*SHAFI NA SHA UkkU. 13*


Aisha ta ɗago za ta yi magana,suka jiyo motsin shigowar Yarima jin muryoyin fadawanshi dake mashi a fito lafiya.

Yana ɗan murmushi ya shigo,su Farida suka durƙushe suna kwasar gaisuwa.

Aymana ta matsa wajan shi,ganin ya ɗan tsaya yana kallon ta,su Farida suka fice.

Aymana tace"Barka da dawowa."

Bai amsa ba yayi hanyar shiga Aymana ta bi bayanshi,a falon ya cire hular shi yana ajewa kan kujerar,kafin ya zauna tare da faɗin"Na sami Gimbiya Lafiya?"

Wani kwanji taji jin ya kambama wajan faɗin sunan tace"Alhamdulillah ko da buƙatar wani abu?"

Zatayi magana Hassatu ta shigo falon riƙe da tire tana sallama,Aymana tace"Za ki iya shigowa."

Gaban Aymana ta durƙushe tana aje tire ɗin,shayi ne a kofi biyu,tana ajewa taɗan tsaya"Za ki iya tafiya."

"Na barku lafiya"

Aymana ta je can gefen kujera ta matso da tebur gaban Yarima ta maida tire ɗin a sama,tsawan lokaci baiyi magana ba.

"Abin motsa baki"ta ce ba tare da ta motsaba


Rufe ido yayi ahankali ya jingina da kujera"Ga dukkan alamu akwai gajiya a tare Da Yarima"

Ɗagowa yayi ya buɗe ido"Nayi ziyara cikin gari don ganawa da talakawan yankin mu"

"Adalin shugaba"ta furta da nuna yabawa

Yarima yasa hannu ya ɗauki kofin ya ɗan kai baki,Aymana ta miƙe ta ɗauki ɗayan kofin"Zan shiga ciki,a huta lafiya"

Binta yayi da ido har ta shige,ya ɗan jima kafin ya miƙe ya wuce ɓangaren shi.

Da Marece Aymana ta fito don shiga cikin gida,kuyangi zasu bita tace Farida da Aysha kawai yayi.

Bangaren bayi da ma'aikatan gidan ta nufa ta zaga ko ina akayita gaisheta,daga nan ta wuce wajan Hajiya mai gado  a ɗaki tace ta shiga bayan gaisuwa kaɗan Hajiya tace"Duk wanda ya tashi gidan sarauta yasan wani abu dangane da bayyana fashewar kwai a gidan sarauta."

Aymana ta kalleta"A wancen gidan ana son kawo sauyin hakanne."tayi matanar da Izza da kuma nuna isa.

Cikin mamaki Hajiya Maigado ta kalleta,kenan tana nufin sune suka ɓoye bayyana Amarcin su,ɗaga baki tayi zatayi magana Aymana ta sunkuya alamar bangirma"Zan gaida sauran mutanen gida,ki huta lafiya"

Wani wawan kallo ta bi bayan Aymana dashi.

Ɓangaren  Yarima Saifu suka nufa bata wani samu karɓuwa daga wajan matar ba, hakan yasa suna gaisawa ta juyo.

A hanya Farida ta ɗan jera da Aymana tace"Allah ya taimake ki,abinda nike gaya maki kenan ɗazu."

Batayi magana ba sai Aysha da take tambaya hanyar da zasubi zuwa sashen Ummi.

Ta samu Ummi tana ɗan hutawa,a gabanta suka fara Gaisuwa,Ummi ta sa hannu ta ɗagota,ta juya tana kallon su Farida"Kuje tana fitowa."

Taja Aymana zuwa kan kujera Aymana ta zame jikinta tana shirin komawa saman kafet"Kiyi zaman ki,bana son wannan janye jikin da kike,bari in tado maki Saratu dama ɗazu nake mata faɗa bataje wajan ki ba."

Murmushi tayi dama ance Yarima yana da ƙanne amma bata gan su ba"Allah ya taimaki Ummi ki barta zan shiga ba sai kin wahalar da kanki ba"

Ummi ta koma ta zauna,ta kalli Aymana tana nazarinta,tana son Yarinyar sosai sannan taga alamun hankali tare da ita.

Miƙewa tayi tana kwalawa yaranta kira,ta dawo ta zauna"A kawowa 'yata abin motsa baki."

Aymana ta yi shiru tana nazari,Umma tace"Yauwa na manta wai kuwa an kaiki Ɓangaren Waziri da Baba Galadima?"

"A'a Ummi"

Ummi ta miƙe "Ya kamata kam,bari nasa a shiga dake."

Wasu kuyangi ta samo Saratu ta fito tana nufota,Aymana ta kauda kai"Ai ba zan karɓi marabar ki ba."

"Allah ya huci zuciyar Uwargidan Yarima"tana maganar tana dariya.

Aymana tace"Kinyi sa a na huce"

Ummi ta yi dariya"Aymana ga Saratu,zata zamar maki 'yar uwa,ina son ku haɗe kanku kunji yarana."

"Zamuyi kamar yadda kika ce  da yardar Ubangijin mu."

"Allah ya baku iko,ku je cikin gida ku gaida kowa,Saratu ku kula sosai."

"To Ummi"

Haka suka nufi ɓangaren Waziri a tsakar haraba suka samu Inna tana kan wani babban kafet tana hutawa.ganin Saratu yasa ta fara faɗin"To yau kuma ke ce a gidana."

"Ummi ce tace na rako Gimbiyar Yarima ta gaida ku."

Taɓe baki tayi daidai shigowar Aymana"To Sannun ku,zaku iya zama"

"Barka da hutawa"Aymana ta faɗa.

Inna ta miƙe"Wannan itace baƙuwar gidan tamu."

Saratu ta yi hanyar shiga ɗakin"Ina Ayda take"

Kafin ta rufe baki Ayda ta fito cikin doguwar rigar atamfa tasha adon duwatsu"Ina kan fitowa"

Aymana ta ɗaga ta ɗan kalleta,Inna tace"Ga Ayda ku gaisa"

Ƙyam Aymana ta kasa ɗaga baki tayi magana,ta na jin mulki da izza na shigar ta,Inna ta kalleta tana miƙewa"Bari akawo maki ruwa."

Tabi bayan Saratu ta shiga ciki,Aymana ta kalli Farida da ido kawai tayi mata nuni hakan yasa ta miƙe daga tsugunnin da tayi.

Ayda ta ɗanyo tattaki"Nayi tunanin zanga ɗan kwarzon yana take bayan abin gaban goshin shi,sai dai hakan ya kasa samuwa ta dalilin rashin wani abun a tarayyar farko."

Aymana bata ɗago kai ba,Aymana ta ci gaba"Akwai lokacin da kowa zai fahimci yaya haɗin gaskiya yake da kuma akasin hakan."

"Na hane ki da kutsa kanki a cikin gidan Magadan sarauta,akwai banbanci mai girma,Sanin tarayyar farko a babban gida sai wanda isar shi tayi isa za a sanarwa,Amma bake maƙasƙanciya a wajen mu ba."Aymana ta aje maganar tana miƙewa.

Farida ta matsa kaɗan,Ayda ta fara huci"Karki ƙara ƙasƙantar dani,koma...."

Hannu ta ɗaga cikin sauri"Kar naji wani zance."

Saratu ta fito tana kallon su,ta juya,tana guntse dariya,Aymana tace"Ki sanar da Inna mun wuce."

Ganin Saratu hakan ya hanata cewa komai,haka suka fice,a hanya Farida ta fara bata haƙuri,Aymana bata yi magana ba har ƙofar gidan Galadima.

Saratu ta shiga Aymana tana binta Mama tana ɗaki tace su shigo,tana sakar masu fuska"Sannun ku da hanya."

"Yauwa Mama ga baƙuwar gidanmu tazo gaidaku."

Aymana ya gaisheta"Maraba Maraba da uwar gidan Yarima Magaji mai adalci."

"Mama tun yanzu zaki fara mata maganar Magaji mai adalci"

"Eh mana dole na faɗa"

Aymana tayi murmushi sai taji matar ta burgeta lokacin data gane tana maganar ne da gaske har zuciyarta,Mama ga aje masu abinci"Ku ci bari in sa akawo maku shayi"

"Mama ki barshi Muna godiya."

"Au ko ke baki shan shayi kamar Yarima"

Saratu tace"Gimbiya Kinga Mama kullum ita takewa Yarima shayi da wasu abubuwan buƙata"

"Allah sarki"

"Ai yanzu na huta"

Ta matso kusa da Aymana,ta kalli Saratu "Tashi ki bamu gu mu gaisa"

"Kai Mama sai na tashi sannan"tana maganar tana miƙewa ta shige cikin ƙurya.

Mama ta kalli Aymana"Na gode Allah da kika zo mata ga Yarima,kuma kema kika fito daga tsatson sarauta,ko ba komai Yarima zai samu tagazawar ki akan kulle kulle da makircin gidan nan."

Aymana ta gyara zama"Me hakan yake nufi Mama"

"Zaman ki a gidan nan ya zama garkuwa gareshi,tashin hankalin Mutanan masarautar nan akan Yarima yake,sam basu buƙatar ya gaji mahaifin shi"

"To amma Mama naga shine Baba kuma magaji"

"Ki kula Aymana,abubuwan kan Yarima yana ɗaga hankalin duk masoyanshi"

Haka suka zauna sukayi ta labari,kamar wasa Aymana ta saki jikinta da Mama,anan sukayi sallar magriba.

Yarima daga masallaci ya wuce nemanta a gidan amma bai tambayi kowa ba,a ƙofar Gidan Galadima ya ga su Farida hakan ya tabbatar mashi tana ciki.

A hankali ya shiga falon yana sallama Mama tace"Au biyo ta kayi"

Yar dariya yayi"a'a Mama lokacin shan shayin Yarima ne yayi"

"Kai dai faɗi gaskiya"

Aymana ta kalleshi ta ɗan saki fuska"mun jima ko?"

Kujerar da take sama ya zauna gefenta,Aymana ta miƙe ta ɗauko kofin shayi ta buɗe butar shayi ta fara zubawa,kawo mashi tayi tana miƙa mashi.

Yarima ya harɗe hannu bai amsa ba Aymana ta kalli fuskar shi,ɗauke da murmushi"Au Mama ko nayi karanbani"

"Bawani karambani"
"Tayi karambani mana,ta jira Mama ta bani"

Aymana tayi dariya har da sauti"Allah ya huci zuciya"

Har ta yi zata aje Yarima ya kamo hannunta,Mama tace" ka gama lafiya Magaji"ta miƙe tana kiran Saratu.

Ahankali Aymana ta koma ta zauna jiki a sanyaye,tana kallon hannunta dake cikin nashi,Yarima bai damu ba ya bata ɗayan hannun,alamar ta bashi kofin,cikin sanyin jiki ta miƙa mashi ya janye hannunshi daga nata,yakai kofin a baki.

Sun jima sosai babu wanda yayi magana sai can Mama ta fito,Yarima Yace"zamu wuce"

"Shikenan ranka shi daɗe,Gimbiya sai kin ƙara shigo mana ko?"

"Inshallah"

Gaba yayi tana biyo bayan shi,juyawa tayi"Na manta tare muka zo da Saratu bari nace tazo mu wuce"

Shiru yayi mata haka ta shiga Mama tace ta fice ta ƙofar baya.

Dawowa tayi"Mu tafi"

A hanya Tace"Zamu biya nayiwa Ummi bankwana."

"Ummi tana sashen Mai martaba"

Shiru tayi suka yi ɓangaren su bata zauna ba ta fara cire kayan adon Hannunta.

Yarima ya zauna kan kujera ya na daukar wani littafi,ya buɗe

Aymana tayi ciki abinta kaya ta fara ragewa don yin wanka, breazier da Undy ya rage jikinta,mutsi ta fara ji kamar wani kwaro yana yawo,matsawa tayi wajan tana dubawa,sai kuma taji shiru.

Kamar wasa ta ƙara jin motsin hakan ya ɗan tsoratar da ita,ja tayi kawai sai taga jaririn ƙadangare,da sauri taja baya tana kwalla ƙara.

Cikin firgici Yarima ya miƙa,"Lafiyar ki?"

Aƙofa sukaci karo,ture shi take nemanyi,ya sa hannuwan shi ya riƙeta duk jikinta kyarma yake alamar tsoro.

"Ka cikani wallahi ƙadangare ne"

Kallon ɗakin yake yi,Aymana ta fara neman fizgewa,jin motsi yasa ƙadangaren son guduwa,tana jin haka ta ƙanƙame shi gam tana shigewa jikin shi"Kaiwa Allah ka barni,wallahi nan zai zo"

Tayi maganar tana rungumarshi ta hanyar ɗaure hannunta duka biyu a bayanshi.

"Babu abinda zai maki fa"Yana magana yana shaƙar ƙamshin ta,sai kuma ya kasa motsawa.

Aymana ta kuma fasa ƙara,Yarima yasa hannu ya dafa kafaɗunta"Bari na fitar maki dashi",Aymana ta aza kanta akan ƙirjin shi tana sauke bugun lumfashin su a tare.

Kasa janye jikinshi yayi,wani yana yi ya fara shigar shi"Don Allah ka fitar da shi."

Yarima ya ɗan janyeta,ta koma bayanshi,tana rije hannunshi,kallonta yayi"To yanzu taya zan fitar da shi kin riƙe hannun"

"To bari in fita saika Kore shi"kallon ta ya fara yi tun daga sama har kan cibiyarta,hankakinta yana kan inda take jin motsin ƙadangaran.

Sakin hannunshi tayi tana nufa ƙofa da sauri"Karfa ki fita"

Ta yi banza dashi ta bar wajan,dakyal ya sa hanki dinshi ya riƙo shi,yana fitowa dashi.

Baiganta ba,har ya fita waje,ya jima kafin ya dawo"Ki fito na fitar dashi."

Ina Aymana tayi can hanyar ƙofarshi"Ka kaishi can can ƙofa kar ya dawo"

*SHAFI NA SHA HUƊU. 14*

Murmushi yayi yabi hanyar ɓangaren shi,a nan ya sameta tsaye jikin bango"Allah ya taimaki Gimbiya an fitar da shi."

Sai lokacin hankalinta ya dawo jikinta,jin kiranta da yayi da Gimbiya tako ta farayi,ya bi bayanta da kallo,tana shiga bata tsaya komai ba sai da ya nemo Farida don gani yake kamar wani abun zai zo mata.

***
Aymana ta fara kwasar kwanaki a gidan,Mai martaba ya ziyarci masarautar Bilyam yayi godiya akan auren da aka ba yaron shi,duka ɓangarorin biyu sunji daɗi kuma sun fahimci juna.

Cikin mutanen da sukayi tafiyar ne,Baba Haroun ƙanin mahaifin Aymana ya bada wani saƙo a kawo mata.

Sai dai cikin rashin sa'a saida ya buɗe saƙon aciki yaga wata doguwar takarda,ya shiga tsananin tashin hankali jin yadda ake jadda mata muhimmancin abinda taje ɗokowa don kar ta shagala.

Ya kiɗima sosai saidai yayi dogon tunani Daga ƙarshe ya yanke shawarar kai mata,kuma bazai baiyyanawa kowa ba gudun matsalar da zai iya saka kanshi.

Tana zaune Farida ta shigo ta zube gabanta"Allah ya taimaki Gimbiya wannan saƙone daga gida,an sanar Baba Haroun ne ya aiko."

Cikin sauri ta karɓa,ta warware ganin akwai tarda ta kalli Farida"zaki iya tafiya."
"To ranki ya daɗe"

A hankali ta miƙe tabar wajan ta ciga ciki,ita kanta tasan yadda Baba Haroun yake son ta mayar da TaKOBI gidansu,kenan har yafi su Mama da Hajiya saka abun a zuciya.

Tsaye ta tashi tana kai kawo,ji tayi ana shirin shigowa ta yi saurin naɗe takardai,Yarima ya shigo da kayan hawa jikin shi,Aymana ta ce"Barka da sirdi."

Harɗe hannuwa yayi"Kowa ya halarci kallon hawa ban da ke me hakan yake nufi."

"Bana da buƙata don a raina ba wannan lokacin naso ka shirya hawanba."

"Miye dalilin ki na ƙin sanar dani?"

"Ina ganin kamar ba hurimina bane"

Juyawa yayi zai fita,sai kuma ya tsaya"Ya zama dole na rinƙa sanin abinda yake zuciyarki,bazan lamunci wannan ba"yayi maganar cikin izzar dake yawo jininshi

Taɓe baki tayi,yana ficewa ta miƙe ta na fitowa karo suka yi da Hassatu riƙe da tire da kayan marmari,ta jima a wajan tana sauraron su duk da ba komai take jiyowa ba.

Zubewa tayi tana faɗin"Allah ya taimakeki abin motsa baki na kawo"

Bata ce komai ba sai barinta da tayi a wajan ta fice zuwa ɓangaren Baba Galadima wajen Mama.

***
"Kar mu saki jiki dasu,bokanya ta sanar dani muna gab da shiga babban haɗari yana tunkaromu."

Inna ta ce"kaje ka samu Yarima Saifu ko yasan wani abu dangane da hakan."

Waziri ya miƙe yayi wajan Yarima Saifu,suna tattaunawa"Ni fa babu abinda na sani illa in gaji mahaifina,koma miye zai tunkaromu dole ne mu fuskance shi."

"Ka kwantar da hankalinka,dukkanmu magoya bayanka ne,babu wanda ya isa zama mamallakin gidannan sai kai."

Cikin sauri Farida ta juya jin abinda su Waziri suke faɗa,wajan Aymana ta nufa ta samu tana salla haka ta zauna tana jira harta ƙarasa ta maido hankalinta gunta,ta labarta mata.

Aymana ta miƙe tsaye"Wannan bai shafi masarautar Bilyam ba,Zaki iya tafiya Farida."

"Allah ya huci zuciyarki,ya kauda maki ɓacin rai,bansan hakan zai taɓa zuciyar ki ba."

"Ya isa!"

Farida ta miƙe tana samun Aisha don gaya mata,sai dai bata sanar mata halin ko in kula da Aymana ta nuna ba.

Aisha ta miƙe"bari in dawo"

Gudu-gudu ta isa ɓangaren Ummi,a ƙofa aka tsaidata akan ta jira Gimbiya Ummi tana ganawa da Yarima.

A'ishah tace"Gimbiya Aymana ce ta Aiko ni""

"Zaki iya shiga"

Yana gefen Umma durƙushe Kuyanga A'isha ta zuɓe"Allah ya taimaki Magajin gobe da Gimbiya Ummi Allah ya hutar daku da aminci"

Yarima ya kai kofin shayi bakin shi.Ummi tace"ki je maganar ki"

"Gimbiya Aymana tana tsoron faruwar wani lamari da aka sanar da ita,hakan yasa ta turoni"

Da sauri Yarima yace"Me ta sanar dake?"

"Shirin Waziri da Yarima Saifu na tunkarar duk abinda zaije ya dawo don mallakar kujerar Maimarta"

Miƙewa Yarima yayi da sauri yana barin wajan,Ummi tana kiran shi amma sam bai saurareta ba.

Ɓangaren ya nufa bai sameta ba,sai Hassatu da ya gani ta na zaune a ƙofa,nemanta ya farayi a gidan sai da yaje ɓangaren Baba Galadima acen ya juyo muryar Mama tana faɗin"Zamuyi komai don kare faruwar  abinda sukace amma Yarima Saifu yarone,Waziri yana amfani dashi ne don jin shirrikan ɓangaren ɗakin su,da kuma shirin da suke yi."

Yarima yayi sallama"Abin da kikaji kin tabbatar?."ya jefa mata tambaya cikin Izza

Aymana ta miƙe tsaye"An sanar dani kamar yadda aka sanar dakai"

Ja baya ya farayi zai fita"Kul kar in ga hakan,yana da kyau ka ɓoye wannan kayi bincike akan shirye shiryen su,mallakar sarautar Maimartaba abune mai wahalar samu,amma ga wanda ya san mulki hakan ba zai yi wahala ba."

Yarima ya tsaya tsak,ya zama dole ya saurareta,don yasan babu abinda bata sani ba dangane da ƙumbiya-ƙumbiyar masarauta.

"Kimtsawa ko tunkarar lamari shine naka,inhar kana son zama asaman su"

Yarima ya juyo dakyal ya iya "Na barku lafiya"

Aymana tabi bayanshi da kallo,Yana fita ta koma ta zauna.

***


Ayda ta kalli Hassatu"ina jinki"

"Uwar ɗakina abinda naji kenan."

"Kina nufin akwai nuna ko inkula daga Gimbiya Aymana."

Hassatu tace"Haka ne Uwarɗakina"

Ayda ta miƙe ta nufi ɓangaren Hajiya Maigado don ganin Kuyanga Fadima.

Waziri kuwa yana can wajan Bokanyar shi,bincike kawai take mashi akan abin.

Da daddare Aymana tana falo,Yarima ya shigo Farida tana binshi a baya da ledoji hannunta,Miƙewa tayi tana faɗin"Barka da dawowa."

"Sannu da gida"yace yana yin hanyar ɓangaren shi Aymana ta anshi kayan hannun Farida,har ta ajiye sai kuma ta ɗauka yabi bayan shi,yau tana son ganin yadda ɓangaren nayi yake.

Kwankwasa tayi yajima bai yi magana ba,don yau baya jin daɗin jikin shi,ta kuma kwankwasawa tare da shiga.

Yana kwance saman gadon shi,ya rufe idanuwanshi,ta koma tana ƙarewa ɗakin kallo tsaf da shi azuciyar ta tace ko waye yake gyara mashi oho.

"Kayan da Farida ta shigo dasu?"

"Ki fitar da naki"Ayamana ta kalle shi yana gyara kwanciya,ta ɗan duba ledar sai taga kayan adone aciki ta aje ɗayar a gefe.

Har ta juya sai kuma tace"Gimbiya tana godiya"

Nan ma shiru Aymana ta fice,anan ta samu an shigo da abincinsu.

Ta shiga tayi wanka ta fito,ta zauna tana jiranshi don cin abincin.

Har huɗu da rabi,Aymana ta fito ta na tammabayr Farida"Ko Kinga fitar Yarima?"

"A'a Gaskiya yana ciki,tunda ya shiga ban ga ya fito ba"

Aymana ta koma ta zauna har ƙarfe biyar ta wuce,hakan ya sa ta miƙe tayi tafiyarta sashen Ummi don yin fira.

Sai Magriba ta dawo ta shiga tayi salla ya kira Aisha don ta kwashe kayan abincin.

Tayi hanyar ɓangaren tana ta kwankwasa shiru,ta sa hannu ta tura,lulluɓe yake da bargo ta kalleshi ta na faɗin"Ko har ka kwanta ne,naga ba'ayi sallar i'sha ba"

Tayi maganar tana zama kan kujerar dake gefen gadon,Yarima kuwa lokacin zazzaɓi yafi ƙarfinshi,saima rawar ɗari da yake duk da rufar da yayi.

Sai da ya nutsu sannan ta ji yadda yake sauke lumfashi,yana nishi,miƙewa tayi ta nufe shi"Lafiya kuwa."

Dakyal ya ɗan buɗe idon shi,sai lokacin ta kula da hannunshi da yasa yana dafe da goshin shi"Subhanalllah me sameka"

Tayi maganar tana riƙe hannun"Ina jin zaz zazzaɓi ne"yayi maganar da kyal ta iya jiyoshi,sai lokacin ta fahimci ashe yana mata magana.

Hannu tasa ta yayi bargon,ta durƙusa kan gadon ji tayi jikin shi zafi rau,tasa hannu ta dafa goshin shi"Yanzu baka da lafiya ba zaka sanar ba."

Ta yi sauri zata sauko ya riƙo hannunta"Karki sanarwa kowa"

Aymana ta zauna"Waye yake duba ka,ina akwatin taimakon gaggawa?"

Yarima ya girgiza kai yana nuna mata wadrop da sauri ta nufi wadrop ɗin ta buɗe,wani ƙaton akwati tagani ta jawo tana nufo shi.

Ta aje gefen gadon,tana buɗewa,ta fara jawo abin awon jini,ta kunna ta hau gadon ta riƙon hannun shi,ta na fara janye hannun rigarshi har zuwa kafaɗa.

Ta ɗaura abin tana dubawa,cikin Mamaki Yarima ya kalleta,sai dai ya kasa magana,ta jima kafin ta cire tana kuma ɗaukar abin auna bugun zuciya ta saka a kunnanta,ta sa hannu tana ɓalle maɓallen rigar shi.

Ta saka abin tana kunnawa tare da saurarrawa,rufe ido Yarima yayi jin ta tunkari kirjinshi.

Ita kuwa ba abinda ya dameta ta kalleshi"Kasha wani magani?"

Kai ya girgiza ta ce"Yanzu miye zanyi gaya ko abinci baka ci ba"

Ta waiwayawa ta nufi karamin firij ta buɗe ta ɗauko ruwa,ta fara duba magunguna tana karantawa,ta ɓallo wasu tace"zaka iya tashi kuwa."

Ya ɗan ɗago kaɗan Aymana ta hau gadon tana dafa kafaɗar shi,tasa filo a bayan shi,hakan yasa ya tashi zaune.

Ruwan data zuba a kofi ta  fara bashi ta janye"Zaka iya riƙe maganin?"

Hannu kawai ya miƙa mata,ya saka maganin abaki ta ƙara aza mashi ruwan.

Har lokacin hannunta guda  yana rungume da kafaɗar shi yana haɗiye maganin ta janye kofin.

Ta ɗauko ruwa don ƙara mashi,sannan tana son yi mashi allura sai dai kuma sirinji ta duba sosai,hakan yasa ta fita cikin sauri.

A ƙofa take kwallawa Farida kira amma bata nan,sai Hassatu ta fito"Ina Farida?"


"Ranki shi daɗe Taje wajan Gimbiya Saratu" 
 
Aymana tace"Maza ina son sirinji"sai kuma yace "jira in fito.

Ɓangaren Yarima ta koma ta buɗe akwatin ta ɗauki littafi tayi rubutu tana fidda takardai Yarima ya kalleta,yana son ce mata tayi a hankali amma ya kasa.

Ta fice da sauri"Ina ne ɗakin maganin gidan an?"

"Baya ne"

"Maza kije ki karɓomin wannan."

Hassatu ta wuce cikin sauri Aymana ta koma ta ɗauki abin shayi dake falon ta haɗa ta saka madara sosai,ta na ta sauri Hassatu tayi sallama tana zubewa gabanta."Ranki shi daɗe ga shi"

"Yauwa Na gode Hassatu"

Hassatu ta kula yau Aymana bata cikin hayyacinta hakan yasa tace"Allah yasa babu wata matsala Uwar ɗak..."

"Lafiya lau zaki iya tafiya."

Tana maganar tayi hanyar ɓangaren Yarima da kofi a hannu,dama a buɗe tabar kofa.

Wajan fuskar shi tayi"Amma Kana ji da sauƙin ko?"

Ɗaga kai yayi,Aymana ta aje kofin ta ɗauko kayan aikin ta fara saka allura a hannunshi don neman jijiya,dakewa Yarima yayi ya rumtse idon shi.

Ta ɗan cakeshi kaɗan ya ɗan janye hannun"Jijiyar ce ta ɓata amma mugani"

Ya kuma miƙa mata hannu cikin Sa'a tace"Yauwa na samu"ta saka ta ɗora kanula ta ɗaure ta ɗauko alluran zazzaɓi tayi mashi.

Kafin ta zawo ruwa ta haɗa,sannan ta ɗan sauke ajiyar zuciya"Da izinin Ubangiji yanzu zaka samu sauƙi"

Yana niyar zame fulo tace"a'a kabari kasha ko shayin nan"

Ta hau gadon tana dafa shi Yarima yace"Bana shan shayi da madara"

"Don Allah kasha kaga bakaci komai ba,Madarar zai janyen maka yunwa."

Ta jingina jikinsu takai kofin bakinshi,baiyi musuba ya sha,.

Yana cikin sha taga yana motsa hannun,ta kalle shi"Da wani abun ne?"

Sai ta kula da wajan da ta saka kanula ya fara kumbura kamar ruwan baya shiga sosai.

Aje kofin tayi tazo ta riƙe "ka miƙe hannun kaga ya fara tsayawa,Ta riƙe hannun ta aza saman cinyarta,tasa hannunta ɗaya tana shafa wajan tana son kumburin ya baje.


Yarima ya buɗe ido yana kallon ta,ji yayi kamar tana mashi wani salo,yasa hannu ya matse hannunta cikin nashi tare da rufe ido.

****

Da sauri Hassatu ta nufi cikin gida don shedawa Ayda akwai wanda bashi da lafiya a gidan Yarima.

Sai dai kafin ya isa ta haɗu da Kuyanga Fadima,tace"Ina zuwa haka cikin sauri?"

"Ke abin allura na ansowa Gimbiya Aymana kuma naga tayi sashen Yarima da sauri gaskiya ina tunanin shine bashi da lafiya."

Fadima ta riƙe baki"Anya dai banji an sanar da mutanen gida ba,kuma na wuto Likita a ɗakin magani."

Hassatu tace"ke ni dai na tafi,sai kiyi ta surutun ki"

Ai itama fadima sai tayi sashen Hajiya Maigado don sheda mata abinda taji.

*SHAFI NA SHA BIYAR. 15*

Sai wajan ƙarfe tara Gimbiya Aymana ta samu nutsuwa ganin bacci ya ɗan ɗauki Yarima,harta zauna sai ta tuna tayi salla ba, banɗaki shi ta je acan tayi alwala ta fito tayi natà sashen,Anan ta samu Farida zaune,sannu tayi mata,Aymana tayi salla,sannan  tace"Farida."


"Allah ya taimake ki?"

"Kije ki sanar da Ummi Magajin gobe ba shi da lafiya,yana buƙatar addu'ar ta."

Har ta miƙa Aymana tace"Ki sheda mata,baya son kowa ya ji hakan,kema ki kiyaye."

"An gama ranki shi daɗe"

Tana zuwa aka sheda mata Ummi tana wajen Maimartaba,hakan yasa ta nufi ɓangaren Maimartaba,sai da ta sheda daga Sashen Yarima aka aikota sannan aka barta shiga.


Ummi ta fito daga turakar shi,tana amsa sallamar Farida,Farida ta duƙa tana kwasar gaisuwa,Ummi tace"Allah yasa lafiya."

"Da sauƙi dai maigidanmu ne bashi da lafiya shine Gimbiya tace nazo na sanar dake,don kiyi mashi Addu'a."

"Subhanalllah me yake damunshi"tayi maganar cikin nuna damuwa.

"Bani da masaniya,kuma ta ce Yarima yayi hani da baiyyana rashin lafiyar shi ga Mutanan gidan nan."

Ummi ta ɗan razana"ki je ina zuwa"

Farida ta miƙe tana cewa"Allah ya kawoki cikin Aminci,na barki lafiya"

Farida tana fita Ummi ta koma turakar sarki,kallon fuskar ta yayi ya gane akwai abinda yake damunta"Fitarki cikin walwala sai kuma kika dawo akasin hakan"

"Magajin Gobe ne ba shi da lafiya."

Da sauri mai martaba ya miƙe daga kishingiɗe da yake"nayi mamaki har wannan lokacin Yarima bai zo yayi mani bankwana ba,ga alama ciwo ya fi karfinshi."

Ummi ta kaɗa kai"zan koma ciki na leƙo shi".

"Dole muje tare"

"Yarima yace kar a sanar,zuwanka zai bayyana rashin lafiyar"

Irin son da Maimartaba yake wa Yarima bazai jure ace bashi da lafiya bai je ya duba shi ba"Zanje ba tare da sanin kowa ba"

Ummi ta miƙe suna fitowa,bafade ɗaya ne suka tafi tare sai wata Kuyanga dake jiran Ummi a wajen.a tare suka yi sashen Yarima.

Aymana tana zaune ta gama canza mashi ruwa saboda na farkon ya ƙare.Ummi ce ta kwankwasa,Aymana ta miƙe sai dai ba asalin ƙofar da ke kaika ciki bane.

Kenan akwai ƙofa ta baya,zuwa tayi tana faɗin"Waye anan."

Kuyangar tace"Ranki ya daɗe kuna da baƙuncin Maimartaba da Gimbiya Ummi

Da sauri Aymana ta buɗe tana basu hanya tare da Faɗin"Sannun ku da hanya."

Ummi ta riƙe hannunta sukayo ciki,Maimartaba ya maye masu baya,Kuyangar taja ƙofar suka tsaya a waje.

A bakin gadon suka tsaya,Aymana ta durƙushe tana gaidasu amsawa sukayi,Maimartaba yace"'yata tun yaushe ne bashi da lafiya?"

"Ga dukkan alamu ya jima da zazzaɓin,amma ɗazu na shigo nasamu baya iya komai"

Shiru Maimarta yayi,Ummi tace"Ɗakin magani basu sanar bashi da lafiya ba."

"Ummi nice na duba shi."

"Kin yi karatun likitanci ne?"ya jefa mata tambaya.

Shiru tayi Ummi ta ruƙota"Na gode Aymana"

Aymana kalli sarki dake dafa kan Yarima,yana faɗin"Allah ya baka lafiya,Ya tashi kafaɗunka"

Amin suka amsa Ummi tace"Amma ko motsinmu baisa ya motsa ba"

"Na haɗa da Allurar bacci ne,hakan yasa yayi baccin mai nauyi"

"Allah yayi maki albarka"

"Amin Ranka ya daɗe Nagode"

"Ni zan maki godiya da kike kularmin da abin faharina, Magaji na."

Murmushi Aymana tayi,Maimartaba yace"zamu iya tafiya Allah ya tashi kafaɗunshi."

"Sauka lafiya Baba,Mun gode"

Baiyi magana ba yayi hanyar waje,Ummi ta bi bayan shi,Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tabbas taga tsantsar soyayya a tare da Maimartaba zuwa ga Yarima.

Kan kujerar bakin gadon ta koma ta zauna.

***
Cikin gida kuwa tunda Hassatu ta sanarwa Ayda Yarima bashi da lafiya bata ƙara samun sukuni ba,kai kawo kawai take kuma ta kasa samun tabbacin hakan.

Hajiya Maigado itace tayi ƙarfin Halin zuwa sashen Mai martaba,Allah yasa lokacin sun dawo.

Jakadiyya ce ya shigo tana faɗin"Akwai Gimbiya Hajiya tana son ganawa dakai."

Maimartaba ya yi murmushin shirma yana ɗaga kai,Jakadiya ta gane me yake nufi ta miƙe tana faɗin"hutawarka lafiya."

Cikin 'yan daƙiƙu Hajiya mai gado ta shiru a matuƙar jijicewa kamar gaske tace"Allah ya taimake ka ina Gimbiya Ummi ko ansanar dakai rashin lafiyar Yarima?'

"Yariman da ya tashi yanzu baki haɗu da shi a hanya ba?"

Ummi ya buɗe wata ƙofa ta fito,Hajiya Mai gado tace"na tsinci labarin Rashin lafiyar magajin gobe,hakan yasa na kiɗima."

Ummi tace"Yanzu fa ya fita."

Cikin munafunci ta sauke ajiyar zuciya"Alhamdulillah na kasa zamane,Allah ya taimakeka"

"Ku kwantar da hankalinku,Yarima yana lafiya yanzu yayi man bankwana."

"Na barku lafiya"tace tare da miƙewa Ummi ta bita da kallo,ta kalli Maimartaba,tana zama.

***

Bacci ne ya ɗauke Aymana akan kujerar ta aza kanta a gefen gadon kusa da  hannun Yarima dake da ƙarin ruwa.

Ƙarfe biyu na dare Yarima yaji hannunshi ya mashi nauyi saboda ruwan daya ƙare har jini ya ɗan fara biyowa.

Buɗe ido yayi ko haske bata kashe ba,ya waiga sai ya ganta a takure,ya jima yana kallonta,sai yaji ta bashi tausayi ya kalli agogon dake kallon shi,zaune yayi ƙoƙarin tashi.

Ya ji ƙarfin jikinshi sosai don yaji babu ma zazzaɓi,sai jikin shi da babu kwari,Hannu yasa ya dafa kanta yana saka yatsunshi cikin gashin kanta.

Ya sauke hannun akan wuyan ta,buɗe ido tayi cikin sauri,hakan yasa Yarima saurin janye hannunshi"Ka tashi ne,bacci ya ɗauke ni"

"Me sa baki kwantaba,baki gudun ciwon wuya"

Aymana ta yi saurin zaro ido"har ya ƙare gashi jini yana  shiga"

Tana maganar ya riƙo hannun,tana kwance kanular ta rufe"Yaya kake jin jikin?"

"Alhamdulillah ina samun sauƙi"

Ya zuro ƙafarshi zai sauko"Zaka iya kuwa?"

Tayi maganar tana gewayowa "ko in taimaka maka?"

Hannunta ya riƙo"Na ji ƙarfi sosai,bari na watsa ruwa."

"Zan haɗa maka ruwan ɗumi"

Tana maganar tayi hanyar ɓanɗaki,ta kunna hita,Yarima ya koma ya kwanta,Aymana ta dawo.

Gashinshi a kwance tace"Ko jikin ne"

Baiyi mata magana ba,hakan yasa ta jingina da bango"Maimartaba ya zo duba ka,da shi da Ummi"

Sai lokacin ya waigo"Na ce asanar dasu ne"

"Nina sanar da Ummi don tayi maka Addu'a"

Tana maganar ta koma banɗakin ta tara mashi ruwa,ta fito"Zaka iya shiga"

"Ki kwanta ki huta"

Itama shiru tayi mashi,ya shiga don yin wanka,ita kuma ta fice,don haɗo mashi ruwan shayi.

Ta jima sosai lokacin data dawo ta samu yana sallolin da suka wuce shi,ta jawo tebur ta aza mashi.

Ya jima yana Azkar kafin ya miƙe"Kina buƙatar hutu fa"

"Kasha ruwan zafin nan,akwai magani yana jiranka."

Ɗauka yayi ya fara sha,saida taga yasha sosai ta miƙa mashi maganin data ɓallo.

***

Washe gari kowa so yake yaga Yarima abisa mamakin su sai suka ganshi kamar lafiya lau,Ayda kuwa sashen Ummi taje tayi zaune tun safe,ƙarfe sha ɗaya Aymana da Yarima suka nufi sashen Ummi.

Saratu tana kari sukayi sallama,Ta amsa tana kallon ɗanuwanta,Ayda ta fito daga ɗakin Saratu.

Aymana tayi kamar bata ganta ba,Yarima ya kalli Saratu"Gimbiya ina Ummi?"

"Tana ciki."

Yayi hanyar shiga Ayda tace"Barka da Safiya Yarima"

Shiru yayi ya tura ƙofa don shiga,Saratu tace"Bari na tada mashi Ummi."

Aymana ta zauna kan kujera, tana ɗaukar littafin da Saratu ta ajiye 

"Har sai yaushe zaki fahimci baki kai matsayin dakike son kai kanki ba a gidannan"Cewar Ayda dake ƙara kusanto Gimbiya Aymana.

Shiru na tsawon lokaci,Aymana tana nazarin kalaman Ayda,sai dai ta sa a ranta ba zata tanka mata ba.

"Matsayi ba kai kake jawoka kanka shiba,zuwanki masarautar nan naɗan lokaci ba zai sa a sauya muhimman al'adun cikinta ba,ada idan Yarima baya jin daɗi akan taru akanshi don dubiya gare shi."

Sai lokacin Aymana ta tabbatar da hasashenta,hakan yasa tace"Ba kowane yake sanin komai na gidan Magaji ba,sai wanda isar shi takai isa,Izzar shi ta isa nunawa,mulkinshi ya isa kwatantawa.wanda suke da darajar sanin rashin lafiyar Yarima sun ji har sun dubo shi."

Ta ƙarashe zancenta tana mai miƙewa tsaye,ta nuna Ayda"Ina mai nusar dake akan shiga gona ta a karon da bazaki iya fisshe da kanki ba"tayi maganar cikin izza.tare da yin hanyar ɗakin Ummi don bin Yarima.

****

"Ya kasance babu wani da ya isa tunkarar ɗaki ko sashen da TAKOBIN gidannan yake,sannan kuma an saka dakarun tsaro,yawanci tawagar sarkin yaƙi a wajan suke,sakamakon hari da ake kawowa Takobin,bayan hakan an sihirce Takobin ta yadda babu wanda ya isa  taɓata, sai magada masarautar dake da mallakinta."

Aymana ta jinjina zancen Mama tace"To amma miye dalilin yin hakan."

"Duk masarautun nahiyar nan gurinsu mallakar Takobin,har ya kai ga an kama wani da yazo fita da TAKOBIN,sai dai ya samu tsattsauran hukunci"

Aymana ta jinjina kai tare da yin shiru,maganganun suna tasiri sosai a zuciyarta.


Ko da ta koma ɓangarenta Farida ta kawo mata kayan lambu a farfajiyar da take hutawa,yau tunaninta kaf akan Takobin gidansune,da kuma hanyoyin da zata bi don mallakarta cikin sauƙi.

***

Maimartaba ne zaune akan karagarshi yau babu annuri a tattare da fuskarshi yana zaman jiran Jakadiya ne bisa aiken da yayi mata domin kiran Gimbiya Ummi da kuma Hajiya Maigado matanshi.

Jakadiya ta shigo da saurinta kamar zata faɗi ta zube gaban Maimartaba"Allah ya taimakeka,Fari mai farar Aniya!turnuƙu kake zaki maganin ƙananun namun daj!."

"Je magana ki!"yace mata yana gyara zama.

"Uwayen ɗakina suna hanyar zuwa don ansa kiran Sarkin sarakuna"

Shiru yayi mata ba tare da yayi magana ba,ta miƙe daidai lokacin Su Ummi suka shigo, Jakadiyya tayi masu sannu ta fice.

Gaishe da shi sukayi kowa ya ja yayi shiru ganin yanayinshi na yau,an ɗauki lokacin kafin ya fara magana"Ya zama kune makusanta na,kune zan fara sanarwa abinda na yanke shawara da kuma abinda xan aiwatar,sai dai hakan baya nufin ina neman shawarar ku ko dogon zance."

"Allah ya taimakeka!"cewar Ummi.

Hajiya Maigado dai tayi shiru,Sarki ya cigaba"Ban fara shedawa kowa ba,ina son sanar daku zanyi Murabus daga kujerata."

Wata iriyar razana su ka yi, Gimbiya Ummi tace"Saboda mi?Mai martaba amma yanzu ba shine daidaitaccen lokacin murabus ɗinka ba"

"Me hakan yake nufi,ko kana da wata matsala da mulkinka?"cewar Hajiya Mai gado.

"Nayi hakanne don karin kaina da kuma al'ummar garina"

Cigaba yayi da sheda musu yadda yake son ya ɗora wanda zai hau mulki na gaba akan daidai kafin rasa shi a doron duniya.

Bai jira cewar su ba ya miƙe yayi ciki,sun jima suna zare zaren ido babu wanda Yayi magana, Ummi ta fara miƙewa kanta yana mata mugun sarawa.Tayi cikin gida.

Hajiya Mai gado tayi ɓangaren Yarima Saifu,tana kiranshi don sanar dashi"Wannan yazo daidai lokacin da kowa zai san kaine ya fi cancanta ka zama Sarki saifu mulki yana gab dawowa hannunnu."

***

Kan Kujera Ummi ta faɗa tana karanto addu'o'i don samun sassaucin abinda take ji,magana ta farayi ita ɗaya"Mesa Sarki zai mana haka?miyasa da wuri haka,miyasa zai jefa mutanan gidanshi a tashin hankali,Mesa zai kauda zaman lafiyar da muke farin cikin mun fara samu"

Tana maganar ta miƙe tana kwallawa wata Baiwa kira don taje kira mata Yarima.

Aymana tana zaune Yarima yana shan shayi ahankali,lokaci bayan lokaci yana duba wani littafin hikaya da yake nazari akai.Baiwar tayi sallama ta durƙusa.

"Barka da hutawa magajin gobe,Lafiya uban gidan talakawa!Magaji kake kafi ƙarfin yaro!Allah yaja zamanin Sarkinmu na gobe!!!"

Yarima bai motsaba sai wajan  sauke kofin hannunshi,ji yayi maganarta ya ƙara mashi wata izza "Me ke tafe dake?"

"Gimbiya Ummi tana son ganawa da kai cikin gaggawa."

Yarima ya miƙe don baya wasa da kiran mahaifiyar tasa,Ya kalli Aymana kamar zai yi magana sai kuma yayi shiru Baiwar ta fice cikin sauri.

Yarima ya isa ƙofar yana sauri a tsaye ya sameta,bata jira komai ba ta sheda mashi ƙudurin Sarki nayin murabus.

Wata kaɗuwa tazo mashi a matuƙar gigice yace"Hakan ba zai faru ba."

Ficewa yayi da sauri,fadar Maimartaba ya shiga,Yana zaune da wani bafade gefen shi.ya rima yayi mashi nuni akan ya fita.

Yarima ya zube gaban shi"Allah ya ƙara maka nisan kwana,banzo don jayaya dakai ba,nazo Don baka hakuri akan janye ƙudirinka"

Babu alamar wani abu a tare da Sarki yace"Wasu nasarori ake sadaukarwa don cimma wasu Nasarorin Yarima.wannan shine lokacin da zanyi murabus domin nasararka Yarima."

Arazane Yarima ya kalli sarki,tare da matsawa gabanshi"Karka yi haka ina mai tuba gareka,ba zani iya kwatankwacin abinda kake yiba."


"Ka yarda mubar muguwar kaza ta shiga akurki?"

Yarima yayi shiru"Inaso ka shirya zan sanar ranar murabus ɗina kaine zaka zama Sarki ga mutanena"

Yarima ya dafe kanshi tare da rufe idanuwanshi ya buɗe su da ƙarfi so yake ya ƙaryata abinda yake ji,sai dai kuma tabbas gaskiya ne abinda yakeji ɗin,A matuƙar razane yace"Bana da gurin ganin zaka sauka mulki nina mallaki mulkin Ya mahaifina,bana son yin gardama amma ina mai roƙo daga gareka."

"Ya isa!"

Abinda Maimartaba yace kenan, Yarima yasani daga faɗin haka babu wanda ya isa ya ƙara magana bayan shi.

Cikin gigita yafice,ya na dafe da kan shi.

*SHAFI NA SHA SHIDDA. 16*

Ɓangaren shi ya nufa a gigice, ahanya wasu bayi suke gaidashi amma sam Yarima baya cikin hayyacin shi,ya sani sarai murabus ɗin Maimartaba dai-dai yake da ɗago fituntunu a gidan.

Tun a farfajiya ya fara ɓalle agogon hannunshi,ya shiga yana mai cire Jabba daya ɗora saman kayanshi,wurgi yayi da rigar kan Kujera tare da agogon daya fitar 

Hakan shi ya ja hankalin Gimbiya Aymana.kaɗan ta kalle shi ta kauda kai.

Kaiwa ya farayi yana komowa.ya fara haɗa hannuwanshi yana taɓawa a hankali ya fara magana"Sam bana son mulki da abinda ke cikinsa,miyasa Maimartaba zai yi murabus kuma yace nine zan hau karagar shi,ba zan iyaba bazan iya mulkar mutanen gidannan ba,Miyasa sai ni bayan yana sane akwai  mutane da suke jiran kujerar shi."

Gimbiya Aymana tana kallon shi ta aza ƙafa daya akan ɗaya.Wani murmushi ta fara yi kafin ta fara magana"Ba a raba harshe da haƙori! 
Kowa ya keta riga tasa, ya san inda zare ya ke! In Allah ya so falke sai kayansa ya tsunke a bakin kaba! Sai wani ya rasa wani kan samu!"

Ta ida zancen tare da miƙewa tsaye,har lokacin Yarima kallon ta yake,maganganunta yake nazari.

"Mi yasa kake jin ba zaka iya mulkar mutanen gidan nan ba?kana son mulki Yarima sai dai kana tsoron sha'anin cikinta,mi yasa sai su zasu so zama Sarakuna kai banda kai?ka manta Wanda Allah ya zuba wa garinsa nono ba zai sha da tsamiya ba! Ko wane gauta ja ne sai dai ba a kai shi rana ba."

Hannunshi ta riƙe"kayi Alfahari da kanka,ka kuma amince zaka iya mulkar duk wanda yake ƙarƙashin ikonka."

Kallonta yake maganganunta na yau sunyi tasiri sosai a zuciyar shi,Yarima ya rungumeta yana aje lumfashi da ƙarfi"Ina ji kamar bazan iyaba Aymana"

Akaron farko da ya kira sunanta"Kaifa ɗan sarkine, Sarkin da babu kamarshi a nahiyarmu,da yardar Ubangijin musulunci zaka yi nasara"

Tana maganar tana janye jikinta,ajiyar zuciya ya sauke tare da komawa kan Kujera ya zauna.

****

Washe gari mai martaba ya kirayi kowa masu riƙe da masarautun gidan don sheda masu ƙudirinshi na son yin murabus,

Waziri,Galadima,sarkin Yaƙi,shantalin sarki,da sauran Yaran shi maza.

Bayan ya gama bayani kowa ya fara magana,sarki ya masu bayanin yana so ne wanda zai mulki ya samu horo daga wajan shi.

Galadima yace"Allah ya taimakeka,kayi uzuri nan da wani lokaci"

Maimartaba baiyi magana ba,Waziri yace"To Alhamdulillah dama muna jiran wannan lokacin,zuwa yaushe ka yanke za a fitar da masu son zama karagarka.?"

Yarima Saifu ya gilgiza kai"Babu buƙatar fitar da wasu sunayi,cancanta kawai za a duba,nine zan hau karagar mulki"

Sarki ya gyara zama,baiyi magana ba.

Yarima Amin ya sunkuyar da kanshi ƙasa,shi baya jin daɗin komai balle bayyana wani abu dake zuciyar shi.

Haka aka tashi daga taron sauran ɓangarorin suna murna zasu zama akan karaga.

Waziri yana isa gida ya shedawa Inna da Ayda,murna suka kama yi.

Ayda tace"Baba daga lokacin da ka hau karagar mulki zaka tilasta Yarima Amin aure na ko baya so"

"Wannan ba shine abu na farko ba,abu na farko Zan ƙara nuna banbanci tsakanin talaka da mu,na kuma kawo sauyi tsakanin gidajen nan,ba zan lamunci yin mulki kamar yadda ake gudanar dashi yanzu ba."

Yana magana ya miƙe don zuwa gun Bokanyar shi,yana son samun bayani akan abinda zaije ya dawo.

****

"Na shedawa Maimartaba nine na cancanta da riƙe kujerar shi."

Gimbiya Mai gado ta sauke ajiyar zuciya"In tururuwa ta tashi lalacewa sai ta yi gashi!ka kwantar da hankalinka Yarima Amin bazai taɓa mulkar muba,kaine zaka hau mulkin gidan nan."

***

Kamar wasa gida ya hargitse akan maganar murabus ɗin Maimartaba,kuyangi,bayi da barori kowa maganar yake,fadawa kuwa hankalinsu ya tashi addu'a kawai suke mulki ya koma hannun Yarima Amin.

Daga sauran Masarautun dake maƙotaka da su Maimartaba yana ta samun saƙon fatan Alkhairi da kuma takardun koyon bayan Yarima Amin a matsayin Sarki,domin shine yake mutunta su da zuwa gaishe dasu baya taƙamar masarautar daya fito itace mafi girma a cikin masarautun yankin.

Maimartaba ya yanke kwanaki Ukku ga dukkanin mutanan dake son hawa kujerar shi,su aiko da takardu na son hawa,yayi hakanne don gane su waye zasuyi jayayya da Yarima Amin.

***

Jakadiya ta turo ƙofar ɗakin Gimbiya Maigado cikin sauri tana mai zuɓewa a gaban ta"Allah ya ja kwananki,uwar ɗakina."

"Me ke tafe dake"

Jakadiyya ta lumfasa tare da faɗin"Ranki ya daɗe an faɗo daga kan dabino ana neman zarcewa cikin rigiya a ɗakin nan"

Arazane ta ɗago"Me hakan ke nufi Jakadiya?"

"Na ji cewar Maimartaba Yarima Amin yake son ɗaurawa a kujerar shi"

Tsaye ta miƙe tare da faɗin"Ƙarya ne!! Hakan ba zai faru ba!! Maraya baya shakkar mutuwar uwar wani!!haka makaho baya tsoron ɓata madubu!!!"

Tayi maganar tana mai jawo Alkebbar data cire,tana ƙoƙarin azawa saman kayan ta, Jakadiya tace"Allah ya huci zuciyar ki,ban faɗi maki don tada hankalin kiba,ina mai tuba a gare ki,ina da shawara."

Gimbiya Maigado har ta kai ƙofa sai kuma ta juyo"Birnin kura ba a sa kare dillanci!!!"

Miƙewa tsaye Jakadiya tayi tana mai sakin shu'umin murmushi tare da kallon Gimbiya maigado tace"A bakin tsoho goro yake da daraja! In da yaro ya tsinci wuri nan ya kan fi saurin tunawa!!!"

Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke tare da dawowa ta zauna"Miye shawarar ki Jakadiya?"

***

Tunda ta tashi take yi shirinta bata jira kowa ba ta fito yau tana son zuwa ɗakin tarihin masarautar,har ta fice Farida ta biyota da sauri"Allah ya taimake ki baki buƙatar rakiya ne?"

Bata waiwayoba ta cigaba da tafiya,hakan ya tabbatar wa Farida babu laifi bin ta.

Sai dai a bakin ƙofa aka tsayar da Farida sai Gimbiya Aymana ce kawai ta shiga.

Littattafan tarihin masarautar ta fara ɗauka tana nazari akansu,ta jima sosai ta miƙe tana kallon zanen TAKOBIN da akayi a jikin wani bango,ta rausayar da kai a fili tace"Masoyin kwaɗo bana kifi bane!!!!"

Ta juya tana ɗauko tsofaffin takardun tarihin mabuƙata sarautar gidan,tana son ganin yadda suke gabatar  ƙudurinsu da kuma yanayin tsarin rubutun su,ta jima tana nazari akansu.

Sosai kanta yayi zafi,hakan yasa ta kifa kanta,tana son samun sauƙi.Yarima Amin kuwa nemanta yayi sosai baiganta ba sai wata Kuyanga ta sanar dashi taga Farida a ƙofa gidan tariyi aganinta suna tare.

Ya jima tsaye akanta,baiyi magana ba,ƙamshin turaren shi ne yasata saurin ɗagowa,Yarima ya harɗe hannuwanshi a ƙirji"Ina neman ki tun ɗazu Lafiya kike nan?"

Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke"Mai nama shi kan nemi wutar gashi!"

Murmushi yayi har sauti yana fita,ya ganota sarai kwanakin nan tana taƙama da kanta"Me hakan yake nufi?"

"Ina duba tarihinku da kuma hanyoyin bi don gabatar da son zama karaga, Alhamdulillah tunda gaka kazo komai zai zo mani da sauki"

Zama yayi kan wata kujera Aymana ta miƙe ta ɗauko abin buɗata wajan rubuta.bata kalleshi ba ta ajiye ta zauna ta fara rubutawa.

Yarima ko motsi baiyi ba zuwa can ta miƙa mashi"Na gama rubuta takardar da zamu bawa fada don ka zama Sarki"

Yarima ya kalleta"Ni na ce maki ki rubuta,ina kikasan cancanta ta irin haka?"

Miƙewa tayi tsaye ta kwaso littattafan data gama dubawa ta ajiye gabanshi"Anan nayi nazari,kuma na gane a duk cikin mabuƙata sarautar babu wanda yake da wankakken hannu kamarka."

"Mine me?"

"Na gama rubutuna,zaka iya gabatar da takardar ga fada"tana maganar tana yin hanyar ficewa don sai yanzu ta fahimci taso tayi karanbani wajan shiga shirginshi.

Sashen Gimbiya Ummi ta nufa don duk yau bata gaida ita ba,daga can ne ta wuce ɓangaren Mama.

Shi kuwa Yarima ya jima a wajan kafin ya miƙe da takardar ya nufi fada don gabatarwa kamar yadda Aymana tace.

***

Kuyanga Fadima ta fito daga ɓangaren Gimbiya Maigado tana sauri da takarda a ahannunta,sashen Aymana ta nufa cikin sa a ta haɗu da Farida ta tsaya cikin nuna tashin hankali.

"Don Allah Farida ki taimakeni ki ƙarasa da saƙon takardar nan zuwa fada,aikena akayi gaya Yarima Amin yana kirana"

Farida batayi niyar amsar takardar ba,jin tace zata amsa kiran Yarima hakan yasa ta amsa tana faɗin"To kiyi sauri"

Farida ta amsa tana saurin nufa Fada,Fadima kuwa ta laɓe tana kallonta har ta shige,fitowa tayi tana cizon yatsa ta koma wajan Hajiya Maigado da Jakadiya tace"Na yi kamar yadda kika ce Allah ya taimakeki."

"Za ki iya tafiya"

***

Gida ya fara sauyawa anfara shirin bikin Murabus ɗin Maimartaba dai-dai ranar kuwa zai sanar da Magajin shi da kuma naɗashi sarautar.

Angama tattara takardun masu buƙatar sarautar,abin mamaki mutane daga waje sunfi yawa  cikin gida daga Waziri,Yarima Saifu sai Yarima Amin.

Babban abinda ya ruɗa mahukunta shine Takardar Mace a cikin jerin masoya karagar mulki,Mai Martaba ya amshi takardai yana dubawa sai lokacin ya gane Aymana ce.

Tsaye yatashi yana mai dogara sandarshi ƙasa da ƙarfi"Ina so a kiramin magajin gobe"Yayi maganar cikin kaushin murya.

*SHAFI NA SHA BAKWAI. 17*

Babu ɓaga lokaci ya iso fadar yana mai durƙusawa"Allah ya ƙara maka nasara..."

Bai idaba Maimartaba ya kalli mutanan wajan,cikin ƙanƙanin lokaci suka fice.

Sarki ya zauna"Mi wannan yake nufi?"

Amsar takarda yayi yana karantawa,cikin gigita ya miƙe yana shirin fita,bincike ya farayi a fadar.kafin ya shiga ciki a ɓangaren Ummi ya barta hakan yasa ya nufi wajan.

Tun a ƙofa ya fara kiran sunanta,kafin ya fara magana"Me wannan yake nufi,kina tunanin zaki iya saka hannunki a jerin manema karagarmu?Nan masarautar Toro ne ba Darul-Bilyam ba,har kike son zama Sarauniya?"

Aymana ta miƙe ganin Yarima ya kai maƙura wajan tunkarota,ja tayi ta tsaya cak,cikin mamaki yau an samu wanda yake mata tsawa yake mata hayaniya akai ba tare da ta ɗau hukunci ba.

"Isa,Izza,mulkin sarautarku a ƙarƙashin mulkin gidanmu yake,ya zama dole ki ƙasƙantar da kanki wajan girmama masarautar mu"

"Dakata!!!" Aymana ta faɗa cikin hucin zuciya.

"Kana min magana akai ta yadda bana fahimtarka,kayi ƙoƙarin tsabtace kalaminka akan masarautarmu bazan laminta ba! Da kake faɗar inason mulkarku akanme?waye yace maka nace zan mulke ku?"

"Gashi ki duba rubutunkine,ko zaki musa,Nace ko zaki min musu!!!"

Yayi maganar cikin ƙara ji,Aymana tasa hannu tana duba takardai abin mamaki kalar rubutunta ne akayi amfani wajan rubutun.

Kankujera ta faɗa tana dafe kai,Yarima ya yarfe hannuwa"Baki da abin cewa kin aikata kenan?"

"Ban aikata ba,sam wannan ba rubutuna bane"

"Amma ke kikayi aiken zuwa fada."

Aymana ta miƙe tana nufarshi,Yarima ya ja baya"kar kizo min nan kar kizo min nan"

"Idan ba ke ki ka yi aiken ba taya Farida zata kai saƙo zuwa fada"

Gimbiya Ummi ta buɗe ƙofa tana fitowa da sauri"Wai me nake ji haka?"

Juyawa suka yi suna kallonta,Aymana ta durƙushe kan guiwoyinta,dai dai ƙafafun Gimbiya Ummi,ta kalli Yarima"Ba magana nake maka ba?"

Aymana tace"Laifinane Ummi Laifinane."

Tana maganar tana miƙewa,ta fice,bajimawa ta dawo Farida tana binta baya,a tsakiyar falon Aymana ta kalli Farida,ta dafa kafaɗunta duka biyu,ta jijjigata.

"Kinyi bacci ne ko me Farida?"

Sai kuma ta fara sauke mata mari a gefen kuncinta,Farida ta zube a gabanta"Ina mai tuba gareki uwar ɗakina."

"Yaushe na Aike ki da wannan takardai zuwa fada?"

Cikin zare ido Farida ta kalla,ta maida idonta kan Yarima dake huci"Wallahi ba ke kika aikeni ba"

Aymana ta miƙe taye ta dafe kai,ta kalli Farida za ta yi magana Gimbiya Ummi tace.

"Zan barku da iyawar ku,idan ba zaku iya yimin bayani ba"

Farida ta matsa gaban Ummi tana gaya mata wadda ta bata takarda zuwa fada.

Da sauri Yarima ya matso yana duƙawa"ke baki da hankali zasu aike ki kije?"

Aymana ta faɗa kan wata Kujera,Yarima ya fice cikin sauri.

Gimbiya Ummi ta kalli Aymana"Kar wannan ya fara gusar da tunaninku!kar ku taɓa tsumayen Alkhairi inda baku ga haske!!"

Tayi maganar tare da kallon Farida"Wannan makircine kar in ƙarajin an sakaki a ciki."

Farida ta miƙe tana ban haƙuri tare da barin ɗakin.

****

Waziri ne zaune gaban Maimartaba yana kora mashi zance akan shigar Aymana jerin mutanen dake son zama kan karagar.

"Allah ya taimakeka,wannan wata tawayace Aminu yasamu,akwai munafuncin matarshi tanason amfani dashi don son cimma wata manufa ta ta"

Gyaran murya kawai yayi tare da faɗin"Zan nemeka zuwa wani lokaci."

Cikin sauri ya miƙe"Allah yaja da ranka"

***
Lokacin da Yarima Saifu yazo da nashi maganar,Maimartaba ya kalleshi"Haka kake gani Saifu?"

"Kwarai kuwa Allah ya taimakeka,tana son amfani da ƙarfin mulkin shi don mulkar nahiyarmu,ganin cewar basu da abokan gaba da suka wuce mu."

"Zan duba zancenka Yarima"

*** 
"Ban taɓa tunanin za a tsaya kaina ayimin irin wannan kalaman ba Mama?"

Mama ta ɗago ta kalleta"Yanzu aka fara Aymana dole Kiji ki ƙi ji,ki gani ki kauda idon ki."

Ajiyar zuciya Aymana tayi Mama ta ci gaba"Makircin Gimbiya Maigado kenan"

Aymana tayi murmushi tare da miƙawa"Zan sanar dasu muguwar miya bata ƙarewa a  tukunya! Haka kuma ba a cewa maci wake ya sha ruwa!! Mai da ruwa rijiya ba ɓanna bane!!"

Tayi maganar tare da murmushi tana ficewa.

A bakin ƙofa akayi kiciɓus Aymana da Ayda dama an kwana biyu ba a haɗu ba,Aymana ta ɗan yi saurin bata hanya don taga tana niyar haɗa kafaɗa da ita.Ayda ta juyo "Dole ƙanwar naƙi!ruwa ya ƙare wa ɗan kaba."

Batayi magana ba sai tsayawa da tayi Ayda taci gaba"Jibi i yanzu mulki yana hannun mahaifina,wanda yazo don son mulki zai tattara komatsai ya koma gida.

Murmushi Aymana tayi ta juyo tana fuskantar Ayda"Ayda kike ko wa? Ina so ki sani komin lalacewar Masa ta fi kashin shanu!!!"


Tana faɗan haka ta yi tafiyata abinta,a ɓangaren ta kuwa, cire kaya tayi ta watsa ruwa ta dawo tayi shiri,sai da ta gama tsab ta koma ta kwanta sai dai maganganun Yarima suna mata yawo a kunnai,musamman yadda ya ƙasƙantar da sarautar gidansu ya fifita tashi masarautar.

Yarima kuwa yana fada acan ya tantance an fita da rubutun takardar da yakaine aka yi anfani wajan yin rubutun takardar,ya so zurfafa bincike amma Maimartaba ya ce ya ƙyale kawai.

Tana tsaye gaban Madubi kallon kanta take tana maganganu"Mi yasa zai raina masarautar dana fito,miye suke taƙama da shi, TaKOBI? Miyasa zai manta asalin takobin daga masarautar mu ta fito."

Ta jijjiga kanta"Ya zama dole na ɗaukaka Masarautar mahaifina,na mayar musu da mulki da ƴancin su ta yadda babu wani da ya isa ya nuna Izzar mulki akan mu!!!!!

Ta ida maganar tana kaiwa Mudubin duka da ƙarci cikin zafin zuciya.

Ƙara yayi tare da fashewa dai-dai lokacin ya shigo ɓangaren yayi ɗakin da sauri.

Tana tsaye dafe dakai"Me faru anan?"

Juyowa tayi tana daidaita tsayuwarta Yarima ya gane tsantsar damuwa atare da ita,yaga kuma abinda ta aikata.

Ya koma kan Kujera ya zauna"Idan a gidannan ne zaki cigaba da azalzalar zuciyarki."

"To miye don zuciyata ta azalzala bayan ina cikin masarautar data zarta Masarautar Bilyam?"

Tayi maganar tana duba hannunta dake zafi,sai taga ashe ta yanke hannu,Yarima ya kalleta cikin sauri ya miƙe,ya nufeta.

Yana kama hannun"Kinga ni Ko?"

"Bar min Hannu na."tace tana janyewa

Yarima ya riƙe ɗayan hannun tare da faɗin"Ayamana"

Tsak ta tsaya,hakan ya bashi damar zaunar da ita bakin gado ya durƙusa gabanta tare da buɗe tafin hannun,sai yaga madubin daya fashe a ciki.

Ya ɗago ya kalleta"Me kike shirin aikatawa wata rana zaki illata kanki"

Tun lokacin daya kira sunanta ya riga ya gama kashe mata jiki,Ya miƙe tsaye yana dube dube,ajikin gadonta ne yaga loka yana duɗewa ya fiddo akwatin taimakon gaggawa.

Ya buɗe tare da fara gyara mata hannun,Aymana ta rufe idonta don ya saka mata ruwan magani mai zafi a ciwon.

Hawaye ta farayi sam bai saniba,yana kusa da gamawa hawayen suka zuba kan hannunshi.

Da sauri ya ɗago,ya ji tausayinta sosai koba komai babu wani nata a kusa da ita yasan shine dalilin dayasa ta aikata hakan.

Zai saka filasta Ayamana tace"Kar ka saka"

Ya aje yana rufe akwatin,ya miƙe ya zauna gefenta,ya ɗan karkata yana son fuskantarta.

Aymana ta juyar da kanta,yasa hannu ya maido da fuskarta kanshi.

Yakai hannun shi yana goge hawayenta,sai dai baiyi magana ba,zuciyar Ayamana ta karye sai ta saka kuka tana ɗora kanta kan cinyarshi.

Wani irin tashin hankali yaji a zuciyar shi"Haba Kar kiyi kuka,saboda laifin da akai miki kike kuka?".

Yayi maganar tare da ɗagota ya mayar da kanta akan kafaɗarshi,yasa hannu yana murza bayanta alamar rarrashi.

Wani sanyi Aymana taji hakan yasa ta fara sauke ajiyar zuciya"Wa ya faɗa maki matar Sarki tana kuka" 

Aymana ta ɗago da kanta"Ina da masaniyar hakan,Amma kuka yakan zo lokacin da rashin muhimmanci ya fara baiyyana a rayuwarsu,ban taɓa tunanin akwai rashin godiya tsakaninka da Masarautar ku ba,sam bamuyi tunanin karramawar da muka yi maku batakai girman dubawa ba."

Tayi maganar tana miƙewa tsaye,Yarima ya miƙe yana murmushi,yasan dole taji zafin
Maganar shi amma alokacin yana cikin zafin zuciya.

*SHAFI NA SHA TAKWAS. 18*

Taku biyu ya ƙara zuwa wajen ta, "Ba na son jin kina faɗar ban ɗauki masarautar ku da muhimmanci ba, ki sani Sarkin Bilyam yana da matuƙar muhimmanci a wajena, yanzu haka ban sanar dake zuwana nawa ba bayan dawowar mu, jiya kamar yanzu ina tare da shi."

Aymana ta juyo ta kalleshi, hakan ba zai sa ta ji sanyi ba, sai dai jinjina kai kawai da tayi, Yarima yayi hanyar fita tare da faɗin "Zan turo Farida yanzu ta gyara maki ɗakin." Yayi maganar yana fita.

Bin bayansa tayi da kallo, ba jimawa sai ga Farida ta shigo ta zube a gabanta "Allah ya huci zuciyar Uwar ɗakina, ya sanyaya zuciyarki, ke mai yafiya ce ga mutanen ki, ina mai tuba gareki akan abin da na aikata ba tare da sani na ba."

Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya, Farida ta lumfasa hakan ya tabbatar mata da Uwar ɗakin ta ta ba zata tanka ba, ta miƙe ta isa wajan da aka ɓata ta hau gyarawa.

***
Washe gari mutanen gidan ko wanne shirye-shirye ya ke don bikin murabus ɗin Mai martaba, Yarima Amin yana tare da Sarki duk wasu shirye shiryen ɓangaren shi ne yake tsaye akai ana aikatawa.

Aymana kuwa a ɓangaren Gimbiya Ummi tayi zamanta, sai marece ta tashi don zuwa wajen Mama ta gaisheta, Mama tana zaune da wasu bayi suna harhaɗa wasu kaya a tsakar gida Aymana ta gaisheta, Bayin suka gaishe da Aymana ta amsa tare da zama kan kafet ɗin gefen Mama.

Mama ta kalleta "Ba ki haɗu da mutumin na ki ba?"

Sai da ta ɗan yi shiru kafin tace "A'a banganshi ba, tun fa safe, sai dai nasan aiyuka sun sha kan shi."

"Gaskiya kam, yanzu ma shayi ne ya kawo shi."

Aymana ta yi shiru Bayin suka kwashe kayan, Mama ta basu umarnin tafiya.

***
Tun safe gida ya ɗau harama baƙi suka fara zuwa daga masarautun Nahiyoyin dake maƙotaka dasu don amsa goron gayyatar masarautar Toro akan Liyafa da Sarki ya shirya don bikin murabus ɗin shi.

Yarima yana kan shirin shi fararen kaya ya saka ɗinkin ya amshi jikin shi, ya aza rawani  sai dai rawajin iya kaine bai gewayo fuskar shiba, sai Asfa da rawanin yake dashi, ya saka takalmi tare da fesa turare ya ɗauko  agogon hannu yana ɗorawa ya fito.

Ya samu Farida tana falon tana ajiye kayan karin su, ɗan tsayawa yayi tare da faɗin "Mai ɗakin ku ta fito kuwa?"

Cikin sauri ta zuɓe tana gaishe shi tare da faɗin "Eh ranka ya daɗe  ta fito, har ma ta bani saƙon kiranta idan na ga fitowaka."

Yarima yayi shiru, Farida ta miƙe ta nufi hanyar ɗakin Aymana, babu jimawa ta dawo tare da rusunawa "Tana zuwa." daga faɗar haka ta fice.

Bata ɓata lokaciba ta fito, takonta ya maido da hankalin shi saboda yadda kayan adon jikinta zuke ƴar ƙara, yana riƙe da agogon.

Aymana tana sanye da wasu kayan saƙi na jinin sarauta rigar ta buɗa sosai sai dai akwai wani abin ɗaurewa  hakan yasa sigar jikinta fitowa.

Ɗan kwalin data naɗa siraran gashinta ya baiyana a gefe da gefen fuskarta,babu kwalliya fuskarta sai dai akwai jan janbaki a laɓɓanta biyu.

Inda yake ta nufa ta bishi da kallo "Barka da fitowa."

Murmushi yayi tare da faɗin"Shigarki ta ƙayatar da zuciyar Sarkin da bashi da Mulki  a masarautar da Izza bata baiyanuwa."

 Aymana wani sanyi ya ziyarceta, jin yabo daga Yarima Amin, ƙarasawa tayi ta kama agogon da yake ƙoƙarin sakawa har lokacin hakan ya bashi damar barinta don ɗaura mashi.

"Da nonon wuri dana ɗari duk farinsu ɗaya!"

Yarima ya jinjina kai jin yabon daya samu daga wajen ta "Zamu iya karyawa kafin mu fita?"

Ta gama saka agogon tare da kallonshi "Kamar bana buƙatar cin komai, hakanan yau farin ciki yake ziyartar zuciyata."

Yarima ya riƙo hannunta "Ni kuma sai na tashi da faɗuwar gaba."


"Sadauki kake faɗuwar gaba bai zama naka ba, dakewa ko wane lokaci shi yafi dacewa dakai." tayi maganar tana zama gefen kujera.

Sai kuma tayi saurin miƙewa "Yana da kyau muje wajan Gimbiya Ummi don karyawa, ko don Addu'o'i da muke buƙata daga wajanta."

"Haka ne zaki iya ɗauko mayafinki."

Aymana tasa hannu ta ja wani babban yadi mai kyalli dake ƙasa yana binta a jikin rigar, da shi ta yane jikinta suna fitowa.

Kuyanga Aisha ce ta gaishe su tare da bin su baya don yi masu rakiya.

Sun jima a wajan Gimbiya Ummi su ka yi kari, Ummi tana son Aymana sosai ganin yadda duk abubuwan yarinyar na kwarin guiwa ne zuwa ga ɗan nata.

Sai da ya miƙe don tafiya wajen taron ya koma gaban Ummi tare da durƙushewa a gabanta, Ummi tasa hannu saman kafaɗar shi "Allah ya yi Albarka a rayuwarku ya tabbatar maka da alkhairi, ya saka maka dangana akan kowane ƙaddara mai kyau ko akasin haka."

"Na gode ranki shi daɗe." ya faɗi tare da miƙewa.

Har yakai ƙofa ya juyo cikin Sa'a kuwa Aymana shi take bi da kallo, murmushi yayi ya fice Ummi tayi saurin kauda idonta akansu.

***

Sarakuna ne makyil a babbar fadar masarautar, ko wanne da shiga ta alfarma, ranar ya'yan sarakuna kansu sun bayyana, kowa yana son ganin ya hallarci wannan babban taron, Yarima Amin sai da ya bi Sarakunan ɗaya bayan ɗaya ya gaidasu cikin girmamawa.

Akan Mai martaba ne Baban Aymana yafi daɗewa, don shi kan shi Sarkin Bilyam yana mai sha'awar ganin Yarima Amin ya zama Sarki don yasan zai gudanar da adalci ga al'ummar dake ƙasan shi.

A irin yadda Mulki da muƙami yake da daɗi yau gashi ɗaya daga cikin sarakunan nahiyar su ya yanke shawarar sauka don karin kanshi.


Sai da aka fara gudanar da taron tare da jawabai daga mahukunta da kuma wasu sarakunan.

Yarima Amin yana zaune gefen yan uwanshi, su Yarima Saifu sai cika ake ana batsewa, yau yana ganin babu wani sama dashi, ganin shi ne ya saka azuciyar shi zai yi mulki bayan mahaifinsa.

Sauran ƴan uwan sarki suna gefe, su Galadima, Sarkin gida, Maga yaƙi, shantali Sai waziri da yasha Babban rawani akai.

Bayan jawabin sarakuna aka ware lokaci mara tsayi don cin abinci da ɗan hutawa ga sarakuna.

Ba jimawa aka dawo, sai dai Mai Martaba ne zai yi jawabi akan saukar shi da kuma godiya ga dubban mutanen da suka halarci taron.

Bayan godiya da Addu'o'i da yayi, ya ciga "Ba sauka ta yana nufin zan saka ido akan abubuwan gudarwar wannan masarautar ba, dole zan kula da wanda zai hau mulki, wanda zuwa yanzu zan sanar da wanda zai hau karagata."

Kowa na wajan ya ɗago yana ƙara mayar da hankali kan Sarki, Nan take ɗakin taron ya hargitse da ƴar hayaniya ƙasa-ƙasa.

Sai dai har lokacin Yarima Amin idon shi a rufe yake tun lokacin da Mai martaba yayi magana.

Yarima Saifu ya gyara zama yana murza hannuwa alamar ƙagara.

Waziri kuwa kallon Galadima yayi tare da faɗin "Lokaci na yayi Galadima."

Gyara alkyabbar shi yayi tare da gyaran murya, hakan ya maido hankalin kowa.

Mai martaba ya ansa wata takarda da magatarda yake miƙo mashi ya cigaba kamar haka.


"Sakamakon goyon baya da kuma ra'ayoyin wasu daga cikin sarakunan da suke goyon bayan masarautar mu, hakan ne ya ba da damar Yarima Amin shine zai hau karagar Mulkin masarautar nan, hak..."
