*SHAFI NA SHA TARA. 19*

Ɗakin taron aka ɗau murna da hayaniya hakan ya ɗan dakatar da Mai martaba daga maganar.

Da sauri Yarima Amin ya buɗe ido yana son tabbatar da abinda kunnuwan shi suka ji, Bilal dake gefen shi ya riƙo hannun shi yana murna, Yarima ya fara Hamdala ga ubangijin shi, kafin ya juya yana kallon duk mutanan wajen.

Take fadawa suka fara kirari, Mai martaba yana ci gaba da zance sai dai wannan lokacin babu mai sauraron shi, kasancewar maganganun da yayi sunyi tasiri wajan janye hankullan mutanen wajan.

Waziri yayi wata iriyar razana wadda har sai da Galadima ya zaunar dashi.

Yarima Saifu ya buga kanshi akan kujerar gaban shi tare da miƙewa yana barin ɗakin taron, ya nufi sashen mahaifiyar shi Gimbiya Mai gado.

Tana zaune kan Kujera da wasu Kuyangi suna tausa mata ƙafafuwanta a hargitse ya shiga yana wata irin ƙara "Ba zai yiwu ba."

"Yarima." Gimbiya ta kira sunan shi.

"Yau Abba ya ƙara tabbatar da banbancin da yake nunawa tsakanina da Amin, yau ya zama ranar da bazan manta ba a tsayin rayuwata, Abba ya miƙa mulki zuwa ga Amin a gaban ɗumbun Al'umma."

A kiɗime Gimbiya Mai gado ta miƙe hakan yasa ta hanɓarar da Kuyangar dake mata tausa.

"Kar ka tambatar min da haka Yarima Saifu."

"Ki kirani da Saifuna don yau..." Sai dai bai ida ba.

Jakadiyya ta buɗe labule cikin sauri tana zubewa gaban su "Yau wane irin juyi duniya take son yi mana? Allah ya taimakeki."

Gimbiya Mai gado ta kalleta tana jinjina kai, take ta fara kai kawo.

***

Da guda Kuyanga Aisha ta isa ɓangaren Gimbiya Ummi, don ta san uwar ɗakinsu Aymana tana can.

Ummi ta kalle ta "Lafiyar ki Aisha?"

Kuyangar ta ƙara sunkuyawa gaban Ummi tace "Na zo shaida maku abin Alkhairi, Ranki shi daɗe, Allah y..."

Kafin ta ida Aymana dake tsaye lokacin ta fito tace "Ki je maganar ki."

"Allah ya taimakeki Yau matar sarki ta zama mahaifiyar sarki, haka ɗiyar sarki ta zama matar sarki a gidan nan."

Da sauri Ummi ta miƙe "Lallai Allah yayi gaskiya, Allah shi ne mai iko."

Aymana ta durƙusa gaban Aisha tace "Waya sanar da ke?"

"Yanzu na ji a gidan nan, Mai martaba ya sanar Yarima Amin shi ne zai hau karagar shi."

Aymana ta miƙe tana murmushi ta juya ta kalli Ummi, cikin Sauri Ummi ta riƙo Aymana suna rungume juna.

Sai lokacin suka fara jiyo guɗa da hayaniya na tashi a gidan.

Ficewa Aymana tayi zata nufi sashen Baba Galadima wajen Mama, ahanya suka haɗu dariya suka yiwa juna Mama ta riƙo Aymana "Kin ga ikon Allah ko?"

Aymana tace "Muje ciki Mama."

Mama tace "Ni fa sai na ƙarasa wajen Gimbiya Ummi don shigar da murnata."

Aymana tace "Zan je ɓangarena, zuwa ku gama.

***

Taro Ya tashi Mai martaba ya sallami kowa sai dai Yarima Amin baya ganuwa ya shige cikin sarakunan dake taya shi murna.

Baba Haroun  ya duƙa gaban Sarkin Bilyam yace "Yana da kyau muga Aymana kafin tafiyarmu."

Baban Aymana ya kalli ƙanin nashi yace "Zamu bari zuwa lokacin dawowa naɗi sai mu duba ta."

Baba Haroun bai so hakan ba, sai dai ya ɗau alwashin ganinta, don baiga abinda take ba har lokacin taƙi maida hankalinta kan takobin gidansu.

Ficewa Yayi daga ɗakin taron, ya fara neman wanda zai kaishi don ganawa da Aymana.

Aikuwa bai sha wahala ba ta fito zuwa wani sashen amsar baƙi.

Ganin shi ne tayi murmushi, tare da durƙushewa gefen kujerar shi "Allah ya taimake ka Baba."

"Ba zan amsa gaisuwar ki ba Aymana, ba ki samu saƙo na ba kwanakin baya?"

"Kayi haƙuri Baba Ina kan bincike daga na ida zan..."

"Yi man shiru! Tun yaushe har gashi yanzu shi ya cika gurin shi ya zama sarki ta amfani da aurenki amma ke kin kasa dawo da martabar gidanku ta hanyar damar da kika samu na auren shi."

Shiru Aymana tayi Baba Haroun ya ci gaba "idan baki sani ba ki sani, ƙarfin ikon auren ki ne ya bashi damar mallakar sarautar nan."

"Baba Amma..."

Miƙewa tsaye yayi "Ki maido martabar gidanku Aymana, mu ma muzama mamallakan sarauta mai girma."

Yayi maganar tare da yin hanyar fita don yasan ba shi da lokaci, Aymana ta dafe kanta, ta san da gaskiyar Baba Haroun ya kamata ace zuwa yanzu ta kawo komai ƙarshe.

Ficewa tayi don komawa tana shiga ɓangarenta ta fara jiyo kirari na tashi.

Miƙewa tsaye tayi tare da yaye labulen takar falon tana kallon zuwan Yarima.

Daƙyal ya samu fadawan suka barshi, yayi saurin shigowa Aymana ta miƙe ta nufo shi Yarima kalleta yana son gane yanayinta, cikin sauri ta nufe shi tana faɗawa jikin shi.

"Barka Barka Barka da arziƙi Yarima, Barka da mallakar sarautar da babu irinta a yankin mu."

Sosai ya riƙeta jikin shi, sai dai kasa buɗe baki don magana, wani sanyi yake ziyartar zuciya shi "Na kasa yarda da yau ɗin nan Aymana, ni bama ji a jikina zan mallaki wannan gida."

"Idan rana ta fito, tafin hannu baya kare ta!"

Ɗaga ta yayi ya kalleta tabbas yasan Aymana garkuwace a gare shi "Na gode Na gode."

Kallon shi tayi tana son tantance godiyar ta miye "Na gode da tayani murna."

Ya faɗa tare da ɗan tattaro izza,Aymana ta kaɗa kai yayi hanyar ɓangaren shi Ayaman ta bishi baya sai ta jiyo sallama.

Hakan yasa ta juyo Farida ta gani "Allah ƙara maki lafiya Uwar gidan Takawa, Ana son ganin Mai martaba Sarkin Toro."

"Wa yake nemanshi."

"Gimbiya Ummi ce."

Aymana ta jinjina kai "kenan baije wajen ta ba?"

"Ba ni tunanin ya je."

"Ki ce yana zuwa."

Tana maganar ta bi bayan shi, sai dai bata same shi ba sai kayanshi data gani a zube kenan wanka ya shiga.

Tattara kayan tayi ta ajiye a mazaunin su, ta buɗe wata ma'ajiya ta aza rawanin ta fito.

****

Bokanya ta girgiza gashinta, ta kalli Waziri dake magana "Sai da nace ki dubamin taurarin Yarinyar nan amma kikace bakiga komai ba, yanzu ga irinta nan."

"Ka kula da abinda na faɗa, Yarinyar ta fito gidan da babu wani da zai saurin cimmata da sauƙi."

"Amma ga shi mu ta dalilinta an cimmana."

Dariya bokanyar tayi "Har yanzu baka yarda na faɗi maka bazaka mallaki gidan nan ba ko?"

"Kin faɗi amma ya kamata ki..."

"In yi me, Na gaya maka abu ɗaya ne ya rage mana wanda zai yiwu."

Waziri ya gyara zama, yana sauraron ta.

****

Ayda ta fasa uban kuka "Inna sai da nace Baba ya bar maganar mallakar gidannan, ya maida hankalin shi don ganin na samu nasarar zama matar Yarima."

"Ke! Yau kece kike zubar da hawaye, akan abun da bai..."

"Ai yanzu kukanne kawai nawa, shi ne zai fiddani, tun Yarima bai min nisaba Baba ya watsar da ƙudirina kan nashi."

"Maza share hawayen ki, karki ƙara saka rauni aranki, hakan zai sa zuciyarki karaya akan ƙudurinki."

Ayda ta miƙe "Ba zan taɓa karaya ba. Giwa bata gudu ɗanta yayi rarrafe!"

"Da kyau!"

***

Marece sosai Amin ya fito ya samu Aymana a  falo da Farida, Farida ta gaidashi ta miƙe ta fice Yarima yace "Bamu amsa kiran Ummi ba tun ɗazu."

Aymana ta rausayar da kai "Zaka iya fita, ban jima da dawowa daga wajenta ba."

Tayi hakanne don bashi damar ganawa da mahaifiyar shi, har yayi hanyar fita sai kuma ya juyo "Muje amsa kiran Ummi."

Ta gane Umarni ya bata, hakan yasa ta miƙe ta gyara mayafinta ta bi bayan shi.

Ummi tana babban falonta ta samu masu taya murna kowa ya fice, zama sukayi mata sannu da hutawa, Yarima ya sunkuyar da kai yayi shiru.

Aymana ta kalle shi, ta ɗan kawar dakai, Yarima ya ɗago "Na gode da kulawarki mahaifiya! Nasarorinmu sun ta'allaƙa da Addu'o'in ki.

"Allah ya tayaka riƙo Amin, ya tabbatar maka da alkhairi, ya baka ikon aiwatar da adalci Aminu."

"Amin" Aymana ta amsa tana komawa gefen Ummi.

Yarima ya ɗago zai yi magana, Ayda tayi sallama da kuyangarta  Hassatu.

Ummi ta miƙe "Zan shiga ciki."

"Ki huta lafiya"

Ganin Ayda Ummi ta tsaya, daga tsaye Ayda tace "Barka da gida."

"Ya Inna?"

"Tace zata shigo taya murna,mutane ne suka mata yawa."

Ummi ta shigewarta, Amin ya miƙe yana komawa kan kujera, Aymana ta kalle shi yana fiddo wayar shi.

"Ina taya ka murnar mallakar Sarautar gidanmu." Tayi maganar tana ƙara dawowa gefen shi.

Amin kamar ba zai yi magana ba sai kuma yaga dacewar maganar "Na amsa!"

Yace don yasan mahaifinta shi ne babba daga cikin masu ƙalubalantar samun mulkinshi, hakan yasa ya tabbatar babu wata murna daga ɓangarensu.

Juyawa tayi tana neman wata maganar da zatayi mashi.

Aymana ta miƙe ta zauna kan kujera gefen Yarima, Yarima ya ɗago ya kalleta "Bilal ne ya min saƙo mutanen Bilyam sun ƙarasa gida lafiya."

Ba ƙaramin daɗi Aymana taji ba, ganin Yarima ya yi mata magana, murmushi tayi mai sauti tace "Ban samu ganawa da su ba."

Yarima zai yi magana Ayda tace "Ba don mahauci ba da mai taro bai ci naman saniya ba!"

Da sauri Aymana ta kalleta, wani abu Yarima yaji wannan wane irin rainine zata zo kanshi tayi mashi maganganu.

Miƙewa yayi tsaye, bazai lamunta ba, ko da kuwa akan matar shi ne, balle a gabanshi, ya zama dole ya ɗau mataki akai, don yaga akwai alamar raina mulki."

Aymana ta miƙe tare da riƙo Yarima, ta juya ta kalli Ayda "Ko an raina ɗan tsuntsu ba a cin shi da gashi! Zakaran da Allah ya nufa da cara ko ana muzuru ana tsaho sai yayi! Ko kin manta da Sarki kike magana yanzu? Ki tsabtace kalamanki kafin hushin zuciyar Takawa ya hauki, ki kiyaye kar ƙaiƙayin bakinki yasa ki saka kanki a halaka."

Hankalin Ayda ya kaɗa akan matashiyar da Aymana tayi mata, amma kuma lallai a maganganunta akwai gori da kuma harshen damu acikin zancen.

Yarima ji yayi kamar sai lokacin aka fara nuna shi mai matsayi ne, wata Izza ya ƙara jin tana bin jininshi. yana fara tako Aymana ta bi bayanshi.

Sai dai kafin sukai ƙofa Jakadiyya ta shigo da sauri ta zube a gaban Yarima "Lafiya bango majinginar bayi! Toron Giwa kake baya goya marayu! Lafiya jinjirin wata sha kallo, Lafiya kwankwason jimina mai wuyar shafawa."

Tsak ya tsaya, duk kirarin da ake mashi bai taɓa samun irin wannan ba, ayau yana jin banbance-banbance na ƙarfin Izzar da ya mallaka a jininsa, kallonta yayi  tare da faɗin "Akwai magana bakin ki?"

"Allah shi taimakeka Mai martaba ya samu baƙuncin Waziri, ya sanar yana neman ka!"


"Zaki iya tafiya."

*SHAFI NA ASHIRIN. 20*

Tana ficewa Yarima ya kalli Aymana sai dai bai yi magana ba amma ta gane nufinshi na zai barta, shi kuma ya tafi amsa kiran Mai martaba.

***

Kwana biyu kowa ya ɗan nutsu a gidan, sai dai ko wane ɓangare da kalar abinda yake shiryawa.

A ɓangaren Gimbiya Mai gado sun tabbatarwa kansu Mai martaba ba zai taɓa janye ƙudirin shi ba na zaman Yarima Amin sarki, hakan ya sa suka kauda baƙin cikin su a fili yayin da zukatan su babu yalwar farinciki a ciki.

Jakadiyya ta gyara zama, ta maida hankalinta kan Gimbiya Mai gado "Allah shi taimake ki ni kaina bana farin cikin komawar mulki hannun Aminu."

"Yanzu miye abin yi?"

Shiru na tsawon lokaci, kafin Jakadiyya tace "ki yi tunani uwar ɗakina."

Ajiyar zuciya ta yi "Ba na so Aminu ya taɓa jin daɗin mulkin shi, bana so ya san farin ciki dangane da mulkin da zai gudanar, ina so ya ji baƙin ciki ta yadda da kan shi zai sauka mulki abaiwa Saifu."

"Hakan yayi komai zai gudana kamar yadda kika buƙata."

***
Tunda aka sanar ranar naɗin sarautar Yarima Amin, ranar zai zama ranar da za a bashi sandar girma, suke ta murna kowa na gidan yasan lokacin gyara yazo a masarautar.

Waziri ne zaune gaban Mai martaba wannan lokacin akwai nuna sanyin jiki da kuma miƙa wuya "Allah shi taimake ka, dama mun riga mun amince da duk hukuncin daka yanke akanmu, kuma muna masu biyayya a gareka."

Mai martaba ya kalle shi sai dai bai yi magana ba Waziri ya cigaba "A karo na babu adadi nake roƙarwa Mai sunan manya (Ayda) alfarmar aurenta da Sarki Amin."

Mai martaba ya kalleshi, sai kuma ya soma tunanin, lallai ya san Waziri shi ne kan gaba a cikin mutanen da  za su shiga hassadar Aminu, haka yasa tun bayan da yace zai ɗaura shi a matsayin Sarki yake ta tunanin hanyar da zai yi don kawar da cuta a tsakaninsu.

Dogon numfashi ya ja, wata zuciyar ta sanar da shi Auren Yarima da Ayda shi ne zai sa ya toshe cutarwa daga Waziri zuwa ga Yarima Amin.

Ɗagowa yayi ya kalli Waziri "Zan zauna da Sultan Amin."

"Na gode ranka shi daɗe." Ya faɗa tare da miƙewa ya sunkuya "Na barka lafiya."

***

Gimbiya Ummi tana gefen Maimartaba ta amsa kiran da yayi mata na gaggawa, sai dai ta soma gundira tare da ƙagaran jin kiran da yayi mata.

"Wace hanya kike gani za mubi don kange Sultan Amin daga Makircin Waziri da magoya bayan shi."

Shiru tayi na tsayin lokaci, maganar ta shige ta, ta san akwai cutarwa mai tsanani "Allah ja kwananka, babu zance a baki na, amma nasan akwai lauje cikin naɗi!"

Miƙewa yayi tsaye "Na yanke shawarar haɗa auren Sultan Amin da Ayda."

Razana Ummi tayi cikin kaɗuwa "Amma Mai mar..."

Ɗaga mata hannu yayi "Na gama hukunci na, hakan shi ne zai ba Sultan kariya, ki yi nazari akan maganar."

Sam Gimbiya Ummi bata son haɗa wani abu da mutanen gidan Waziri balle yaronta ɗaya tilo, shiru tayi na daƙiƙu, ta tabbatar haɗa aurenne kawai mafita, idan ma zata ƙi amincewa babu wata hanya ta yin gardama da hukuncin Mai martaba.

"Allah ya ba shi ikon riƙewa" cewar Gimbiya Ummi.

Mai martaba yasan bai ta ɓa samun gardama daga wajan taba, duk yadda bata son abu tofa tana daurewa wajan aikatawa ko bin umarnin shi.

Hakan yasa bayan ya sallameta ya kira Waziri ya shaidamashi zai ɗaura Auren Sultan Amin da Ayda a ranar Naɗin sarautar Amin.

***

Aymana ta na gefen Mama suna fira, sosai hankalinta ya karkata wajan firar magabatan masarautar da Mama take bata.

Kuyanga Hassatu ta shigo tana gaishe su, Mama tace "lafiya kuwa?"

"Dama Inna tace nazo na gani idan kina ciki."

"Eh ina nan."

Hassatu ta juya.

Aymana ta miƙe "Bari in tafi ciki, akwai yuwar za ta zo wajanki ne."

"Kiyi zaman ki mana."

"A'a bana son wani abunda zai ja tsegumi" tayi maganar tana yin hanyar fita.

Sai dai kafin ta kai ƙofa Ayda ta shigo cikin sauri, tana mai bin Aymana da kallo, Aymana tayi kamar bata ganta ba zata fice.

"Ƙarya zata ƙare daga lokacin da bori ya kashe boka! Lokaci yana gabatoni da zan matsayin da wasu suke taƙama dashi, daga lokacin Aurena da Sarki Amin za asan biri asan gatan sa."

Wani dogon tsaki Aymana taja "Iska tana wahalar da mai kayan kara!"

Dariya Ayda tayi "Ranar bayar da sandar girma ga Sarki Sultan ranar sabon angwancin shi."

Mama ta dakawa Ayda tsawa "Wai me haka Ayda, ku har kullum neman rigima ne aikin k..."

"A'a Mama barni na faɗa, da ta ji inda zata ji haushi ai ƙara ni na sanar da ita Mai martaba ya amincewa Sarki Amin neman aurena da yake ba tun yanzu ba."

Wata irin faɗuwar gaba Aymana taji, ba yau suka fara karo da Ayda ba, amma bata taɓa makamanciyar wannan maganar ba, tabbar tasan akwai rina akaba.

Mama za ta yi magana Aymana tace "Ingarma gidan talaka haramun! Kuwwa da kuwwa bata korar buzu! Ina so ki sani har a naɗe ƙasa ungulu ba ta rama gayyar zabuwa!"

Tayi maganar tana ficewa, sai dai fa yau ita kanta ba ta san irin yanayin da take jin kanta ba ga gabanta da yake dukan tara-tara.

A hanya take ta sauri sai hango Farida tayi da ɗan gudunta, Aymana ta dai-daita nutsuwarta da kyal dai-dai lokacin Farida ta iso "Uwar ɗakina tun ɗazu nake neman ki sai dai ban ganki ba."

Aymana ta ƙagara taji abinda Farida zata ce hakan ya sa ta tsaya tare da faɗin "Me ke faruwa a gidan nan Farida?"

 "Allah ya saka sanyi a zuciyar uwar ɗakina, Akwai zancen Takawa dake yawo a..."

Hannu Aymana ta ɗaga mata "Abinda aka faɗi man gaskiya ne kenan?"

"Ina mai tuba a gareki hak..."

Kafin ta ida Aymana ta fara sauri zuwa ɓangrenta, wani irin nauyi kanta yake mata, Farida ta bita baya da gudu-gudunta har suka  shiga.

Kuyanga Aisha suka samu tana goggoge kayan falon, Aymana ta shire Alkyabbar dake jikinta tare da yin wurgi da ita.

Farida ta zube agabanta, tana mai bata haƙuri cikin kalaman girmamawa.

Aymana ta miƙe tsaye "Dole na janye rainin dake tsakanina da Yarinyar nan."

Aisha ta durƙusa gaban ta "Ki bani izinin aiwatar da komai ya uwar ɗakina."

Aymana ta kallesu, sai kuma taga kamar su na ɗauka ko kishi ne, hakan yasa ta kalli Aymana "Sultan Amin zai auro Ayda ya zama dole yarinyar tasan akwai banbanci tsakanina da ita."

***
"Yin gardamarka tamkar bijirewa maganar Mai martaba ne, hakan zai sa ya ga damar daya baka ta sa zaka iya tsallake maganar shi."

Yarima Amin ya gyara zama sam bai taɓa tunanin maganar Auren Ayda zata samu karɓuwa a wajan iyayen na shi ba, bai san taya zai ɓullowa labarin ba.

Miƙewa yayi tare da sunkuyawa gaban Gimbiya Ummi yace "Na barki lafiya."

Ba ta yi magana ba ta bishi da kallo.

***

Shigowa yayi yana nufa ɓangaren shi don baya son wata hayaniya abinda ya dame shi ma ya dameshi hakan ya sa ko Aymana bai nema ba.

Tunani kawai yake yadda Mai martaba zai amincewa Baba Waziri auren shi da Ayda.

Tun Aymana tana tunanin shigowar shi har ta fara shirin bacci, zama tayi bakin gado tana fara tunanin tasan zuwa wannan lokacin Yarima yasan da zancen Auren kenan ya amince zai yi Auren, tun da gashi bai mayi ta kanta ba.

Bargo ta ja tare da kwantawa tana mai karanta Addu'o'i, zuciyarta tayi mata zafi wanda bata san dalilin hakan ba.

Bayan dawowar shi sallar Asuba yake son ganinta sai dai yasan ta koma nata Baccin.

Ƙarfe goma ya fito cikin shirin shi don zuwa fada, tana zaune akan kujera da kofin shayi a hannunta, tana jinshi ta yi shiru tana kauda kanta.

Tsayawa yayi kamar yadda ya ke yi ko yaushe, sai dai bai samu bakinta wajan faɗar sannu da fitowa ba.

Zama yayi kan kujerar dake fuskantar kujerar ta "Fatan Gimbiya ta tashi lafiya."

Ajiye kofin Aymana tayi, sam bata yi niyar magana ba, amma tasan bata isa aikata hakan ba, sai dai wata zuciyar ta fara karanto  babu dalilin ɗauke mashi tunda har ba soyayya ne a tsakanin suba.

"Barka da fitowa Sultan."

Shiru na tsawon lokaci, kafin ya ɗaga baki "Jiya ban samu ganawa da ke ba, ina son zama dake na musamman."

"Yanzu haka zamu iya magana!" Tace tana mai janye idonta akan shi.

Yarima ya miƙe tsaye ya harɗe hannuwa a ƙirjin shi ya ɗan fara tattaki "Ina son sanar dake abinda ke faruwa a gidan nan."

Hannu Aymana tasa tana yin tagumi ta kalle shi "Mai martaba ya sanar da haɗa aurena da Ayda ƴar gidan..."

Miƙewa tayi "Allah ya taimaki Sultan an sanar dani Mai martaba ya amince da Aurenka kamar yadda ka daɗe kana buƙata, ai babu aibu ga mabuƙaci idan ya mallaki ƙudirin shi, wannan sanarwar gareni Sultan zai samu farin cikin da ya jima yana so..."

*SHAFI NA ASHIRIN DA ƊAYA. 21*

*NA SADAUKAR DA WANNAN FEJI GABA ƊAYAN SHI GAREKI, RAMLAT A MANGA (MAI - DAMBU).*   
*MARUBUCIYAR ƘWARƘWARA, UWAR ƊAKIN MAGAJIN IZZA, FARIN CIKIN BOROROJI, ABIN FAHARIN MATAR MALAM, CIKARKIYAR  BAHAUSHIYA, MAZAUNIYAR DAULA BIYU, YAYAR ƳAR GIDAN YADIKKO, KAWA A WAJAN MRS AMIDUD, DA CIWO A RAYUWA SAI DAI RUWA BIYU DA YAKANA YA KAUDA KISHI A TSAKANIN ZUBDA JINI, INA DA BURU A MASARAUTAR JODAN, INA SO YA ZAMA DA'IMAN ABADAN A CIKIN ALHUBBU FIHI MARARATUN.🥰🥰*


Ta ɗan jinkirta ba tare da ta ƙarashe maganar ba, ta duƙa kan teburin data aza kofin shayinta ta ɗauki kofin tana mai fizzar kai don nufa cikin ɗakinta.

Lokaci kaɗan ran Yarima Amin ya ɓaci zuciyar shi ta ɗugunzuma da jin kalamanta, hannu yasa tare da fizgo hannunta da ƙarfin shi.

Kofin shayin ya faɗi tare da fashewa, hakan yasa ta ɗago ta kalle shi, sosai ya matse hannunta cikin zafin rai, tare da kallon ƙwayar idanuwanta  yace "Mai-maita abinda kika faɗa!"

Jim ta yi batare da ko motsi ba, wani zafin izza take ji, ganin shima Izzar tashi ne take tasiri a jikin shi.

Yarima ya ce"Na ce ki mai-maita abinda kika faɗa!" Yayi maganar tare da sakin hannunta.

Aymana ta girgiza kai, cikin cikar izza tace "Ai na fito daga gidan da magana ɗaya ake, ba a magana biyu!"

Tana faɗar haka ta yi ciki abinta don canza kaya saboda shayin daya ɓata jikinsu.

Yarima ya dafe kai tare da komawa sashen shi, sai dai ya kasa canza kayan sai ma faɗawa da yayi kan kujera yana huci.

***

Bayan kwana biyu Aymana ta ƙara ɗan janye jikinta a gare shi, saninta ne Amin baya son Ayda to amma miye zai sa ya nuna farin cikin shi akan lamarin.

Yau Mama ce ta shigo sashenta su ka ɗanyi fira Mama tace "Ni kuwa Gimbiya  me kike shiryawa na ranar naɗin sarautar Sultan Amin?"

"Ban fara wani shiri ba kum..."

"Yana da kyau kiyi hakan Aymana, mijinki fa zai karɓi mulki, ai ko don kar ayi maki dariya a gidannan kin jajirce."

Aymana ta ɗan yi shiru "Shi kenan Mama me kike ganin zan shirya?"

"Lokaci ya ƙure amma bari zan duba."

"Ko mi za a yi, ki sanar dani zanyi komai kika ce Mama."

***

Yau Ayda tana gidan Baba Maga yaƙi shine ƙanin Mai martaba, duk wani shirye-shiryen hidimar bikinta a gidan ne suke yi.

Goggo itace uwar gidan Maga yaƙi kuma itace ta zama kamar uwar ɗakin Ayda  da yaranta.

Ayda ta aje kayan da ta amsa hannun Kuyangarta, ta ajiye Goggo ta kalleta "Zauna nan, ni ban fahimci komai ba."

"Wajan mi fa Goggo?"

"Har yanzu ba a turo daga cikin gida Mai martaba na nemanki bane?"

Shiru Ayda tayi don dama tana jimawa bata saka Sultan a ido ba balle yanzu da ya zama Sarki tasan zai mata wahalar gani.

"Gaskiya da sake Ayda, sai kin dage, ki jifa yadda yayi ta rawar jiki lokacin da akayi auren shi amma ke ko alamar hakan babu."

"Miye abin yi Goggo?"

Goggo ta miƙe zuwa ɗakin Mijinta, yana ɗan kishingiɗe ta zauna gefe Baba Maga yaƙi ya kalleta, kafin ta fara magana "Na zo akan maganar Ayda ne, har yanzu fa Sultan Amin bai nemi ganinta ba."

Baba Maga yaƙi ya tashi yaushe "Kar kice min bata gana da Sarki Amin ba har yanzu."

Yana maganar ya miƙe yayi hanyar wace tare da faɗin "Ina zuwa" ya fice.

Wajan Mai martaba ya nufa, sun ɗan yi fira yake shigar mashi da zancen Sultan Amin fa bai buƙaci ganin Ayda ba har kawo wannan lokacin.

***

Gimbiya Ummi ta kalli Aymana dake durƙushe gabanta, nazarin yarinyar take akan maganganun da su ka yi Ummi tace "Mi ye ra'ayinki akai Aymana?"

Sunkuyawa tayi tace "Hukuncinku shine dai-dai Allah ya taimakeki."

Murmushi Gimbiya Ummi tayi "Allah yayi maku albarka."

"Amin" tace tana shirin miƙewa, shigowar Yarima Amin ya dakatar da ita.

Ta rusuna tana mashi sannu, Amin ya zaune gefen Ummi yana gaida ita.

"Ka wuni Lafiya Sultan?"

"Alhamdulillah aiyuka sun sha kaina, ina son jin miye buƙatun mutanen gidan nan na hidimar naɗin nan."

Murmushi Ummi tayi "Gimbiya Aymana ta kula da komai yanzu take sanar dani."

Ya juya ya kalleta, har lokacin kanta yana ƙasa, murmushi yayi tare da faɗin "Gimbiya matar sarki, fatan kin kula da jin daɗin Bayi da kuyangu a ranar."

Aymana ta miƙe ta koma gefen shi "Na tanadi kayan sakawar kowanne, na kuma mayar da ranar ta zama ranar walwalarsu ko da so ɗaya ne a rayuwarsu."

Gimbiya Ummi ta miƙe "Zan iya barinku?"

"A'a Ranki shi daɗe ki zauna don jin shirye-shiryen ko da akwai gyara." Cewar Aymana.

Yarima Amin ya maida hankalinshi kanta "Ina jinki"

Gimbiya Ummi ta zauna, Aymana ta ci gaba "Sai ɓangaren baƙi mata da Masarautar za ta yi, shima akwai shiri na musamman, ta bangaren jin daɗin su."

Haka Aymana ta cigaba da yi mashi bayani, wanda duka abubuwan Mama ce ta tsara mata ita iyakarta gudanarwa.

"Kasancewar ranar naɗin ya kasance ranar ankwamcin Sultan na biyu, na shirya kaya  ga kowane ɓangare na gidan nan, zuwa gobe da safe za a aika ma kowa nashi."

Ɗaure fuska Yarima yayi kaɗan, tare da faɗin "Me hakan yake nufi?"

"Zai zama anko ga magadan   gidan nan."

Yarima ya miƙe ya na faɗin "Muje ciki."

Aymana ta tashi suka yiwa Ummi bankwana suka fice.

Sai dai suna isa ɓangaren, Aymana ta yi hanyar ɗakinta, bai damu ba sanin kwanin nan haka suke a tsakaninsu.

***

Washe gari yakama saura kwanaki Ukku Naɗin sarautar, haka Aymana ta aika da kayayyaki zuwa ga mutannen gidan, wasu ɓangarori sun karɓa, sai dai wasu ɓangarorin sunyi watsin Allah tsine da kayan.

Gimbiya Mai gado ce zaune tare da Ummi acewarta tazo jin abinda ke tafiya na shirin, amma sam Gimbiya Ummi bata yarda ta sanar da ita wasu muhimman abubuwa ba.

***

Sultan ne durƙushe gaban Mai martaba, yana gaya mashi lallai ya sa Ayda tazo don ganawa da shi.

"Ya zuwa yanzu bai kamata komai sai na tunasar dakai ba Sultan, duk tunani na ka gana da Yarinyar kafin yanzu, amma sai gashi daga cikin gida an zo min da zancen."

Yarima ya russhuna "Allah ya taimakeka zanyi kamar yadda kace, ina mai bada haƙuri akan rashin aikata hakan."

Bayan barinshi turakar Maimartaba ya aika da saƙon ganin Ayda, ya bada umarnin samun shi a babban falon shi na fadar cikin gida da yamma.


Tsaye yake a cikin falon yana jiran shigowar Ayda kamar yadda Mai martaba ya bashi Umarnin zama da ita.

Shigowa tayi tana ɗan yamutsa, Yarima ya ja ya zauna kan kujera cikin mulki da taƙama, Ayda ta zauna itama tare da faɗin "Ka zo lafiya!"

Shiru yayi na tsayin daƙiƙu Ayda ta ci gaba "Na san ba zaka amsa min ba, kasancewar aurena da babu shiri a tare da kai, kuma..."

"Dakata!"

Kamar ya rufe bakinta haka tayi shiru "Na zo don jin ko akwai abubuwan buƙata daga ɓangaren ki."

"Akwai buƙatu, sannan kuma akan shirin da ake yi a gidan nan, ni sam ban amince ba saboda rashin neman shawarata wajan gudanarwa."

Yasan sarai akan abubuwan da Aymana tayi ne a gidan "Da amincewata komai ya gabata! Ki tsara buƙatunki ki bawa Jakadiyya ta isar min cikin lokaci."

Yayi maganar yanayin hanyar fita sai kuma ya juyo tare da faɗin "Zata iya bayarwa ga Gimbiya zata gabartar gareni" ya fice cikin sauri.

Ayda ta miƙe cikin baƙin ciki, wato komai Aymana ce zata yi, kenan tana da fifiko, ta wuce tana tunane-tunane.

***

Goggo ce da Inna zaune suna tsarawa Ayda abin da zata nema daga wajan shi.

Goggo tace "Ki fara neman yardar shi na a fara ɗaura aurenku kafin a naɗa shi, hakan zai sa kema ki zama cikin taƙamar kafin naɗa shi ke matar shi ce, don haka babu abinda za a goranta maki."

Inna tace "Haka ne kuma kinga idan har aka ɗaura auren kafin naɗi zamu Kaita da wuri, zai zama itace zata tare shi idan an zo dawowa da shi gida."

Ayda ta cigaba da rubuta takardarta kamar yadda suke tsara mata, haka ta rubuta sai dai ta buƙaci kuɗaɗe ne da zata yi hidimarta don ba tsarin wani zata bi ba.

***

Aymana tana cikin farfajiyar sashen ta, kayan lambu ne gabanta inibi ne a hannunta tana sha, Jakadiyya ta shigo da sallama tare da zubewa a gabanta.

"Allah ya ja da ran Gimbiya, ƴar sarki matar sarki, uwar gida awajan Sultan! Uwar ɗakin mu, kwalwalar mutanan gida!"

Aymana ta gyara nutsuwarta tare da ƙare mata kallo tace "Akwai wani abu ne a tare dake?"

"Sun taras suna gab samu!"

Aymana ta ƙura idonta kan Jakadiyya tana son gane zaren maganar  "Mi ki ke da masaniya akai?"

"Saƙo ne zuwa ga Sarki Sultan."

Tana maganar tana fiddowa, Aymana ta kalli takardu guda biyu tace "Daga wa ne ɓangarene wannan!"

"Ƴan son shiga, masu son handama da baba kere."

"Za ki iya zuwa ki dawo zuwa lokacin ya shigo?"

Jakadiyya tayi dariya "Sultan ya ɗaga darajar mai daraja, ya bada umarnin a baki, ke kuma ki isar masa."

Bata ce komai ba ta miƙa hannu ta ansa, Jakadiyya tace "Na barki lafiya Allah ya taimakeki." Tayi maganar tare da ficewa.

Aymana tayi hanyar ɗakinta, sai dai tana son ganin abinda ke cikin saƙon a falon ta zauna ta na buɗewa, cikin sa'a kuwa ta fara da takardar son fara ɗaura auren kafin naɗin sarautar shi.

Aymana ta kasa idawa sai tunani data fara yi, akan miye dalilin yarinyar na neman wannan buƙatar, tasan tabbas akwai wani abu.

Kai kawo ta farayi, ta kasa samo dalilin hakan, ta shiga ɗakinta tana zama, kaka ce ta faɗo mata arai, cikin Sauri ta jawo waya tare da yin murmushi tasan tabbas Kaka zata yi mata fashin baƙi akan takardai.

[10/29, 11:26 AM] Rahma gr: *MASARAUTA.*

*SHAFI NA ASHIRIN DA BIYU. 22*

Layin Bilkisu ƙanwarta ta kira, Bilkisu ta ɗauka suna gaisawa ta ce "Dama gobe mu ke son zuwa don taya ki shirin naɗin nan."

"Ni ba wannan ba, ki tashi ki je ki kai ma Kaka waya ina son tambayarta wani abu."

Haka suka ci gaba da waya har ta isa wurin Kaka, ta bata wayar Kaka ta amsa ta saka a kunne "Sai yau kika tuna da ni tun tafiyarki?"

Aymana tayi dariya "tsegumi ne ko Kaka?

"Dole inyi yaro har ya fiki kula damu, amma..."

"Kaka dan Allah ki saurara ni fa tambaya na kira na maki."

Kaka tace "ina jinki."

Aymana ta ci gaba da yi mata bayani tun farko har zuwa wannan lokacin Kaka ta numfasa ta ce,"Wannan wata martaba ce ake son yarinyar ta samu, kuma ba na tunanin ita ce ta tsarawa kanta, sai dai wanda yasan muhimmancin tarar sarki a ranar naɗin shi."

"Yanzu me zanyi Kaka?"

"Ki ba shi takardar sai mu saurari ranar, tun nan zamu ga ne ra'ayin shi Yarima akan yarinyar."

Haka Kaka ta ci-gaba da koyar da Aymana wasu abubuwan, sun jima kafin suka yi ban ƙwana, Aymana ta fito ta zauna a falo ta na jiran shigowar shi.

Ya ɗan jima bai shigo ba sai zuwa yamma, tana zaune kan Kujera ta ɗan zame jikinta dan hutawa, wani littafi ne hannunta akan sarauta da al'adun wasu masarautun tana karantawa.

A bakin ƙofa fadawan shi suka juya Yarima ya shigo yana sallama, Aymana ta amsa tare da miƙewa tsaye ta ajiye littafin tana ɗan saukar da kai ƙasa "Sannu da dawowa Allah ya taimakeka."

Matsawa ya yi kusa da ita, tun lokacin da aka sanar shi ne zai hau mulki ya kula da ita yadda take girmamashi wajan gaisuwa da kuma magana, sai dai yasan lokuttan da tata Izzar ne ya motsa tofa akwai aiki a gabansa.

"Fatan kina Lafiya?"

"Alhamdulillah" ta faɗa.

Sultan Amin ya zauna kan kujera hakan ne ya bata damar zama ita ma, shiru suka yi na lokaci Aymana tana son ba shi saƙon sai dai kuma bataso ya ga kamar ta ƙagara ta ba shi ɗin ne.

"Sultan zai samu abun motsa baki kuwa?" Ya faɗa yana kallonta.

Aymana ta miƙe ba tare da ta yi magana ba ta yi hanyar farfajiya, Farida ta nema ta bata umarnin kawo shayi da kayan lambu.

Lokacin da ta koma Yarima ya jingina da kujera ya ɗan saka hannu ya dafe kan shi, ta jima a tsaye tana kallon shi, tana son gane miye damuwar shi.

Farida ta shigo da tire ita da Kuyanga Aisha suka zube suna gaisuwa tare da ajewa suka fice.

Yarima bai motsa ba Aymana ta jawo tebur a gaban shi, ta mayar da tiren sama.

"Ga shayin ka"

Ta faɗa tana ɗaukar kofi ɗaya ta miƙa, Yarima ya ɗago ya amsa sai kuma ya ajiye gefe tare da ɗaukar tuffa ya kai bakin shi, duk yau bai saka komai cikin shi ba.

Nazarin shi ta yi kaɗan, ya ajiye sauran tuffa akan tire ɗin Aymana tasa hannu ta ɗauki ayaba ta ɓara tare da miƙa ma shi ya amsa ya kai bakin shi a hankali har ya cinye.

Ta gane akwai rashin cin abinci a tare da shi hakan yasa ta ɗauko za ta ƙara ma shi ya ce,"Shayi ya rage."

"Ko a kawo maka abinci? kamar akwai yunwa a tare da kai?"

Kurɓar shayin ya yi "Ba na buƙata yanzu."

Miƙewa ta yi "Yauwa na manta na samu saƙo daga Jakadiya."

Bai yi magana ba ta miƙa ma shi, ya ci gaba da kurɓar shayin shi yana ajewa ya miƙa mata hannu, Aymana ta ba shi.

Yarima ya buɗe sai da ya gama karanta duka takardun, ko da ya gama karantawa, ya jima yana nazari sai dai har lokacin bai yi magana ba.

Aymana ta miƙe ta bar wajan, ya jima a zaune kafin shi ma ya shiga ciki.

Washe gari mutanen gidansu Aymana sun zo sosai, ita kanta ta yi mamakin yadda suka zo mata, haka ta yi ta shirye-shiryenta da 'yan uwanta.

***

Ranar naɗi kuwa shiga suka yi ta alfarma, Yarima Amin cikin fararen kaya da suka sha aikin sarauta launin  toka, sai alkyabba ita ma fara ce da aiki sai sheƙi ya ke, takalmin ƙafar shi jinin sarauta sawu ciki, rawanin kan shi fari ne sai dai bai gewaye fuskar shi ba.

Aymana ta ɗago ta kalle shi tana ɗauko turaruka ta fara saka ma shi, Yarima ya ɗago ya kalleta "Ke fa naki shirin?"

"Na ka yafi nawa muhimmanci a yanzu."

Ya juya ya fara tattaki baya ta maye ma shi, idan ka ganta zaka ɗauka ta yi shiri amma sam bata kai ga shiryawa ba.

A falo ya ja ya tsaya tare da kallon Agogon Hannun shi "Za ki iya shiryawa mu fita."

Ya zauna kan kujera, Aymana ta kalle shi tana nazarin jiran da zai mata "Ka ga na dakatar da kowa akan shigowa don ka gama shiryawa, bai..."

Kasa idawa ta yi lokacin da take kallon yadda Yarima Amin ya cika kujera ya aza hannuwan shi akan hannun kujerar, tabbas tasan Yarima ya can-canci zama Sarki na duk nahiyar.

Juyawa ta yi ta shige sashenta, cikin sauri ta shirya, duka shirin ya ɗauketa  daƙiƙun da basu wuce talatin da biyar ba ta fito.

Leshi ne jikinta launin albasa mai ɗan haske, gaba ɗaya wuyanta hannuwa da kunnanta kayan adon sinari ne.

Wani ƙaton mayafi ne hannunta ya yi kalar alkyabba sai dai kuma ba alkyabba ba ne, ta ziro ƙafarta da tasha takalmi masu kwalliyar duwatsu.

Fuskarta Yarima ya fara kallo, ya yi mamakin ganin kwalliya a fuskarta duk da ba wani yawa ne ta yi ba, amma akwai bambanci da sauran ranakunta.

Miƙewa ya yi cikin azama yana nufarta tare da kamo hannunta, Aymana jikinta ya ɗan yi sanyi suna zuwa ƙofa, anan fa mamaki ya kamasu, ɗumbun al'umma da ke jiran fitowarsu.

Busa aka fara yi da kirari, ga masu kiɗa suna yi kuyangi da bayi sai guɗa suke.

Jakadiyya ta biyo bayansu cikin kirarin ban girma.

Sai da Aymana ta raka shi har babbar ƙofar fita cikin gida, kafin ta tsaya fadawa suka mara ma shi baya.

***

Cikin gida kuwa Ayda ta gama duk abubuwanta sun gama komai na shigarta ɗaki.

Gimbiya mai gado da mutananta, yau wani baƙin ciki ne a tare da zuciyarta, ganin yadda ƙudurin Waziri ya ke neman cika, ta sani daga inda Ayda ta haihu kenan yaron ne zai zama magajin gidan.

A yanzu ba ta Yarima suke ba, sun san babu makawa ya zama Sarki, sai dai suna ta yadda zasu hana shi samun magaji ne.

***

Ayda ce gaban bokanyar mahaifinta, kanta a sunkuye ta ke magana "Ina so na zama ni ce mai gudanar da komai, ni ce zan zauna a matsayin abin faharin shi, ina so ya zama yaron da zan haifa shi ne magajin masarautar nan."

Wasu layu Bokanyar ta aje tare da faɗin "Ɗaya a ƙarƙashin katifar shi, ɗaya a rufe a ƙofar farko ta shiga ɓangaren shi, ɗayar kuma za ki ajiye, yaron da zaki haifa za a jiƙa a ba shi ruwan."

***

Jakadiyya ta kalli Gimbiya mai gado ta ce "Yanzu zamu jira mu ga yadda zai iya mulkar gidan nan, ina mai tabbatar maki ba zai iya ba."

Gimbiya mai gado ta ce "Naji wannan sai ɗayar maganar."

"Ina mai tabbatar maki da mulki zai dawo hannun Yarima Saifu."

***

Masarautar ta yamutse da murna, musamman ɗakin taron wanda komai ya burge kowa ana gudanar da taron da ba a taɓa yin kalar shi ba duk faɗin nahiyar.

Lokacin da aka buƙaci Yarima zuwa gaban ƙaura don naɗin sai lokacin Yarima ya ƙara tabbatarwa.

Rawanin kan shi aka cire tare da fara naɗa ma shi wani a kai shi ma ɗin farine sai dai wannan lokacin an yi naɗin rawanin ya gewaye fuskarsa har ya ɗan sauka a ƙirjin shi.

Miƙewar da aka ba shi damar yi hakan yasa Fadawa gewaye shi tare da kirari "Gyara kimtsi, Lafiya jan zaki! Toron Giwa kake!!Lafiya  ɗan sarki jikan sarki!!!"

A hankali Sultan Amin ya yi gefe yana tsayawa a inda za a ba shi sandar girma.

***

Bilkisu ta ja hannun Aymana zuwa ɗaki tare da faɗin "Ai na sanar da ke, Sultan Amin ba zai taɓa barin a fara ɗaura aure kafin naɗin ba."

Aymana ta ya mutsa baki "Wannan bai shafe ni ba."

Farida da ke saka wasu kaya cikin jakunkuna ta yi gyaran murya, sam bata san hali irin na uwar ɗakinta ba.

Aymana ta juyo ta kalleta "Kina da magana ne?"

"Allah ya taimakeki" kawai ta ce tana ɗaukar jakar kayan ta fice.

***

Ayda ta fesar da ruwan da ta kwankwaɗa a bakinta tare da faɗin "Ba zai yiwu ba!"

Zubewa Hassatu ta yi "Allah ya huci zuciyarki, haka ya aiwatar, yanzu ne za a yi ɗaurin auren."

Kofin hannunta ta yi wurgi da shi, Gwaggo da ta jiyo ƙara ta shigo "Ke Ayda ina so ki sani ba duk abin da kike so za ki samu ba, amma da jajircewarki komi zai zama na ki."

Ayda ta yi fuuu ta bar ɗakin tana barin ɓangaren.

***

Gimbiya Ummi sam bata kowa take ba, ita dai burinta bai wuce ganin ta sallami kowa ba taro ya tashi lafiya.

Sai kuyangi da take aike zuwa sabon sashen Sultan Ameen wanda acan ne za a nufa da shi idan ya shigo.

Wata Kuyanga ta aika kiran Aymana, babu jimawa Aymana ta shigo tana mai bata girma, Gimbiya Ummi ta durƙusa ta kamo kunnen Aymana ta matse.

Aymana ta riƙe tare da faɗin "Daga ji ran Mahaifiyarmu ya ɓaci ina mai tuba a gareki."

"Me kike jira har yanzu baki nufi sabon ɓangaren ku ba?"

"Allah ya baki nasara, har wasu daga kaya sun yi gaba, ina jiran zuwan Sultan ne."

"Sultan acan zai sauka ku yi gaggawar tafiya."

Aymana ta miƙe ta ɗan sunkuya, tare da faɗin "Na gode!" Ta fice.

Babban ɓangare ne da aka tsara sak ginin sarauta, ɓangaren Ayda yana kallon na Aymana.
   Sai ɓangaren Sultan da ke ɗan nesa kaɗan da nasu.

   A cikin ɓangaren Aymana babban falo ne da ya ke gewaye da kujeru da kayan adon sarauta, an rufe shi da makeken kafet a tsakiya.

Wasu ƙofofi ne da ke sada ka da ɗakunan ɓangaren, akwai wajen cin abinci a falon labulayen kansu abin kallo ne.

Hotunan Sarki Amin jefe a babban bangon falon.

Aymana ta ɗan taɓe baki tana zama kan kujera, Mama dake cikin ƴan rakiya ta ce, "Ki tashi ki canza kaya don zuwa ɓangaren Sultan."

Aymana ta kalleta "Ni da ina ganin babu buƙatar hakan, abar masu son tarar shi su tare shi."

"Kul! Inda Mai martaba ya so su tare shi, ba zai watsa masu kasa a ido ba wajan buƙatar su."

Aymana ta miƙe zuwa ɗakin, ta ɗan watsa ruwa tare da saka wasu kayan, wannan lokacin wani yadi ne mai laushi-launin jinin kare, yana da kwalliyar launin ƙasa-ƙasa mai sheƙi.

Ta fito falon tana zama Farida ta fito da alkyabba launin ƙasa-ƙasa da zanen launin jinin kare.

Aymana ta miƙe Farida ta taimaka mata wajen sakawa, sosai asalin kyanta ya fito, ta saka takalma, Bilkisu ta fito tana fesheta da turare, kafin suka fice zuwa ɓangaren Sultan Amin.

A bakin babbar ƙofar hatimin TAKOBIN masarautar su ne zane, Aymana ta ja ta tsaya tana kallon zanen, lallai wanda yayi zanen ya iya zane domin babu wani banbanci a ido sai dai don wannan yana zane.

Bilkisu ta kalleta ta kalli zanen da take kallo a zuciyarta ta ce wannan shi ne abin da ya hanaki maida hankali don fuskantar kanki.

***

Ana gama ɗaura Aure Sultan bai jira sallamar baƙi ba, wani kalar yanayi ne yake ji, tun lokacin da aka miƙa mashi sandar sarauta, ciki kawai ya shiga.

Ɓangare-ɓangare na gidan sai da aka raka Yarima Amin ya gaisa da kowa, kafin aka yi ɓangarensa da shi.

A harabar aka rinƙa gaishe da shi, hannu kawai ya iya ɗaga musu, sai murmushi da ya ke yi wanda ba a ganewa kasancewar rawani daya rufe kumatunshi.

A bakin ƙofa fadawa da 'yan rakiyar suka tsaya, Yana shiga wani bafade ya ja ƙofa ya rufe.

Aymana tayi saurin miƙewa tana kallon shi, rawanin ta ke kallo, yau ya fito da kyawun da kamala kalar ta sarakuna,  wani yanayi ne ya shigeta, lokaci guda tsikar jikinta ta tashi, ba ta san lokacin da murna ta bayyana a ɓangarenta ba.

Cikin sauri ta nufe shi,Yarima yasa hannu ya ja rawanin shi ƙasa kaɗan, hakan ya bata damar ganin murmushin da ke tare da fuskarshi.

Sauri ya ɗan yi wajan dafa kafaɗarta tare da ƙara shige mata "Ashe lokacin nan zai zo, ashe zanga wannan rana?"

Aymana ta faɗa jikinshi, Yarima ya ƙara rungumeta jikin shi, ya hannuwanshi ya harɗe a bayanta yana sauke numfashi, ya ɗan duƙar da kanshi zuwa saitin wuyanta Aymana ta fara jin hucin numfashin sa, yau so yake ya mata sumba ko da a karon farko ne.

Bakinshi ya aza akan wuyanta ya sumbaceta cikin sauri ta ɗago tana kallon shi, Sultan Amin ya yi sauri wajan ɗaga kanshi daga gefen wuyanta.

Jikin Aymana ya mutu sosai, hakan yasa ta ɗan ja baya kaɗan, Yarima ya janye jikinshi yana cire rawanin.

Ya haɗa da Alkyabba ya aje akan kujera Ayamana ta kalleshi "Fatan taro ya tashi Lafiya."

Babbar rigarsa yake cirewa bai yi magana ba "Alhamdulillah zan ce, amma akwai sauran mutane har shigowata."

Hanyar wata ƙofa yayi Aymana ta kwashi kayan tana bin shi a baya, suka shiga ɗakin Yarima ya zauna, Aymana ta buɗe wani firij ta ɗauko ruwa tana ɓalle mashi marfin,Ya amsa tare da kaiwa baki, yasha sosai kafin ya fara ajiyar zuciya, Aymana ta gane babu abinda ya saka cikin shi duk wunin ranar, hakan yasa ta kalleshi.

"Zaka iya watsa ruwa." Ta faɗa tana yin hanyar fita.

Yarima ya bita da kallo, kafin ya miƙe yayi shirin wanka.

Aymana kuwa cikin gida ta nufa ta nemi masu haɗa abinci, a gabanta suka jera komai a falon kafin suka fice.

Ta nufi cikin ɗakin sai ta sameshi zaune da wasu kaya mara nauyi yana danna wayar shi ta zauna gefen kujerar da yake "Ranka ya daɗe abincinka ya kammala."

Ya ɗago, ba tare da yayi magana ba, ya miƙe yana nufa falon, Aymana ta bishi, akan kafet ya zauna tare da jan wani tuntun, dama can Yarima baya cin abinci a kan kujerun cin abinci.

Bata ɓata lokaci ba ta hau zuba mishi, ya fara cin abincin a hankali sai kuma ya ɗago ya kalle ta "Me Gimbiya take jira?"

"Ni na ci nawa."

Shiru yayi ya ajiye cokalin ya ɗauki abin motsa baki da akayi da fulawa, ya ci sosai kafin ya ɗora da lemu.

Guɗa da hayaniya suka fara jiyowa daga waje, saurare Aymana ta fara yi, lokaci kaɗan ta fahimci Ayda ce aka kawo, saboda kalaman dake fitowa daga ƴan rakiyar.

Ji tayi gabanta ya buga da ƙarfi, sunzo wucewa ta gaban  sashen Yarima ne ta ƙara jin maganganun su "Ke ce ta biyu kinfi ta farko, kainuwa kike dashen lillahi! Amarya abin son Sultan."

Sultan Amin ya kalli Aymana data rufe idanuwanta, yana son fahimtar wani abu.

Ita kuwa Aymana wata ƙuna zuciyarta take mata, tare da tunane-tunane don tasan dole ne dama mutanen gidan su zama ƴan bayan Ayda.

Wata zuciyar ta ce ina ruwan ki? Miye naki a ciki, koma mi zasu ce ke dai ba shi ne burin ki ba. Anan ne fa ta samu kwarin guiwa ta buɗe ido.

Sultan ya kauda idon shi daga kallon ta ya miƙe zuwa kan kujera, Aymana ta ce "Ko da wani abun buƙata ne?"

Tana maganar tana miƙewa "Ina za ki je?"

"Yana da kyau na ba Kainuwa dashen lillahi waje don kula da mijinta!"

Gyara zama yayi sam baya son su fara haka da ita, sai dai ya fahimci kishi a tare da ita, amma kuma ya sha alwashin ba zai taɓa barin ɗaya daga cikin matan shi su fahimci wacce ya fi so a ciki ba.

"Lokacin fitar ki baiyi ba, Sultan yana son hutawa."

"Ka san ina da baƙi, mutanen Bilyam ma ban gana da suba."

"Na yi magana da Baba ya sanar dani zai yi wani zuwan saboda ke, amma ya tafi yanzu."

Aymana ta kalle shi "Haka fa yayi mani lokacin taron murabus,  bai neme ni ba dana tambaya aka sanar dani yace sai lokacin Naɗi"

Shiru yayi, Aymana  dama akwai haushi tare da ita gashi kuma taso ganawa da mahaifin nata amma bata samu hakan ba. 

"Me ya sa baka faɗa mashi ƴar sa tana son magana da shi ba? Kenan Mai martaba ya daina so na, dama na san daga ya bayar da ni zai fita zance na"

"Aymana!"

Shiru tayi bata amsa mashi ba, jin bai ce komai ba ta ci gaba "Yanzu ga shi bai damu da ko ina da damuwa ko wata matsala ba, bai san wane hali na ke b..."

Yarima ya miƙe ya nufeta "Zan shiga ciki, bana son hayani, ina son hutawa."

Banza tayi da shi, ya tsaya kanta "Kar na kuma jin wannan kalaman a Turakata!"

Aymana ta ɗago "Me acikin turakar taka? Don ka yi Aure zaka faɗi haka a gare ni?"

Sam ba nufin Sultan kenan ba, ta ja baya tana mashi wani kallo "Zan bar maka Turakar ka" ta faɗa tana yin hanyar waje.

Binta yayi da kallo tare da shigewa ciki.

***

Tunda aka kai Ayda aka sanar da ƴan rakiyar Aymana tana wajan Mai martaba Sultan suke ta leƙen ɓangaren, har suka ga fitowarta.

Sun sha mamakin yadda Aymana zata je tayi zaune wajen Sultan tun shigowar shi, abin da basu sani ba shi ne ma ya hanata  fita, domin kuwa idan ya barta ba zata yi zaune haka ba.

Lokacin da Aymana ta fita kasancewar Yamma tayi sosai hakan yasa yawancin gidan kowa ya tafi sai makusanta ne kawai.

***

Kamar wasa zuwa dare babu kowa duk mutane sun tafi, sai Aymana da kuyanginta, Ayda ma haka sai Goggo da aka bar mata.

Sultan Amin kuwa tunda ya dawo Sallar i'sha ya shiga ɓangaren shi, yana son ganin Aymana amma yasan ba zata so ba, haka kuma ba zai aika kiranta ba don baya son ta fahimci wani abu ba.

Hakan yasa bayan ya samu abinda ya ci ya yi zaman shi falon ya na danna wayarshi tare da tura saƙon godiya musamman zuwa ga Abokanan shi.

Ayda ta fito daga ɓangaren ta tana takowa ta gaban ɓangaren Aymana, sashen Sultan zata nufa kamar yadda Goggo ta turata, duk da sunyi tsumayen aiken shi akan ta zo amma bai buƙaci ganinta ba.

Kuyanga Aisha ta durƙusa gaban Aymana tare da faɗin "Allah ya taimakeki, ko kin bada damar maye gurbin ki tun yanzu?"

Aymana ta ji shiru, kafin ta fahimci inda zancen Aysha ya nufa hakan yasa ta kalleta "Na yi sallama da Sultan ai!" Ita kanta bata san lokacin data ƙirƙiri ƙaryar hakan ba.

Aisha tayi shiru tare da miƙewa, tana fita Aymana ta miƙe tare da fita ɗage labulen  taga, anan taga fitowar Jakadiyya daga ɓangaren Sultan tana ganin lokacin da taba Ayda izinin shiga.

Komawa tayi ta shigewarta ɗaki ta fara shirin kwanciya.

Lokacin da Ayda ta shiga Yarima ya shigewarshi ɗaki hakan ya sa ta shiga ciki.

Baiyi magana ba bayan gaisuwarta daya amsa, Ayda ta ɗan yi shiru, Yarima ya zauna bakin gado, tare da sanar da ita zai kwanta ne saboda gajiyar dake tare dashi.

Ayda ta numfasa, Yarima ya kwanta tare da faɗin "zaki iya yin bacci idan kina da buƙatar hakan."

Ko rufe baki baiyi ba, Ayda ta cire mayafin data rufo jikinta, sai lokacin na  kula da kayan baccin dake jikinta.

Kan kujera ga ajiye mayafin ta haye gadon tare da komawa gefen shi.

***

Bayan Aymana tayi sallar Asuba, ta koma ta kwanta, shigowar Jakadiyya ukku don ganawa da ita amma ana sanar da ita tana bacci ne.

Can cikin bacci take jiyo guɗa tare da hayaniya a gidan sai kuyangi dake ta kai kawo suna kallon Jakadiya dake riƙe da zanin gado da wani ruwan sassaƙen icce a cikin kwarya.

Duk Aymana bata san abinda ke faruwa ba, tana dai kwance abinta, Farida ta dafe kai tana mamaki ita kanta ba ta yi tunanin Yarima yana son Ayda irin haka da za a sanar da ranar farkon su a gidan ba.

Ɗakin Aymana bakin kofar ta tsaya ta na bubbugawa da ƙarfi, Aymana ta murza idonta, ta ɗauki lokaci kafin ta tambayi waye, jin Farida ce hakan yasa tace ta shigo.

Farida tana shiga Aymana ta tashi zaune tana faɗin "Hayaniyar me nake ji a gidan nan?"

"Allah ya taimakeki, abinda nazo sanar dake kenan, dama suna da burin ganin ranar nan ta kusantar Sultan."

Aymana ta zabura tana fitar da ƙafafunta daga cikin bargo "Farida!"

"Allah ya huci zuciyar ki."

Aymana ta dafe ƙirji, wata irin ƙuna zuciyarta ta take mata "Ke nan sun sanar da haɗuwar Sultan da Ayda?"

"Yanzu Jakadiyya tabar nan da kayan, ta shiga cikin gida don shedawa kowa."

"Za ki iya tafiya!" Kawai ta iya cewa Farida.

*SHAFI NA ASHIRIN DA UKKU. 23*

Farida ta miƙe tana bin umarnin uwar ɗakinta, Gimbiya Aymana ta miƙe tsaye tana dafe ƙirjinta jin yadda yake harba mata, ta koma ta faɗa kan gado, a zuciyarta ta fara tunanin miye dalilinta na ciga tsanani irin kaga "Kishi" wani ɓangaren zuciyarta ya amsa mata.

Girgiza kai tayi alamar ƙaryata zuciya a fili kuwa ta ce "Babu dalilin hakan." cikin sauri ta dai daita nutsuwarta, ta hanyar sauke ajiyar zuciya.

Hanyar ban ɗaki ta yi don shiga wanka, bata ɗauki lokaci ba ta shirya ta na fito babban falonta, anan ta samu an ajiye mata kayan kari, sam bata buƙatar komai, fita take son yi, amma sam ba ta son ganin duk mutanen gidan don tasan kowa da abinda zai yi tunani akan ta da kuma Yarima.

Tana zaune dai babu wani tsayayyar shawara a tare da ita, har rana ta take sosai, dole ne ta je gaida Sultan don ita kanta tasan ƙa'ida ne hakan, ko don matsayin da yake da shi a yanzu.


Mayafi ta ɗauka ta yane kanta, ta yi sa a babu kowa a farfajiyar hakan ya bata damar kwankwasawa tare da jira, babu amsa hakan yasa ta jima kafin ta murɗa tare da tura ƙofa.

Babu kowa a falon sai ƙarar na'urar sanyaya ɗaki dake fita a hankali, wai gawa tayi tana yin hanyar ɗakin shi.

  Abinda bata sani ba, Sultan Amin yana gefen kujeru kishingiɗe saman kafet, binta yake da idanuwa ganin zata shige hakan ya sa yace "Aymana!"

Cikin sauri ta juyo ta kalli inda taji sautin, wani kallo ta ɗan bishi da shi, har ta isa wajan da yake sam ta kasa ko kyabtawa zuciyarta take raya mata wai Yarima ne har ya kusanci Ayda.

Zaune ya tashi shima ɗin ita yake kallo yana son tantance kallon da take ma shi.

"Barka da Safiya Sultan!" Ta ce tana zama gefen kafet ɗin.

"Baki duba lokaci ba kafin ki fito!"

Aymana tayi jim, Yarima ya ce "Ba yanzu bane lokacin gaisuwa zuwa ga Sultan." 

Aymana ta gane yana nufin bata zo gaishe shi ba har wannan lokacin, shi kuwa Yarima Allah ya sani tun Asuba ya ƙagara ya ganta, in da yana da damar zuwa dubata da zai yi hakan ne.

"Allah ya huci zuciyar..."

Bata ida ba ya katseta "Kin yi bacci kuwa?"

Don shi sam hakan ya ƙauracewa idanuwan shi, musamman kusantar Ayda da ya farayi kafin Aymana, hakan ya ɗan taɓa zuciyar shi. Aymana ta ce "Bacci sosai! Bacci mai nauyi kuwa Sultan."

Ƙurr ya ƙura mata ido ya miƙe, ya yi kan kujera ya zauna hakan ya bata damar tashi ta bi shi.

"Ni nake da lokacin bacci saɓanin wasu! Ta yaya kura da shan bugu gardi da anshe kuɗi!"

Shiru yayi ya fahimci maganarta amma ba ya ra'ayin maganar "Kun gana da Gimbiya Ummi?"

Hankalinta ta maida kanshi, don tana ba iyaye muhimmanci "Tun jiya rabo na da ita, lokacin data ja kunne, amma yanzu daga nan can zan nufa."

"A miƙa gaisuwata kafin in fito."

Aymana ta miƙe ta ɗan sunkuya "Na barka lafiya."

***

Tun da jakadiyya ta baiyana tsakanin Ayda da Yarima Hakan ya raunana zuciyar Ummi, anan ta fara tunanin yadda har Yarima ya ɓoye tsakanin shi da Aymana amma gashi ya baiyana akan Ayda.

Mama kuwa a nata ɓangaren tana da alamomin tambaya akan Aymana, amma kuma ta yi alƙawarin ba zata tambayeta ba, don kar taga kamar ta saka ido akan su, bata so hakan ya taɓa mu'amalarta da ita.

A sashen Waziri da gidan Baba Maga yaƙi murna tsalle Innar Ayda harda rawa.

Shi kuwa Waziri ya san ya cika gurinshi tunda har zai ƙara samun wani girma daga wajen Sarki Amin.

***
Bayan dawowar Aymana daga wajan Gimbiya Ummi, suna tare da kuyanginta guda  huɗu, suna zuwa wucewa gaban ɗakin Sultan Ayda tana  fito.

Aymana ta kauda kanta kamar bata ganta ba, Ayda ta ja ta tsaya tana ƙare mata kallo, daidai Aymana ta wuce kaɗan Ayda ta ce "Dole gyaɗa tayi mai idan ta ƙi ta sha murza! Mai lafiya shi yake shan jar miya! Mai waje ne ya zo dole mai tabarma ya naɗe!"

"Ƙarya ki ke!" Aymana ta faɗa, tare da fuskantar Ayda

"Kin san komai lokacine, duniya kuwa juyin wainace, ko nace rawar ƴan mata, na gaba ya gewaya ya koma baya." Ayda ta ƙara faɗa.

Murmushi Aymana ta saki, ta kalli Ayda sama da ƙasa kallo na wulaƙanci "Waya faɗa maki ƴar sarki na fargaba ko shakkun juyin da zata gani? Ni banga sauyi ba, duk da samunki hakan bai hana shi karkata tunanin akan Gimbiyar shi ba."

Shiru Ayda tayi tana tunanin Sultan da kuma yanayin da suka kasance, zuciyarta ta fara yarda da maganar Aymana.

"Hmmm! Maganar ki a baki take, ko kin ga alamar Sultan bai samu gamsuwa ba, ina canjin da kikace kin dawo da hana baiyanar fashewar kwai a..."

Aymana ta fusata tare da faɗin "Ɗan Dakata!" 

"Ko anan baki ga banbanci ba, Alhamdulillah kin bawa kanki amsa, Sultan ya ɓoye komai akan sashen zuciyar shi ne don hakan ya zama sirri a gidajen mu". Ta faɗa tana wucewarta.

Ko da ta isa sashenta, anan ta fara saƙa da warwarar yadda zaman su zai kasance, akwai matsala indai har za su rinƙa haɗuwa Ayda tana taƙalarta rigima.

A irin rayuwar da tayi gidansu ita bamai magana bace akan komai, sai dai wanda ya mata ta hukunta shi daidai da laifin da ya aikata.

***

Aymana ta fara kai kawo, tabbas tana buƙatar Liyafar data shirya don murnar tarewar  Yarima Amin da  Gimbiya Ayda ya kasance an ƙayartar da Walimar tana so ta zama abin nunawa da ban mamaki ga mutanen gidan.

Sanarwar da mutanen gidan suka samu na Shirya Walimar karrama Ayda,  hakan ya kawo gutsuri tsoma da ƴan gulamace-gulmace daga cikin gida, musamman ɓangaren Waziri, ɗakin Gimbiya Mai gado, ɓangaren Gimbiya Ummi da kuma sauran mutanen gidan da suka haɗa da bayi, kuyangi da barorin gidan.

Aymana kuwa duk yadda sauran makusantan ta na gidan suka so hana ta shirya wannan taron ba ta saurare su ba. Babban burinta shi ne ta ƙuntatawa Sultan, ta nuna mashi babu damuwarta da kishi akan shi.

Ta sani Sultan zai gabatar da kyaututtuka na musamman ga Ayda, haka sauran mutanen gidan za su bawa Ayda kyautar samun matsayi na musamman.

Ta saka lokacin Liyafar ƙarfe takwas  na dare, ta sa a sanar da kowa ne zai halarci taron.

Lokacin da Sultan Amin ya ji zancen ya yi nazari sosai akan lamarin, murmushi kawai ya yi wa Jakadiyya lokacin da take sanar da shi.

Ayda kuwa a yanzu ta san tana da matsayin da babu ya ita a gidan, tunda har ta samu matsayin da za a shirya taro dominta, gaya ta zama tamkar tauraruwa ga mutanen gidan ganin zancenta ya karaɗe ɓangarorin masarautar.

***

Ƙarfe takwas na dare Babban ɗakin taron masarautar an ƙayatar da komai kamar yadda Gimbiya ta bada umarni, a wannan  lokacin da yawan mutanen gidan suna can, don kashe kwarkwatar ido da kuma son fahimtar dalilin shirya taron.

Fadawa da maroƙane bayan Sarkin Amin Yana tafiyarshi cikin taƙama da Izza alkebbar jikinshi aikin ta yanayin saƙi ne, takalmin ƙafarshi kanta abin kallo ne, Sultan Amin ya kasance mai soyuwa ga farin rawani, hannun shi dumtse da amawali fari da wata sanda a hannunshi yana ɗan azata ƙasa cikin tafiyar Sarauta.

Ya isa ɗakin taron cikin mamakinshi na ganin harda manyan masarautar a wajan, Gaishe da shi ake tayi tare da kirari har ya isa ga karagarshi ya zauna.

Sai lokacin Ayda ta shigo da kuyangi bayanta, shigar Alkebba ta yi launin ja, kowa na wajan ta burge shi saboda kyawun da tayi.

A bisa Mamakin kowa har lokacin Aymana ba ta ƙaraso wajen ba, an ƙara ɗaukar lokaci aka fara ƙananun maganganu a ƙasa-ƙasa.

Kuyangin Aymana ne suka fara shigowa cikin shigar wani kayan ja da launin bulu mai turuwa sosai.

Haka suka fara raba kansu tare da buɗe hanya alamar akwai mai tahowa bayansu.

Kacau! Kacam! Kacau! Kwas! Kwas ! Kwas! Wannan shi ne ƙarar sautin sarƙar ƙafa da kuma sautin takalmin Gimbiya Aymana. 

Awarwaro da sarƙoƙin zinarin da ta yi ado dasu sautin su yana fita da salo mai ɗaukar hankali. 

Sanye take da Alƙebba launin  bulu mai haske, da aikin bulu mai turuwa, jikin Alkebbar da wasu duwarwatsu da ke fitar da nasu salon sutin, ga ƙyelli da suke fitarwa. Fuskarta ɗauke da kwalliya da kuma yalwataccen Annuri.

Hankalin kowa ya koma inda ya ke jiyo sautin, Sultan Amin kansa sai da yayi saurin ɗagowa tare da maida hankalin shi kanta, sosai Aymana ta burge kowa musamman yadda ta shigo da tsantsar izza cike da mulki a tare da ita.

Mazauni aka nuna mata da ke fuskantar kujerar da Ayda take zaune, wani tashin hankali ya ziyarci Ayda ganin shigar Alfarma da Ayamana ta yi.

Wasu daga cikin mutane su ka fara ƙus-ƙus akan yadda Aymana tafi wacce aka haɗa taron don ita yin shigar alfarma.

Kuyangin Aymana suka matsa ganin uwar ɗakinsu ta samu muhalli, Anan aka yi jawabin gabatarwa da kuma faɗar musabbabin taron.

Tun shigowar Aymana  gaba ɗaya hankalin Sarki Amin ya koma kan ta, ya san lallai Aymana ta fito ne daga Babbar masarauta, sanin halinta ne ya sa bai yi mamakin Izzar da take gudanarwa ba a wajen.

An fara gabatar da kyaututtuka zuwa ga Ayda akan matsayi data samu na tarawa da Sarki Amin ya yi da ita, Saƙon Gimbiya Ummi ya iso, da sauran iyayen masarautar, Mai martaba ya aiko da tashi kyautar ta musamman.

Kowa na wajen ya gama Ajiye kyaututtukan shi, abin ya zama abin murna ga kowa, Aka tattara kayan aka kai su gefe kafin aka fara maganar Sarki Amin zai bada tashi kyautar ga Ayda.

Anan wani bafade ya  gabatar da wasu silallar zinari akan kyautar Sultan Amin zuwa ga matar shi Gimbiya Ayda, kyautar da ta zama tukuicinta na kasancewar su a karon farko.

Gimbiya Aymana ta saki wani ƙayataccena murmushi tare da ɗan kaɗa ƙafarta cikin Izza.

Kallonta kawai ya ke ya na jin ƙaunarta na ƙara shigar zuciyar shi.

Mutanen wajan sun yarjewa zuciyarsu lallai Ayda ta yi goshi.

Aymana ta miƙe daidai lokacin da Kuyanga Farida da Aysha  suke shigowa da wasu jibgin kaya suka zube agabanta.

Hakan ya dawo da hankalin al'umma zuwa gare su.

Farida ta fara miƙo Wani Yadin karan-miski na Alkebba, Aymana ta Amsa ta ba Aysha.

"Wannan kyautar Yadin karan-miski ne daga Gimbiya Aymana zuwa ga Gimbiya Ayda" Aysha ta faɗi tana ajiyewa tsakiyar wajen.

Ta cigaba "Sai kuma wanann asalin Munduwar Sinari ne, zuwa ga Gimbiya"

Farida ta ci-gaba da fiddo Alkebba daga cikin jakunkunan su, ta warware su,tana miƙawa, tsadaddun kayan kwalliyar sarauta ne da suka firgita mutanan wajan, Alkebba ce kusan guda goma sha biyar ko wacce da mahaɗin kayanta da takalmin haɗunsu.

Cikin Mamaki mutanen gida su ke yadda sam babu alamar kishin komai a tare da Aymana.

Yarima Amin ya gyara zaman shi yana kallonta, tabbas ba ƙaramin daɗi yaji ba, ya tabbatar Aymana macen nunawace da kuma taƙama.

Ƙarar kwasar Silallar zinarin da Farida tayi ya kuma ɗaga hankalin kowa, aka ajiye akan wata kyautar, ba ƙaramar dukiya aka ajiye ba.

Aisha ta ce "Haka kuma akwai  kyautar Kuyangi guda biyu daga Gimbiya Aymana, wanda zasu riƙa yiwa Gimbiya Ayda hidima."

Aymana tana gama gabatar da kayan ta koma ta zauna, kowa na wajen ya san muhimmancin kayan da aka damƙawa Ayda.

Abinci aka fara kawowa da abubuwan motsa baki, Anan aka sanar da fitar Mai martaba, Sultan ya miƙe don barin wajen. Saboda taron ya kammala, iya abinci ne kawai ya rage.

Yana fita Aymana ta miƙe ta fara tafiyarta cikin taƙama itama ta fice, bayinta suka maye bayanta.

Wannan  Al'amari da mutanen gidan su ka gani ya sa Aymana ta ƙara martaba a idanun jama'ar gidan, darajarta ta ƙara ɗaukaka.

Manyan Bayi da kuyangin da suka manyanta a masarautar,  har cewa suke wannan wace irin mace ce da ta san darajar kanta, ta yi ƙoƙarin ɓoye kanta, ta ɓoye asalin fuskarta da kishi, ta fitar da fuskarta da farin ciki a wajen.

Haka sauran mahukuntan masarautar da masu riƙe da wasu masarautun gidan.

Mai martaba kuwa takanas ya aika kiran Sultan Amin don tattaunawa akan Aymana da yadda ya ji daɗin abinda ta yi, ya ƙara bawa Sultan Amin goyon baya da kuma nuna mashi yadda Aymana ta  zama ginshiƙin shi.

Lokacin da ya je wajen Gimbiya Ummi ita kam ba ta ɓoye mashi farin cikin ba "Lallai na yarda da maganar Mai martaba da ya ce, yarinyar zata zamar maka bango a mulkinka"

Murmushi kawai Amin yayi, yanzu ya kauda abinda ya saka a zuciyar shi na cewar kishi ne yayi tasirin akan Aymana.

Ko da ya shiga ɓangarensa Jakadiyya ya tura don kiranta, Zuciyarta tana harba mata don ba ta san miye zai ce akan abinda ta yi ba.

Tattara nutsuwarta ta yi, ba ta so ya fahimci kishin da ke tattare da ita da kuma zafin da ta ji na taron data haɗa. amma ta sani kishinne ya jagoranceta ta aikata hakan.

Ya na zaune ta shiga tare da zama "Allah ya hutar da gajiyar dake tare da Sarki Amin" ta faɗa tana sunkuyawa.

Idanuwanshi akan ta, ƙaunar ta tana tasiri a zuciyar shi, murmushi ya sakar mata da ya fitar da sauti har Aymana ta ɗago.

Sarki Amin ya ɗaya baki ahankali ya ce "Kin taimakeni! Kin fitar dani kunya abinda ki ka yi, Allah ya yi maki Albarka."

*SHAFI NA ASHIRIN DA HUƊU. 24*

Sunkuyar da kanta ta yi jin yadda yau Sarki Amin ya saka mata Albaraka, sai dai bata ƙarasa tunanin ba ya cigaba "Tabbas kinyi matuƙar ƙoƙari, kin kuma cancanci yabo Aymana!" Ya yi maganar da nuna maryabawa gareta.

Aymana ta ɗago ta kalle shi a karo da biyu, ta fara tunanin yadda ta samu yabo daga gare shi, wani ɓangare na zuciyarta ya tuna mata yadda Kaka ta jajirce tare da nusar da ita muhimmancin yin wannan Walimar.

Awanni kaɗan bayan Aymana ta shiga hali akan Ayda ta kasance ta farko da Sultan ya tara da ita, lokacin data rasa mafita da kuma hanyar do sa, Kaka ta kira ta na kuka tare da sanar da ita halin da take ciki.

Kasancewar Kaka tsohuwar data fito daga Babbar masarauta hakan yasa ta ba Aymana shawara da kuma umarnin shirya wannan taro zuwa ga Sultan Amin.

Don tasan yin Walimar zai samarwa jikanyarta martaba a idon Sultan da mahaifinshi.

Yarima ya katse mata tunani da faɗin "Ina mai godiya gareki a karo na biyu!".

A zuciyarta tace Kaka ce ta cancanci ka yiwa godiya, sai dai a fili ta ɗan jajirce wajan faɗin "Girman ka ne, Allah ya taimakeka."

Bayan ta bar wajan Yarima tana komawa ta samu kiran Kaka ta sheda mata yadda akayi taron da kuma yadda Sultan ya nuna jin daɗin shi.

***

Haka aka ɗauki ƴan kwanaki, har girki ya dawo hannun Aymana, babu abinda bata yiwa Yarima Amin ba kamar yadda take mashi, sai dai yana gama cin abinci ta kalle shi "Zan je in kwanta."

Ta faɗi tana miƙewa, tayi sashen ɗakunan shi, hakan ya sa ya kwantar da hankalin shi, don yayi niyar idan har ta ce ɓangaren ta zata tafi tofa za suyi rigima.

Abinda bai sani ba, ita kanta Aymana tana yiwa kanta yaƙi ne kar mutannen gidan su fuskanci wani abu.

Ko da ya tashi ya shiga ciki yayi mamakin ganin bata ɗakin shi,ya shiga yayi wanka ya fito ya saka kayan bacci.

Ɗayan ɗakin dake kallon nashi ya shiga, kwance ya sameta har tayi bacci, ya jima yana ƙare mata kallo, tabbas yasan Aymana itace a cikin zuciyar shi, yana jin ƙaunarta sosai, musamman data kasance mashi wani bango daya jingina har ya kai shi ga matsayin da yake a yanzu.

Haka ya gama ƙare mata kallo har ya gaji ya fice, tun daga wannan ranar ɗakin ya zama ɗakin Aymana domin kuwa duk ranakun girkinta anan take rayuwar ta.

***

Komai ya daidaita gare shi ta ɓangaren gudanar da mulkinshi, da kuma samun haɗuwar kan al'ummar dake ƙarƙashin shi hakan yasa bashi da wata damuwa.

Damuwar shi ta ɓangaren Waziri da Yarima Saifu ne, suna ƙoƙari wajen son ganin sun shige mashi, da kuma kawo wasu tsare-tsare na su a masarautar, hakan ya sa ya gane su ya fara nuna ƙarfin mulkin shi akansu da duk wanda yake ganin zai kawo mashi cikas.

Ya zama na ya daina sakasu a cikin mashawartan shi, duk wani abinda ya shige mashi duhu ya kan je wajan Mai martaba ya sanar dashi, shi kuma ya ɗora shi akan hanya.

***

Yau Aymana daga cikin gida ta dawo da saurinta ta nufo sashen su, tana son ganawa da Sultan ne game da zancen da taji yana yawo akan zai naɗa Sarkin sarakunan Nahiyar, wato ɗaya daga cikin masarautun nahiyar zai bawa sarautar.

Ta san tabbas idan aka yi hakan kenan Masarautar Bilyam da mahaifinta yake mulka za ta ƙara ƙanƙanta, bayan kuma ada itace babbar masarauta.

Idan har Sultan Amin ya yi wannan naɗin to masarautar zata zama itace ta biyu a duk nahiyar, wani ɓangare tana mai gudun naɗin ya kawowa shi kanshi Sultan ɗin nakasu ya zama waccen masarautar ce zata ringa jagorantar masarautun nahiyar ba shi ba.

Karo su ka yi da Jakadiyya ta yi saurin nufarta "Yauwa na ce ko Sultan yana ciki?"

Jakadiyya ta rusuna "Allah ya baki nasara yana ciki"

"Ko zaki sanar masa ina son ganawa da shi cikin gaggawa." 

Ta yi maganar tana kallonta "To ranki shi daɗe."

Kai kawo ta farayi babu jimawa Jakadiyya ta fito "Allah ya baki nasara, ai sai dai idan ba ke ba! Sultan ya yi maraba da saƙon ki."

Aymana ta yi mata ɗan murmushi ta buɗe ƙofar tare da sallama.

Yana zaune da wasu kayan sarauta gabanshi, ya saka farin tabarau a idon shi, ya ɗago ya kalleta Aymana ta zauna ɗan nesa da shi.

Sarki Amin ya ga ne kamar tana da damuwa, hakan yasa  ya yi shiru don bata damar fara magana "Barka da hutawa."

Bin ta yayi da idanuwanshi, ba tare da ya amsa ba Aymana ta ci gaba "Allah ya taimake ka, akan maganar naɗin dana tsinkaya za ka yi..."

"Me a cikin naɗin?" Ya katseta ta hanyar tambaya.

"Allah ya baka nasara, ina ganin kar kayi saurin saka hannu a takardai, ya kamata kayi nunani kafin..."

"Aymana! Na riga na amsa takarda, an kawo lokacin da na sanar dasu, sa hannuna ya rage, idan nayi magana bana sauyaw..."

"To Amma ai..."

Miƙewa ya yi yana barin wajan, ba tare da ya ƙara saurararta ba, yana sane yayi mata hakan, don taji halin ko in kula da take mashi idan akwai daɗi.

Haka Aymana ta bar ɓangaren jiki a mace, ammafa ta saka a ranta zata koma mashi.

Hakan ya faru kuwa, da yamma tayi shiri ta koma, sai dai ya fita, hakan ya sa ta nufi ɗakin data mayar nata a ɓangaren.

Sai da taji shigowar shi bayan fadawa sun bar falon  ta fito, karo su ka yi a hanya, ta fito shi kuma yana nufa nashi ɗakin.

Chak ya tsaya yana kallon ta, sam ita bata kwalliya kamar kishiyarta amma ko yaushe kyawunta yasha banban.

"Gimbiya!"

Ya kirata tare da riƙo yatsun hannunta da take wasa dasu, ɗagowa tayi ba ta yi maganaba.

Bai sake mata hannu ba, haka ya yi hanyar ɗakin shi, babu musu ta bi shi, sai da suka shiga ya saki hannun tare da fara warware rawanin shi.

Cikin sanyin jiki Aymana ta nufeshi tare da ɗaga hannunta ta kama rawanin tana taimakon shi wajen warware rawanin.

Yana kafin ta saka hannunta kan Alkebbar jikin shi tana cirewa Yarima ya fahimci rawar jikinta lallai akwai zance a tare da ita, ajiyewa tayi gefe, yana ƙoƙarin cire Babbar rigar ta kama mishi.

"Sannu!" Ya ce mata, Aymana ta sunkuyar da kanta "Uhmm"  kawai ya iya faɗa, ta zaune kan kujera, akwai tsananin shakku a tare da ita, ta san Sarki kaifi ɗaya ne ba lallai ya saurareta ba, ko tayi nasarar canza ra'ayin shi.

"Hmmm" ta kuma maimaitawa cikin salo ya Sarki Amin ya kuma kallonta, yanzu ya ƙara tabbatarwa da magana bakinta.


Ta ɗan ɗago don ganin ko da wani abun da yake yi, ta kalleshi lokacin da yake zama kayan cikin ɗinkin matasan zamani ne, wuyan ya ɗan kamashi ga wasu maɓallai da aka jera.

"Ko da buƙatar Ruwa?" Ta tambaya ganin ita yake kallo.

"A'a bana buƙatar komai" ya faɗa ya na ɗan sakin fuskar shi, tare da ɗaurewa cikin wani salon izza, Aymana ta ɗan ƙara shan jinin jikinta. A wannan zama dai sam ta kasa ƙara tunkarar Sarki da maganar dake zuciyarta na son dakatar da shi akan naɗin.


Washe gari Aymana ta zo gaidashi, ya na kishin giɗe ya tashi zaune, a yanzu ya ɗan damu da yanayin da take ciki na damuwar dake baiyane a fuskarta hakan yasa ya ce "Ko da buƙatar wani abu?"

"Hmmm!" Ta ce ƙasa-ƙasa tare da matsawa kusa da shi ta ɗan sunkuya.

"Allah ya baka nasara."

Shiru yayi yana kallonta "Gimbiya tana da abun cewa ga Sultan!"

Ɗan kwarin guiwa ya shigeta ganin yana son jin abinda ke tafe da ita.


"A gafarceni Sultan."

"Ina jinki!"

"Ko Sultan bai yi tunanin akwai wata manufa a cikin naɗinnan ba? Baka tunanin hakan zai janyo ƙasƙanci ga Masarautar ka ne?"

"Kenan ba zaki bar zancen nan ba?"

"Afuwarka nake nema! Ba zan lamunci ganin wani abu makamancin haka ba, su waye su ka kawo shawarar naɗin?"

Yarima yayi jim sai lokacin Waziri ya faɗo mashi, Aymana ta ci gaba "Allah ya ja zamanin Sarki Amin! Banyi tunanin mantuwa zata same ka ba."

"Mantuwa!" Ya faɗa.

Aymana ta ce "Ka manta masarautar da kake son ɗaukakawa itace masarautar da ɗan Sarkin masarautar ya fito yana son mulkin Masarautar ka?"

Miƙewa yayi cikin sauri, sosai maganganunta suka shige shi, tabbas ya san dole akwai abinda su ke shiryawa don ganin ya ƙasƙanta, a yanzu ya tabbatar akwai gaskiya sosai a tare da Aymana.

Itama miƙewa tayi tana mai sunkuyar da kanta.

 Yarima ya fara kai kawo, dole ba zai yadda ya karɓi batunta ba sai ya ɗugunzuma zuciyarta, hakan yasa yace  "Aymana idan mu na tuna wasu abubuwan ba zamu taɓa zama lafiya a nahiyoyinmu ba..."

Wani faɗuwar gaba taji, kenan wannan lokacin ma bai saurareta ba, kenan ba zai janye maganar naɗin ba.

Bin shi tayi baya tare da ruƙo hannun shi "Dama haka ne, duk wanda yake da tsarkakar zuciya ya kan maye Sharri da Alkhairi ne, amma ina so kasani, ba kowane mai aikata sarri bane yake aikata alkhairi a sauƙaƙe, zai yiwu nayi kuskuren fahimta ne, amma ka gafarce ni, nayi hakanne don gujewa ƙalubalen mulkinka."

Sultan Amin ya fara murza hannuwan Aymana acikin nashi, ya riƙe hannun ta  duka biyun suna fuskantar juna,  wani yanayin farin ciki yana shigar shi, samun mata da zata ɗora shi akan hanya, ya aminta da kalamanta sosai.

Ya ƙara taƙi daya wajan ƙaya kusantar ta, Aymana ta ɗaga kanta kaɗan don kallon fuskarshi kasancewar ya fita tsayi.

Hannu ya sa ya dafa kafaɗunta "Shi kenan komai ya wuce na janye maganar naɗin, na Kum..."

Bai idaba Aymana ta faɗa jikinshi tana mai jin daɗi, ji yayi ta kashe jikin shi sosai, Hannuwanta ta rataya bayan shi tana shafa bayan "Na gode! Na gode!"

Ɗagowa ya yi tare da ɗago fuskarta yana kallo, kanshi ya aza saman goshinta ya sumbaci goshin wanda har sai da sauti ya fita.

Aymana tayi sauri ta ja jikinta, tare da aza hannunta kan goshin, Sultan Amin ya juya yana barinta, kallo ta bishi dashi har lokacin bata sauke hannunta kan goshinta ba.

Washe gari Sultan Amin ya sheda dakatar da naɗin tare da fidda takardun daga fadar shi.

Yana zaune Ayda ta turo ƙofa "Allah ya taimakeka, Me dalilinka na fasa naɗin? bayan duk munyi shirin shagali a gidan nan"

"Dalilin ki ke son sani?" Ya tambayeta cikin izza.

Shiru tayi Sultan Amin ya miƙe tsaye yana yin hanyar ciki "Wannan bai shafi cikin gidaba, iya fada ta ne, ki tsaya a matsayin ki, wannan ba hurumin ki bane!."

Ba ƙaramin haushi ta ji ba, saboda an turo ta ne don lallashin shi da kuma son sanin dalilin shi.

***

Kwata-kwata Aymana ta fidda kanta da harkokinta daga Ayda, duk in da tasan zasu haɗu bata bi.

Ya zuwa yanzu mutanen gidan sun fara fahimtar fifita Aymana da Sarki Amin yake yi, amma ita sam Aymana bata fahimci hakan ba, Jakadiyya ce ta bayyanar da fificin ganin komai zai yi zai ce a kira Gimbiya Aymana.

***

Kuyanga Aysha ce take gefen Aymana da zancen ɓangaren Ayda a bakinta, amma bata san ta ina zata fara ba.

"Gimbiya!" ta kira Aymana.

Bata ansa ba saboda lemun data saka nakinta "Ni kuwa ina son sanar dake wani abu, amma ina tsoro."

Aymana ta gyara zama "Me abun Aisha?"

Farida ta shigo tana zubewa gabanta "Ranki ya daɗe an..."

"Shi ne nake kan sanar da ita." Inji Aisha daka kallon Farida.

"Wai ba zaku faɗa man ba" don ta so ta ji.

Kuyanga Aisha tace "Dama akan juna biyu da ke jikin Gimbiya Ayda ne."

Zabura tayi tana faɗin "Juna biyu!"

Ta faɗa tana kallon Farida,  Farida ta ce "Tabbas tana ɗauke da juna biyu na Kum..."

"Yaushe kika san haka Farida?"

"Na kwana biyu da ji amma ina tsor..."

Zaro ido tayi ta kalleta "Kin kwana biyu amma baki sanar dani ba?" Tayi maganar tana miƙewa tsaye "Lallai dole sai na hukunta ki Farida"

"Don Allah ki..."

"Wallahi sai kin ƙarɓi hukuncinki akan ɓoye wani abu da ki ka yi, ba tare da sanar dani ba, Me amfanin ki?"

Farida ta hau bata haƙuri Aymana ta nuna mata ƙofa "Maza kibar min ɗaki, kar ki yarda idona ya ƙara ganin fuskar ki, kar na ƙara ganinki anan, har sai lokacin dana buƙata, idan na kuma ganinki tabbas sai na azabtar dake."

Wani tashin hankali Farida ta shiga "Don Allah ki gafarceni, ki yafe ni, wallahi banyi hakan da wata manufa ba kum..."

Tsawa ta daka mata wadda ba Farida ba hatta Kuyanga Aisha saida ta miƙe tabar wajan.

Faɗawa tayi kan kujera tare da furta "Shi kenan komai ya faru, burin su zai cika, Sultan zai samu Magaji daga ɓangaren Ayda."

Ta sa hannu ta dafe kanta, tabbas ta tabbatar Sultan yana cikin farin ciki na samun Magaji, burin shi zai ƙara cika na samun tabbatar Mulki a gidan shi, ta san yaron da zai haifa zai zama shi ne magajin gidan.

A fili ta ce "Mi ye ribata?"

"Ba ki da wata riba tunda har kika kasa farfaɗo da martabar masarautar mahaifinki" abinda zuciyarta ta bata amsa kenan. 

Miƙewa tayi ta fito da ka ganta kasan bata cikin nutsuwarta, dole ne tayi zama da Yarima ta ƙara tabbatar mashi tana son lallai ya mayar musu da TAKOBIN su, babu amfanin ɓoyo da jan jiki da take yi, tunda dama tun asali yasan da ƙudirin hakan a tare da ita.

A ƙofar ɓangaren shi ta tsaya, tana niyar shiga Ayda ta fito Aymana ta bita da kallo sama da ƙasa ta tsayar da idanuwanta akan cikin Ayda.

Ayda ta ja baya "A'a wallahi duk abinda za ki yi banda Magajin Sultan, idanuwanki su kauce daga abin faharin Sultan, don idan ya fahimci wani abu daga ɓangaren ki na akasin farin ciki dole ki amshi fushi daga gare sh ..."


"Ban yi tunanin akwai wani Magaji daga wani wajen ba bayan daga Ɓangaren Gimbiyar data fito daga masarautar Bilyam"

Tana gama maganar ta raɓa ta shiga ciki tana huci, Yarima Amin yana kan karagar shi dake fuskantar ƙofa ya ƙura ido akan Aymana da ke shigowa.

Daga tsaye ta fara faɗin "Barka da hutawa"

"Me ke tafe dake a cikin yanayin da ban saba ganin ki ba?"
