*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA HUƊU. 34*


Ta riƙe hannunshi suna zama kan kujera, binta yayi da ido sosai kyawun jikinta ya ƙara fitowa hasken fatarta ya ƙara bayyana, jikinta ya ƙara laushi, ta ƙara mulmulewa abinta, hakan yasa ya tabbatar ƙasar ta amshe ta.

Ana zuwa ɗaukar su suka nufi Jedda tun a hanyar zuwa masauki Aymana take kallon yana yin garin ta gilashin mota.

Sultan yasa hannu yana riƙo hannunta, Aymana ta kalle shi tana riƙe nashi hannun itama, ko wanne da abunda yake saƙawa a ranshi.

Daga zuwansu wanka sukayi, tare da cin Abinci, Marece nayi Sultan yana shirin zama don hutawa Aymana ta hana shi don dole ya tashi suka fice.

*Dhaban marine park* suka nufa, wani babban wajan shaƙatawa wajen yana da kyau sosai, akwai ɓangaren wasanni da kuma wajan wasan yara, sosai Sultan ya maida hankali wajan kallon motocin wasan yara da kuma   yadda iska yake sanyaya wajen.

Aymana ta ja hannun shi zuwa wajan wata kujera, suka zauna, Sultan ya kalleta "Sam wajen nan yafi dacewa da suwa da yara, kasancewar komai na wajen don jin daɗin yara ne."

Murmushi Aymana tayi, ta maida kanta akan kafaɗar shi tare da saka wani abin motsa baki tana sha "Hakan yana nufin wata rana Sultan zai so da Yaran shi."

Hannu yasa yana shafa kafaɗarta, sai dai baiyi magana ba, haka sukayi hotuna sosai.

Washe gari a *Masjid Al Rahama* sukayi sallar la'asar, Masallaci ne da ke tsakiyar  wani kogi wanda wajan yana da sanyi da kuma daɗin zama.

Gewayawa suka yi wajan ruwan bayan sun fito daga masallacin. Aymana ta tsugunna tana saka hannuwanta a cikin ruwan, Sultan ya kalli yadda rigarta take shiga ruwan ya duƙa tare da saka hannu yana fitar mata "Kin ga zaki jiƙa kayan ki."

Ɗagowa tayi tana kallon shi taɗebo ruwan sosai tana watsa mashi tana dariya, Sultan ya kalli yadda ta jiƙa mashi kaya yace "Ni kika yiwa Haka ko."

Yana maganar yana ɗibar ruwan Aymana ta miƙe tana ɗan gudunta Sultan ya bita baya, Sai dai lokacin da ya kamata ruwan da ya ɗiba a hannun shi sun zube.

Dariya tayi mashi, Sultan ya harareta iska yana ƙaɗa mayafin dake jikinta har gashin kanta yana fitowa.

Hannu yasa yana gyara mata gashin tare da rungumeta "Yauwa yanzu ne dai-dai lokacin da zan rama."

Numfashi take saukewa sosai "Allah ka barni, ko gudun da ka saka ni ai ka ram..."

Kafin ta ida Sultan ya haɗe bakinsu, yana harɗe hannuwanshi bayanta, gaba ɗaya ya kashe musu jiki, ta saka hannunta tana riƙe shi jin kamar ƙafafun ta ba zasu iya ɗaukarta ba.

Sai da suka kwana biyu suna yawon shakatawa a Jedda. Yanzu ma shiri take yi sosai lokacin marece yayi lis, samun shi tayi falo zaune da wasu kaya marasa nauri, wandon iyakar shi guiwa, sumar kanshi tasha gyara sosai.

Aymana ta zauna tare da shafa sumar ta ce "Allah ya baka nasara, na ga baka shirya ba."

Maido hankalin shi yayi akanta, doguwar riga ce mara nauri, tana da maɗauri a tsakiya, sai wani siririn mayafi data ɗora, ta mashi kyau  sosai "Ki canza kaya dai, ba zanje dake a haka ba."

"Au ni na fita da kai jiya da wando iyakar shi ƙasan guiwa."

Dariya yayi ya kama hannunta suna miƙewa "Yau ina so mu huta a gida."

Hanyar ɗakin shi suka nufa Aymana ta cire mayafin ta ajiye, Sultan ya faɗa kan gado "Ki min tausa."

"Allah shi taimakeka ina jin bacci ne fa."

Dariya yayi ya tashi yaune "Don na hana fita shine ba za a min ba."

Yayi maganar yana miƙe mata hannu "zo mu kwanta." Faɗawa tayi jikin shi tayi lamo kowannansu babu wanda yake motsi.

Ranar haka suka wuni a gida daddare suka ci abinci, Sultan ya miƙe ya shiga ciki yayi wanka lokacin da Aymana ya gama saka kayan baccin shi.

Bata mishi magana ba, ta matso tana kama hannun shi tare da gyara mashi maɓallin da yake ƙoƙarin sakawa.

Tana gamawa ta juya ta shiga ɓanɗakin, ya jima yana jiranta, zuwa can ya ji motsin ruwa alamar yana wanka ne.

Tsawon lokaci ta fito ɗaure da towel iyakar shi rabin cinyarta, hannun ta rike da  ƙaramin towel tana tsane jikinta.

Zama tayi bakin mudubu ta na gyara kanta kafin ta fara shafa turaruka.

Sultan yana zaune kan gado ya jingina, ƙafafuwan shi a miƙe, bayanta yake kallo yadda take shafa man gashi tana rirriƙe towel ɗin don bata so ya faɗi, sai da ta gama amfani da duk abubuwan muƙata kafin ta miƙe ta buɗe wata jaka cikin jakunkunan da ta zuba sabin kayan ta.

Wata rigar bacci ta ɗauko launin ruwan madara mai santsi, ta fara sakawa tare da janye towel ɗin ta zauna bakin gadon ɗan nesa dashi.

Ƙoƙarin gyara rigar take kasancewar rigar bayanta babu komai sai wasu zaruruwa da ake ɗaurewa.

Kallon gadon bayanta yake  yana kallon yadda take ƙiƙiniyar gyarawa amma ta kasa.

Ta miƙe tsaye, rigar iyakarta cinya, ta nufe shi tana zama kusa da shi tare da juya bayanta.

Ya gane me take nufi sai dai baya iya ko motsawa saboda yadda kayan jikinta suka kashe mashi jiki.

Juyowa tayi tare da fadin "Kana kallo  na fa."

Murmushi yayi a hankali yakai hannuwanshi akan bayanta, atunanun Aymana saren zai ɗaura mata.

Ji tayi ya zura hannuwanshi ta gaba ya tallabo dukiyar fulaninta, ya na cika hannuwanshi tare da mummurzawa, Aymana ta ɗan gantsare tana tallabe hannuwan nashi.

Sultan ya fara diriricewa, Ya jawo ta sosai jikinshi yana juyo da ita, cikin wani irin salo.

Ɗaga baki tayi zatayi magana Sultan ya haɗe bakinsu, Aymana tana jiyo yadda yake tsotsar harshen ta kamar alewar da tayi mashi zaƙi, cikin sauri da rikicewar jiki Aymana ta riƙe Sultan tana fara mayar mashi da nata salon.

Hannuwanshi ya ɗora saman kafaɗarta yana yin ƙasa da rigarta zuwa cibinta, ya mayar da kanshi akan dukiyar fulanin guda yana murza ɗayan da hannunshi guda.

Aymana ta maƙalƙale jikinta cikin nashi tana wani numfashi, ta mayar da bakinta akan kunnashi tana hurawa kafin ta zura harshenta.

Sultan ya yi ƙara rikicewa yana sauke numfashi, ya mayar da hannuwanshi kan cikinta, yana mai janye kanshi ya fara tsotsar cikiyarta, ya fara ƙoƙarin ƙara yin ƙasa da rigarta, yana mai shafa ƙasan mararta.

Cikin wani irin yanayi yake jin santsi a hannunshi, dabarbarcewa yayi tare da ƙara shafawa.

 Aymana tunda take bata taɓa jin wannan yanayin ba, haka kuma koda Sultan yake shafar jikinta bai taɓa zuwa babbar majalissar ba.

Gaba ɗaya Sultan ya fara ficewa hankalinshi, kam tunanin shi baya jikinshi, abinda ya fara zo mishi yau jikin Aymana ne yake jin wannan yanayin, abinda ya jima yana son ji.

Cikin kwarewa da muguwar sha'awar kasancewa tare da ita, ya fara sarrafata yana mai fara janye kayan jikinshi, musallan wandon shi da Hajiya Babba take neman fasawa ta fito.

Sam Aymana bata kawowa ranta komai ba, sada taji Sultan ya kawar da kayan shi tare da rungumar ta, yana mata wani irin salo da hura mata iska.

Hannunshi ya fara shafa bayanta, yana ɗaga ƙafarta, ya kai hannunshi yana lalubar Hajiya Babba tare da nema mata muhalli.

Sai lokacin Aymana ta fara zuzzullewa, tana ƙaƙarin haɗe ƙafarta Amma sam Sultan baya ma jinta.

Can sama sama yake jiyo yadda take ƙoƙarin hana shi, a ƙasa maƙoshi ya fara faɗin "Please Aymana you're my..."

Ya kasa ƙarasawa yana mai neman majalissar da yake buƙata, a bayyane ya fara karanto Addu'ar saduwa da iyali, ji tayi yana ƙoƙarin shirgarta, ta yi wata irin ƙara tana zullewa, Sultan ya gama da riƙeta gam ta yadda ba zata taɓa kubuce mashi ba.

Ganin da gaske yake hakan yasa ta fasa kuka dai dai lokacin da wani yanayi ya shigeta, jin yadda Sultan yake aika jikinshi cikin nata cikin salon iya sarrafawa, amma sam Aymana bata gane hakan ba, zai zafi da kukan da ta fara sakar mashi.

Cikin duniyar daɗin shi yake jinta, amma baya iya hana kanshi, sai Numfashi shi da yake canza salo yana fita da ƙarfi da ƙarfi.

Roƙonshi Aymana ta farayi, tsawon lokaci ta fara rasa karfinta, jikinta ya gama mutuwa kuka shaɓe-shaɓe take yi, gaba ɗaya jikinta ya saki, ta yi lamo sai hawayen azaba dake gangarowa wani yana korar wani.

Wani hanzari ya ƙara shigar shi ganin shi ne yake sarrafa ta, Sultan ya daɗe bai iya samo kanshi ba, wani abu ke bin jijiyoyinshi don daɗi.

Sai da yaji ya na zuba kafin ya ɗagota yana yin ahankali-ahankali har Numfashin shi ya sauka.

Kan gadon ya faɗa yana mai murgina ta jikinshi, ya na sauke nannauyar Ajiyar zuciya tare da ƙara maƙalƙaleta, wata ƙaunarta ce ta ƙara ziyartar shi, karon farko daya tara da Aymana kwanciyar hankalin yake ji, wasu hawaye yake jin suna fitowa daga idanunshi.

Sai lokacin ya tuna da kukan da ya jiyo tana yi, cikin sauri ya ɗagota yana mai kallon fuskarta.

Sai dai idanuwanta a rufe kuka kawai take, cikin hanzari ya goge nashi hawayen yana mai kallonta ya kuma azata jikin shi tare da rungubeta sosai, yana bubbuga bayanta ahankali ahankali.

Sun shima a haka kafin Aymana tayi shiru, sai lumfashi da take saukewa, jin hakan yasa ya janyeta daga jikinshi tare da janyo filo ya ɗora ta akai.

Banɗaki ya shiga cikin hanzari ya fara haɗa mata ruwan ɗumi, kafin ya dawo ya saka hannu cak ya ɗaga ta akan kafaɗun shi, sam baya son abinda zai wahalar da ita.

Ajiyeta yayi Aymana ta maƙale jikinta, Sultan ya kashe ruwan saboda kwamin daya cika, ya taɓa ruwan yana ƙoƙarin sakata Aymana ta maƙale kafaɗa "Bana so, Bana so."

Bayanta ya shafa yana lallashinta, ya yi hanzarin fara sakata aruwan yana jijjuyata, Aymana ta ji wajan ya ɗau zafi tayi ƙoƙarin miƙewa, cikin lallashi Sultan ya rinƙa gasa mata jikinta.

Ganin akwai ciwo hakan yasa ya cigaba da lallaɓa ta, ji yake kamar ya mayar da ciwon a jikinshi.

Kuka ta saka mashi, ta miƙe a cikin ruwan, ya ma rasa wace irin riritawa zai mata, soyayyarta da tausayinta suna tasiri a zuciyar shi.

Sun jima a toilet ɗin da kanshi ya tsabtace mata jikinta, kafin ya ɗagota yana fitowa da ita, kallon gadon yayi yadda zanin gadon ya ɓaci da fatsi-fatsin jini.

Kujerar zaman gaban mudubi ya jawo ya ɗorata, cikin hanzari ya yaye zanin gadon yazo ya na shimfiɗa wani.

Aymana ga yadda take jin ciwo amma kuma tana kallon yadda Sultan ya zage yau yana aiki gareta.

Sai da ya gyara sosai ya zo ya kamata ya ɗorata akan gadon ya kwantar da ita, yana shafa gashin kanta da ke jiƙe.

Wayar shi ya ɗauka ya danna kira yayi odar ruwan zafin da zata sha. Tare da maganin da yake buƙata akawo mata. Sannan ya je ya wanke zanin gadon cikin hanzari.

Ya dawo Aymana tana rigingine ta rufe idanuwanta yasa hannu ya dafa kanta yakai bakinshi yana sumbatar goshinta.

Yayi hanzarin shiga banɗakin ya yi nashi wankan ya fito yana shiryawa da sauri cikin wata farar jallabiya.

Falon ya fita ya jima kaɗan ya dawo hannunshi ɗauke da tire lokacin ta buɗe idonta, tana ganin shi tayi saurin rufewa.

Zuwa yayi ya ɗagota Aymana ta langwaɓe tare da faɗin "Kabar ni"

Hannu yasa ya share hawayen da suka gangaro mata, ya kai kofin bakinta "Ki sha zaki samu sauki."

Babu musu taɗan kurɓa ta kauda kai, haka yayita lallaɓata har ta sha sosai, ya ɓalle maganin ya bata. Kafin ya maidata akan filo.


Ɓandaki ya shiga ya ɗauro alwala ya zo yana shimfiɗa abin salla kafin ya kaffara salla don gabatar da Nafila, ya jima yana Addu'o'i.

Ya miƙe ya zo don kwantawa, lokacin ya gane bacci ya ɗauketa bargon ya yaye ya saka ƙafafuwanshi ya kwanta bayanta tare da rungumota sosai jikinshi.

Tunani ya farayi yadda ya faɗa soyayyar ta Amma kuma yau yana jin soyayyar tasha banban da kowane lokaci, kaunar ta ta mamaye zuciyar shi sosai, bai taɓa sanin yana ƙaunarta ba sai yau, wani irin kishinta yake ji a zuciyar shi.

[11/2, 7:39 PM] Rahma gr: *MASARAUTA.*

*2021*
      *HAƘƘIN MALLAKA*
*HALIMATU KANGIWA.*
       (AuntyHaliloss).

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA BIYAR. 35*

Ya jima kafin bacci ɓarawo ya ɗauke shi, da asuba bacci bai ishe shi ba haka ya lallaɓa ya zame jikinshi daga nata ya shiga banɗaki yayi wanka tare da ɗoro Alwala ya  fita Masallaci, bai ɗauki lokaci ba ya dawo don baya son ta tashi baya kusa.

Shigowa yayi ya zauna bakin gadon yana binta kallo mai ɗauke da tsananin soyayya, ya matsa a hankali yakai hannunshi, yana mai dafa kanta tare da fara shafa gashin kanta cikin wani irin yanayin so.

A cikin baccin Aymana take jiyo shi, buɗe idanuwanta tayi a hankali tana sauke su akan shi.

Yarima ya gyara kwanciyarshi tare da faɗin "Na tashe ki ko?"

Cikin sauri Aymana ta rufe idon ta don wata kunyar shi ta ziyarceta, tasa hannu ta ja bargon tana rufe fuskarta.

Ƴar dariya Yarima yayi ya gane kunyace ta jagoranceta, hakan yasa ya jawo ta jikinshi "Lokacin Sallah yayi, ki tashi naga lafiyarka." Ya faɗa cikin kulawa.

Jin bata bashi amsa ba, ya sa hannu yana shirin janye bargon, Aymana ta sa hannunta tana rufe fuskarta Yarima yayi dariya "Yau kuma Sultan ɗin ake jin kunya."

Da murmushi ɗauke a fuskarta "ka barni naje nayi salla."

Ɗagota yayi "Ni fa ba na riƙe ki bane."

Ido rufe Aymana ta fara lalubar son tashi tana ƙoƙarin saukowa, amma jikinta wata irin zafi tayi saurin komawa ta zauna, Yarima ya riƙota "Muje na taimaka miki."

"Bana so."

Dariya yayi yana mai tuno maganganun ta na daren jiya hakan ya sashi faɗin "Bana so, Mai martaba ka barni na daina."

Sauri tayi ta buɗe idonta, ta na kai mashi duka a kirji, tsaye ya miƙe "Au ni ko? Ai kuwa yanzu zan kuma."

Yana maganar yana jawota, cikin sauri ta zulle "Tuba nake Allah shi taimakeka."

Dariya ya saka ya riƙo hannunta tare da miƙewa "Shi kenan muje na gani, na shirya miƙi."

Ba jiranta yayi ba, hanyar banɗaki kawai ya nufa da ita, ya zaunar da ita "Zauna bari na haɗa ruwan."

Aymana ta jingina kanta da bango tana kallon shi, ya haɗa ruwan ɗumi ya juyo ya kalle ta cikin nuna kulawa "Kin gaji ko?" 

Shiru tayi hakan yasa ya nufi wata ma'ajiya ya ɗauko burosh da abin wanke baki, ya matsa, ya zauna gefenta, yakai burosh ɗin bakinta, yana son fara yi mata kafin ruwan su gama taruwa.

Da taimakonta ya gama mata ya wanke ya juya ya kashe ruwan, yasa hannu ya na janye rigar da ya saka mata, wata kunya ta ƙaraji, sam Sultan bai damuba, baya son ganin zata wahala.

Cikin ruwan ya sakata, yana gaggasa mata jikinta, ya jima sosai kafin ya mata wanka, da kanshi ya saka mata towul kafin ya riƙota zuwa ɗakin.

Komai Sultan ne yayi mata idan tazo yima zai anshe yayi, mamaki sosai tare da ita, yau ya ƙara canza mata tana ganin kamar ba Sultan ɗin da ta sani ba.

Da taimakon ta ya saka mata kaya, ya shimfiɗa mata abin salla, ganin ta kabbara sallar hakan yasa ya fita falon don shigo da kayan abincin da ya yi oda.

Sai da ya aje komai, Aymana ta jima tana Addu'o'i tare da roƙon Allah farinciki a rayuwarsu mai ɗorewa.

Ganin baya nan hakan yasa ta ci gaba da zamanta, tsawon lokacin sai gashi ya shigo ɗakin, bisa mamakinta, da shiri taganshi kenan wanke yaje ɗayan ɗakin yayi.

Kauda idonta tayi, Sultan ya zauna gefenta tare ɗaukar kayan abincin ya haɗa bai jira komai ba ya cigaba da bata, ta ci sosai kafin ya bata ruwan shayi don gasa cikinta.

Ya miƙe ya kama hannunta ya zaunar da ita kan gado, ta mirgina tana son ƙara kwantawa don hutawa.

Sultan ya ƙara balle magungunanta, ya zauna bakin gadon ya ɗagota "Tashi kisha magani kar..."

"Ni fa ba zan sha ba."

Zaro ido yayi "Me yasa ko so kike jikinki yayita ciwo."

Kauda idonta tayi daga kallon shi, Sultan ya ce "Tashi kisha za ki samu sauƙin."

"Na warke." ta faɗa tana ƙara kame fuskarta, sosai ya gane Izzarta ce take son motsawa.

Dariya yayi don shi sam yana ganin ba lokacin Izza bane yanzu.

Kofin hannun shi ya aje ya miƙe tsaye ya fara ɓalle maɓallin rigarshi, yana cirewa ya rage daga shi sai singileti, dariya yake riƙewa lokacin daya zama daga shi sai gajeren wando.

Ya taka zuwa gadon "Ba damuwa, Tunda Gimbiya ta warke sai mu ɗora daras..."

Ai kafin ya ida Aymana ta yi saurin miƙewa tana yin kan kofin daya aje "Ina ka aje maganin."

Dariya ya saka mata "Kin warke f..."

"Allah A'a."

Maganin ya bata ya kwantar da ita saman kirjinshi, ya na mai shafar bayanta, soyayyar ta da shaƙuwarta suna tasiri sosai a zuciyar shi, tabbas yana jin Aymana ta zama wani ɓangare na rayuwar shi.

"Aymana!" Ya kirata sai dai kiran ya shiga zuciyarta sosai, hakan yasa ta ƙara narkewa jikin shi.

Ɗago fuskarta yayi "Thank you  so much, you really made my day, i much enjoyed it, I had a good time with you, am so lucky to have you, Thanks for such an amazing night, I wish this moment will last longer and forever, I love you." 

*(Na gode sosai, tabbas kin ƙayatar da rana ta yau, na ji daɗin sosai, na samu kyakkyawan lokaci tare da ke, tabbas ni mai sa'a ne na samunki, na gode da dare mai kyau tare dake, ina fatan wannan yanayin yayi tsawo ya zama har abada, Ina son ki.)* 

Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya, tayi saurin ƙara kallon shi jin yau Sultan yana faɗin yana sonta, yaga tsantsar mamaki a tare da ita hakan yasa yace "Sosai sosai Aymana, ina son ki, bana iya musaltawa, ke ɗin ta dabance a zuciyata, ina son ki so na haƙiƙa."

Aymana ta saka hannuwanta a ƙirjinshi tana mai riƙo shi sosai, Sultan ya matseta jikin shi "Na gode farincikina, Allah yayi maki Albarka."

Ƙasa-ƙasa ta amsa mashi da amin, tana mai jin ta shi soyayyar tana fizgarta, a haka maƙale da juna bacci ya ɗauke su.

Wunin ranar a haka sukayi rayuwarsu, babu wanda yake son yin nisa da ɗan uwanshi, abinci kuwa sai dai akawo musu har dare babu inda suka leƙa.

Haka da daddare duk yadda Sultan yayi ƙoƙarin danne sha'awar shi da son ƙara kusantarta ya kasa, solo yayi mata na tausayawa da kuma binta a hankali, Aymana ta samu gamsuwa sosai a tare da Sultan, wannan lokacin bata ji jiki ba, ta ɗan daure mashi sosai.

Da safe tana zaune tana taje gashin kanta, tana gyarawa da wasu mayuka masu laushi, Sultan ya matso yana faɗin "ki yi sauri fa kike min yanga."

Dariya tayi "yanga kuma?"

"E mana, kin manta kince da wuri zamu fita." Yayi maganar yana amsar matajin gashin ya yi sauri ya gyara mata, ya ɗaure ya ɗago fuskarta "Je duba mudubi, na fiki iyawa ashe."

Dariya tayi ta ɗauki Mayafinta ta yane kanta sosai, ta saka hannu zata ɗauki turare don fesawa Sultan ya riƙe hannunta.

"Sam ba zan lamunta ba, kenan kina so wani yaji min ƙamshin mata?"

Sororo tayi tana kallon shi, ɗaga mata jira yayi "ba ki ganin yawancin mutanan dake ganin nan kafurawa sun ciga shi, don shaƙatawa, kina kallo fa."

Tsantsar kishi ta gani a tare da shi, hakan yasa ta daure tana hararar shi "Ban yadda kallo a miki ba balle..."

Ya kasa ida maganar saboda hannunta daya maida kan jikinshi, yana fesa turaren a kayan shi.

"Me hakan ke nufi." Ta faɗa tana miƙewa tsaye "Na ki ne na saka shikenn."

"Ba zan amince ba nima" Dariya yayi "Muje."

"Sai ka sauya kayan kafin mu fita, taya zaka hanani sakawa, kai kuma ka saka, kenan ni bana kishinka?" Ta ƙarashe maganar dai-dai lokacin da Ayda ta faɗo mata arai, hakan yasa jikinta yayi sanyi, tunda tasan cewar tabbas Sultan ba nata bane ita kaɗai.

Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke, tare da faɗin "Ranka shi daɗe, zamu iya tafiya."

Da murmushi a fuskarshi, ya nufi ma'ajiyar kayansu, yana fiddo wasu, zai fitar Aymana tace "Ina mai tuba a gareka."

Bai saurareta ba ya sauya, koba komai yana son nuna mata tana da matsayi a zuciyar shi.

Yana gamawa ya kamo hannunta "Ke ɗin ta dabance, komai za ayi dominki, ina mantawa da akwai wani rawani a kaina a wanann lokacin."

Murmushi tayi ta na faɗin "Na gode!"

"Kiyi a hankali kar ki susutar da Sultan ya koma faɗar shi, a kasa gane kanshi."

Gaba ɗaya sukayi dariya tace "Lallai da fushin Mai martaba ya tabbata kanmu."

A hanya ya fara tunanin abinda zai saya mata da zai zama tukuicinta na faranta zuciyar shi, da kuma mallaka mashi kanta.

Duk abinda yayi tunani yana ɗaukar shi bai kai ya zama tukuiciba.

 Sai da suka sha kwanakinsu cikin farin ciki, kafin suka haɗa kayansu don zasu fara tura kayanne kafin zuwansu.

Da kanshi ya haɗa komai, ya koma falo ya sameta, ya zauna yana faɗin "Zo kiji."

Aymana ta maƙe kafaɗa "Na ƙi wayon."

Dariya yayi ya isa wajan da take ya zauna "Kin ga saura kwanakinmu Ukku mu koma gida, sam na rasa me zai zama tukuicin Gimbiya na faranta ran Sultan da mallaka mashi tabbataccen farin ciki."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi, bata ce komai ba ta ce "Babu buƙatar hakan Allah ya taimakeka."

"Hakan yana da muhimmanci ganin ke kanki kinsan darajar hakan."

Dariya tayi tagane yana son tuno mata haukan da tayi akan daren farkon shi da Ayda.

Sai kuma ta ɗaure fuska "Ina da buƙata." Ta faɗa.

Ya gyara zaman shi, yana son dama ta faɗi ra'ayinta ne.

"Ina jinki."

"Gimbiya ta gama aminta da ƙaunar da Sultan yake mata, babu buƙatar wani abun more rayuwa da zai gushe wata rana, Na ɗauki ƙaunar da kake min a matsayin tukuici na."

Murmushi yayi ya na janyota jikinshi, ya sumbaceta a goshi Aymana ta ci gaba da magana "Ina rokon Alfarma."

Sauri yayi wajan faɗin "Zanyi ko me akan ki Aymana."

"Ina son na dauwama a zuciyar Sultan."

Dariya yayi ya matseta gam jikinshi "Kin samu hakan Aymana."

Ana gobe zasu baro ƙasar Saudiyya Sultan ya ce ta zauna gida shi ɗaya ne zai fita, Sayayya sosai yayi mata, kafin ya gama yanke shawarar abinda zai mata na tukuicinta idan sun koma gida, sai dai hakan ba yana nufin za su baiyana komai ga mutanen gidan ba, zai zama tsakanin shi ne da ita.

A wannan fitarne bai bari ya manta da sayayya mai yawa ga Ayda ba, itama nata jakunkunan daban ya haɗa mata, da ita da yaronta Abul, wanda shi rabin sayyyar shi duk kayan wasa ne.


Dawowa yayi a gajiye Aymana ta kalli yadda wasu ma'aikata suke shigo da kaya, suna fita ta nufeshi "Duk yadda naso karmu kwashi kaya wajan tafiya hakan bai samu ba."

Ajiyar zuciya yayi "Ina tare da gajiya ina buƙatar taimakon ki."

Hannun shi ta kama sukayi ƙurya, ta taimaka mashi yayi wanka ya shirya kafin suka zo suka huta.

***

Washe gari girgin safe su Aymana zasu bi don dawowa Toro, Sultan ya gama shirin shi na Alfarma cikin kayan sarauta da suka amshe shi sosai, yau rawanin kanshi launin makuba ne, hakan ya fito da hasken fatar shi.

Aymana ta gyara Alkebbar jikinta "Kwana biyu da Sultan bai saka rawani ba, sai naga yau Sultan ya fi kullum yin kyau."

Shiru baiyi magana ba, sai ƙofa da yake nufa cikin tafiyar Sarauta, jin bai amsa mata ba Aymana ta gane yau fa ya mayar da Izzarshi, hakan yasa ta bi bayanshi tana mai tafiyar  ƙasaita, wanda ita kanta sarƙar ƙafarta tana fitar sauti mai rikitarwa.

Lokacin da suka isa motoci ne suka zo ɗaukar shi, da fadawa masu tarin yawa, wasu daga cikin motocin suna ɗauke da busa da algaita.

Sam su Aymana basuyi mamakin ganin yadda aka ƙayatar da gidan ba, hakan ya tabbatar musu da ana shirya wani shagali ne don dawowar Sultan.

Umarni Sultan ya bada akan nufa dashi wani ɓangare na sirri don su shirya kafin su fito.

Ayda ta ci kwalliya wannan lokacin don tarbar Sultan a cewar ta itace matar da zata tare shi.

Kuyangi da bayin gidan sai kai kawo suke, Jakadiya kuwa bi take ɗaki ɗaki don leƙo wainar da ake toyawa.

Wanann lokacin sam dawowar Sultan baiyiwa Waziri da Yarima Saifu daɗi ba, saboda tun tafiyar Sultan ɗin  Waziri yake zama fadar safe shi kuma Yarima Saifu ya zauna fadar yamma.

Farfajiyar gidan ta ƙayatu da adon sarauta da kujeru, mutanen gidan kowa yazo, hatta mai martaba da iyalanshi sun fito Sultan ne kawai ake jira da Aymana.

Ayda tana daga gefe cikin Alkebba launin ja, sai cika take tana batsewa ga kuyangi na gewaye da ita.

Sultan ne da Aymana suka dirfafo wajen yayinda fadawa da kuyangi suka biye dasu.

Kowa na wajen ya miƙe tsaye don girmamawa  lokacin da Sultan ya ke niyar zama.

Abin mamaki Ayda tana zaune, Aymana kuwa tana tsaye tana jiran zaman Sultan kafin ta zauna.

Murmushi Sultan yayi ya fasa zama, ya ja alkebbar shi tare da nufa wajan Ayda ko ba komai dai yayi kewar shirmenta kwana biyu.

Kowa ya maida hankalin shi wajen, Sultan ya je gaban kujerarta ya ɗan sunkuya kamar yana mata raɗa "Gimbiya." 

Ya faɗa, Ayda ta saki murmushi tana kallon shi, Sultan ya miƙe ya kamo hannunta.

Aymana tayi saurin kauda idonta jin wani abu daya daki zuciyarta, kishi taji marar musaltuwa.

Wata kujerar Sultan ya canzawa Ayda, Ayda ji take kamar ya ƙara mata girma akanta, ta zauna tana saka hannu ta dafa cikinta, ko don cikin jikinta tasan dole ya kulata.

Take aka fara kirari ga Ayda da kuma Sultan.

Juyawa yayi don komawa mazaunin shi, ta gaban Aymana yazo wucewa, cikin sauri ta sunkuya alamar ban girma saida taga ya wuce ne ta ƙara dai-daita tsayuwarta.

Sultan ya zauna sannan kowa ya zauna, ya sanar bayason bata lokaci don yana son shiga ya huta.

Haka yasa aka gabatar da komai na murnar dawowarshi cikin sauri, masu wasannin gargajiya suka gabatar, kowa na wajen ya ji daɗi.

Sultan yayi jawabi da godiya gasu waziri da suka riƙe karagar shi har ya dawo.

Aymana kanta yana ƙasa, da kyal ta samu ta daidaita kanta, Sultan ya ɗan kula da hakan, sai dai bai damu ba.

Farida ta zauna gefenta daga ƙasa tare da yi mata raɗa ahankali "Allah ya ja kwananki, ina mai tuba, Amma hankalinki baya tare da taron nan."

Cikin sauri Aymana ta nutsu ta mayarda hankalinta, dai-dai lokacin aka fara jawabi akan Sultan yana son gabatar da bada Hula da kuma naɗi.

Sultan ya miƙe tsaye aka miƙa mashi wata hula ta mata ƙirar hular sarakuna mata. (Tiara) sai dai ƙiyar hular ƙirar sarakunan gargajiyane, wanda aka yiwa ado da madubai da zagayen zinari mai kyalli.

Mai gabatarwar yace "Sultan zai sakawa Gimbiya Aymana hular naɗi da kuma bata sarautar Sarauniyar matan Nahiyarmu. Saboda haka mai martaba yana son ganin Gimbiya Aymana a gaban shi."

Wata irin faɗuwar gaba ta shigi Aymana ta ɗago a gigice, tana kallon mutanan wajen kowa yana cikin mamaki yadda Sultan zai yi naɗi ba tare da ya nemi shawarar kowa ba.

Sultan yana kallonta cikin soyayya, tabbas dole ya bata girma da kuma bata tukuici mai tsoka akan daran farkon su, amma kuma yana ganin sarautar da zai bata hakan zai sa ba za a taɓa mantata a nahiyar ba, kasancewar itace mace ta farko da ta riƙe wannan Sarautar.

Kowa ya fara murna, ana ihu da tafi, Jakadiyya ta ci gaba da rangaɗa guɗa.

Aymana ta kalli Sultan dake kallon wajan da take fuska ɗauke da murmushi.

Mama dake nesa tayi saurin nufo Aymana cikin murna, ganin ta kasa tashi.

Kuyanga Aisha da Farida suka ƙara matsowa, Mama ta riƙo hannun Aymana suna miƙewa don kaita gaban Sultan.

Farida tayi saurin riƙe wani yadin karan-miski dake jan ƙasa jikin kayan Aymana.

Ayda tayi saurin miƙewa tana dafa kujera cikin gigicewa, ta yadda za a ɗauki sarauta mai girma aba Aymana bayan itace take kawo magadan sarautar gidan su.

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA SHIDDA. 36*

   Ana zuwa gaban Sultan Aymana ta sunkuyar da kanta ƙasa, Sultan yayi murmushi yana mai saka hannu ya fara ɗago kanta, Jakadiyya ta matso da salon kiraki.

Sultan ya ɗago hular ya ɗorata akan Aymana, murna aka kama yi, Aymana wani sanyi ya ziyarceta, tabbas tasan darajar sarauta, hakan yasa take jin kamar ya bata duk wani farin ciki da zata iya nema.

Ɗagowa tayi a hankali tana mai son mayarda hawayen farin ciki dake neman zubar mata, Sultan ya koma kan kujerar shi ya zauna, Ayman ta tsuguna a gaban shi alamar godiya da kuma girmamawa.

Sultan yayi murmushi kawai, Mama ta kamo hannun Aymana suka koma mazauninta.

Mai martaba kuwa yasan tabbas hakan yana nufin Sultan ya samu farin ciki na tafiya da Aymana, shi kanshi yasan tabbas Aymana ta cancanta a yaba mata.

Waziri kuwa zuciyar shi kamar zata huda kirjinshi ta fito, wani baƙin ciki yake ji, lallai Sultan ya tabbatarwa mutanan gidan babu wani bayan Aymana.

Goggo dake gefen Ayda ta riƙe hannunta "Ki daure Kar ki..."

Fizge Hannu Ayda tayi tana mai barin wajan sanin cewar idan har ta tsaya tabbas sai tayi abinda zai ja hankalin kowa, tun kafin ta isa sashenta take kuka, Allah ya taimaketa babu kowa mutanen gidan suna farfajiyar.

Haka aka tashi taron masu murna sunayi masu baƙin ciki kamar suyi hauka. 

Sultan sashen Gimbiya Ummi ya wuce don gaida ita, sai da ya gaida kowa kafin ya wuce sashen shi.

Aymana kuwa ita kanta bata samu kanta ba, saboda masu taya murna dake zuwar mata da kuma Barka da dawowa.

Jin ance Sultan ya shigo hakan yasa tayi saurin miƙewa don zuwa wajan shi, kasancewar tasan Ayda ce zata amshe shi.

Yana zama Aymana tana shigowa da sassarfarta ta ƙarasa gaban shi ta durƙusa "Allah ya ja kwanan ka, ina godiya, ina jin farin ciki har bansan taya zan yi godiya ko bada tukuicin wann..."

"Ba a biyan tukuici don wani tukuicin."

Aymana ta ɗago, Sultan ya miƙe yasa hannu ya ɗagota suka miƙe tsaye ya riƙe kafaɗunta "Wannan shine tukuicin ki da kika kasa zaɓar abinda kike so."

Murna tayi tare da rungumoshi ta kai bakinta tana sumbatar shi "Na gode."

"Shi kenan dai a fidda ranar fidda shagali don taro akan..."

"Ranka shi daɗe bana buƙatar hakan, Sam bana so sarautar ta zama zan rinƙa gudanar da ita, babu buƙatar shagali."

"Me hakan ke nufi Aymana?"

Murmushi tayi ta lakaci hancin shi "Mai kula da Sultan ba zai samu lokacin gudanar da wani mulki ba, iya kula dakai ma mulki ne."

Dariya yayi jin yadda ta zaɓe shi akan sarautar daya bata "Allah ya maki Albarka."

Bayan fitar Aymana haka tasa aka fitar da kayan tsaraba ga kowa har da Maimartaba a ciki.

Bayi da kuyangi sunyi murna sosai, Jakadiyya tsarabarta ta dabance, ita kau da ma ba tun yanzu ba Aymana ta gama da ita tunda ta kaita ƙasa mai tsarki.

Ranar Ayda sai da ta taɓo mashi zancen banbanci da ya nuna tsakanin su, shiru yayi ya ƙaleta ganin duk kalmar da zai yi mata ya riga ya taɓa yi mata wajan nusar da ita akan abinda yayi niya bazai fasa ba.

Bayan kwana biyu ta rinƙa karɓar zugar wasu daga cikin mutanen gidan, hakan yasa suka dawo kamar da ita da Aymana da sun haɗu sai gorin haihuwa da habaice Habaice, Aymana kuwa ta sake hannu ta toshe kunnuwanta a yanzu ta yi alƙawarin ba zata kuma kula Aymana ba.

Mai martaba ne zaune da Sultan suna fira, Gimbiya Ummi ta shigo Sultan ya gaida ita yana shirin tashi don bar musu wajen Gimbiya Ummi ta kalle shi "Alhamdulillah Sultan na fahimci komai ya maka dai dai a fadar ka."

Sultan ya sunkuyar da kai sai lokacin ya tuna bai faɗa masu yadda yake jin ya samu komai lafiya ba.

"Ayi min Afuwa Gimbiya Ummi, nayi shiru ne akan maganar ina gudun kar mutanen gidannan su fahimci ina..."

Dariyar girma Mai martaba yayi "Ai ko baka faɗa ba mun fahimta."

"Allah dai yayiwa yarinyar nan albarka." Cewar Gimbiya Ummi.

Shiru Sultan yayi tare da miƙewa "Na barku lafiya."

Yana fita Gimbiya Ummi ta kalli Mai martaba "Ni kam wallahi ma Yarinyar ta fara bani tausayi."

"Wajan me kenan?"

"Hmm yau dai ko yaya ne zan faɗa, akan haihuwa, duk yadda yarinyar nan Ayda take mata gori ina sane amma Aymana ko kallonta bata yi."

"Kinzo da maganar da na jima ina son yi, amma abin mamaki shi Sultan ɗin bai taɓa kulawa ba."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi ta ce "Wannan lokacin ba zamu zuba ido ba, zan zauna da shi, ya kai yarinyar nan Asibiti a dubata."

"Yana da kyau yin hakan." Mai martaba ya bata amsa.

***

Sultan ne ya riƙe hannun Aymana da take shafa kirgin shi, ya kalleta yana murmushi "Wai Gimbiya Ummi ce ta ce na kai ki Asibity ki ga likita."

Aymana ta ɗan razana tare da faɗin "Saboda me, lafiya ta lau."

"Tace tana buƙatar ganin jikanta daga wannan ɓangaren." Yayi maganar yana mai shafa cikinta.

Dariya tayi "Allah sarki ni wallahi har hankali na ya tashi."

Hannunshi yakai saman kafaɗarta "Zan faɗawa Gimbiya zai yiwu ma ta shirya ganin Magaji nan da..."

"Haba ni ba wani abu a tare sani."

Sultan ya ja hannnunta "kin tabbatar?"

Dariya tayi "Eh mana."

Miƙewa tsaye yayi tare da ɗaukarta tsagwayam "Shi kenan muje na baki magajin yanzu."

Yana maganar yana hayewa dasu kan gado, Aymana ta miƙe ta dafa kafaɗar shi "Shi kenan ba damuwa zan karɓa."

Tayi maganar tana saka hannu ta fara ɓalle maɓallin rigarshi, Sultan ya kai kanshi akan kumcinta, da taimakon ta ya kawar da kayan jikinshi, kafin nata kayan, wani salon wasa Sultan ya cigaba da aika mata sai da ya tabbatar ya kaita inda ba zata iya juraba kafin ya hautsine na shi tunanin ta hanyar kai kanshi yana tsotsar jikinta.

Ya sani sarai salon yana tasiri wajan kawar da tunanin Aymana nishi ta fara sakar mashi tana ƴar ƙara, sosai yake tsotsa ta, ya miƙar da hannuwanshi yana lalubar ƙirjinta tare da mummurzawa cikin salo, Jin Aymana ta fara mashi numfashi hakan yasa shi saka nashi hannun akan Hajiya Babba dake ƙakƙandarewa ya janye kanshi tare da mayar da jikin shi yana fara sarrafara cikin lumshe ido yana jin gamsuwa na shigarshi.

****

Ayda ta dafa cikin dake gabanta daya turo sosai ta ci gaba da magana "Da banbanci fa har yanzu, ko baki fahimci hakan ba, kin kasa gane kowa yana ganin gazawar ki, ko da yake babu buƙatar hakan, Sultan ya riga ya samu mai gadon shi, saura ma mai zuwa nan da ɗan lokaci.

"Ayda!"

Aymana ta faɗa tana fara nunata da yatsa wannan lokacin ta kai ta ƙarshe, sai dai kafin ta ƙara ɗaga baki don magana Gimbiya Saratu ta shigo farfajiyar.

Aymana ta juya tana kallon ta, Ayda ta aikawa Saratu wani mugun kallo, Saratu tayi kamar bata ganta ba tayi kan Aymana "Gimbiya zo ki ji."

Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tabi bayan Saratu, suna shiga ɓangaren ta Gimbiya saratu  tace "Wallahi baƙo gare ku ni kumu ban san taya zanwa Sultan bayani ba."

"Baƙo kuma?"

Dariya Saratu tayi "Sirikin ku mana."

Aymana ta jawota "kaji ni da mara kunyar yarinya, Sultan ɗin ne kika rasa taya zaki sanar dashi."

"Wallah kuwa."

"Shi kenan yaushe zai zo, zan sanar dashi."

"Gobe ne, yace yana son ganawa da Sultan ne, amma zuwan safe zasuyi."

"Babu damuwa zan tashi Sultan ɗin da wuri kar ki damu."

***

Da daddare Aymana tana zaune tana jiran shigowar Sultan yau kanta yana mata ciwo sai dai tana son isar da saƙon Saratu kafin ta kwanta.

Bisa mamakinta sai gani tayi Sultan ya fito hannunwan shi ɗauke da kofin shayi guda biyu.

Binshi tayi da kallo cikin daurewa ta ce "Ban yi tunanin kana ciki ba."

Murmushi yayi yana ɗan kallonta ganin bata taso ta karɓe shi ba "Allah yasa lafiya."

"Lafiya lau Alhamdulillah." ta bashi amsa, tare da kauda zancen da bata son ya gane bata jin daɗi.

"Ina can ina haɗa shayi ga Gimbiya" ya faɗa yana miƙa mata kofin.

Aymana ta ƙarɓa, suracin shayin yana fita da ƙamshin sinadarin da aka haɗa ma Shayin.

Ɗan yamutsa fuska tayi jin yadda ƙamshin ya doki hancinta, ya aje kofin tare da faɗin "Ko miye Sultan yayi Shayin da shi."

Ajewa yayi ya matso ya jawota jikin shi "Kamar akwai damuwa tare da ke."

"A'a saƙon saratu ne nazo isarwa" tayi maganar tana gaya mashi.

Dariya yayi "Allah ya kaimu gobe."

Ameen tace, Sultan ya ci gaba da shan shayin shi Aymana ya miƙe Sultan ya bita da kallo, ya kalli kofin da ta bari bata sha ko kaɗan ba.

Ya ajiye kofin yana binta baya ya samu tana rage kayan jikinta "Ba ki da sha Shayin ba?"

Ya faɗa cikin sanyin jiki, don ya damu, Ayman ta ɓalle bireziyar jikinta, ta nufe shi tana wata irin tafiya da salon jan hankali, ga dukiyar fulanin ta dake girgizawa.

Sultan ya kalleta lokacin da tazo gab da shi "Na faɗa maka Shayin yana ƙamshi mara daɗi, ban san me ka saka ba."

Hannuwanshi yasa ya riƙo dukiyar fulanin da ke mashi yawo a ido, bai bata amsaba, ya kai bakinshi akan ɗaya yana fara tsotsa. Aymana ta rinjaye su suna faɗawa kan gadon ɗakin.

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA ƊAYA. 31*

Aymana ta ji wani tashin hankali da maganganun Sultan "Wannan wace irin rayuwa ce Sultan?"

Shiru yayi tare da jingina jikin shi ga kujera "Wanann shi ne abinda ya faru, wanda na san ba kowa ne zai gane hakan ba Aymana. Allah ya gani ina tausayin Abul."

Hawaye ne suka gangaro daga idanuwanta, ta saka hannu tana gogewa, lallai ta san sun saka rayuwar yaron a cikin hatsari, ta juya ta kalli Sultan "Ba a jiye su, don Allah a fara nema mashi sauƙi tun kafin abun ya zama wata matsalar kuma."

"Zan saka shi a Addu'o'i na, ina sha Allah."

"Ameen" ta amsa tare da miƙewa ta matso mishi da kayan lambu, ta sa hannu ta ƙara gyara fuskarta, kafin ta yi hanyar barin wajen, ido kawai Sultan Ameen ta bita dashi.

***
Sai da aka ƙara ɗaukar lokaci, kafin maganar rashin lafiyar Abul ta baiyana a gidan, Ayda ce tsaye gaban Sultan tana kukanta, tsawon lokaci bai mata magana ba "Taya za a ɗau ciwo a ɗorawa yarona, wannan ai sharri ne."

"Ayda!"

Ta ɗago ta kalleshi "Ke baki kula da Abul ɗin bane ko me?"

Sarai ta sani amma bata san ta ina zata ɓullowa lamarin ba "Ai nasan dole sai Abul ya ga taskun rayuwa a gidan nan, musamman ga mutanen da suka zo don neman shiga da kuma..."

Wata irin tsawa Sultan ya daka mata, saboda ya fahimci tana so ta ce Aymana ce tayiwa yaronta sihiri, abun ya baki mamaki wai su ba zasu taɓa yin hankali ba. "Sai yaushe hankali zai shige ki ne, ba ki ta lalurar yaron ki, sai ma neman abin abun ki ke?"

"Amma ai..."

Kafin ta ida Sultan ya nuna mata ƙufa cikin zafin zuciya ba tare da yayi magana ba, ta gane ran shi ya ɓaci Ainun, hanyar fita tayi tana mai kuka.

Kuyangin dake wajen suka bita da kallo tare da fara gulamace-gulmace, ɓangaren  Waziri ta nufa ta same shi tsaye yana kai kawo Ayda ta fasa kuka mai tsuma zuciya, Waziri ya bita da kallo "Dama baƙin ciki ake kar yaro na ya gaji sarauta shi yasa aka yi mashi haka."

"Ayda ba da ke suke yi ba, wannan faɗan da ni suke wallahi, yanzu yaron da muka ɗaura burin mu akan shi shi ne sukayiwa haka."

Inna ta aje tire ɗin hannunta "Amma wallahi ban yafe ba, kuma idan har ba a ɗau mataki ba ..."

Gani tayi Waziri yayi zama dirshen a ƙasa ya dafe kai, yana karanto salatin da babu shi a zuciyar shi, wasu zafafan Hawaye suka biyo kuncin shi "Duk daɗewar da nayi cikin son ganin na jagoranci gidan nan har yau ban samu sa'a ba, wallahi wallahi wallahi na yi alƙawarin sai dai ayi biyu babu." Yayi maganar tare da miƙewa ya nufi cikin gida.

***

Jakadiyya ta yi shewa tana mai kallon Gimbiya Mai gado "Me na faɗa maki? Wannan kaɗan ma suka gani, ai sama tayiwa yaro nisa."

Gimbiya Mai gado ta buga cinya ciki tana sakin shu'umin murmushi "Sai dai abi wani sarki, amma nan dai zance ya ƙarare, ba ki ga Waziri har ya fara tada kafaɗa ba, wai shi jikanshi zai yi mulki duk daɗewa.

"Allah ya taimakeki ba zasu taɓa samun nasara ba."

***

Sultan Amin ne zaune kan kujera ɓangaren Gimbiya Ummi, Aymana kuwa tana daga gefen shi, shiru babu wanda yake magana har shigowar Gimbiya Ummi, gaisheta sukayi ta zauna tana amsawa tare da faɗin "Ko Sultan ya dubo jikin Gimbiya Ayda?"

Ɗan dafe kai yayi "Yanzu nake son wucewa daga nan."

"Ina tunanin kamar har da damuwa da ta saka wa ranta akan ciwon Abul"

Shiru Aymana bata saka masu baki ba, sai dai ta ji tausayin Ayda, gudun kar su ga kamar wani abu hakan ya sa tace "Tana ɗakin magani ne?"

Sultan ya juyo ya kalleta "Haka aka sanar dani."

"Sai ku je ku dubota gaba ɗaya har ke Aymana." Cewar Gimbiya Ummi.

"Akwai yuwar sai na je turakata kafin zuwan." Sultan ya faɗa yana miƙewa.

Aymana ta miƙe tana ɗan sunkuyawa don yiwa Gimbiya Ummi bankwana, Sultan ma hakan, suna zuwa hanyar fita Saratu ta shigo "Allah ya taimake ka barka da fitowa."

"Bana amsa kalar wannan gaisuwar." Ya faɗa yana wucewa.

Dariya Saratu tayi tana mai bin bayansu, ta riƙo hannun Aymana suka fito tare, a hanyan Aymana take mata tsegumi akan dole Sultan yaƙi amsa gaisuwarta tana ƙanwarshi amma bata damu da sha'anin kowa na gidan ba, balle mulkin shi.

Dariya tayi tace "Ni fa ba na son hayaniyar mutanan gidanan ne."

"Kin fi son zama kina danna waya, shi ya sa ga ki nan babu abinda kika sani na Sarauta."

Taɓe baki tayi tana murmushi, ta tsaya tana faɗin "Sauka lafiya, Ni komawa zan yi, zan zo neman afuwa gun Sultan."

Dariya Aymana tayi, Saratu ta juya ita kuma ta bi bayanshi suna tafiya kamar yadda suke.

***

Yamma na yi Sultan ya aikawa Aymana akan ta fito za suje duba Ayda. A zaune ta same shi sanye da shadda launin bulu mai haske, babbar riga da rawanin shi suna akan kujera, Sumar kan shi ta sha gyara sosai, ta kwanta, kamar yadda sajen shi ya gewaye farar fuskar shi.

Shiga tayi tana ɗan murmushi "Allah ya taimaki namijin zaki."

Binta yayi da kallo yana nazarinta, sai dai bai yi magana ba, ta ɗan sunkuya ta ɗauki rawanin tana dubawa, ta matso kusa da shi "Barka da hutawa."

Ƙamshin turarenta ya doki hancinsa, hakan yasa shi ɗan lumshe ido "Sultan bai gama shiri ba kenan?" Ta faɗa ba tare da jin komai na rashin amsawar shi ba, don ta san komai na sarauta, shiru ma amsace a wasu lokutan.

Gaban shi ta tsaya ta saka hannu tana fara shafa lallausar sumar shi, cikin wani irin salo, sai lokacin ya ɗan yi murmushi "Sabon aski ne aka..."

"Lallai da Gimbiya tana kusa da ta bada lada mai tsoka ga mai askin." Tayi maganar tana aza mashi rawanin, hakan yasa ya riƙo hannuwanta duka biyu, ya kalleta, tare da miƙewa tsaye.

"Ko Gimbiya ta manta da babbar riga da Alkebba kafin rawani?"

Sai lokacin ta tuna, hakan ya sa ta saki murmushi mai sauti ta ce "kyawun sajen Sultan ma ka ɗai ya isa mantar da ni." Murmushi yayi shima yau yana ganin kamar akwai tsokana a tare da ita, sai dai kuma ganin shi ne yasata shiga wani irin shauƙi.

Ta ɗan janye hannun ta daga riƙon da yayi mata ta aza rawanin akanta saman ɗankwalinta, Sultan ya bita da kallo, tana kwasar Alkebba ta nufo shi, ta bude babbar rigar ta ɗan ƙara tsayi tana saka mashi ta dawo tana gyara wuyan rigar da kuma naɗewa akan kafaɗa.

Har lokacin rawanin yana akanta, hakan ya ɗan yi mata kyau, kasancewar yau rawanin bula ne mai turuwa, tana aza mashi alkebba ta aza hannu akai zata cire rawanin.

Sultan ya riƙe hannunta "Ki bar shi a haka Aymana."

Zaro ido tayi tana kallon shi, ɗaga mata gira yayi "Akan ki naga yafi kyau, akan ki ya dace ya zauna Aymana, na fi son ganin shi anan, Me amfanin shi akai na bayan kece komai nawa a mulkina." Yayi maganar cikin sanyin murya da sam Aymana bata san Sultan yana da shi ba.

Ta ƙara matsawa sosai gaban shi, zata yi magana ya katseta "Kullum ke ce mai tagazawa rawanina, me don ya koma akan ki?"

    A hankali ya gewaya zuwa bayan ta tare  da zagaya hannun shi akan cikin ta, kanshi ya daura a kafaɗar ta, yana goga  hancin shi cikin tsananin damuwa da bukatar kasancewa da ita na har abada.

   Mutuwa jikinta yayi bata san lokacin da ta rufe idanun ta ba, tana kara jingina bayanta a faffaɗar kirjin shi. Zuciyarta tana wani irin bugawa, wani irin kaunar shi da begen shi yana ƙara tabbatar a zuciyarta, bata san yadda aka yi hakan ba.

Sai dai bururrukan da suke danƙare bisa zuciyarta ba zai barta ta cimma matsaya akan Sultan dinta da yake shirin bata kome na shi ba.

A hankali ta cire rawanin ta riƙe a hannunta sannan ta janye jikinta daga na shi , ta ɗan sunkuya cikin girmamawa "Ina mai neman afuwar Sultan akan rawanin shi da na saka, lallai rawani yana da girma na sani, idan da wani yayi amfani da shi ba ni ba, lallai hukunci zai zama mai tsanani, zai yiwu ma ko waye ya aikata hakan ya zama cikin bayi marasa galihu."

Ajiyar zuciya Sultan yayi ya kama kafaɗarta tare da haɗata da ƙirjin shi, Aymana ta cigaba da magana "Idan kuwa har hakan ya faru na san Mai martaba ba zai taɓa amfani da rawanin ba, don zai iya kasancewa ko akwai wani sihiri da za a aiwatar ta hakan."

Cikin sauri Sultan ya anshi rawanin daga hannun Aymana ya aza akan shi, sam babu wani zargi tsakanin shi da Aymana, haka ne maganarta za a iya yiwa sarakuna sihiri ta amfani da rawanin su.

Ya gyara rawanin sosai ya ƙara matseta jikin shi "Ina so Gimbiya ta sani, Sultan ba shi da amintacce kamar matar shi, haka babu zarginta a tare da shi" yayi maganar tare da ɗago kanta suka haɗa idanuwansu yace "Ko kin manta ke ce malamar lafiyata?"

Murmushi tayi har kumcinta ya lotsa, Sultan ya duƙar da kanshi, cikin bugawar zuciya ya kai bakinshi akan wuyanta  yana mai sumbatarta, sai da tsikar jikinta ta tashi, cikin dakewa ta janye jiki, tana mai nuna mashi ƙofa.

    Har zai fita kawai ya tsinci kan shi da sake janyo ta. Ya manna ta da bango, cikin wani irin zazzafar kaunarta wanda ya sashi aikata abinda bai shirya mishi ba.

Ya shiga sauke mata wasu tagwayen sumbata da yasa ta kasa tsayawa da kafaffunta, numfashin su yana haɗuwa a tare,  cikin wata wahalalliyar yanayi ta kuma rike harshen shi tana kara tsotsar shi.

  Hannun shi ya kai k'ugun ta, yana kara mannata da jikin shi, bai tab'a kawowa yau zai ji irin gudunmawar da zata bashi ba, sai gashi baki daya ta sussuta  mishi al'amarin shi. Cikin wani irin kwarewa yake tafiyar da hannun shi har cikin rigarta.

 Ƙamƙame shi tayi sakamakon tab'o dukiyar fulaninta, masu laushi, yana kara shafa ta, har zuwa cikin ta, baki daya ta gama narke mishi.

Daga shi har ita basu san zasu iya samun kan su a haka ba, sai dai a fahimtar da tayiwa Sarki Sultan ɗin nata ta fahimci yana bukatar yaja al'amarin ya wuce haka jim yadda yake zuge mata zip din rigarta, hakan yasa ta janye bakinta daga nashi, tana me kifa kanta a kirjin shi, sumbatar kanta yayi tare da cewa.

"Me yasa?"

"Aydah" ta faɗa, baki daya ya manta da wani zancen Aydah, dan haka ya janye jikin shi bayan ya kalle ta, murmushi yayi ƙasa ƙasa ya ce

"Haka Gimbiya zata tafi da kayanta a yamutse?" Ya fada tare da mai da dariyan shi murmushi.

Tura baki tayi domin tasan ba iya kayanta ba, har wanka ya haura kanta,itama cikin zolaya tace mishi.

"Da fatan Sultan zai gana da ruwa!" Murmushi yayi

"Zoki taimaka min" Maƙale kafaɗa tayi cikin kunya tace "Allah ya baka yawan rai, a haka so ake a cinye ni danye ina kuma na kai kaina bandakin ka."

Jinjina kai yayi yana rage kayan jikin shi tare da cewa "Ai haka!" ta gane nufin shi kafin ya gama yunƙurawa ta fice da sauri tana dariya.

Murmushi yayi sannan yace.
"Da kin tsaya mana." 

Bayan mintin kamar talatin suka kuma fitowa cikin farin ciki da annashuwa, ko wannan su yana jin daɗin yanayin da ya kasance ayau.

Ɗakin magani suka nufa, Ayda tana kwance lokacin bacci ya ɗauketa, sun jima a tsaye bakin gadon, Aymana ta nunawa Sultan kujera bai mata magana ba, hakan ya sa ta gane baya buƙata.

Sultan yana kai kawo ya ɗan maida hannuwanshi bayan shi, Aymana ta kalli takardun dake aje gefen gadon da Ayda take kwance, ta bi takardun da kallo.

Ta ɗan jima kafin tayi tunanin duba takardun, ko da akwai shawarwarin da zata basu ta fannin lafiyar Ayda.

Buɗe fayil ɗin tayi, ta fara karantawa Sultan ya bita da kallo kafin ya koma kan kujerar da Aymana ta nuna mashi ya zauna.

Ɗaya bayan ɗaya take karanta takardun, bataga wata matsala ba sosai amma akwai alamar ciwon zuciya ko bugawar zuciyar Ayda ya sauya hakan yasa ta ɗago ta kalli Sultan tare da faɗin.

"Kaga abinda Gimbiya Ummi ya faɗa ko?" ya  kalleta ba tare da yayi magana ba, ta miƙe tsaye tana nufa kan tebur da kayan likitoci suke har zata ɗauka ta duba Ayda sai kuma wata zuciya ta haneta.

Ta dawo ta na ida bin takardun tana karantawa, wata takarda da ta ɗan tsaya kanta, tana ware ido, ta sa hannu tana murza idanuwanta, don gani take kamar gizo takardun ke mata.

Ta ɗago ta kalli Sultan sai taga ya rufe idanuwan shi tare da jingina da kujera.

Gabanta ne ya fara dukan tara-tara, idan har ta karanta takardar dai dai *CIKI* ne ta gani Ayda tana ɗauke da shi.

Aymana ta ƙara karantawa tabbas Ayda tana ɗauke da cikin sati biyar, ciki kaɗuwa da tashin hankali Aymana ta rufe takardun.

Tana dafe kirjinta dake lugude kamar zai faɗo, idanuwanta sun kaɗa sunyi ja, kanta yana sara mata, tunda take duniya bata taɓa tsintar kanta a makamancin wannan tashin hankalin ba.

Ta ɗago ido tana kallon shi, har lokacin idon shi a rufe yake, ta maida kallon ta ga Ayda, da ke kwance, ta fara  tunanin kalar soyayyar da Sultan yake ma Ayda, yau har gashi tana ɗauke da ciki na biyu.

Wani shahararran kishi take ji, ji take kamar ta fasa ihu, ta miƙe tana maida takardun ahankali, ta koma ta yi saurin jingina da bango don ji take ƙafafuwanta ma ba zasu iya ɗaukar ta ba.

Sultan ya buɗe idon shi, cikin sauri Aymana ta daidaita nutsuwarta, ya miƙe tsaye "Ko zamu tafi zuwa dare ma dawo?"

Aymana ta yi sauyin yin hanyar ƙofa jin hawaye na niyar wanke mata kumci.

Bayanshi tabi har ƙofarshi suna shiga, ya zauna yana mai kallonta ita kuma ta nufi ɗakinta dake cikin ɓangaren shi.

Da sauri ta rufe ƙofa, tare da durƙushewa tana sakin kuka, ta saka hannuwanta tana daɗe bakinta.

Wani irin kuka take da sam bata iya riƙe kanta, bata san miye dalilin Sultan na yi mata irin wannan ƙiyayyar ba, a hankali taja jiki ta koma kan gado tana ƙara canza salon kukanta.

Haka tayita zama aganin kukan ba zai fissheta ba yasa ta fara tunanin mafita, wannan Lokacin bata neman shawarar kowa amma dole komai ya zo ƙarshe ta bar mashi gidan shi, duk wani abu da suke ɓoyewa dole su baiyyanar da shi.

Saboda kuka da tasha hakan yasa fuskarta tayi kumburi, fatar idanuwanta suka yi ja, lokaci kaɗan zazzaɓi mai zafi ya rufeta, jikinta ya hau rawar sanyi, barkon dake kan gadon taja ta rufa dashi.

Hawaye sun kasa tsayawa a idonta, kishi ke lallasar zuciyarta, wata zuciyar ta sanar da ita ta bar mashi gidan shi, wata zuciyar ta fara tambayarta miye ribarta nayin hakan bayan bata cimma mata burin ba.

Shawarwari ta farayi, yadda zata ɓullowa lamarin, a take ta yanke shawarar zata yi amfani da damar zuwa lokacin da zai samu lafiya, komai na mulkin shi ya daidaita, daga lokacin zata Ɗ
dauki *TAKOBIN* gidan su, ta barshi tunda babu amfanin zamanta.

***
A tunanin Sultan Aymana wani abu zata ɗauko ta fito, hakan yasa ya barta, sai dai shirun da yaji yasa shi kallon hanya duk bayan wani lokaci.

Agogo ya kalla ya miƙe don yaje yin shirin tafiya masallaci sallar magriba,har ya yi Alwala ya fito, bai gantaba, ya fice masallaci.

Sai da aka gama sallar isha yayi bankwana da kowa, kafin ya dawone ya biya ya duba jikin Ayda kafin ya nufi ɓangaren shi, a ƙofa ya tambaya aka sanar dashi ba aga fitar ta ba, shiga yayi ɗakin shi yayi wanka ya fara shirin bacci.

Wasu fararen kayan bacci ya saka rigar tana da botira a gere gaba, sai dogon wando, ya saka turaruka, ya ɗauki wayar shi har zai kwanta sai ya miƙe ya nufi ɗakinta.

Tura ƙofa yayi ya shiga, kallon gado yayi tana cikin bargo, ya kalli na'urar sanyaya ɗaki dake ƴar ƙara ya nufi bakin gadon yana harɗe hannuwa a ƙirji tare da mamakin yadda har tayi bacci.

Gani yayi tana rawar sanyi, ya matsa gaban gadon sosai tare da faɗin "Gimbiya."

Shiru tayi tare da saka  bargo ta ƙara rufe kunnuwanta haushin muryar take ji, cikin mamaki ya taka gadon kaɗan, ya saka hannu yana buɗe fuskar ta, cikin sauri ta kawar da kanta ɗayan gefen zata mayar da bargon ya riƙo hannunta.

Zaro ido yayi jin yadda jikinta yayi zafi sosai, da sauri ya hau gadon ya na faɗin "Jikin ki da zafi lafiya kuwa?"

Ya yaye bargon ya kalli fuskarta Innalillahi ya fara karantawa ganin yadda ta kumbura, ga kuka da take yi har lokacin "Baki da lafiya ne?"

Ya kai hannun shi ga wuyanta, ya ɗagota ya ɗan janye mayafin data naɗa tun lokacin da zasu fita.

"Yanzu baki da lafiya irin haka ba zaki sanar ba Haba Aymana."

Ya mayar da ita ya sauko yaje ya kashe na'urar data saka ɗakin yin sanyi, ya dawo yaɗagota "Me ke damun ki?"

Sam ji tayi ma bata son ganinshi, ta fashe da kuka, tana kwantawa sosai jikinshi saboda jikinta babu kwari.

Ya ƙara matseta sosai ya saka hannu yana share mata hawayen "Yi shiru bari na kira azo a duba ki."

Aymana ta kaɗa kai, tana riƙo hannunshi da yake danna waya, ya gane nufinta kar ya kira "To haka zaki zauna, bazan lamunta ba." Ya faɗa cikin damuwa, janye jikinta tayi ta koma kan gadon sosai "Kar ka kira, ka bani magani kawai a cikin lokar can."

Tayi maganar cikin rawar murya, Sultan ya miƙe da sauri ya duba, yana nuna mata wanda take nufi, ya kawo mata, ya koma kan ƙaramin firij ya ɗauko robar ruwa da taimakon shi tasha.

"Kin ci abinci."

Kaɗa kai tayi, ya sauke ajiyar zuciya, ta kwanta tana rufe idanuwanta "Sannu." Yace Aymana tayi shiru kawai, shi kuwa gani yake zafin ciwon ne.

Ya ɗauki bargon yana rufa mata, ya sauko daga gadon ya fice, Aymana ta lallaɓa ta miƙe ta samu ta sauya kaya zuwa goduwar rigar bacci ta mata launin fure, rigar tana da wani raga-raga a gaba, sai siririn hannu, iyakar rigar guiwa, ta ɗauki wata hular bacci ta saka ta koma ta kwanta ta rufa, tana mai maida lumfashi da ƙarfi da ƙarfi.

Tsawon mintuna goma sha biyar Sultan ya turo ƙofa da kofi hannun shi, tsaftatacciyar madara ce a ciki, kan gadon ya zaune ya buɗe bargon.

Ya na faɗin "Tashi  ki sakawa cikin ki wani abu."

Shiru tayi mashi, ya sa hannu ya ɗagota tare da bin rigar jikinta da kallo, ya mannata jikin shi, ya kai kofin bakinta, tana son janye jikinta amma tana jin ta samu muhalli ta ɗan sha kaɗan ta janye bakinta.

Ya kuma maida mata "ki ƙara kinga fa baki da lafiya."

Ya faɗa yana ɗan jijjigata alamar rarrashi wasu hawayen baƙin ciki suka ƙara kwararowa ta ƙara kurɓa kaɗan ta janye jikinta, Sultan ya aza kofin saman lokar gefen gadon.

Ya saka hannuwan shi biyu ya gyara mata kwanciya sosai a jirjin shi, ya ja fulo ya jingina bayanshi, ya maida hannunan yana shafa bayanta.

Saukar hawayenta ke ƙara rikitashi, ya rufe idanuwanshi, sam baya son kuka, balle kuma kukan Aymana, kan shi ya aza saman kanta, ya kai hannunshi ya kuma share mata hawaye "Shi kenan ki daina kuka, ba na so."

Yayi maganar yana zame jikinshi, ya kwantar da ita tare da gyara tashi kwanciyar ta hanyar haɗe jikinsu, sosai yake jiyo zafin jikinta hakan yasa ya ƙara haɗe jikinsu, ya kai hannunshi yana shafa bayanta ahankali ahankali.

Aymana ta rufe idanuwanta ta Sultan ya kalleta ya ɗago ya ƙara taɓa wuyanta ya kai kanshi a kumatun ta, ya sumbaceta, cikin wani irin shauƙi dake fuzgar shi, sai da tsikar jikinta ya tashi.

Tayi ƙarfin halin gyara kwanciyarta ta hanyar juya mashi baya, hakan yasa hannun Sultan da yake shafa bayanta ya koma kan cikinta.

Haka ya ƙara shige mata sosai, ya cigaba da shafa cikinta kamar yadda yakewa bayanta.

Aymana jikinta ya ƙara mutuwa, Sultan kuwa yanajin wani yanayi yana ratsa shi, haka yake yawo da hannuwanshi yana shafa cikinta har zuwa kan dukiyar fulaninta, wani abu yake fuzgar shi, cikin kwarewa da lallaɓawa yake shafasu duka biyun.

Aymana ta ɗan sauya yanayi ta ɗauki ɗayan hannunta ta ɗora akan nashi hannun da yake shafa jikinta da shi ta na riƙe hannun.

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA BIYU. 32*


Riƙe hannunshi da tayi hakan ya sa shi tuna cewar bata da lafiya, nutsuwar shi ya nema, tsawon lokaci Aymana tana riƙe da hannun shi, har bacci ya kwashe ta, sai da ya sauke ajiyar zuciya ganin bacci ya ɗauke ta, ya ƙara gyara kwanciyar shi, ta hanyar ƙara haɗe jikin su, ya jima kafin shima baccin ya ɗauke shi.

Asuba nayi Sultan ya lallaɓa ya janye jikinshi, don tafiya masallaci, ba ya son tashinta, abinda bai sani ba Aymana tana jinshi, ta yi kamar bacci take, tana jin fitar shi ta miƙe ta shiga banɗaki tayi wanka ta fito tana gabatar da salla.

Kafin shigowar shi ta bar ɓangaren zuwa nata, ta jima tana zaune tama rasa abin yi sai tunane-tunane take, can wani tunani ya faɗa mata, ta miƙe ta  fara shirinta.

Sultan yana ɗakin shi, bayan ya tabbatar ta fita, shiri yake don fita fada.

Ƙarfe tara dai-dai Jakadiya ta fara maganganu da guɗa bayan taje dubo Ayda, ta samu labarin tana da ciki.

Kowa na gidan sai da ya shiga kaɗuwa, kafin kace me, gida murna ake kowa na gidan ya samu zancen cikin Ayda.

Aymana tana zaune ta miƙe tana son zuwa wajen Sultan a karo na biyu don taya shi murna.

Sultan ya tsinkayi maganganu dake wakana a gidan, hakan ya ɗaga hankalin shi, kan kujera ya koma ya zauna yana mai dafe kanshi, kenan Ayda ciki ne da ita.

Sai da ta buga ƙofa kafin ta shigo, ganin shi tayi dafe da kai ta yi murmushi "Allah ya ƙara tsawon kwana ga Sultan, Zan zo ace saƙon da aka sanar dani nice zan fara maka albishir."

Ɗagowa yayi ya kalli yadda Aymana ta durƙusa gaban shi, kallon shi take sosai tana son gane yanayin data tsinkaye shi, ganin tana nazari hakan yasa ya fara neman tattaro Izzar shi da mulkinshi.

Ya gyara zaman shi "Ina jinki."

Murmushi tayi "Allah ya taimaki Sultan, Sarki ɗaya tamkar da dubu, idan an bani dama ina da zance baki na."

"Ina jin ki!" Ya faɗa babu alamun fara'a sai Izza dake bibiyar jinin shi.

Aymana ta fahimce shi sosai, hakan ya sa ta fara neman ta ta Izzar tare da faɗin "Farin ciki zuciyar masoyan Sultan, Ina mai sanar dakai Gimbiya tana gab ƙara kawo mana Yaro."

Kuri yayi mata da ido, wai ita baisan kalar halinta ba, sam baison taya zai jawo farinciki ya nuna ba, murmushin yaƙe yayi "Wa ya sanar da ke?"

Ta ɗan sunkuya "Allah ya baka nasara!" Ta faɗa ba tare da ta bashi amsa ba.

Take zuwan su Ɗakin magani ya faɗo mashi, ya kalleta sosai tare da miƙewa "Allah ya riƙa mata!"

Ya faɗa Aymana ta kalle shi, ya gane tana da ko tambaya ya juyo da sauri "Gimbiya zata samu tukuici don sanar da Sultan ƙaruwar da za a samu a gidan shi."

Gyaran murya tayi "Na gode!" Sultan ya cigaba da kai kawon da baima san yana yi ba, Jakadiyya ta turo ƙofa, tana kwasar gaisuwa.

"Allah ya ja zamanin Sarki."

"Da buƙatar wani abu?" Ya tambaya, jiki babu kwari ganin yanayin Sultan tace "Allah ya maka tsawon rai, Abul yana gab samun ɗan uwa!"

Sultan ya juya ya nufi kujerar shi ya zauna, lokaci guda jakadiyya taga Sultan ya fara murmushin da babu shi a azuciyar shi.

"A bata kulawa da abinda ke cikinta."

"Saƙon taya murna daga mutanan cikin gida."

"Na amsa." Ya faɗa.

Miƙawa tayi tare da faɗin Na barku lafiya. Aymana ta miƙe tsaye tare da faɗin "Jakadiyya."

Chak Jakadiyya ta tsaya tare da juyowa tana rage tsayinta "Allah ya taimaki Gimbiya."

"Tukuicin ki yana zuwa gareki."

Murmushi tayi "Allah ya ja zamanin uwar gidan Sultan."

Ta fice, Aymana ta mayar da hankalinta wajen Sultan, ta jima ba ta yi magana ba, haka shima na shi ɓangaren, tana son shigar mashi da maganar bakinta amma kuma tana ɗan shakku a lokacin.

Cikin wani salo da yanayin da ta rasa gane kanta, ta matsa wajen shi tare da zama saman kujerar da yake, ta haɗa kafaɗun su, hannunta ta ɗora bayan shi tana shafa bayan a hankali, Sultan ya fara sauke ajiyar zuciya.

Ya juyo kaɗan yana ƙare mata kallo, a zuciyar shi yana tunanin miyasa cikin ba ajikinta ba, ya yi saurin kai hannu yana riƙo hannunta, ya fara murzawa cikin wani irin salo.

Ya ƙara matsewa jikinta yana haɗe jikinsu, fuskar shi yakai kan tata fuskar sumba ya yi mata a kumatu, kafin ya mayar da bakin shi akan nata cikin sauri da ƙwarewa ya kuma fara tsotsar laɓɓanta kafin ya zura hashen shi yana neman nata harshen.

Cikin rawar jiki Aymana ta ƙara riƙe shi, saboda yadda take jin ba zata iya jurar wannan salon na shi ba.

Hannuwanshi ya sa yana fara shafar dokin wuyanta yana saukowa har kafaɗarta, Aymana ta rufe idanuwanta tana mai ƙara riƙe shi, saboda wani shauƙi dake bibiyar tafikan ƙafafuwanta har saman kanta.

Mayar da hannuwanshi yayi yana matseta yana mayar da numfashi, Aymana ta ɗan janye fuskarta ta mayar ɗayan gefen, ta na jin yadda numfashin shi ke fita da sauri da sauri.

Anan ta samu tana ɗaga bakinta "Sultan yana shirin ƙara samun Magaji, Sai dai ina cikin damuwa."

Ɗago kanta yayi "Damuwa kuma Aymana?" Cikin muryar shi data fara sukuikuicewa.

"Akan Lafiyarka Sultan, Ina nemar mana mafita." Tayi maganar tana janye jikinta daga nashi, tare da nuna damuwa.

"Muna iya bakin ƙoƙarin mu, da aiwatar da Addu'o'i, ina son sanar dakai na shirya maka tafiya zuwa *SAUDIYYA* don neman lafiyarka da kuma ƙara kusanci ga ubangijinmu."

Ajiyar zuciya yayi yana nazarinta, Aymana ta gane yana da tambaya hakan yasa tace "Ina so ne Magajin ka da zai zo, ya samu mahaifinshi acikin mulki da kuma cikar Izza."

Hannuwanta ya kamo, tare da faɗin "Kalle ni Aymana."

Cikin sauri ta kalle shi, tana son fahimtar shi, sai taga ya lumshe idanuwanshi yana sakin murmushi.

Aymana ta miƙe takai mashi sumbata a hanci.

***
Tunda Ayda taji batun cikinta ba shiri ta baro ɗakin magani, dole sai ta fito ta zagaya mutanen gida, haka kuwa akayi ta fito tana cika tana batsewa, duk wata damuwa da take ji akan Abul ta kau, tunda gashi zata kuma kawo wani Magajin.

Lokacin da taje sashen su, bata taradda Waziri ba, Innar ta sanar da ita yana fada yana amsar taya murnar da ake mashi.

***

Iya maƙura hankalin Gimbiya Mai gado yakai ƙarshe wajan tashin, wannan lokacin kowa ya gane baƙin cikinta, ta kalli Yarima Saifu dake kai kawo tace "Lallai Waziri damu yake zance, don ance Ayda tana da wani cikin shine ya wulakantaka agaban mutane."

"Wallahi ya ci darajar bana so zance nayi mashi rashin kunya ya samu Mai martaba, da ko ance ya kalle ni ba zai kuma kallo na ba."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi ta ce "Bari tsohuwar Jakadiyya tazo, lallai ko Ayda ko cikin jikinta ko mu, sai an samu gwani a cikinmu."

***

Ya na durƙushe gefen Gimbiya Ummi da Mai martaba, Mai martaba yayi shiru bayan taya Sultan murnar samun Magaji da zai yi, Sultan ya ɗago ya kalli Mai martaba ya ce "Allah ya taimake ka, dama na zo da magana ne, ina son zanje saudiyya don yin Addu'o'i akan lafiya ta."

Kafin Mai martaba yayi magana Gimbiya Ummi tace "An ya Sultan zaka bar gidan nan a irin wannan lokacin?"

Mai martaba yayi gyaran murya ya kalli Gimbiya Ummi "Ko kayi magana da Aymana akan hakan?" Sanin Mai martaba ne Aymana tana taka muhimmiyar rawa wajan  nemar mashi mafita.

Murmushi Sultan Yayi "Allah ya ƙara tsawon Rai itace ma ta nemi nayi hakan."

Ajiyar zuciya yayi, ya kalli Gimbiya Ummi "Ai shikenan, Allah ya dawo dakai lafiya, Amma wani hanzarin ba guduba."

Kallon shi sukayi, hakan ya bashi damar ci gaba da magana "Lallai dole ka tafi da mata ɗaya cikin matanka."

Gimbiya Ummi ta ɗaga baki zatayi magana Mai martaba ya ɗan ɗaga mata hannu don suba Sultal damar yin magana "Baba ban kaiga shirya hakan ba." Ya faɗa yana mai duƙar dakai.

Mai martaba ya ce "Kaje ka fidda wacce zakayi tafiyar da ita, Sauka lafiya!"

"Na gode!"

Ya miƙe ya fice, Gimbiya Ummi ta kalli Mai martaba "Miye Ayda za ta je ta yi mishi banda rawar kai na banza, yarinyar da bata damu da lalurar shi ba."

Murmushi Mai martaba yayi "Ki bar su dai ki gani."

***

Ayda ce tsaye turakar Sultan, sai dai lokacin baya ciki, ta zauna kan kujera tana jiran shigowar shi, Aymana ta fara buga ƙofar kafin ta buɗe ta shiga.

Ganin Ayda zaune yasa ta ɗan danasanin shigowar har zata juya sai kuma ta fasa, Ayda ta ya mutse fuska ta kalli Aymana ta miƙe tsaye.

Ganin yanayin da Ayda take haka ya tabbatarwa Aymana akwai abinda take son faɗa. Bata ida tunanin ba taji tana faɗin "Har yanzu dai tufa na kariya ga matsiranta, wasu basa gajiya da shiga da fita a cikin turaka amma kuma ba sa yunƙuri mai sauti, Ga wani magajin wannan lokacin sai dai muce aniyar kowa ta bishi." Tayi maganar yana mai taɓe baki.

Aymana ta yi hanyar shiga ciki sam batayi niyar tanka mata ba, cak ta tsaya jin Ayda ta cigaba da magana "Ɗiyar Sarki, matar sarki, hakan kuma bai sa an iya amsar saƙo ta daidai ba, sai gashi ƴaƴan da ba sarautar a gidansu su suke haifar ƴaƴan Sarkin."

Juyowa Aymana tayi cikin ƙololuwar ɓacin rai ta tsaya ɗan nesa da Ayda "Kenan kinsan akwai banbanci tsakanin Mulki da talakawan da ake mulka? Maza ki gyara kalaman ki Ayda kar ki yadda fushin zuciya ya hau kanki."

Ta ƙarashe maganar tana yin hanyar ƙofar fita, don ta fasa shiga ciki, Ayda ta taɓe baki, tasa hannu ta shafi cikinta tana dariya, tare da faɗin "Duk baƙin cikin ki, sai kin ƙara ganin wani yaron nawa."

***

Bayan kwana biyu Aymana tana kishingiɗe a wani wajen zaman hutawa, wayar tace hannunta tana dannawa, Farida ta shigo farfajiyar da saurinta ta rusuna gabanta tare da gaida ta.

Aymana bata ɗagoba "Me ke faruwa?"

"Allah shi taimakeki, Mai martaba ne yake son ganawa dake."

Cikin sauri Aymana ta kalle ta  "Naga kamar lokacin tashin shi fada bai yi ba."

"Haka ne! Allah ya baki nasara."

Saurin miƙewa tayi, Farida ta sa hannu ta gyara mata takalminta Aymana ta zura ta fice Farida tana binta baya.

Yana tsaye a babban falon shi, Aymana ta shiga da sallama, ciki ciki ya amsa mata, ta ɗan ƙara matsawa har lokacin bai juyo ba.

Hakan ya sa tace "Allah ya taimake ka, Na amsa kira cikin gaggawa, ina mamaki kamar lokacin shigowarka bai yi ba."

Juyowa yayi cikin taƙama yace "Ina da muhimman abubuwan yi ne, hakan ya sani shigowa."

"Amma ina Uzairu yake?" Wato bawan da ke kula da shi a fada.

Shiru yayi bai bata amsa ba "Ki shirya tafiyar ki zuwa Saudiyya jibi, jirgin safe zamu bi." Yayi maganar ba tare da kallonta ba.

Aymana ta matsatso "Me hakan ke nufi?"

Ya nufi kujera tare da faɗin "Tafiyar da kika shiya mana ce."

Shiru na wani lokaci, wani sanyi ya ratsa zuciyar Aymana, ba zata iya musa mashi ba, ta matso gare shi.

"Ayda!" 

Sultan ya ɗago ya kalle ta, ta kauda idonta, Murmushi yayi tare da faɗin "Mu duka zamu je."

Aymana ta yi saurin dakewa, ta kawar da kanta "Allah ya nuna mana."

Ta juya cikin sauri tana nufar ɓangaren ta, da tsantsar tunane tunane, yadda za a yi wannan haɗin tsakaninta da Ayda, take ta fara tunanin komawa don sanar da shi, ita zata zauna gida don ta kula da komai.

***

Washe gari mutanen gidan kowa ya san da tafiyar Sultan  zuwa ƙasa mai tsarki, ɓangarorin Yarima Saifu murna suke sun san kafin dawowar shi zasu ɗanɗani romon dake cikin mulkin shi.

Waziri kuwa ya riga yasan Yanzu gari na shi ne idan har Sultan ya tafi, tunda shi za a barwa riƙon gari kafin dawowar Sultan.

***

Ranar daddare Sultan Yana durƙushe gaban Gimbiya Ummi sai lokacin yake son sanar da ita ya yanke shawarar da Aymana zai yi tafiyar.

Ita kuwa Aymana ta gama shiri don zuwa sheda mashi tana neman alfarma yabarta tayi zamanta, don sam bata son abinda zai danganta ta da Ayda, lokacin da taje ake shaida mata yana sashen Gimbiya Ummi.

Aymana ta yi ajiyar zuciya, ta san idan tayi maganar gaban Gimbiya Ummi to dolen shi ya amince.

Sallama tayi tare da shiga, ta nufe su tana zubewa gaban Gimbiya Ummi daga ɗayan ɓangaren da Sultan yake.

"Barka da hutawa Ranki shi daɗe."

"Yauwa Aymana, ki na Lafiya."

Aymana ta juya ga Sultan "Allah ya baka nasara."

Sai lokacin ta kula da yadda ya kafeta da idanuwa, kai ya ɗaga mata, Ya juya kan Gimbiya Ummi dake faɗin "Ina jinka Sultan."

"Akan tafiyar mu ne, sai yanzu na samu damar sanar da Mai martaba gobe ne tafiyar."

"Allah ya dawo daku lafiya."

Yayi ajiyar zuciya tare da faɗin "Sannan kuma bisa duba da nayi na ƙaramin cikin dake jikin Ayda, ganin yadda take jin jiki a kwanakin nan, hakan ya sa na yanke shawarar zan tafi da Aymana ne..."

Kafin ya ida ta kalle shi cikin sauri, tare da sauke ajiyar zuciya, cikin taimakon Allah babu wanda ya ji ta.

Gimbiya Ummi tace "To Madalla! Allah ya baku iko, ya kuma baku nasara akan abinda kukaje nema, Allah ya dawo mana daku Lafiya."

Da sauri Aymana ta ƙara matsawa gaban Gimbiya Ummi tana ƙara sunkuyawa alamar girmamawa tare da faɗin "Mun gode!"

Sultan ya matsa kaɗan tare da faɗin "Ameen."

Gimbiya Ummi ta dafa kafaɗar Aymana, sosai take jin son yarinyar, ganin yadda take tagazawa Sultan, aranta tana so ace Aymana ce da ciki, ji take kamar ta basu shawarar yo addu'a ga Aymana don itama ta samu nata Magajin, amma saboda dattako irin na Gimbiya Ummi ta kasa furta hakan.

***

Gidan ya gama kacamewa da hayaniyar tafiyar Mai martaba da Aymana, Mama ta shigo da saurinta wajen Gimbiya Aymana tana dariya tare da faɗin "Kai kina nan zaune ina can ina kallon dirama a gidan Waziri."

Aymana ta miƙawa Farida wata riga data ɗauko, tare da faɗin "Za ki iya bamu waje Farida!"

Farida ta rufe akwatin matafiya da take haɗawa Aymana kaya ta sunkuya tare da faɗin "Na barku lafiya."

Aymana ta kalli Mama tana dariya "Ina jinki!"

 "Ayda  kuka harda turje-turje wai Sultan yana nuna banbanci a tsakanin ku."

Dariya Aymana tayi "Allah wadan naka ya lalace."

Itama Mama dariyar tayi "Kin ganni harda shiga bada haƙuri, a zuciyata nace dam ta ɓarar da cikin garin hauka."

Aymana ta yi Murmushi "Ai babu kyau fatar mugun abu ga bawa."

Mama tace "Haka ne Aymana, yanzu dai kowa ya ƙara tantance darajar ki a gidan nan."

Wata dariya tayi "Haba Mama don Allah kibar zugani,  ai..."

"Aymana wai bakya ganin tsantsar soyayyar ki ga Sultan?"

Aymana bata yi magana ba Mama tace "To kema kiyo addu'a, muna son ganin Magaji daga wajen ki Aymana."

"Hmm." Kawai Aymana ta faɗa.

***

Ayda tana baro ɓangaren Waziri tayi turakar Sultan, yana tsaye tare da Uzairu, wasu kayane jibge a falon Uzairu yana haɗawa.

Ayda babu ko sallama, ganin Uzairu yasa ta dakatawa, Uzairu ya gaida ita, sai dai bata da sukunin amsawa.

Uzairu ya yi hanyar fita, Sultan ya koma ya na neman kujera ya zauna tare da bin Ayda da kallo, yana son ɗan kwantar mata da hankali ganin koba komai tana da hakkin akan shi.

"Ko Gimbiya na da buƙatar wani abu." Ya faɗa tare da ɗan faɗaɗa murmushi.

Wani kallo tayi mashi, wanda ba zaka ɗauke shi harara ba saboda tasan bata isa kallon tsabar fuskar Sultan ta harareshi ba.

"Dama kace haka man, har zaune zaka bar nuna wannan banbancin? Don Aymana ta fito daga gidan sarauta ko me? Don gidansu yana babbar masarauta ai bai fi masarautaka ba da zaka yi tsoron..."

Cikin hanzari Sultan ya miƙe tsaye, yanayin maganarta ya zaburar da zuciyar shi hannu ya ɗaga mata "Dakata!"

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA UKKU. 33*

SADAUKARWA GA:
_Rahama Niger tare da Ummi Zariya._


Cikin jin tsoron tsawar da Sultan yayi Ayda ta ja baya, ya gane ta tsorata ne hakan ya sa shi kasa ida magana, sam bai san ta yaya zai ɓullowa Ayda ta gane rayuwa ba, a ganin shi rawar kanta ya yi yawan da har take wuce muhallinta.

Ƙofa ya nuna mata tare da rufe idanuwanshi, cikin tsanannin ɓacin rai, jiki babu kwari ta fice, cikin takaicin kalar wulaƙanci da Sultan yake mata aduk lokacin da tazo mi shi da zance.

Ajiyar zuciya ya sauke tare da koma wa ya zauna samar kujera yana kawar da ɓacin ranshi.

***
Washe gari tun safe suka gama shirin su, mutanen gida kowa ya fito don ganin tafiyar Sultan.

Aymana ta fito daga ɓangaren ta, tare da kuyanginta, sai dai a babbar ƙofar falon shi suka barta, ta tura ƙofar tana mai gyara Alƙebbar ta.

Fitowa yake daga sashen ɗakunan shi, cikin wasu kayan Sarauta da suka amshe shi, ya rike wata sanda a hannun shi, yana ɗan azata ƙasa cikin tafiyar Sarauta.

Aymana ta ja ta tsaya sam bai ganta ba, saboda wani maɓallin Alƙebba da ya ɗan cire, ji yayi ya kaiwa mutum karo, cikin sauri ya ɗago yana kallon ta.

Aymana ta yi Murmushi tare da faɗin "Barka da fitowa ."

"Yauwa" ya faɗa yana ƙoƙarin gyara maɓallin, Aymana tayi saurin saka hannu tare da faɗin "Ko zan iya taimakawa Sultan."

Bar mata yayi tare da maida hankalin shi akan shigarta, ta burgeshi sosai yanayinta yayi kamar Sarauniyya dake jagorantar nahiya mai girma.

Ɗagowa tayi daidai lokacin da ta gama gyara mashi, Sultan ya yi murmushi kamar yadda ya gani a fuskarta.

"Ana jiran fitar Sultan."

"Sultan yana son keɓewa da matar shi." Yayi maganar yana mai ƙara tako zuwa gareta, Aymana ta ƙara shaƙar ƙamshin shi, tasa hannu tana dafa kafaɗar shi, cikin sauri Sultan ya sunkuya yana riƙota "Adon sarauta yana maki kyau Aymana"

"Ba kamar Yadda yake wa sarkin ba."

Ji tayi ya manne jikinsu, tare da sumbatarta a kumatu, cikin sauri ta matsa tare da faɗin "Kar ganin ruwa yaga Sultan."

Murmushi yayi yana tako zuwa fita, Aymana ta take mashi baya suna ficewa, haka suka samu ana ta jiran fitowarsu.

A bakin ƙofa suka haɗu da Ayda, don dolenta ta fito rakiyarshi tana gudun abinda zai ce ya dawo.

Sultan ya cigaba da tafiya suna binshi, a bakin farfajiyar cikin gidan duk matan gidan sunfito, iyayen su da sauran ahalin gidan.

Hannu ya rinƙa dagawa yana fitar da Murmushi, Gimbiya Ummi ta na tsaye ƙofar sashenta, wajan ta suka nufa, suka sunkuya, tare da kwasar Gaisuwa.

Ta kallesu bata nuna wani abu a fuskarta ba saboda matan gidan dake wajan.

Sultan ya matsa wajen sashen Gimbiya Mai gado ya sunya mata. Kafin ya juyo yayo hanyar fita.

Sai lokacin Aymana ta iso wajen shi, waigawa yayi sai yaga Ayda can nesa har ta tsaya.

Hakan yasa ya gyara tsayuwarshi tare da kallonta, kowa ya juya yana kallonta, kai Sultan ya ɗaga mata cikin salon da baya so a gane bai yi niyar zuwa da ita ba.

Ayda ta gane kamar kiranta yake, ta ɗaga ƙafa ta isa wajen, Sultan ya ƙara matsowa gab da ita "Zamu tafi ki kula da abinda ke cikin ki."

Kallon cikinta tayi, hakan yasa kowa na wajan yaɗan fahimta, take aka fara faɗin "Allah ya baka nasara, sauka lafiya."

Murmushi ya ƙarayiwa Ayda, ko ba komai dai ya nuna yana son abin da ke jikinta hakan ya sata jin daɗi, ta saki fuska.

Aymana tayi saurin zuwa ta dafa kafaɗarta "Magajin Sultan yana son kulawar ki."

Tayi maganar cikin salo, Ayda ta kalleta zata harareta sai kuma taga Aymana ɗauke da murmushi, ta juya kawai abinta, Haka su Sultan suka fice tare da ƴan rakiyarsu zuwa filin jirgi.

***

Isarsu ƙasa mai tsarki Madina. motoci sosai suka zo kwasar su da kayansu, Aymana bata yi mamakin hakan ba kasancewar tasan Sultan Sarkine da za a sanar da zuwan shi ga mahukuntan ƙasar.
 
Babban masaukin baƙi na MADINA HILTON aka nufa dasu, masaukin baƙi ne da ya  kan amshi baƙuncin manya-manyan mutane tare da masu ji da kansu.

Aymana tana gefen Sultan wanda a lokacin sun shiga tsakiyar askarawan dake tsaron lafiyar su, wanda a lokacin sun zagaye Masaukin bakin babu shiga ba fita, har sai Sultan ya isa ɗakin shi da iyalin shi.

Ɓangare ne  mai ɗauke da babban falo, sai wajan cin abinci daga gefe, da kuma banɗaki, sai gerin ɗakuna guda biyu a cikin wani korido, kowanne ɗaki yana ɗauke da ban ɗaki da kuma gado.  

Falo suka fara tsayawa suna sakin Ajiyar zuciya, Aymana ta kalleshi tana mai fitar da Alkebbarta ta aza akan kujera tare da Hamdala ga ubangijin ta.

Tun lokacin da Sultan ya isa ƙasar ya ke jin kwanciyar hankali na ratsa shi, Aymana ta zauna kan kujera, Sultan ya fara rage kayan jikinshi, saboda gajiyar da ke tare dashi.

Yana cire babbar Giga ya zauna tare da kallon Aymana "Ko akwai gajiya tare da Gimbiya."

Murmushi tayi tare da faɗin "Ba sosai ba." 

"Zamu ci abinci mu huta kafin..."

"Bana jin zan iya hutawa, ba tare da na samu hanyar ganawa da Sheikh Mansur ba." 

Wani babban Malamin Islama dake a ƙasar Saudiya, Sheikh yayi fice sosai wajan bada magungunan Addinin musulunci da kuma fannin waraka akan sihiri.

Cikin mamaki ya kalle ta "Sheikh Mansur kuma?" Don yasan shi da kuma matsayin shi.

Murmushi tayi tare da faɗin "Dama tafiyar don mu samu taimako ne a wajensa, nasan InashaAllah idan mun sanar dashi masalolinka zai..."

"Amma mai yasa baki sanar dani tun wuri na nemi son ganawa da shi ba?"

Ajiyar zuciya tayi ta miƙe ta dawo kan kujerar da yake ta riƙo hannunshi "Akwai wata ƙawata Ruƙayya, munyi karatun likitanci da ita, tana zaune da mujinta anan, har na gama magana da ita, mijinta yana da alaƙa mai ƙarfi da Sheikh Mansur, shi ne zai kaimu don ganawa da shi."

Wani irin kallo Sultan yake wa Aymana, ita dai damuwarta akan lalurarsa ne,   kenan bata da wani burin da ya wuce taga ya samu lafiya.

Hannunta ya matse sosai, wannan lokacin wani soyayyarta yake ƙara dirar ma sa wadda bai taɓa jin kalarta ba, wani yanayi ya fara shigar shi.

A hankali ya janyota jikinshi "Na gode!" Ya faɗa tare da matseta sosai suna jiyo bugawar zuciyar junansu, ya sa hannu yana shafata har kanta, hakan yasa ɗankwalinta ya zame, Sultan ya mayar da hannuwanshi akan lallausan gashin kanta yana shafawa cikin wani irin shuƙi dake fuzgar shi.

Ya maido hannuwanshi akan dokin wuyanta tare da mayar da tsinin hancinshi yana wasa da laɓɓanta, kafin ya canza salon shi ta aika mata da zazzafar sumba yana mai farawa da tsotse labbanta.

Aymana ta fara diriricewa tana saka hannunta akan kunnuwanshi tana murzawa tare da wasa dasu cikin wani irin salo, hakan ya ƙara rikita Sultan.

Ya kasa riƙe kanshi, janta yayi suka faɗa kan kujerar Sultan ya saka hannuwanshi bayanta yana zuge Zip ɗin rigarta, tare da saurin yin ƙasa da rigar, surar jikin Aymana ta bayyana sosai ta ɗan ƙame jikinta ya saka hannu yana ɓalle bireziyar jikinta.

Cikin salo ya mirginata kan kujerar tare da yin wurgi da bireziyar, ya fara shafata zuwa cikinta, har lokacin bakinsu a haɗe yake, ya mayar da hanuwanshi duka biyun a kan dukiyar fulaninta ya fara murzawa cikin wani irin salo.

Aymana ta ƙara riƙe shi tana ɗan zuzzullewa, ya janye harshenshi yana dawo dashi kan jikinta, ya fara sarrafa harshen tun daga wuyan shi har kan dukiyar fulanin.

Dakewa tayi jin tana niyar sakin ƴar ƙara, Sultan ya ƙara diririce sosai, jin yanayin da laushi da santsin jikinta, Yana fara lalubarta, Aymana tayi ƙarfin halin janyewa tana matse jikinta alamar bataso ya ganta.

Rungume juna sukai suna mayar da numfashi, da kyal ta iya janye jiki tana shigewa ɗakin don tsarkake jikinta, haka shima nashi ɓangaren.

***
Da daddare Aymana ta shiga ɗakin da ya zama shine na shi, ita kuma zata zauna a ɗakin dake kallon na shi, Shiga tayi da rigar baccinta iya guiwa, sigar jikin ta ta bayyana sosai. hannunta riƙe da kofin shayi da aka kawo musu.

Yana zaune lokacin ya gama saka wasu kayan bacci launin ruwan ƙasa da takalmansu, ya ɗauki turare ya fesa.

Aymana ta Aje kofin shayin, ta zauna bakin gadon "Ina tare da gajiya."

Ya juyo ya aje matajin daya gyara sagen shi, ya zo ya zauna ya ɗauki shayin ya kurɓa "Kina buƙatar wani abu."

Kallon shi tayi "Nayi magana da Ruƙayya tace gobe zasu zo ɗaukarmu mu je wajan Shaikh."

"Da sauri haka Aymana, nayi tunanin zamu bari sai mun gama Ummara, sannan muje akan maganar."

Miƙewa tayi ta nufi rawanin shi daya aje ta buɗe ma'ajiyar kaya tana ajewa "A'a hakan ba dabara bane, mu fara ganin shi, Sai mu yi Ummara, muna ibadunmu haka kuma kana amfani da shawarwari da kuma magungunan da ya bamu."

Ta saka rawawin ta dawo ta zauna Sultan yana Binta da kallo dan yanayin shigar da tayi. Ta ce "Hakan zai bamu dabar tabbatar da yanayin jikinka kafin mu koma gida."

"Shi kenan zamuyi kamar yadda kika ce."

"Na gode! Allah ya baka nasara."

Sun jima suna zaune kaɗan kadan sukan jefo fira a tsakaninsu, kafin Aymana tayi bankwana da shi ta tafi makwancinta.

Washe gari suka samu baƙuncin Ruƙayya da mujinta,  sun ji daɗin ganinsu sosai, atare sukaje don ganin Sheikh Mansur, sosai suka samu ƙarɓuwa a wajen shi, saboda alaƙar dake tsakaninshi da Mijin ruƙayya.

Sun faɗa mashi komai game da ciwon Sultan hakan bai zamar mashi abu mai wahala ba, tun a lokacin ya fara ɗora shi akan magunguna da kuma Addu'o'in don gabatarwa.

Suna dawowa Aymana bata zauna ba, ta fara haɗa mashi magunguna. Ya fara amfani dasu.

Washe gari suka fara gabatar da ibadan su da zasu gabatar a Madina, sun samu kwanciyar hankali sosai, don Sultan ya manta da duk wani rikicin kanshi, Aymana kuwa hankalinta ya karkata akan Addu'o'i ga mijinta da neman ɗaukakar shi.

Sunyi ziyarar ibadun  Madina, Sunje wajan dutsen Uhud, sun ziyarci masallacin Quba sun gabatar da salla raka'a biyu,  wadda falallarta tana da girma sosai, tare da Addu'o'i sosai, sun ziyarci maƙabartar da aka rufe matan Annabi (s.a.w) tare da ma sauran salihan bayi. 

Sun yi hotuna sosai da Sultan kala-kala a duk wajajen da sukaje.

Lokacin da suka samu kammala ibadun sune. Aymana ta shirya don zuwa MAZAIA MALL acan tayi sayyya sosai, ganin cewar idan sun bar Madina ko zasu dawo ba zata samu bin shaguna don sayyya ba, haka yasa Ruƙayya ta kuma rakata banban wajan sayayya mai suna  TAIBA ARAQ saiP dai babu nisa zuwa MADINA HILTON da suka sauka. Anan tayi sayayyawa mutanen gidan sosai.

***

Sun gabatar da kwanakin su, kafin suka wuce  Makka, don yin Ummara, sun samu masauki a  JABAL OMAR HILTON SUIT, kusan zan iya cewa shine babban masaukin baƙi da sai wanda ya amsa sunan sa yake yada zango a can. 

 Kullum Aymana cikin tambayar Sultan yanayi ko halin da yake jin jikinshi take, Alhamdulillah yana kwantar mata da hankali ganin ta damu, haka kuma yana jin nutsuwa a tare dashi, ya fara rage duk wata fargaba da yake ji.

A Makka ma Aymana ta je manyan kasuwanninsu, wannan lokacin Sultan da kanshi ya bata kuɗaɗe don yin sayya, a kasuwar SHARA MANSOOR da kuma CITY MALL tayi sayayya, wannan lokacin tafi mayar da hankali akan sayyyar kayanta da na Sultan ɗin ta.

***

Ranar da za su tafi Jedda, acan ne suke son shaƙatawa na wasu kwanaki tunda sun kammala ibadunsu.

Yana tsaye yana waya akan Masaukin baƙin da yake so a kama musu Aymana ta matso tasa hannunta tana kauda wayar daga kunnan shi tace "Na fison Hilton."

Take ya bada Umarnin sauyawa zuwa zaɓinta, yana gama yawar ya juyo ya kalleta "Me yasa kike son Hilton, bayan anan ..."

"Saboda yana kusa da kogin Maliya, ina son shaƙatawa a wajen."

Sultan ya ɗan yi murmushi "Hakane a Jedda Hilton Hotel ɗin su kana hango ruwan maliya."

Aymana ta ɗaga kai "Hakane Mai martaba."

Hannu yasa ya lakaci hancinta don ta bashi dariya ganin kwana biyu ba a kirashi da Mai martaba ba.
