*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA HUƊU. 34*


Ta riƙe hannunshi suna zama kan kujera, binta yayi da ido sosai kyawun jikinta ya ƙara fitowa hasken fatarta ya ƙara bayyana, jikinta ya ƙara laushi, ta ƙara mulmulewa abinta, hakan yasa ya tabbatar ƙasar ta amshe ta.

Ana zuwa ɗaukar su suka nufi Jedda tun a hanyar zuwa masauki Aymana take kallon yana yin garin ta gilashin mota.

Sultan yasa hannu yana riƙo hannunta, Aymana ta kalle shi tana riƙe nashi hannun itama, ko wanne da abunda yake saƙawa a ranshi.

Daga zuwansu wanka sukayi, tare da cin Abinci, Marece nayi Sultan yana shirin zama don hutawa Aymana ta hana shi don dole ya tashi suka fice.

*Dhaban marine park* suka nufa, wani babban wajan shaƙatawa wajen yana da kyau sosai, akwai ɓangaren wasanni da kuma wajan wasan yara, sosai Sultan ya maida hankali wajan kallon motocin wasan yara da kuma   yadda iska yake sanyaya wajen.

Aymana ta ja hannun shi zuwa wajan wata kujera, suka zauna, Sultan ya kalleta "Sam wajen nan yafi dacewa da suwa da yara, kasancewar komai na wajen don jin daɗin yara ne."

Murmushi Aymana tayi, ta maida kanta akan kafaɗar shi tare da saka wani abin motsa baki tana sha "Hakan yana nufin wata rana Sultan zai so da Yaran shi."

Hannu yasa yana shafa kafaɗarta, sai dai baiyi magana ba, haka sukayi hotuna sosai.

Washe gari a *Masjid Al Rahama* sukayi sallar la'asar, Masallaci ne da ke tsakiyar  wani kogi wanda wajan yana da sanyi da kuma daɗin zama.

Gewayawa suka yi wajan ruwan bayan sun fito daga masallacin. Aymana ta tsugunna tana saka hannuwanta a cikin ruwan, Sultan ya kalli yadda rigarta take shiga ruwan ya duƙa tare da saka hannu yana fitar mata "Kin ga zaki jiƙa kayan ki."

Ɗagowa tayi tana kallon shi taɗebo ruwan sosai tana watsa mashi tana dariya, Sultan ya kalli yadda ta jiƙa mashi kaya yace "Ni kika yiwa Haka ko."

Yana maganar yana ɗibar ruwan Aymana ta miƙe tana ɗan gudunta Sultan ya bita baya, Sai dai lokacin da ya kamata ruwan da ya ɗiba a hannun shi sun zube.

Dariya tayi mashi, Sultan ya harareta iska yana ƙaɗa mayafin dake jikinta har gashin kanta yana fitowa.

Hannu yasa yana gyara mata gashin tare da rungumeta "Yauwa yanzu ne dai-dai lokacin da zan rama."

Numfashi take saukewa sosai "Allah ka barni, ko gudun da ka saka ni ai ka ram..."

Kafin ta ida Sultan ya haɗe bakinsu, yana harɗe hannuwanshi bayanta, gaba ɗaya ya kashe musu jiki, ta saka hannunta tana riƙe shi jin kamar ƙafafun ta ba zasu iya ɗaukarta ba.

Sai da suka kwana biyu suna yawon shakatawa a Jedda. Yanzu ma shiri take yi sosai lokacin marece yayi lis, samun shi tayi falo zaune da wasu kaya marasa nauri, wandon iyakar shi guiwa, sumar kanshi tasha gyara sosai.

Aymana ta zauna tare da shafa sumar ta ce "Allah ya baka nasara, na ga baka shirya ba."

Maido hankalin shi yayi akanta, doguwar riga ce mara nauri, tana da maɗauri a tsakiya, sai wani siririn mayafi data ɗora, ta mashi kyau  sosai "Ki canza kaya dai, ba zanje dake a haka ba."

"Au ni na fita da kai jiya da wando iyakar shi ƙasan guiwa."

Dariya yayi ya kama hannunta suna miƙewa "Yau ina so mu huta a gida."

Hanyar ɗakin shi suka nufa Aymana ta cire mayafin ta ajiye, Sultan ya faɗa kan gado "Ki min tausa."

"Allah shi taimakeka ina jin bacci ne fa."

Dariya yayi ya tashi yaune "Don na hana fita shine ba za a min ba."

Yayi maganar yana miƙe mata hannu "zo mu kwanta." Faɗawa tayi jikin shi tayi lamo kowannansu babu wanda yake motsi.

Ranar haka suka wuni a gida daddare suka ci abinci, Sultan ya miƙe ya shiga ciki yayi wanka lokacin da Aymana ya gama saka kayan baccin shi.

Bata mishi magana ba, ta matso tana kama hannun shi tare da gyara mashi maɓallin da yake ƙoƙarin sakawa.

Tana gamawa ta juya ta shiga ɓanɗakin, ya jima yana jiranta, zuwa can ya ji motsin ruwa alamar yana wanka ne.

Tsawon lokaci ta fito ɗaure da towel iyakar shi rabin cinyarta, hannun ta rike da  ƙaramin towel tana tsane jikinta.

Zama tayi bakin mudubu ta na gyara kanta kafin ta fara shafa turaruka.

Sultan yana zaune kan gado ya jingina, ƙafafuwan shi a miƙe, bayanta yake kallo yadda take shafa man gashi tana rirriƙe towel ɗin don bata so ya faɗi, sai da ta gama amfani da duk abubuwan muƙata kafin ta miƙe ta buɗe wata jaka cikin jakunkunan da ta zuba sabin kayan ta.

Wata rigar bacci ta ɗauko launin ruwan madara mai santsi, ta fara sakawa tare da janye towel ɗin ta zauna bakin gadon ɗan nesa dashi.

Ƙoƙarin gyara rigar take kasancewar rigar bayanta babu komai sai wasu zaruruwa da ake ɗaurewa.

Kallon gadon bayanta yake  yana kallon yadda take ƙiƙiniyar gyarawa amma ta kasa.

Ta miƙe tsaye, rigar iyakarta cinya, ta nufe shi tana zama kusa da shi tare da juya bayanta.

Ya gane me take nufi sai dai baya iya ko motsawa saboda yadda kayan jikinta suka kashe mashi jiki.

Juyowa tayi tare da fadin "Kana kallo  na fa."

Murmushi yayi a hankali yakai hannuwanshi akan bayanta, atunanun Aymana saren zai ɗaura mata.

Ji tayi ya zura hannuwanshi ta gaba ya tallabo dukiyar fulaninta, ya na cika hannuwanshi tare da mummurzawa, Aymana ta ɗan gantsare tana tallabe hannuwan nashi.

Sultan ya fara diriricewa, Ya jawo ta sosai jikinshi yana juyo da ita, cikin wani irin salo.

Ɗaga baki tayi zatayi magana Sultan ya haɗe bakinsu, Aymana tana jiyo yadda yake tsotsar harshen ta kamar alewar da tayi mashi zaƙi, cikin sauri da rikicewar jiki Aymana ta riƙe Sultan tana fara mayar mashi da nata salon.

Hannuwanshi ya ɗora saman kafaɗarta yana yin ƙasa da rigarta zuwa cibinta, ya mayar da kanshi akan dukiyar fulanin guda yana murza ɗayan da hannunshi guda.

Aymana ta maƙalƙale jikinta cikin nashi tana wani numfashi, ta mayar da bakinta akan kunnashi tana hurawa kafin ta zura harshenta.

Sultan ya yi ƙara rikicewa yana sauke numfashi, ya mayar da hannuwanshi kan cikinta, yana mai janye kanshi ya fara tsotsar cikiyarta, ya fara ƙoƙarin ƙara yin ƙasa da rigarta, yana mai shafa ƙasan mararta.

Cikin wani irin yanayi yake jin santsi a hannunshi, dabarbarcewa yayi tare da ƙara shafawa.

 Aymana tunda take bata taɓa jin wannan yanayin ba, haka kuma koda Sultan yake shafar jikinta bai taɓa zuwa babbar majalissar ba.

Gaba ɗaya Sultan ya fara ficewa hankalinshi, kam tunanin shi baya jikinshi, abinda ya fara zo mishi yau jikin Aymana ne yake jin wannan yanayin, abinda ya jima yana son ji.

Cikin kwarewa da muguwar sha'awar kasancewa tare da ita, ya fara sarrafata yana mai fara janye kayan jikinshi, musallan wandon shi da Hajiya Babba take neman fasawa ta fito.

Sam Aymana bata kawowa ranta komai ba, sada taji Sultan ya kawar da kayan shi tare da rungumar ta, yana mata wani irin salo da hura mata iska.

Hannunshi ya fara shafa bayanta, yana ɗaga ƙafarta, ya kai hannunshi yana lalubar Hajiya Babba tare da nema mata muhalli.

Sai lokacin Aymana ta fara zuzzullewa, tana ƙaƙarin haɗe ƙafarta Amma sam Sultan baya ma jinta.

Can sama sama yake jiyo yadda take ƙoƙarin hana shi, a ƙasa maƙoshi ya fara faɗin "Please Aymana you're my..."

Ya kasa ƙarasawa yana mai neman majalissar da yake buƙata, a bayyane ya fara karanto Addu'ar saduwa da iyali, ji tayi yana ƙoƙarin shirgarta, ta yi wata irin ƙara tana zullewa, Sultan ya gama da riƙeta gam ta yadda ba zata taɓa kubuce mashi ba.

Ganin da gaske yake hakan yasa ta fasa kuka dai dai lokacin da wani yanayi ya shigeta, jin yadda Sultan yake aika jikinshi cikin nata cikin salon iya sarrafawa, amma sam Aymana bata gane hakan ba, zai zafi da kukan da ta fara sakar mashi.

Cikin duniyar daɗin shi yake jinta, amma baya iya hana kanshi, sai Numfashi shi da yake canza salo yana fita da ƙarfi da ƙarfi.

Roƙonshi Aymana ta farayi, tsawon lokaci ta fara rasa karfinta, jikinta ya gama mutuwa kuka shaɓe-shaɓe take yi, gaba ɗaya jikinta ya saki, ta yi lamo sai hawayen azaba dake gangarowa wani yana korar wani.

Wani hanzari ya ƙara shigar shi ganin shi ne yake sarrafa ta, Sultan ya daɗe bai iya samo kanshi ba, wani abu ke bin jijiyoyinshi don daɗi.

Sai da yaji ya na zuba kafin ya ɗagota yana yin ahankali-ahankali har Numfashin shi ya sauka.

Kan gadon ya faɗa yana mai murgina ta jikinshi, ya na sauke nannauyar Ajiyar zuciya tare da ƙara maƙalƙaleta, wata ƙaunarta ce ta ƙara ziyartar shi, karon farko daya tara da Aymana kwanciyar hankalin yake ji, wasu hawaye yake jin suna fitowa daga idanunshi.

Sai lokacin ya tuna da kukan da ya jiyo tana yi, cikin sauri ya ɗagota yana mai kallon fuskarta.

Sai dai idanuwanta a rufe kuka kawai take, cikin hanzari ya goge nashi hawayen yana mai kallonta ya kuma azata jikin shi tare da rungubeta sosai, yana bubbuga bayanta ahankali ahankali.

Sun shima a haka kafin Aymana tayi shiru, sai lumfashi da take saukewa, jin hakan yasa ya janyeta daga jikinshi tare da janyo filo ya ɗora ta akai.

Banɗaki ya shiga cikin hanzari ya fara haɗa mata ruwan ɗumi, kafin ya dawo ya saka hannu cak ya ɗaga ta akan kafaɗun shi, sam baya son abinda zai wahalar da ita.

Ajiyeta yayi Aymana ta maƙale jikinta, Sultan ya kashe ruwan saboda kwamin daya cika, ya taɓa ruwan yana ƙoƙarin sakata Aymana ta maƙale kafaɗa "Bana so, Bana so."

Bayanta ya shafa yana lallashinta, ya yi hanzarin fara sakata aruwan yana jijjuyata, Aymana ta ji wajan ya ɗau zafi tayi ƙoƙarin miƙewa, cikin lallashi Sultan ya rinƙa gasa mata jikinta.

Ganin akwai ciwo hakan yasa ya cigaba da lallaɓa ta, ji yake kamar ya mayar da ciwon a jikinshi.

Kuka ta saka mashi, ta miƙe a cikin ruwan, ya ma rasa wace irin riritawa zai mata, soyayyarta da tausayinta suna tasiri a zuciyar shi.

Sun jima a toilet ɗin da kanshi ya tsabtace mata jikinta, kafin ya ɗagota yana fitowa da ita, kallon gadon yayi yadda zanin gadon ya ɓaci da fatsi-fatsin jini.

Kujerar zaman gaban mudubi ya jawo ya ɗorata, cikin hanzari ya yaye zanin gadon yazo ya na shimfiɗa wani.

Aymana ga yadda take jin ciwo amma kuma tana kallon yadda Sultan ya zage yau yana aiki gareta.

Sai da ya gyara sosai ya zo ya kamata ya ɗorata akan gadon ya kwantar da ita, yana shafa gashin kanta da ke jiƙe.

Wayar shi ya ɗauka ya danna kira yayi odar ruwan zafin da zata sha. Tare da maganin da yake buƙata akawo mata. Sannan ya je ya wanke zanin gadon cikin hanzari.

Ya dawo Aymana tana rigingine ta rufe idanuwanta yasa hannu ya dafa kanta yakai bakinshi yana sumbatar goshinta.

Yayi hanzarin shiga banɗakin ya yi nashi wankan ya fito yana shiryawa da sauri cikin wata farar jallabiya.

Falon ya fita ya jima kaɗan ya dawo hannunshi ɗauke da tire lokacin ta buɗe idonta, tana ganin shi tayi saurin rufewa.

Zuwa yayi ya ɗagota Aymana ta langwaɓe tare da faɗin "Kabar ni"

Hannu yasa ya share hawayen da suka gangaro mata, ya kai kofin bakinta "Ki sha zaki samu sauki."

Babu musu taɗan kurɓa ta kauda kai, haka yayita lallaɓata har ta sha sosai, ya ɓalle maganin ya bata. Kafin ya maidata akan filo.


Ɓandaki ya shiga ya ɗauro alwala ya zo yana shimfiɗa abin salla kafin ya kaffara salla don gabatar da Nafila, ya jima yana Addu'o'i.

Ya miƙe ya zo don kwantawa, lokacin ya gane bacci ya ɗauketa bargon ya yaye ya saka ƙafafuwanshi ya kwanta bayanta tare da rungumota sosai jikinshi.

Tunani ya farayi yadda ya faɗa soyayyar ta Amma kuma yau yana jin soyayyar tasha banban da kowane lokaci, kaunar ta ta mamaye zuciyar shi sosai, bai taɓa sanin yana ƙaunarta ba sai yau, wani irin kishinta yake ji a zuciyar shi.

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA BIYAR. 35*

Ya jima kafin bacci ɓarawo ya ɗauke shi, da asuba bacci bai ishe shi ba haka ya lallaɓa ya zame jikinshi daga nata ya shiga banɗaki yayi wanka tare da ɗoro Alwala ya  fita Masallaci, bai ɗauki lokaci ba ya dawo don baya son ta tashi baya kusa.

Shigowa yayi ya zauna bakin gadon yana binta kallo mai ɗauke da tsananin soyayya, ya matsa a hankali yakai hannunshi, yana mai dafa kanta tare da fara shafa gashin kanta cikin wani irin yanayin so.

A cikin baccin Aymana take jiyo shi, buɗe idanuwanta tayi a hankali tana sauke su akan shi.

Yarima ya gyara kwanciyarshi tare da faɗin "Na tashe ki ko?"

Cikin sauri Aymana ta rufe idon ta don wata kunyar shi ta ziyarceta, tasa hannu ta ja bargon tana rufe fuskarta.

Ƴar dariya Yarima yayi ya gane kunyace ta jagoranceta, hakan yasa ya jawo ta jikinshi "Lokacin Sallah yayi, ki tashi naga lafiyarka." Ya faɗa cikin kulawa.

Jin bata bashi amsa ba, ya sa hannu yana shirin janye bargon, Aymana ta sa hannunta tana rufe fuskarta Yarima yayi dariya "Yau kuma Sultan ɗin ake jin kunya."

Da murmushi ɗauke a fuskarta "ka barni naje nayi salla."

Ɗagota yayi "Ni fa ba na riƙe ki bane."

Ido rufe Aymana ta fara lalubar son tashi tana ƙoƙarin saukowa, amma jikinta wata irin zafi tayi saurin komawa ta zauna, Yarima ya riƙota "Muje na taimaka miki."

"Bana so."

Dariya yayi yana mai tuno maganganun ta na daren jiya hakan ya sashi faɗin "Bana so, Mai martaba ka barni na daina."

Sauri tayi ta buɗe idonta, ta na kai mashi duka a kirji, tsaye ya miƙe "Au ni ko? Ai kuwa yanzu zan kuma."

Yana maganar yana jawota, cikin sauri ta zulle "Tuba nake Allah shi taimakeka."

Dariya ya saka ya riƙo hannunta tare da miƙewa "Shi kenan muje na gani, na shirya miƙi."

Ba jiranta yayi ba, hanyar banɗaki kawai ya nufa da ita, ya zaunar da ita "Zauna bari na haɗa ruwan."

Aymana ta jingina kanta da bango tana kallon shi, ya haɗa ruwan ɗumi ya juyo ya kalle ta cikin nuna kulawa "Kin gaji ko?" 

Shiru tayi hakan yasa ya nufi wata ma'ajiya ya ɗauko burosh da abin wanke baki, ya matsa, ya zauna gefenta, yakai burosh ɗin bakinta, yana son fara yi mata kafin ruwan su gama taruwa.

Da taimakonta ya gama mata ya wanke ya juya ya kashe ruwan, yasa hannu ya na janye rigar da ya saka mata, wata kunya ta ƙaraji, sam Sultan bai damuba, baya son ganin zata wahala.

Cikin ruwan ya sakata, yana gaggasa mata jikinta, ya jima sosai kafin ya mata wanka, da kanshi ya saka mata towul kafin ya riƙota zuwa ɗakin.

Komai Sultan ne yayi mata idan tazo yima zai anshe yayi, mamaki sosai tare da ita, yau ya ƙara canza mata tana ganin kamar ba Sultan ɗin da ta sani ba.

Da taimakon ta ya saka mata kaya, ya shimfiɗa mata abin salla, ganin ta kabbara sallar hakan yasa ya fita falon don shigo da kayan abincin da ya yi oda.

Sai da ya aje komai, Aymana ta jima tana Addu'o'i tare da roƙon Allah farinciki a rayuwarsu mai ɗorewa.

Ganin baya nan hakan yasa ta ci gaba da zamanta, tsawon lokacin sai gashi ya shigo ɗakin, bisa mamakinta, da shiri taganshi kenan wanke yaje ɗayan ɗakin yayi.

Kauda idonta tayi, Sultan ya zauna gefenta tare ɗaukar kayan abincin ya haɗa bai jira komai ba ya cigaba da bata, ta ci sosai kafin ya bata ruwan shayi don gasa cikinta.

Ya miƙe ya kama hannunta ya zaunar da ita kan gado, ta mirgina tana son ƙara kwantawa don hutawa.

Sultan ya ƙara balle magungunanta, ya zauna bakin gadon ya ɗagota "Tashi kisha magani kar..."

"Ni fa ba zan sha ba."

Zaro ido yayi "Me yasa ko so kike jikinki yayita ciwo."

Kauda idonta tayi daga kallon shi, Sultan ya ce "Tashi kisha za ki samu sauƙin."

"Na warke." ta faɗa tana ƙara kame fuskarta, sosai ya gane Izzarta ce take son motsawa.

Dariya yayi don shi sam yana ganin ba lokacin Izza bane yanzu.

Kofin hannun shi ya aje ya miƙe tsaye ya fara ɓalle maɓallin rigarshi, yana cirewa ya rage daga shi sai singileti, dariya yake riƙewa lokacin daya zama daga shi sai gajeren wando.

Ya taka zuwa gadon "Ba damuwa, Tunda Gimbiya ta warke sai mu ɗora daras..."

Ai kafin ya ida Aymana ta yi saurin miƙewa tana yin kan kofin daya aje "Ina ka aje maganin."

Dariya ya saka mata "Kin warke f..."

"Allah A'a."

Maganin ya bata ya kwantar da ita saman kirjinshi, ya na mai shafar bayanta, soyayyar ta da shaƙuwarta suna tasiri sosai a zuciyar shi, tabbas yana jin Aymana ta zama wani ɓangare na rayuwar shi.

"Aymana!" Ya kirata sai dai kiran ya shiga zuciyarta sosai, hakan yasa ta ƙara narkewa jikin shi.

Ɗago fuskarta yayi "Thank you  so much, you really made my day, i much enjoyed it, I had a good time with you, am so lucky to have you, Thanks for such an amazing night, I wish this moment will last longer and forever, I love you." 

*(Na gode sosai, tabbas kin ƙayatar da rana ta yau, na ji daɗin sosai, na samu kyakkyawan lokaci tare da ke, tabbas ni mai sa'a ne na samunki, na gode da dare mai kyau tare dake, ina fatan wannan yanayin yayi tsawo ya zama har abada, Ina son ki.)* 

Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya, tayi saurin ƙara kallon shi jin yau Sultan yana faɗin yana sonta, yaga tsantsar mamaki a tare da ita hakan yasa yace "Sosai sosai Aymana, ina son ki, bana iya musaltawa, ke ɗin ta dabance a zuciyata, ina son ki so na haƙiƙa."

Aymana ta saka hannuwanta a ƙirjinshi tana mai riƙo shi sosai, Sultan ya matseta jikin shi "Na gode farincikina, Allah yayi maki Albarka."

Ƙasa-ƙasa ta amsa mashi da amin, tana mai jin ta shi soyayyar tana fizgarta, a haka maƙale da juna bacci ya ɗauke su.

Wunin ranar a haka sukayi rayuwarsu, babu wanda yake son yin nisa da ɗan uwanshi, abinci kuwa sai dai akawo musu har dare babu inda suka leƙa.

Haka da daddare duk yadda Sultan yayi ƙoƙarin danne sha'awar shi da son ƙara kusantarta ya kasa, solo yayi mata na tausayawa da kuma binta a hankali, Aymana ta samu gamsuwa sosai a tare da Sultan, wannan lokacin bata ji jiki ba, ta ɗan daure mashi sosai.

Da safe tana zaune tana taje gashin kanta, tana gyarawa da wasu mayuka masu laushi, Sultan ya matso yana faɗin "ki yi sauri fa kike min yanga."

Dariya tayi "yanga kuma?"

"E mana, kin manta kince da wuri zamu fita." Yayi maganar yana amsar matajin gashin ya yi sauri ya gyara mata, ya ɗaure ya ɗago fuskarta "Je duba mudubi, na fiki iyawa ashe."

Dariya tayi ta ɗauki Mayafinta ta yane kanta sosai, ta saka hannu zata ɗauki turare don fesawa Sultan ya riƙe hannunta.

"Sam ba zan lamunta ba, kenan kina so wani yaji min ƙamshin mata?"

Sororo tayi tana kallon shi, ɗaga mata jira yayi "ba ki ganin yawancin mutanan dake ganin nan kafurawa sun ciga shi, don shaƙatawa, kina kallo fa."

Tsantsar kishi ta gani a tare da shi, hakan yasa ta daure tana hararar shi "Ban yadda kallo a miki ba balle..."

Ya kasa ida maganar saboda hannunta daya maida kan jikinshi, yana fesa turaren a kayan shi.

"Me hakan ke nufi." Ta faɗa tana miƙewa tsaye "Na ki ne na saka shikenn."

"Ba zan amince ba nima" Dariya yayi "Muje."

"Sai ka sauya kayan kafin mu fita, taya zaka hanani sakawa, kai kuma ka saka, kenan ni bana kishinka?" Ta ƙarashe maganar dai-dai lokacin da Ayda ta faɗo mata arai, hakan yasa jikinta yayi sanyi, tunda tasan cewar tabbas Sultan ba nata bane ita kaɗai.

Ajiyar zuciya ta sauke, tare da faɗin "Ranka shi daɗe, zamu iya tafiya."

Da murmushi a fuskarshi, ya nufi ma'ajiyar kayansu, yana fiddo wasu, zai fitar Aymana tace "Ina mai tuba a gareka."

Bai saurareta ba ya sauya, koba komai yana son nuna mata tana da matsayi a zuciyar shi.

Yana gamawa ya kamo hannunta "Ke ɗin ta dabance, komai za ayi dominki, ina mantawa da akwai wani rawani a kaina a wanann lokacin."

Murmushi tayi ta na faɗin "Na gode!"

"Kiyi a hankali kar ki susutar da Sultan ya koma faɗar shi, a kasa gane kanshi."

Gaba ɗaya sukayi dariya tace "Lallai da fushin Mai martaba ya tabbata kanmu."

A hanya ya fara tunanin abinda zai saya mata da zai zama tukuicinta na faranta zuciyar shi, da kuma mallaka mashi kanta.

Duk abinda yayi tunani yana ɗaukar shi bai kai ya zama tukuiciba.

 Sai da suka sha kwanakinsu cikin farin ciki, kafin suka haɗa kayansu don zasu fara tura kayanne kafin zuwansu.

Da kanshi ya haɗa komai, ya koma falo ya sameta, ya zauna yana faɗin "Zo kiji."

Aymana ta maƙe kafaɗa "Na ƙi wayon."

Dariya yayi ya isa wajan da take ya zauna "Kin ga saura kwanakinmu Ukku mu koma gida, sam na rasa me zai zama tukuicin Gimbiya na faranta ran Sultan da mallaka mashi tabbataccen farin ciki."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi, bata ce komai ba ta ce "Babu buƙatar hakan Allah ya taimakeka."

"Hakan yana da muhimmanci ganin ke kanki kinsan darajar hakan."

Dariya tayi tagane yana son tuno mata haukan da tayi akan daren farkon shi da Ayda.

Sai kuma ta ɗaure fuska "Ina da buƙata." Ta faɗa.

Ya gyara zaman shi, yana son dama ta faɗi ra'ayinta ne.

"Ina jinki."

"Gimbiya ta gama aminta da ƙaunar da Sultan yake mata, babu buƙatar wani abun more rayuwa da zai gushe wata rana, Na ɗauki ƙaunar da kake min a matsayin tukuici na."

Murmushi yayi ya na janyota jikinshi, ya sumbaceta a goshi Aymana ta ci gaba da magana "Ina rokon Alfarma."

Sauri yayi wajan faɗin "Zanyi ko me akan ki Aymana."

"Ina son na dauwama a zuciyar Sultan."

Dariya yayi ya matseta gam jikinshi "Kin samu hakan Aymana."

Ana gobe zasu baro ƙasar Saudiyya Sultan ya ce ta zauna gida shi ɗaya ne zai fita, Sayayya sosai yayi mata, kafin ya gama yanke shawarar abinda zai mata na tukuicinta idan sun koma gida, sai dai hakan ba yana nufin za su baiyana komai ga mutanen gidan ba, zai zama tsakanin shi ne da ita.

A wannan fitarne bai bari ya manta da sayayya mai yawa ga Ayda ba, itama nata jakunkunan daban ya haɗa mata, da ita da yaronta Abul, wanda shi rabin sayyyar shi duk kayan wasa ne.


Dawowa yayi a gajiye Aymana ta kalli yadda wasu ma'aikata suke shigo da kaya, suna fita ta nufeshi "Duk yadda naso karmu kwashi kaya wajan tafiya hakan bai samu ba."

Ajiyar zuciya yayi "Ina tare da gajiya ina buƙatar taimakon ki."

Hannun shi ta kama sukayi ƙurya, ta taimaka mashi yayi wanka ya shirya kafin suka zo suka huta.

***

Washe gari girgin safe su Aymana zasu bi don dawowa Toro, Sultan ya gama shirin shi na Alfarma cikin kayan sarauta da suka amshe shi sosai, yau rawanin kanshi launin makuba ne, hakan ya fito da hasken fatar shi.

Aymana ta gyara Alkebbar jikinta "Kwana biyu da Sultan bai saka rawani ba, sai naga yau Sultan ya fi kullum yin kyau."

Shiru baiyi magana ba, sai ƙofa da yake nufa cikin tafiyar Sarauta, jin bai amsa mata ba Aymana ta gane yau fa ya mayar da Izzarshi, hakan yasa ta bi bayanshi tana mai tafiyar  ƙasaita, wanda ita kanta sarƙar ƙafarta tana fitar sauti mai rikitarwa.

Lokacin da suka isa motoci ne suka zo ɗaukar shi, da fadawa masu tarin yawa, wasu daga cikin motocin suna ɗauke da busa da algaita.

Sam su Aymana basuyi mamakin ganin yadda aka ƙayatar da gidan ba, hakan ya tabbatar musu da ana shirya wani shagali ne don dawowar Sultan.

Umarni Sultan ya bada akan nufa dashi wani ɓangare na sirri don su shirya kafin su fito.

Ayda ta ci kwalliya wannan lokacin don tarbar Sultan a cewar ta itace matar da zata tare shi.

Kuyangi da bayin gidan sai kai kawo suke, Jakadiya kuwa bi take ɗaki ɗaki don leƙo wainar da ake toyawa.

Wanann lokacin sam dawowar Sultan baiyiwa Waziri da Yarima Saifu daɗi ba, saboda tun tafiyar Sultan ɗin  Waziri yake zama fadar safe shi kuma Yarima Saifu ya zauna fadar yamma.

Farfajiyar gidan ta ƙayatu da adon sarauta da kujeru, mutanen gidan kowa yazo, hatta mai martaba da iyalanshi sun fito Sultan ne kawai ake jira da Aymana.

Ayda tana daga gefe cikin Alkebba launin ja, sai cika take tana batsewa ga kuyangi na gewaye da ita.

Sultan ne da Aymana suka dirfafo wajen yayinda fadawa da kuyangi suka biye dasu.

Kowa na wajen ya miƙe tsaye don girmamawa  lokacin da Sultan ya ke niyar zama.

Abin mamaki Ayda tana zaune, Aymana kuwa tana tsaye tana jiran zaman Sultan kafin ta zauna.

Murmushi Sultan yayi ya fasa zama, ya ja alkebbar shi tare da nufa wajan Ayda ko ba komai dai yayi kewar shirmenta kwana biyu.

Kowa ya maida hankalin shi wajen, Sultan ya je gaban kujerarta ya ɗan sunkuya kamar yana mata raɗa "Gimbiya." 

Ya faɗa, Ayda ta saki murmushi tana kallon shi, Sultan ya miƙe ya kamo hannunta.

Aymana tayi saurin kauda idonta jin wani abu daya daki zuciyarta, kishi taji marar musaltuwa.

Wata kujerar Sultan ya canzawa Ayda, Ayda ji take kamar ya ƙara mata girma akanta, ta zauna tana saka hannu ta dafa cikinta, ko don cikin jikinta tasan dole ya kulata.

Take aka fara kirari ga Ayda da kuma Sultan.

Juyawa yayi don komawa mazaunin shi, ta gaban Aymana yazo wucewa, cikin sauri ta sunkuya alamar ban girma saida taga ya wuce ne ta ƙara dai-daita tsayuwarta.

Sultan ya zauna sannan kowa ya zauna, ya sanar bayason bata lokaci don yana son shiga ya huta.

Haka yasa aka gabatar da komai na murnar dawowarshi cikin sauri, masu wasannin gargajiya suka gabatar, kowa na wajen ya ji daɗi.

Sultan yayi jawabi da godiya gasu waziri da suka riƙe karagar shi har ya dawo.

Aymana kanta yana ƙasa, da kyal ta samu ta daidaita kanta, Sultan ya ɗan kula da hakan, sai dai bai damu ba.

Farida ta zauna gefenta daga ƙasa tare da yi mata raɗa ahankali "Allah ya ja kwananki, ina mai tuba, Amma hankalinki baya tare da taron nan."

Cikin sauri Aymana ta nutsu ta mayarda hankalinta, dai-dai lokacin aka fara jawabi akan Sultan yana son gabatar da bada Hula da kuma naɗi.

Sultan ya miƙe tsaye aka miƙa mashi wata hula ta mata ƙirar hular sarakuna mata. (Tiara) sai dai ƙiyar hular ƙirar sarakunan gargajiyane, wanda aka yiwa ado da madubai da zagayen zinari mai kyalli.

Mai gabatarwar yace "Sultan zai sakawa Gimbiya Aymana hular naɗi da kuma bata sarautar Sarauniyar matan Nahiyarmu. Saboda haka mai martaba yana son ganin Gimbiya Aymana a gaban shi."

Wata irin faɗuwar gaba ta shigi Aymana ta ɗago a gigice, tana kallon mutanan wajen kowa yana cikin mamaki yadda Sultan zai yi naɗi ba tare da ya nemi shawarar kowa ba.

Sultan yana kallonta cikin soyayya, tabbas dole ya bata girma da kuma bata tukuici mai tsoka akan daran farkon su, amma kuma yana ganin sarautar da zai bata hakan zai sa ba za a taɓa mantata a nahiyar ba, kasancewar itace mace ta farko da ta riƙe wannan Sarautar.

Kowa ya fara murna, ana ihu da tafi, Jakadiyya ta ci gaba da rangaɗa guɗa.

Aymana ta kalli Sultan dake kallon wajan da take fuska ɗauke da murmushi.

Mama dake nesa tayi saurin nufo Aymana cikin murna, ganin ta kasa tashi.

Kuyanga Aisha da Farida suka ƙara matsowa, Mama ta riƙo hannun Aymana suna miƙewa don kaita gaban Sultan.

Farida tayi saurin riƙe wani yadin karan-miski dake jan ƙasa jikin kayan Aymana.

Ayda tayi saurin miƙewa tana dafa kujera cikin gigicewa, ta yadda za a ɗauki sarauta mai girma aba Aymana bayan itace take kawo magadan sarautar gidan su.

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA SHIDDA. 36*

   Ana zuwa gaban Sultan Aymana ta sunkuyar da kanta ƙasa, Sultan yayi murmushi yana mai saka hannu ya fara ɗago kanta, Jakadiyya ta matso da salon kiraki.

Sultan ya ɗago hular ya ɗorata akan Aymana, murna aka kama yi, Aymana wani sanyi ya ziyarceta, tabbas tasan darajar sarauta, hakan yasa take jin kamar ya bata duk wani farin ciki da zata iya nema.

Ɗagowa tayi a hankali tana mai son mayarda hawayen farin ciki dake neman zubar mata, Sultan ya koma kan kujerar shi ya zauna, Ayman ta tsuguna a gaban shi alamar godiya da kuma girmamawa.

Sultan yayi murmushi kawai, Mama ta kamo hannun Aymana suka koma mazauninta.

Mai martaba kuwa yasan tabbas hakan yana nufin Sultan ya samu farin ciki na tafiya da Aymana, shi kanshi yasan tabbas Aymana ta cancanta a yaba mata.

Waziri kuwa zuciyar shi kamar zata huda kirjinshi ta fito, wani baƙin ciki yake ji, lallai Sultan ya tabbatarwa mutanan gidan babu wani bayan Aymana.

Goggo dake gefen Ayda ta riƙe hannunta "Ki daure Kar ki..."

Fizge Hannu Ayda tayi tana mai barin wajan sanin cewar idan har ta tsaya tabbas sai tayi abinda zai ja hankalin kowa, tun kafin ta isa sashenta take kuka, Allah ya taimaketa babu kowa mutanen gidan suna farfajiyar.

Haka aka tashi taron masu murna sunayi masu baƙin ciki kamar suyi hauka. 

Sultan sashen Gimbiya Ummi ya wuce don gaida ita, sai da ya gaida kowa kafin ya wuce sashen shi.

Aymana kuwa ita kanta bata samu kanta ba, saboda masu taya murna dake zuwar mata da kuma Barka da dawowa.

Jin ance Sultan ya shigo hakan yasa tayi saurin miƙewa don zuwa wajan shi, kasancewar tasan Ayda ce zata amshe shi.

Yana zama Aymana tana shigowa da sassarfarta ta ƙarasa gaban shi ta durƙusa "Allah ya ja kwanan ka, ina godiya, ina jin farin ciki har bansan taya zan yi godiya ko bada tukuicin wann..."

"Ba a biyan tukuici don wani tukuicin."

Aymana ta ɗago, Sultan ya miƙe yasa hannu ya ɗagota suka miƙe tsaye ya riƙe kafaɗunta "Wannan shine tukuicin ki da kika kasa zaɓar abinda kike so."

Murna tayi tare da rungumoshi ta kai bakinta tana sumbatar shi "Na gode."

"Shi kenan dai a fidda ranar fidda shagali don taro akan..."

"Ranka shi daɗe bana buƙatar hakan, Sam bana so sarautar ta zama zan rinƙa gudanar da ita, babu buƙatar shagali."

"Me hakan ke nufi Aymana?"

Murmushi tayi ta lakaci hancin shi "Mai kula da Sultan ba zai samu lokacin gudanar da wani mulki ba, iya kula dakai ma mulki ne."

Dariya yayi jin yadda ta zaɓe shi akan sarautar daya bata "Allah ya maki Albarka."

Bayan fitar Aymana haka tasa aka fitar da kayan tsaraba ga kowa har da Maimartaba a ciki.

Bayi da kuyangi sunyi murna sosai, Jakadiyya tsarabarta ta dabance, ita kau da ma ba tun yanzu ba Aymana ta gama da ita tunda ta kaita ƙasa mai tsarki.

Ranar Ayda sai da ta taɓo mashi zancen banbanci da ya nuna tsakanin su, shiru yayi ya ƙaleta ganin duk kalmar da zai yi mata ya riga ya taɓa yi mata wajan nusar da ita akan abinda yayi niya bazai fasa ba.

Bayan kwana biyu ta rinƙa karɓar zugar wasu daga cikin mutanen gidan, hakan yasa suka dawo kamar da ita da Aymana da sun haɗu sai gorin haihuwa da habaice Habaice, Aymana kuwa ta sake hannu ta toshe kunnuwanta a yanzu ta yi alƙawarin ba zata kuma kula Aymana ba.

Mai martaba ne zaune da Sultan suna fira, Gimbiya Ummi ta shigo Sultan ya gaida ita yana shirin tashi don bar musu wajen Gimbiya Ummi ta kalle shi "Alhamdulillah Sultan na fahimci komai ya maka dai dai a fadar ka."

Sultan ya sunkuyar da kai sai lokacin ya tuna bai faɗa masu yadda yake jin ya samu komai lafiya ba.

"Ayi min Afuwa Gimbiya Ummi, nayi shiru ne akan maganar ina gudun kar mutanen gidannan su fahimci ina..."

Dariyar girma Mai martaba yayi "Ai ko baka faɗa ba mun fahimta."

"Allah dai yayiwa yarinyar nan albarka." Cewar Gimbiya Ummi.

Shiru Sultan yayi tare da miƙewa "Na barku lafiya."

Yana fita Gimbiya Ummi ta kalli Mai martaba "Ni kam wallahi ma Yarinyar ta fara bani tausayi."

"Wajan me kenan?"

"Hmm yau dai ko yaya ne zan faɗa, akan haihuwa, duk yadda yarinyar nan Ayda take mata gori ina sane amma Aymana ko kallonta bata yi."

"Kinzo da maganar da na jima ina son yi, amma abin mamaki shi Sultan ɗin bai taɓa kulawa ba."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi ta ce "Wannan lokacin ba zamu zuba ido ba, zan zauna da shi, ya kai yarinyar nan Asibiti a dubata."

"Yana da kyau yin hakan." Mai martaba ya bata amsa.

***

Sultan ne ya riƙe hannun Aymana da take shafa kirgin shi, ya kalleta yana murmushi "Wai Gimbiya Ummi ce ta ce na kai ki Asibity ki ga likita."

Aymana ta ɗan razana tare da faɗin "Saboda me, lafiya ta lau."

"Tace tana buƙatar ganin jikanta daga wannan ɓangaren." Yayi maganar yana mai shafa cikinta.

Dariya tayi "Allah sarki ni wallahi har hankali na ya tashi."

Hannunshi yakai saman kafaɗarta "Zan faɗawa Gimbiya zai yiwu ma ta shirya ganin Magaji nan da..."

"Haba ni ba wani abu a tare sani."

Sultan ya ja hannnunta "kin tabbatar?"

Dariya tayi "Eh mana."

Miƙewa tsaye yayi tare da ɗaukarta tsagwayam "Shi kenan muje na baki magajin yanzu."

Yana maganar yana hayewa dasu kan gado, Aymana ta miƙe ta dafa kafaɗar shi "Shi kenan ba damuwa zan karɓa."

Tayi maganar tana saka hannu ta fara ɓalle maɓallin rigarshi, Sultan ya kai kanshi akan kumcinta, da taimakon ta ya kawar da kayan jikinshi, kafin nata kayan, wani salon wasa Sultan ya cigaba da aika mata sai da ya tabbatar ya kaita inda ba zata iya juraba kafin ya hautsine na shi tunanin ta hanyar kai kanshi yana tsotsar jikinta.

Ya sani sarai salon yana tasiri wajan kawar da tunanin Aymana nishi ta fara sakar mashi tana ƴar ƙara, sosai yake tsotsa ta, ya miƙar da hannuwanshi yana lalubar ƙirjinta tare da mummurzawa cikin salo, Jin Aymana ta fara mashi numfashi hakan yasa shi saka nashi hannun akan Hajiya Babba dake ƙakƙandarewa ya janye kanshi tare da mayar da jikin shi yana fara sarrafara cikin lumshe ido yana jin gamsuwa na shigarshi.

****

Ayda ta dafa cikin dake gabanta daya turo sosai ta ci gaba da magana "Da banbanci fa har yanzu, ko baki fahimci hakan ba, kin kasa gane kowa yana ganin gazawar ki, ko da yake babu buƙatar hakan, Sultan ya riga ya samu mai gadon shi, saura ma mai zuwa nan da ɗan lokaci.

"Ayda!"

Aymana ta faɗa tana fara nunata da yatsa wannan lokacin ta kai ta ƙarshe, sai dai kafin ta ƙara ɗaga baki don magana Gimbiya Saratu ta shigo farfajiyar.

Aymana ta juya tana kallon ta, Ayda ta aikawa Saratu wani mugun kallo, Saratu tayi kamar bata ganta ba tayi kan Aymana "Gimbiya zo ki ji."

Aymana ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tabi bayan Saratu, suna shiga ɓangaren ta Gimbiya saratu  tace "Wallahi baƙo gare ku ni kumu ban san taya zanwa Sultan bayani ba."

"Baƙo kuma?"

Dariya Saratu tayi "Sirikin ku mana."

Aymana ta jawota "kaji ni da mara kunyar yarinya, Sultan ɗin ne kika rasa taya zaki sanar dashi."

"Wallah kuwa."

"Shi kenan yaushe zai zo, zan sanar dashi."

"Gobe ne, yace yana son ganawa da Sultan ne, amma zuwan safe zasuyi."

"Babu damuwa zan tashi Sultan ɗin da wuri kar ki damu."

***

Da daddare Aymana tana zaune tana jiran shigowar Sultan yau kanta yana mata ciwo sai dai tana son isar da saƙon Saratu kafin ta kwanta.

Bisa mamakinta sai gani tayi Sultan ya fito hannunwan shi ɗauke da kofin shayi guda biyu.

Binshi tayi da kallo cikin daurewa ta ce "Ban yi tunanin kana ciki ba."

Murmushi yayi yana ɗan kallonta ganin bata taso ta karɓe shi ba "Allah yasa lafiya."

"Lafiya lau Alhamdulillah." ta bashi amsa, tare da kauda zancen da bata son ya gane bata jin daɗi.

"Ina can ina haɗa shayi ga Gimbiya" ya faɗa yana miƙa mata kofin.

Aymana ta ƙarɓa, suracin shayin yana fita da ƙamshin sinadarin da aka haɗa ma Shayin.

Ɗan yamutsa fuska tayi jin yadda ƙamshin ya doki hancinta, ya aje kofin tare da faɗin "Ko miye Sultan yayi Shayin da shi."

Ajewa yayi ya matso ya jawota jikin shi "Kamar akwai damuwa tare da ke."

"A'a saƙon saratu ne nazo isarwa" tayi maganar tana gaya mashi.

Dariya yayi "Allah ya kaimu gobe."

Ameen tace, Sultan ya ci gaba da shan shayin shi Aymana ya miƙe Sultan ya bita da kallo, ya kalli kofin da ta bari bata sha ko kaɗan ba.

Ya ajiye kofin yana binta baya ya samu tana rage kayan jikinta "Ba ki da sha Shayin ba?"

Ya faɗa cikin sanyin jiki, don ya damu, Ayman ta ɓalle bireziyar jikinta, ta nufe shi tana wata irin tafiya da salon jan hankali, ga dukiyar fulanin ta dake girgizawa.

Sultan ya kalleta lokacin da tazo gab da shi "Na faɗa maka Shayin yana ƙamshi mara daɗi, ban san me ka saka ba."

Hannuwanshi yasa ya riƙo dukiyar fulanin da ke mashi yawo a ido, bai bata amsaba, ya kai bakinshi akan ɗaya yana fara tsotsa. Aymana ta rinjaye su suna faɗawa kan gadon ɗakin.

[11/5, 10:40 PM] AuntyHaliloss✍🏼: *MASARAUTA.*

*EXQUISITE WRITER'S FORUM.*

*2021*
      *HAƘƘIN MALLAKA*
*HALIMATU KANGIWA.*
       (AuntyHaliloss).

*SHAFI NA TALATIN DA TARA. 39*


Tun daga ƙafafuwanshi zuwa   fuska ta ke kallo tayi saurin ɗagowa ta sauke idanuwanta akan fuskar shi.

Wata iriyar razana ya shigeta ganin Baba Maga yaƙi, zaro ido ta yi za ta fara ja baya ya daka mata tsawa, hakan ya yi sanadiyar tashin sauran masu tsaron wajan.

Gaba ɗaya su ka zare makaman su suna yo kan su, Baba Magayaki ya fara magana "Me ya kawo ki nan? Ba ni abinda ya ke hannunki."

Aymana ta tsaya cak tana kallon shi "Na ce ki bani Takobin, Lallai ashe da gaske abinda kika zo ɗauka ne da gaske?"

Wani daga cikin mutanan wajan ya fara salati zai fara maganganu Aymana ta ɗaga mashi Hannu "Kar na ji bakin ka, Takobin taku ce ko tamu?" Tayi maganar tana foddo Takobin ta riƙe hannunta.

Baba Maga yaƙi ya juya yana salati shima "Ke kuwa kin san darajar Takobin nan a masarautar nan."

Yana maganar aka kama hayaniya kowane yayo ca da maganganu, gaban Aymana ya fara dukan tara-tara far gaba ya shigeta, ta fara waigawa tana gudun kar wani na gidan ya ji su.

"Tabbas kin Aikata babban kuskure, ya zama dole a ɗau mataki akan ki, yanzu da ban farka na fito ba haka zaki fitar da ita..." Yana maganar ya kalli wani tare da faɗin "Maza-maza ka sanar da Tsohon Sarki."

Gaban Aymana ya faɗi ji take kamar ta tsaga kasa ta shige ƙarfin haline kawai ya tsayar da ita, yanzu ta fara tunanin lallai abin kunya ne asameta da aikata hakan, wane hali zata shiga idan mutanen gidan nan suka ji.

Mai martaba ya farka lokacin yana son yin shirin fita masallacin Asuba, ɗan Aiken bai jira ba ya shiga yana son a barshi don ganin Sarki.

Hayaniya aka fara ana sanar dashi sai ya jira idan za ya tafi masallacin, yana faɗar dalilin shi, za a shiga sai gashi ya fito yana tambayar "Lafiyar ku? Me ya ke faruwa ne?"

"A gafarceni Ranka shi daɗe, daga wajan Maga yaƙi ne, yana son ganin ka a babban ɓangaren..."

"A wannan lokacin?"

"Tabbas wani abu ya faru, An kaiwa takobin gidannan hari har an fito da it..."

Kafin ya ida Mai martaba yayi saurin faɗin "Me?" Yayi hanyar fita da sauri.

Samu yayi an kunna hasken wajen cikin tashin hankali ya je, yana faɗin "Me ya ke faruwa?"

"Allah ya taimakeka Aymana ce muka kama tana ƙoƙarin fitar da Takobi zuwa..."

Tattaki Mai martaba yayi yana kallon ta, don sam bai kula da ita ba saboda hayaniyar da ake, takobi ya gani hannun Aymana.

Wata razananniyar tsawa ya daka mata "Waye ya saka ki?"

Ya nufeta cikin sauri, Baba Maga yaƙi ya ce "Ai zance ya ƙare lokacin da muka sanar dakai akwai munafunci a zancen Auren Sultan da ita gani kayi kamar..."

Bai sauka ga maganar ba Sai ga Waziri ya fito da riga 'yar shara, yana mummurza ido alamar bacci ya ke ya fito, tsayawa yayi yana bin kowa da kallo, lokacin ya fahimci abinda ke faruwa.

Aymana ta fara zubar da hawaye, ta sunkuyar da kanta ƙasa Waziri yace "Karshen tukakuki tuk! Manufar ki da mahaifinki ta fito."

Mai martaba ya miƙa hannu zai amshi takobin Waziri yace "Allah ya taimake ka, dole a sanar da Sultan don..."

Mai martaba ya ci gaba da fitar da huci, da wani irin zarewar lamari, ya kalli wani bafade yace "Maza ka sanar da Sultan ina neman shi."

"Tabbas yanzu na yarda da maganar ku, Sarkin Bilyam ya haɗa wannan aurenne don samun damar mallakar Takobi, ya turo Aymana zuwa masarautar mu don satar takobi ta mayar  da ita."

Aymana ta matso jin abin zai koma kan mahaifinta tace "A'a Ba..."

"Yi mana shiru." Cewar mai martaba.

Sultan yana fitowa zai tafi massallaci, kiran Mai Martaba ya sameshi, ya yi hanyar sashen Mai martaba ɗan Aiken yace "Allah shi taimakeka Mai martaba yana  sashe Babban  ne."

Sauri ya ƙarayi yana jin faɗuwar gaba, ya ƙara sakin ƙafa yana sauri, yana isa wajan bai kula da Aymana ba, ya sunkuya tare da Faɗin "Barka da Asb..."

Mai martaba ya kalli yanayin shigar sarautar da Sultan yayi, ya tabbatar yaron shi Sarki ne mai girma.

Ya dafa kafaɗar shi da sauri "Ina hankalin ka yake Sultan, taya ka bari hakan ya faru." Sultan ya ɗago cikin sauri, Mai martaba ya ɗaga hannu yana nuna mashi Aymana da ta riƙe takobin tana duƙar da kai.

Yau ita kaɗai tasan bala'in da take ciki, yau ta zamar mata ranar da bata taɓa jin ƙasƙanci ba.

Cikin rashin fahimta Sultan ya nufeta "Aymana!"

"Ga Aymana nan, ka ga abinda Darul-Bilyam sukayi mana, sunyi amfani da aura maka ita don satar Takobin gidan nan."

Wata irin razana Sultan yayi ya nufe ta da sauri ya riƙe ta yana jijjigata "Aymana!"

Wani irin kuka ta saka, tana sakin takobin tana shirin faɗuwa, Sultan ya riƙo takobin da sauri don yana tsoron ya faɗi.

Sam Sultan bai taɓa jin tashin hankali irin na yau ba, kenan ƙudirin da take da shi na son dawowa da martabar gidan su yana nan.

Kallon takobin yayi ya fara neman abinyi, ya kalli Mai martaba ya na mai sunkuyawa "Ba zan lamunta ba Sultan, wane irin mulki ka gudanar da har ka kasa fahimtar Aymana tana son mallakar ƙarfin mulkin mu?"

Sultan ya waiga yana kallon mutanen wajan tare da faɗin "Zaku iya tafiya." Kowa ya ja baya suna saurin bin umarnin shi.

Mai martaba ya ce "Kasan hukuncin da akayiwa mutanen da sukayi yunƙurin Aikata abinda ta aikata yanzu."

Baba Waziri ya ce "Lallai akwai yaudara a lamarin nan, tabbas mutanen Bilyam sun cuce mu kum..."

"Zaku iya tafiya sallah, ina son ganinku bayan masallaci."

Sultan ya juya ya kalli Aymana dake tsaye  ya daka mata tsawa "Ki bar wajen nan."

Aymana zata fara tafiya mutanen gidan suka fara tururuwa suna fitowa.

Sultan kam wannan ta zamar mashi baƙar rana a rayuwar shi, Aymana ta ja mishi bala'e da ba zai iya kawar da shi ba a gidan nan.

Take matan suka kama salallami da tsegumi, da jinjina abinda Aymana ta aikata, Aymana jikinta ya mutu tana ganin duk darajar data samu ta ɓare ayau.

Mai martaba ya bar wajan afusace, Sultan ya kalli Jakadiyya da ta rufa da zanin atamfa yace "Jakadiyya! Ki je da Aymana sashenta, ki tsareta har zuwa shigowa ta, haka kuma kar ki bari ta gana da kowa."

"An gama ranka shi daɗe."

Wani tashin hankali ya shigi Aymana, ta juya tana kallon Sultan daya figi alkebba cikin sauri.

Aymana tana gaba Jakadiya tana binta, mutanen gidan suka kama binta da kallo, A bakin ƙofa taga Farida tsaye sai sharɓar kuka take, Aymana ta kawar da kanta ta shiga, Jakadiyya ta mara mata baya ta ja kofar ta rufe.

Aymana ta faɗa kan kujerar tana sakin wani irin kuka, tare da faɗin na shiga Ukku.

***

Ana fitowa Salla kuwa aka haɗu kamar yadda Mai martaba yace, Yana zaune kan kujera Sultan ya zaune kujerar dake gefen shi, Baba Maga yaƙi da Waziri, Sai lokacin naga Baba Galadima wannan lokacin har su Maga takarda da kuma shantali, gaba ɗaya ahalin manyan masarautun sun haɗu wajan.

Mai martaba ya yi gyaran murya fuska babu annuri ya fara magana, yana mai tabbatar da girman laifin da Aymana ta aikata.

"Wannan wani laifi ne da ga masarautar Bilyam, dole mahukunta zasu shiga maganar, tabbas zamu tuhumi Sarkin Bilyam akan abinda ya aikata mana."

"Hakan yana da kyau, hakan zai sa duk wani mai harin takobin ya ji tsoron Aikata hakan." Cewar Baba Galadima wanda shima lokacin ya gama yadda da Aymana tazo gidanne don tafiya da takobin.

Har lokacin Sultan bai iya yayi magana ba, sai zuciyar shi da take tafarfasa tare da bugawa kamar zata ɓalle ƙirjinshi ta fito.

Waziri ya muskuta yace "Yanzu dole a ɗau tsatstsauran mataki akai, haka kuma dole a raba auren Sultan da Ay..."

Cikin Sauri Sultan ya ɗago ya kalli Waziri, sai lokacin ya ƙara jin tashin hankali.

Baba Maga tarda yace "Zan tsara komai na wasiƙar son zama da Sarkin Bilyam da kuma mahukuntar nahiyar nan."

Shantali ya kaɗa kai "Ayi komai yadda ya kamata, a yi hukunci kamar yadda aka umarta."

Sultan ya sa hannu ya dafe ƙirji shi, ya ɗago ya kalli Mai martaba "Allah ya huci zuciyarka, Ina mai bada haƙuri akan abinda ya faru, muna jiran zuwan Mahukunta akan maganar."

Mai martaba ya ɗaga kai cikin gamsuwa da maganar Sultan.

Mutanen wajen a tunanin su, Sultan zai kare ai mana ko kuma ya nema mata afuwa, sai suka ji saɓanin hakan, hakan da yayi ya tabbatar baya bayan Aymana."

Haka aka tashi wannan zama kowa ya nufi ciki.

Kowane sashe da abinda suke gulma akai, Ayda kuwa rabonta da sashenta tunda labari yaje mata, sai bi take gida gida ana taɗin abinda ya faru da ita, taso ace zata gana da Aymana ta gaya mata iya maganganun dake kanta.

Mama kuwa tayi kaikawo taso shiga wajan Aymana amma an sanar da ita Umarnin Sultan na hana kowa ganinta.

Haka Farida ta bi Mama don sam bata son zama sashen ganin yadda ake jifarta da habaici.

Hajiya mai gado kuwa yau shar a wajen su, Yarima Saifu wannan lokacin yana ganin Sultan ya aikata lafin da lallai sai Mai Martaba ya sauke shi daga karaga.

***

Sultan kuwa tabbas dole ya je wajen Aymana don jin dalilinta na aikata hakan.

Yana shiga ɓangaren aka kama gaisuwa zuwa gare shi, Kuyanga A'isha ce ta kwankwasa ƙofar daga ciki, Jakadiyya take tambaya, A'isha ta ce "Sultan ne."

Cikin Sauri Jakadiya ta buɗe Sultan, tana rusunawa gare shi, bai amsa ba ya shiga ciki.

Tana kife saman kujera, ta gama sharɓar kuka tare da sakawa kanta kwarin guiwa akan abinda ta aikata, tunda har tana da gado akan hakan, shi me yasa ya wulaƙantata da abinda ke cikinta.

Harɗe hannuwa yayi yana tafiya, yana ji a jikin shi Jakadiyya bata fita ba, hakan yasa ya ce "Jakadiyya Sultan yana buƙatar sirri."

"Allah ya baka nasara." Ta faɗa tana ficewa.

Aymana tayi saurin juyowa saboda maganar shi da taji ya daɗe a tsaye tana ƙare mashi kallo, a yadda yaga idanuwanta ya tabbatar da kukan da tayi.

Tattaki yayi yanzu ya tabbatar babu gaisuwa da za mashi hakan yasa ya sauke rawanin shi zuwa gemun shi ya ce "Kin ga abinda kima jawo mana ko, Me ya sa kika aikata hakan, kenan ƙudirin ki yana nan a zuciya baki sauya tunani ba, ko kin san kuwa abin da kika aikata."

"Na sani!"

Ta bashi amsa, Sultan yayi saurin maido hankalin shi akanta, sam bai ga dakewa a tare da ita ba, akwai tsabar tsoro a wanann lokacin, sai dai tana son kauda hakan ne.

"Me kike faɗa?"

"Na ce nasan abinda nayi, Takobin masautar Darul-Bilyam  da take a Masautar Toro ita ce na shiga na ɗauko."

Masawa yayi yana duƙawa saitin fuskarta "Kin san halin da kike son jefa mu kuwa? Kin san hukuncin da fada suke neman zartarwa akan..."

Yasa hannu ya jijjigata "Bana buƙatar sani Sultan, a shirye nake da komai a yanzu, kuma"

"Me dalilinki Aymana."

Miƙewa tayi tsaye ta saka hannu ta dafa cikin jikinta "Nayi don martabar yaro na, don ba shi gatan da ya rasa daga baban shi, na yi hakan don ɗaukaka dajar shi, nayi ne akan yaron da ya rasa shagalin murnar samun shi, yaron da mahaifiyar shi ta rasa tukuici daga babban shi, yaron da aka fifita wasu akan shi, yaron da aka dakawa mahaifiyar sa tsawa aka sanar ba shine magajin farko ba gidan nan."

Ta sauke ajiyar zuciya tare da janye hannun ta akan cikinta "Taya za a gorantawa yarona Takobi bayan takomin gadon mahaifiyarsa ce, nayi hakan don Cikin jikina Sultan?"

"Karya kike Aymana!"

Ya faɗa yana ja baya "Sam wannan ba gata bane kike neman bawa cikin dake jikin ki Kum..."

Komawa yayi ya zauna kan kujera "Nan ne gatan yaron ki me yasa..."

"Sam ba haka bane Sultan taya zaka aibanta shi kuma kace."

Miƙewa yayi tsaye tare da riƙo hannunta ya zaunar da ita da ƙarfi yan huci "Ashe baki da hankali Aymana! Ashe tashin da kikayi a gidan sarauta bai maki amfani ba, lallai na yadda hayaƙi ne kan ki lokacin da kike tunƙaho ke 'yar babbar masarauta ce."

Aymana ta ja baya "Dama bayau ka saba faɗar cewa Masarautar mu ƙaramar masarauta bac..."

"Taya ya? Taya kike son na fito na sanar da ko na baiyana ina son yaron cikin ki a gaban mutanen gidan nan, kin san kuwa irin Makircin da zasuyi don cutar kin da yaro na?"

Aymana tayi saurin kallon shi "lokacin da aka sanar kina ɗauke da juna biyu, kowa yana nan shin kina so na nuna farin ciki hakan ya taɓa ki da abin da kike ɗauke."

"Ko kin san tunda aka sanar da Cikin jikin ki, ba a ƙara bani lokaci na sirri don ganawa dake ba."

Ya miƙe tsaye yana tattaki "Aduk lokacin da zan shigo wajan ki ana bibiyata da duk wani tako na akan ku, ranar da na faɗa maki akwai wani cikin a jikin Ayda ko kinsan ana tsaye bayan labule don jin firata tsakanina dake."

Ya sauke nannauyar Ajiyar zuciya "Kin bawa Jakadiyya kujerar Makka, a tunaninki zata ɓoye tsakanin mu dake ga mutanan gidan nan? Wannan shine dalilin da ya sa gaban ta na ce kar ki kuma shigo min turaka, taya zan faɗa maki ina son yaron cikin ki ya gaji sarautata."

Jin gina yayi da bango cikin rashin kwarin guiwa "Wane ido kike so masarautata ta kalli Mai martaba Sarkin Bilyam da tuhumar abinda mahukunta suka zartar, Me ya sa ba ki yi tunani ba, Aymana ta yaya zan haifa ɗa na kyamace shi?"

Ya sauke numfashi mai ciwo "Ina ganin kalmar farinciki tayi kaɗan wajan musalta halin dan shiga lokacin da naji cewar kina ɗauke da juna biyu, Allah ne kaɗai yasan yadda nayi tsayuwar dare tare da roƙar wa yarona dake tsari daga sharri mutanen gidannan."

Aymana ta ɗaga baki za ta yi magana Sultan ya ɗaga nata hannu "Na ji baƙin cikin kasancewata Sarki, saboda rashin nuna farin ciki a gareki don nasan mulki nane ya jawo hakan, a iya musaltawa na soyayyar da nakewa abinda zaki haifa soyayyar ta wuce hankali Aymana."

Ya ida maganar yana zama saman hannun kujera, Aymana ta shiga kaɗuwa tabbas ta yadda da maganganun shi ɗari bi sa ɗari, wasu hawaye suka gangaro mata, ta saka hannu tana shafar cikinta, ta yi saurin nufar Sultan tana faɗawa jikin shi.

Ajiyar zuciya ya fara saukewa tare da matseta jikin shi, ya aza kanshi akan ƙafarta yana shafa bayanta.

[11/5, 10:40 PM] AuntyHaliloss✍🏼: *MASARAUTA.*

*HALIMATU KANGIWA.*

*SHAFI NA ARBA'IN. 40*

Kuka Aymana ta sakar mashi, Sultan ya ɗagota ya zaunar da ita akan kujera, tare da raɓata a jikin shi, tsawon lokaci tana sauke ajiyar zuciya, sunkai daƙiƙu goma sha biyar babu wanda ya kuma magana.

Sultan kuwa a zuciyar shi ya gama ƙaryata ta akan cewar tayi abinda ta yi don cikinta, tabbas yasan tun kafin cikin  tana son aikata hakan, tayi amfani da cikinne ta hanyar kare kanta.

Ɗago kanta yayi daga kafaɗar shi, a bisa mamakin shi sai yaga bacci take yi, hakan yasa ya barta, don yasan tabbas bata yi bacci ba duk daren ranar.

Sallar la'asar aka fara kira hakan yasa ya fara ƙoƙarin janyeta, Sai lokacin take ƙoƙarin gyara kwanciyarta, cikin mamaki take kallon shi tare da murza idanuwanta.

Ta gane anan tayi bacci, hakan yasa ta kai hannunta akan kafaɗar shi, lokacin ta ga har ya cire rawanin kanshi "An fara kiran Salla fa."

"Duk yau ban yi wanka ba, tun da zan fita Asuba."

Aymana ta kalli jikinta, ya gane abinda take nufi, hakan yasa ya ja hannunta suka shige ciki.

Lokacin da Sultan ya fito kowa ya kama gulma, wai tun ɗazu yake ciki amma har yanzu bai fito ba.

A ƙofa ya samu Jakadiyya ya ƙara bata umarnin kar wanda ya shiga wajan Aymana, a tunanin su yana ƙara mata wani hukuncine, shi kuwa yayi hakan ne don kar wani ya shiga ya gaya mata babu daɗi.

Lokacin Da aka fito salla, Mai martaba yake sanar da shi Waziri ya kawo mashi zancen wani bafade da yace an bashi  wasiƙa daga Bilyam ya kawowa Aymana, ya sanar da abinda ke cikin takardai.

Wannan lokacin a tsaye suka tattauna, Sultan yana son zuwa wajanta dan tabbatarwa, amma kuma Mahukunta sun zo don zama da shi, haka ya hakura, yaje sukayi wannan zaman, shi dai kawai yana amsawa amma yana cikin tashin hankali akan cewar an yi Aike  ana son ganin Sarkin Bilyam.

Sai dare ya samu kanshi, hakan yasa ya nufi sashen ta, ya samu jakadiyya ta shigar mata da abinci.

Wannan lokacin jakadiyya bata jira Sultan ya bata umarnin fita, Sultan ya nufi Aymana "Bana da idanuwan kallon Mai martaba gobe, ba na jin zan iya kallon shi akan ina tuhumar shi da Aikata laifi."

Aymana ta ji mugun tashin hankali da tsoron mahaifin ta,  hawaye suka fara gangaro nata, Sultan ya duƙa yace "Ina takardar da aka kawo maki lokacin da Tsohon Sarki yaje..."

Aymana ta zaro ido, Sultan ya ɗaga mata kai "Nifa ba a kawo min komai ba."

Yasan hakan zai faru, ita kuwa tasan idan har Sultan ya ga takardai, zai tabbatar ba don cikinta tayi hakan ba.

Ya san ba zata taɓa nunawa ba, haka ya miƙe ya fara shiga ɗakinta, Aymana ta bishi baya, ta samu yana ta neme neme, ganin ya ɗauko akwatin da ta aje takardai hakan ya sa ta riƙe shi.

Sultan ya juyo "Wai ba zaki bar ni ba, wallahi zan hukunta ki Aymana!"

"Kar ka buɗe Sultan."

Har ya riƙe ta zai tureta sai kuma yayi tunanin ba ita ɗaya bace, ajiyar zuciya yayi ya ce "Sakar ni na ce."

Kuka ya saka mashi tana maƙale shi, sam bai taɓa ganinta cikin ruɗani irin hakanba, ya fara ƙoƙarin buɗewa, Aymana ta kama turashi suka kama kokoyi, karo yayi da gado, hakan yasa Aymana ta tura shi ya saki akwatin ƙasa marfin akwatin ya ɓalle abubuwan ciki suka zube.

Yana ƙoƙarin tashi ta faɗa jikin shi, tana sauke numfashi mai ƙarfi na wahala, Sultan ya rufe idanuwan shi, yana sauraronta, kuka take sosai, Sultan ya matseta jikin shi.

"Ba na son kukan nan nace maki zan yi wani abu da takardai ne. Saman bakin shi ta rufe da harshenta, Sultan ya kasa aiwatar da komai, Aymana ya fara sakar mashi wasu irin saƙonni kasancewar tayi kwana biyu ba tare da jin gumin mijin ta ba.

Sultan ya mirginata yana saurarenta, wannan lokacin da karfinta ta ci gaba da sarrafa shi, cikin salo ta kawar kayan nauyin dake jikin shi takai kanta akan ƙirjin shi tana fara sosai shi, tana murza ɗayan da kannunta, Sultan ya fara zullewa yana mata dariya, ya fara lalubarta yana mayar mata da saƙonta, tsawan mintuna Sai da ko wannen su ya samu nutsuwa kafin Sultan ya janye jikin shi.

Aymana ta ja bargo ta rufe kanta, Sultan yana zuro ƙafarshi yaga takarda cikin Sauri ya ɗauki rawanin shi, tare da saka takardai a ciki, ya faɗa banɗaki yana tsabtace jikin shi.


Lokacin da ya fito sai da ya nemi bafaden da aka aiko da saƙon, Sultan ya fara mashi bala'i da masifa akan rashin sanar da shi, zai yi bayani Sultan ya hana shi tare da sakawa a kai shi ɗakin horo.

***

Ƙarfe sha ɗaya na safe da tashin hankali Sarkin Bilyam ya iso Masarautar Toro, Sultan yayi saurin fitowa ya tare shi.

Mai martaba ya riƙe hannun Sultan yana faɗin "Yanzu abinda yarinyar nan ta yi kenan."

Cikin Ladabi Sultan ya sunkuya "Allah ya taimake ka kayi haƙuri."

Dai dai lokacin suka shiga fada Mai martaba tsohon Sarki yana zaune Sarkin Bilyam ya ci gaba da yiwa Sultan magana "Amfanin me zata maka da ka barta baka fitar da ita a cikin gidan ka ba? Me ya sa ka barta Sultan?" Tsakani da Allah yake magana.

Amma duk mutanan gidan suna mashi kallon munafuncin ne, Banda Sultan da yake ta rusunawa cikin ladabi.

Sarkin Bilyam ya cigaba da gaisawa da mutanan wajan, kafin aka nuna mashi mazaunin shi.

Sultan ya je ta shi karagar ya zauna, anan aka bawa Sultan damar fara magana, kasa cewa komai yayi an ɗauki lokaci kafin ya kalli mahukuntan yace "Ku na da labarin komai, za ku gabatar da komai da bayanan ku." Sam yasan idan yayi magana kamar yayi rashin ɗa'a ne.

Wani daga ciki ya fara bayani, Sarkin Bilyam baya da wata nutsuwa, bayan gama jawabi  aka bashi damar magana, Anan ya musa zargin da ake mashi na aurawa Sultan Aymana son son mayar da takobin su.

Ba su yadda ba hakan yasa aka kama jayayya, anan Sultan ne kawai zai raba wannan gardama, amma an saka shi a tsakiya bashi da ikon kare kowa.

Cikin mahukunta wani ya yi tsawa tare da faɗin "A bisa baya nai da muka gama daurara, Mai martaba Sultan ya na zartar da kukunci kamar yadda mahukunta suka yi, saboda haka Sarkin Bilyam zai fuskanci Hukunci na Tsayar da shi daga mulkin shi, haka kuma Sultan ya ƙasƙantar da masarautar shi, hukunci na ƙarshe auren da Sarkin Bilyam ya haɗ..."

Kafin ya ida Sultan ya yi gyaran murya, jin za a taɓa ɓangaren auren shi, ga ya har lokacin tsohon Sarki baiyi magana ba.

Sarkin Bilyam ya jinjina kai, cikin ƙunar zuciya, ya ɗan sunkuya ga mahukunta. "Haka kuma za a hukunta Aymana a cikin masarautar nan na tsawon loka..."

Wani irin huci Sarki yake yi, ya miƙe yana sunkuyawa gaban Sultan "Komai zai tafi kamar yadda ka tsara Sultan, Amma kafin nan ina neman izinin ganawa da Aymana, haka kuma na ɗauki hukuncin da ka yanke akan masarautar Bilyam."

Mai martaba zai yi magana Sultan yace "Ina neman Alfarma, zan gabatar da wata takarda gare ku, haka kuma ina son ganin Bafaɗen Yunus."

Sultan ya miƙa takarda maga takarda ya karanta, maga takarda ya karanta, Sarki Bilyam yayi mamaki, anan aka sheda cewar Baba Haroun shine ya bada saƙon ba mai marta ba ba.


Anan komai ya koma baya, aka fara tunanin me abin yi akan zaman, Mahukunta suka ce Lallai abasu lokaci zuwa marece a dawo zama.

Kowa ya tashi banda Sarkin Bilyam dake jingine, Sultan ya durƙusa gaban shi "Ina mai neman afuwanka, ba Ni da wani iko akan abinda ya faru."

"Sultan ka bani izinin ganawa da Aymana."

Sultan ya miƙe ya bada umarni, babu jimawa sai ga Jakadiyya da Aymana.

Aymana ta shigo jiki babu kwari, Jakadiyya ta juya, cikin sauri take nufar Mai martaba "Kar ki zo min nan Aymana, sam bana son ganin ki kum..."

Zubewa tayi ƙasa Sultan yayi saurin faɗin "Allah ya huci zuciyar ka, don Allah kar ka yi mummunar magana..."

"Aymana yaushe na saka ki aikata abinda kika aikata."

Zata fara magana Mai martaba ya fusata zai kai mata bugu da bayan hannu, cikin sauri Sultan ya jawo ta jikin shi, suna durƙushewa kasancewar dama a durƙushe yake.

Mai martaba ya kalli Sultan "Kasan abinda ka aikata kuwa, Sam bata cancanci zama tare da kai ba, a tunani na na haɗaku aure don ɗaukaka darajarta ashe, kaine take son zubarwa da mutuncin, Ni kuma ta tozarta Ni a idon duniya, ina mai baka umarnin barin Aymana tunda nine na haɗa su..."

Cikin tashin hankali Sultan ya kama bada haƙurin da sam baisan zai iya bayarwa ba.

"Don Allah Baba ka..."

"Ba na son ganin ki..."

Yayi maganar yana miƙewa, Sultan ya ɗagata yana ba Mai martaba haƙuri, amma ya fice ba tare da sauraron su ba.

Aymana ta rikice, tana kuka mai tsuma zuciya, wannan lokacin Shi kanshi ya karaya "Don Allah kaba Baba hakuri, wallahi ba zan iya rayuwa babu kai na, kaine jigo na, farin ciki na, don Allah kar a min hukunci ta hanyar rabamu."

Ta fashe da wani kukan tare da kallon shi "Sultan kana da dama, don Allah kar ka..."

"A'a Aymana, bana jayayya da hukuncin manya, tun lokacin Auran mu na sanar maki duk hukuncin da Baba ya kafa bana iya musu akai."

*Page 41*

Aymana ta fashe da kuka tare da ƙanƙame shi, wani irin ciwo zuciyarta take mata, tabbas ta san ko zata jure komai to banda nisantar Sultan dinta.

Hankalin Sultan kanshi ya tashi yanzu ya sakawa kan shi lallai tashin hankalin da ake zai iya taɓa lafiyar  Aymana da kuma yaron cikinta.

Ajiyar zuciya yayi "Ki tashi muje ciki, zan bawa Baba haƙura, sam Sultan ba zai taɓa rabuwa da ke ba."

Haka suka tashi Sultan babu nauyin mutanan gida haka ya wuce da Aymana a hannunshi har ɓangaren shi, yanzu ya sawa ranshi komai zai faru babu wanda zai kuma magana da Aymana don ba zai yadda wani abu ya same ta ba.

Ayda ce ta shigo falon, lokacin Aymana tana cikin ɗakin shi, yana tsaye yana kai kawo "Sultan zai buƙaci wani abu kuwa?"

Ɗagowa yayi babu wani annuri a fuskar shi, ya san ba don Allah take tambayar ba, haka kuma sam bata iya salon tambayar ba.

"Ba na buƙata."

"Me zai damu Sultan bayan Allah ya taimake ka, babu abinda ya faru, haka kuma bata fita da Mulkinka ba, tunda Ashirinta ya tonu sai..."

Tsawa ya daka mata, yana nuna mata hanyar fita, Ayda ta gyara mayafin kanta "Na san kana cikin ruɗu da ɓacin rai amm..."

Rufe idanuwanshi yayi "Na ce ki fita."

***

Gimbiya Ummi duk yadda ta so ganawa da Sultan bata samu hakan ba, hankalinta ya tashi ainun, ta yadda aka sanar da ita Aymana ta aikata laifi babba irin wannan.

Saboda Soyayyar da take mata sai ta ke ji aranta kamar ba gaske ba, ko da ta tabbatar abin ya faru hanyoyi take nema na wanke Aymana.

Ɗakin Gimbiya Maigado kuwa, farinciki fal zuciyar su, sun tabbatar koda ba a ce Sultan ya sauka mulkiba, idan aka raba auran to ya samu wani naƙasu a mulkinshi domin sun gama tabbatar da Aymana itace komai na shi.

***
Ƙarfe Hudu aka kuma wani zaman, mahukunta su ka yi jawabi sosai, wannan lokacin sun saka fahimta a cikin lamarin, kowane ɓangaren ya ƙara kare kanshi.

Tsohon Sarki ne ya tabbatar yana so a gabatar mashi da Baba Haroun da duk wani wanda yake da burin son mallakar Takobin, da sauran masu hannu a cikin saka Aymana hakan.

A iya bincike da sanin da Sultan yayi ya tabbatar idan har aka cika bincike, duk ilahirin 'ya 'ya da matan Sarkin Bilyam ba zasu tsira ba, hakan ya sa ya yi gyaran Murya tare da fara magana.

"Bi sa yarda da amincewar jawabai daga kowane ɓangare, Sultan yana mai wanke Sarkin Bilyam abisa zargin da ake mashi, haka kuma Masarautar Toro ta na buƙatar Baba Haroun a kan lokaci."

Sai da yayi jim kafin ya cigaba da magana ta hanyar kallon Tsohon sarki "Haka kuma ina mai nemarwa Sarkin Bilyam sassauci akan hukuncin da za akayi mashi, ya zama kamar yadda bashi da hannu a maganar mallakar takobin, shi ma kar laifin wani ya shafe shi, ina riƙon wanann Alfarmar Ya Adalin sarki."

Sarkin Bilyam ya fara sauke ajiyar zuciya, Mai martaba ya jima baiyi magana ba, zuwa can ya ce "Ko Sultan yana da wata maganar kuwa?"

Sai da ya duƙar da kai kafin ya ce "Akan hukuncin Aymana, ina so ayi duba tare da wanke ta, ganin cewar abinda ta aikata ba shine ƙudurinta ba, hakan kamar an saka mata karsashi ne da kuma horar da ita son aikata hakan, wanda ta aikata hakan ba cikin kwanciyar hankali ba."

Sultan ya ɗago sai lokacin ya ga hankalin kowa ya dawo kanshi, cikin sauri ya ce "Duk hukuncin da aka yanke akanta yayi, amma ina roƙar mata alfarma akan juna biyu da take dauke dashi, bayan ta haihu zata ɗauki duk horon da aka ba ta."

Mai martaba ya fara murmushin manya, ya kalli mahukunta "Duk abinda Sultan ya faɗa ba yana neman alfarma bane, yana yanke hukuncine a mulkin shi, Takobi ta shi ce, haka kuma shine yake da iko akan ta, jawabin shi anan ya gamsar da mu Sultan yayi afuwa ga Sarkin Bilyam da kuma Aymana shi, sai dai yana son zama da Baba Haroun, ya kuma tsayar da bincike akan abin."

Kowa na wajan ya jinjina maganar, tabbas kowa ya amince da hakan, Iyakar matsalar a wajan Waziri da Yarima Saifune sai suma Baba Maga yaƙi dake bayansu.

Sarkin Bilyam yayi godiya sosai. Ya kuma tabbatar zai gabatar da Baba Haroun cikin lokaci.

Gaba ɗaya aka kama jawabai da jan hankalin mutanen wajan akan illar rashin son juna da ke gudana a masarautun nahiyar su.

Sai da Sarkin Bilyam yayi jawabi akan hakanne suka ƙara tabbatar da kyawun zuciyar shi.

***
Baba Galadima ne ya shiga cikin gida wajan Mama zaune ya sameta tana girki, sai Farida dake gefe ta rafka tagumi, miƙewa tayi ta nufeshi cikin sauri tare da tambaya "Ya abin yake yanzu, wallahi na kasa samun nutsuwa."

Murmushi yayi yace "Karki damu, komai ta daidaita, kuma laifin bana Aymana bane da mahaifinta, laifi na wani yayan Sarkin Bilyam ne dake son zama karagar shi.

Ajiyar zuciya Mama tayi Farida kuwa bata san lokacin da ta matso wajan ba Mama ta ce "Alhamdulillah Allah muna godiya gareka."

Daɗi Farida ta ji "Wallahi hankalina ya tashi, na ɗauka Uwar ɗakina ba zata taɓa samun adalci ba."

Ta koma ta na ba Mama labarin irin Halin Baba Haroun shi kanshi Baba Galadima sai da yace "Haka kubar Mamaki ba gamu da irin suba a cikin mu."

"Lallai ne, Allah ya ganar dasu."

Amin suka amsa.

****
Fitar Sultan daga fada ɗakin Gimbiya Ummi ya nufa da gajiya sosai a tare da shi ya zauna yana sauke hular alkebba daga kanshi ya kalle ta, har lokacin bata yi magana ba, yana son gane wane yanayi ta ɗauki Aymana a yanzu.

"Kin ga abinda ta aikata ko, a tunaninta hukunci zai ƙetare kanta?"

Da sauri Gimbiya Ummi ta miƙe " Me kake faɗa Sultan? Ke nan zaka hukunta Ayaman, bayan naji cewar ba itace ta saka kanta ba, taya zaka bata hukunci, baka tausayin abin da ke cikinta."

Sultan ya miƙe tsaye "Na sanar hakan zai faru ne bayan ta haihu." Yayi maganar yana fara tattaki kamar zai fita.

Gimbiya Ummi ta ce "Tabbas idan ka hukunta Aymana zaka ga fushin zuciyata Sultan."

Da sauri ya juyo yana kallonta, sai yanzu ya tabbatar da gaske take, ya dawo ya zauna gabanta "Ina tuba gare ki, hakan ba zai faru ba da izinin Ubangijin musulunci."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi "Wannan dama rubutacce ne, sai hakan ya faru, amma ina so ka sani Aymana itace gatan ka Sultan, kar ka manta mace tana da rauni duk shekarunta."

Sultan ya ji da ɗin fahimtar da Gimbiya Ummi tayi, hakan yasa ya saki jiki, suka cigaba da tattaunawa akan maganar.

***

Ƙagare Sarkin Bilyam yake ya isa ida, tabbas sai ya nuna tsananin ɓacin ranshi akan mutanen gidan wannan lokacin ba zai bar su ba, ganin suna barazanar kawar da shi daga karagar shi.

Bai shiga ciki ba, sai da ya bada umarnin zaman gaggawa a fadar shi, hankalin kowa ya tashi, anan ya shiga faɗa masu ya ci darajar Sultanne da ba zai taɓa dawowa da rawanin shi ba, haka kuma za a kawar da sarautar daga hananun su tunda an tabbatar ba mutanen kirki ba ne.

Gida ya hargitse, Maza da mata sai shige da fice ake don lokacin ne suka samu labarin abinda Aymana ta aikata.

Umma ta ji takaici sosai tabbas tasan makircin mutanen gidanne ya yi tasiri akan Aymana.

Nene kuwa ta tausayawa Ɗanta zai lokacin tayi dana sanin goyon bayan mutanen gidan da tayi, musamman da taji cewar Baba Haroun yafi ƙarfi cikin al'amarin.

Kaka ta gallamata harara jin kalamanta Nene na dana sani "Tafi can, sai da gumu tayi kumu kika san da haka, da girman ki kika bigewa yara."

"Ni dai Kaka ayi man Afuwa."

Umma ta ce "Haba Nene ai wannan ba wani abu bane, Ni kaina sai da suka so jan ra'ayi na Allah ne ya taimake ni."

Hajiya Babba ce tayi sallama ɗakin Mama cikin sauri, ai kuwa ta sameta tana tana yane mayafi "Dama yanzu zani wajan ki."

"To hutas. Gani da kaina, kinji abinda ya faru?"

Mama ta ce "Kinga sai da yarinyar nan ta kusa jefa m..."

Hajiya Maigado tayi dariya "Da Allah rabu da su, ashe Baba Haroun munafuki ne, mulkin da Yarana su ke so shi ma shi ya ke so."

"Allah ya ƙara ai gashi inda ta kai shi." Cewar Mama.

Hajiya Maigado ta lumafasa "Ai da yardar Allah ya tafi kenan, hukunci zasuyi mashi mai tsanani."

"Yanzu ita ina Aymana, nasan dai koba komai zata ɗan-ɗana zawarci."

Jinjina kai Hajiya Maigado tayi "Ke wannan Son da Sultan yake mata ai ba zai iya ba, cikin mutanen da sukace wani yaban labari a gaban fada Sultan ya wanketa."

***
Jakadiya ce duƙe gaba Ayda da salon gulmarta take sanar da ita Sultan ya nemi a yafewa Aymana laifinta kamar yadda ta ji labari.

La ƙaramin tashin hankali Ayda ta shigaba, ta buga tebur ɗin gaban ta "Wai sai yaushe Sultan zai bani yanci na, sai yanzu sihirin Aymana zai barshi? Yanzu ace duk girman Laifin data Aikata hakan baiyi tasiri ba."

Jakadiya ta sunne kai "Allah ya baki nasara, farko na ɗauka horata yake lokacin da ya saka ni tsaronta, amma yanzu na gane ta na ƙasa ta na dabo!"

Ayda ta kiƙe tsaye ta fara tattaki "Lallai ganin gida kare yakan zagi kura, amma a daji sai gudu sai tuba!"

***

Da tire ɗin Abinci Jakadiyya ta shiga, Aymana tana zaune abinta sai kiran mutanen gidan su dake shigowa amma ta kasa ɗaukar wayar.

Da sallama Jakadiyya ta shigo, ta ajiye kwanikan abinci ta rusuna tare da faɗin "Allah ya baki nasara, abincin ki ya kammala."

Aymana ta kawar da kanta "Bana buƙata."

"Allah ya huci zuciyar ki."

Wayarta ta kuma ruri Aymana ta wurgar da ita tana  jan tsaki, Jakadiyya ta fahimci bata cikin nutsuwa, cikin son fara sanar da ita Sultan yayi mata afuwa ta ce "Allah ya ja kwanan ki, Mamallakan gidan kan faɗa tunanin rashin wani abu a cikin Mahaifiyar Magajin gobe."

Aymana ta kalleta Jakadiya ta yi shu'umin murmushi ta ci gaba "Sai dai fa magauta suyi haƙuri amma na gaba yayi gaba, dumun kuwa kin zama wuƙar figar kura, ba nauyi sai kaifi."

"Ba na son kalamin komai Jakadiya."

Jakadiya ta matsa ta zauna ƙasan kafet ta ce "Har da daddaɗan labari, To bari na naɗe labari na, zai yu ba nice zan sanar dake kin sama ƙadangaren bakin tulu ba."

Tana shirin miƙewa Aymana ta ce "Dakata!"

Da murna ta zauna "Me kike tafe da shi?"

"Sultan ya wanke Sarkin Bilyam da ga laifi, ya kuma nemar mashi afuwa akan hukuncin da za ayi mashi, san nan kuma ya banbanta Uwar gidan shi da sauran 'yan gaɗar bayan fage."

Aymana ta gyara zama "Ban fahimceki ba."

"Sultan ya hana hukunta Gimbiya, haka kuma ya ..."

Kafin ta ida Aymana ta miƙe tsaye ta fara kai kawo, wani sanyi ya shigeta, da mamakin irin soyayyar da Sultan ya ke mata, a iya saninta babu wanda zai aikata wanann laifin bai saka an bashi azama mafi tsanani ba.

Da murmushi Aymana ta juyo, tana sun canza Jakadiyya da kuma dai do da ita bayan ta, ta ce "Na ji daɗin labarin ki, har na rasa me zan baki ladar labari mai daɗi."

"Allah ya taimake ki, Aike mai bayar wa ce kuma..."

Kafin ta ida Aymana ta kai hannu kunnuwanta, ta fara jire 'yan kunnan ta sake salƙi na tsadadden Zinari, ta fitar da duka biyun, ta duƙa kan Jakadiyya tare da miƙa mata "Uwar masu gida wannan naki ne."

Cikin ruɗewa Jakadiyya ta amsa ta fara godiya, tana durgushewa.

Aymana ta kalleta "Za ki iya tafiya."

Tana fita Aymana ta miƙe ta yi saurin shiga ɗakin Sultan, banɗaki ta faɗa ta fara shirin ta, yanzu bata so gogan nata ya sameta da kayan da ya barta, ko ba komai ya zama dole ya nuna mishi jin daɗi da farin cikinta.

Doguwar rigar wani yadi mara nauyi ta saka, rigar ta sha adon duwatsu sai walainiya suke ta kimtsa jikinta ta fesa turarukan ta.

Ta sako gashin kanta da yasha gyara, sam bata tunanin zata ci komai ba tare da Sultan ya shigo ba.

Cikin Sa'a kuwa ta jiyo ana mashi sannu da shigowa, haka yasa ta yi saurin fitowa.

Yana shigowa aka ja ƙofa aka rufe.

Da tafiyar shi a hankali ya shigo, Aymana ta yi tsaye tana kallon shi, ya aje sandar gayun dake hannun shi, ya fitar da Alkebba tare da ajewa kan kujera, ya fara warware rawanin shi.

Cikin Sauri Aymana ta matso wajen tana saurin riƙe hannun shi "Babban Sarki kamar Sultan bai kamaci samun kanshi da wahalar da gabbanshi ba, dole Sultan ya kasance yana da hadimai da kuma mahidimta."

Tayi maganar tana ida warware rawanin ta aje gefe, tasa hannu ta kwantar da sumar kan shi, tare da ɗago babbar rigar shi tana cire wa "Wannan mahidimta dole su zamo makusanta, haka kuma  dole su zamo masu sadaukarwa kamar uban gidansu."

Ta ajiye Babbar rigar, ta kama hannunshi ta cire agogon ta duba agogon "Tabbas lokaci baya adalci tunda har baya komawa baya, ta yadda zai wanke gurɓatattun abubuwan da suka faru a cikin sa."

Sultan ya sauke ajiyar zuciya, Aymana ta kama hannun shi, ta fara cire links  ɗin hannun kafin ta koma kan maɓallin gaban rigar shi "Na so ace lokaci zai yi adalci kamar yadda sarki Sultan ya kasance mai adalci, ta yadda yake afuwa ga duk girman laifin da aka aikata mashi."

Ta kalli fuskar shi "akwai kalamai manya-manya amma sun zamo masu ƙanƙanta wajan yin godiya, tare da ban haƙuri zuwa ga Sultan."

Ta mayar da Hannunta ta dafa kafaɗar shi, ta fara murmura idanuwanta, ta fara neman hawaye cikin salon kissa da kuma tsumuwar zuciya, hawaye suka tara sharara Sultan ya fara jin bugawar zuciyar shi yana ƙaruwa.

Ga kalamanta cikin salo da hikimar sanyaya zuciya, ta aza kanta akan ƙirjin shi "Nasa Sultan zai yi fushi da Gimbiyar sa, amma don Allah kayi afuwa gare ni, ba a irin wannan lokacin ba, ina mai tuba gare ka."

A karo na farko da hakuri ya fito bakinta, a hankali Sultan ya fara shafa gashin kanta, hakan da Aymana taji ya tabbatar mata da zuciyar shi tayi sanyi, saboda Izza irin ta Sultan har lokacin ya kasa ɗaga baki yayi magana.

Harɗe shi tayi ta rungumeshi tare da matsewa Sultan Ya ce "Aymana!"

Aymana ta lafe jikin shi "Na yadda na amince, babu wani mamallaki ga TAKOBIN sai kai Sultan, ban taɓaji a jikina zata amfanu ga kowa bayan kai ba, lallai kaine kake da iko da ita, Mulkin ka ne, Izzarka ce, sarautar ka ce, kai ne kake da iko akan ta."

Ajiyar zuciya ya sauke baiyi magana ba, ya duƙa ya ɗago fuskarta, ya kai mata sumbata a goshi, ya saka Hannuwanshi ya ƙara rungumarta da ƙarfi, ya kai bakin shi a nata yana zura harshen shi, wata irin sumba yake mata da shafar wuyanta, Aymana ta rufe idanuwanta dake da kwanciyar hawaye, ya janye bakin shi ya fiddo harshen shi ya na goge mata hayen ta hanyar lashe wa da tsinin harshen shi.
