*Page 42*

Washe gari gidan komai ya lafa musu, hankalin kowane ɓangare ya kwanta musamman masoyan Aymana da Sultan, iya ɓangaren Ayda da Hajiya Mai gado ne suke nasu ƙumbiya ƙumbiyar.

Aymana kuwa a dakewar Izza ta fito, ta sha gaisuwa ga kowa, Farida kuwa murna kawai ta ke Uwar ɗakinta ta fito.

Aymana bata bawa kowa fuskar ta da zance ba, Sai dai kuma tana jin kunyar zuwa ɓangaren Gimbiya Ummi, lokacin da ta je tayi tunanin samun sauyi, amma saboda dattako irin na Ummi ko nuna hakan bata yi ba.

Bayan ya dawo ne ta shirya rubutun ban haƙuri zuwa ga Mai martaba, ya ji daɗi sosai kuma ya samu nutsuwa, sai dai bai mai da mata wata amsa ba iya soƙon gaisuwa ya faɗa mata.

Washe gari aka gabatar da Baba Haroun ga Masarautar Toro, ananne zai ƙarɓi hukuncin shi, na laifin abinda ya saka Aymana ta aikata.

***

Lokaci ya fara tafiya, komai ya dai-daita, watannin Haihuwar Ayda yayi, hakan yasa duk suke murnar Magajin Sultan.

Aymana kuwa cikinta yayi girma ya fito, har tana jin nauyin yawo a gidan.

Yau tana zaune akan kafet ta miƙe ƙafafuwanta da wani kwanon abinci gabanta, Sultan ya shigo da wasu fadawa bayan shi, da kayyayaki, suka ajiye tare da gaida ita suka juya.

Dariya ya zauna yana mata, Aymana ta juyar da kanta gefe, Sultan ya durƙusa gabanta ya saka hannu yana shafa cikinta, ta ture hannun tana faɗin "Ka barni kawai, ji fa yadda nake ta cin abinci kamai wata rugiya."

Zama yayi kusa da ita "Ni banga wani cin abincin da kike ba, har yanzu babu wata ƙiba da kika yi."

Aymana ta dafa zata miƙe, Sultan ya kamota, suna yin hanyar ciki, Jakadiyya ta turo cikin sauri, Sultan ya ja ya tsaya, yana ɗan sakin hannun Aymana daya riƙe.

"Barka da Wannan lokacin Sarkin sarakuna, na zo sanar da kai, Gimbiya Ayda ta sauka."

Cikin sauri Aymana ta juyo tare da faɗuwar gaba, Sultan ya daidaita nutsuwar shi yana nuna murnar shi, wanda bai nuna a lokacin haihuwar Abul na ya ce "Alhamdulillah Jakadiyya a sanar Sultan yana zuwa."

Aymana ta kalli Jakadiyya "Me aka samu?"

Duƙar da kai Jakaddiya tayi, Sai lokacin Sultan ya tuna bai ma tambaya ba, Ya yi tattaki zuwa gare ta, Jakadiyya ta ƙara rusunawa "Budurwa aka samu, Allah ya taimake ki."

Sultan ya yi hanyar fita, Jakadiyya ta bi shi baya, Aymana ta koma ciki don canza kayan jikinta, tare da taya Ayda murna. Tayiwa kanta Addu'a itama ta sauka lafiya.

Kowa yana ɗakin Ayda, ashe lokacin ma har an shirya ta an gyra ko ina.

GIMBIYA Maigado tana zaune saman kujera, da jaririya a hannunta, Goggo ta gefe, Jakadiyya da Sultan suka shigo.

Gaishe su ya fara yi, ya koma wajan Gimbiya Mai gado ya zauna, yana bin yarinyar da kallo, Gimbiya Mai gado ta miƙa mashi da 'yar munafukar dariyarta.

Sultan ya amsa da murnarshi, ya kalli yadda aka yiwa yarinyar Ado, ya azata a kafaɗar shi, dai dai lokacin Aymana ta shigo tana tafiya a hankali.

Duk suka bita da kallo, ta rusuna ta gaishe da su Goggo kafin ta kalli Gimbiya mai gado dakewa Sultan wani irin kallo, hakan ya ɓata ranta.

Tsaye tayi bayan kujerar da Sultan yake ta sa hannu tana shafa kan yarinyar Gimbiya Ummi ta shigo da wasu kuyangi suna Binta, tayi mamakin ganin Sultan a wajan.

Gimbiya Ummi ta yi masu sannu tana Barka, ta kalli Sultan ta ce "Allah ya taimake ka, ko ka manta akwai masu buƙatar ganin jaririyar ne."

Murmushi yayi ya jawo hannun Aymana ta zauna kujerar jefe, kafin ya mayar da hankalin shi akan jaririyar, ya duƙar da kanshi yana mata addu'o'i.

Tsawon lokaci kafin ya bawa Aymana yarinyar, Dai-dai lokacin Ayda ta fito ta tsaya tana jingina da bango kawai sai ta saka kuka.

Gaba ɗaya aka juyo ana kallonta, tare da tambayar ko lafiya "Yanzu duk burin da na ci akan samun Namiji hakan bai samu ba, Allah ya gani b..."

Sultan ya miƙe tsaye ya kalli Jakadiyya tare da faɗin "Jakadiyya akwai tukuicin sanar dani samun ƙaruwata da kika yi, haka kuma ga duk hadiman gidan nan na gabatar da wani sabon tsari saboda murnar zuwan 'yata a duniya."

Ya matsa a hankali ya kalli Ayda "Kina da tuƙuicin sulallar zinarin, akwai kambu dana tanadar miki, na gabatar da Alkabba sabi guda ishirin gare ki."

Ya juya ya kana ɗan nazari kafin ya kamo hannunta "Ina farin cikin samun ƙaruwa, mai zai saka ki kuka, duk sauran lokutan ina bari ana maki tukuici ne, Amma wannan lokacin Sultan da kanshi, sannan ina son ki kuma zaɓar wani abun don tuƙuicinki."

Kowa na wajan yayi mamakin Sultan, amma ban da Aymana da ta riga ta harbo jirgin shi, baya so lokacin da zata haihu ace ya nuna bambanci kenan.

Ayda ta fara murmushi, ko ba komai yau Sultan zai ɗaga tata darajar kamar yadda yakewa Aymana.

Ta ce "Ina son Tukuicin wata sarauta daga gare ka."

Sai da yayi shiru kafin ya fara tunani, tana son yin amfani da damar ne don ta ɗaga darajar kanta.

Hakan ya sa ya ce "Sultan zai yi tunani akan hakan."

Cikin Sauri ya sunkuya yana yiwa su Gambiya bankwana, Gimbiya Ummi azuciyarta tana tunanin ko da wane hankalin zata riƙe wata sarauta.

Bayan Aymana ta koma sashenta, haka ta haɗa kaya na gani na faɗa aka kaiwa Ayda da jaririyarta.

Sultan ma nashi kayan daban suke, wanda ko lokacin haihuwar Abul bai mata ba.

Gimbiya Ummi kuwa turamen  atamfofi da turaruka ta bada.


Waziri kuwa tunda aka sanar Ayda mace ta haifa ya kasa zaune balle tsaye, daga ƙarshe ya yanke shawarar zuwa wajan Bokanyar shi don  shaida mata lallai kar Aymana ta haihu lafiya, in kuma har zata haihu to ya kasance mace itama zata haifa.

Yana gama bayanin shi Bokanya ta ce "So nawa zan sanar da kai, bana ganin komai idan na zo duba taurarun yarinyar nan."

"Me abin yi?"

"Sai dai ayi duk yadda za'ayi ka kawar da cikin shi ne kawai."

Waziri yayi dariya "Ni dama hakan na fi so."

Daga wajan Bokanyar ya wuce don ganawa da Hajiya Mai gado, yana gama yi mata bayanin yadda yayi da bokanya akan kar Aymana ta haihu don yana son duk daɗewa Yarima Saifu ya hau karaga.

Wani kallo Gimbiya Mai gado tayi mashi, tasan sarai yaƙin shi akan kan shi ne ba su ba hakan ya sa tace "Ni kaina na sa ayi komai, kuma an tabbatar min Aymana ba zata taɓa haihuwar Namiji ba balle."

Farida dake tsaye bakin ƙofa, ta yi saurin barin wajan cikin sanɗa, hankali tashe ta isa ga Aymana.

Ta durƙusa tana haki, Aymana ta kalleta "Lafiya kuwa."

"Na ji abinda ya firgita ni ya uwar ɗakina."

Aymana ta riƙota, Farida ta fara hawaye tare da faɗin "Ba na son abinda zai wargaza rayuwarki Ranki shi daɗe, da ke na saba rayuwa, hakan yasa bana son ganin za a cutar da ke."

Cikin son jin abinda ke faruwa take "Ki sanar dani."

Tana shasshekar kuka, ta bata labarin duk abinda taji Waziri da Gimbiya mai gado suke tattaunawa.

Hankalin Aymana ya tashi, ta kalli Farida "Kar ki damu, ki tafi, da yardar mahaliccin mu, babu abinda zai same ni."

Farida ta miƙe ta fice, Aymana ta saka hannu ta dafa cikinta ta fara Addu'a "Ya Allah kar ka ɗorasu akanmu, ya Allah ka kuɓutar dani da abinda nake ɗauke, Allah kar ka saka wahala acikin rayuwar bayinka."

Haka ta share hawayen da suka zubar mata, koda Sultan ya dawo ya fahimci akwai damuwa a tare da ita, amma ta kasa sanar dashi,

Sai bayan nan ne ta daure ta faɗa mashi, don tana so shima ya yi mata Addu'a.

***

Ranar suna kamar wasa mutanen gidan suka tsunkayi, sunan Innar Ayda Sultan ya sakawa yarinyar amma zasu rinƙa kiranta Khair.

Kowa ya kama maganganu akan duk makircin Aymana, abinda basu sani ba wannan lokacin Aymana ta kanta take, shiyasa komai ya suɓuce mata.

Kwarya kwaryar liyafa aka haɗa da wasannin gargajiya, ga masu kiɗan kwarya, Aymana bata zura jikinta ba sosai daga ɗakinta ne ta rinƙa aikawa da kyaututtuka ga masu gabatar da wasannin.

***
Lokaci yana tafiya Aymana da Sultan sun dage Addu'o'in akan cikinta da kuma nemarwa kansu kariya.

Amma duk da haka Sultan ya na nuna soyayya mai tsanani ga Khairat da Abul, wanda Abul a yanzu ya ƙara wayo sai dai duk da haka ɗabi'un yaron sunsha banban da sauran yara masu lafiya. Sultan yana tausayin yaron sosai.

Mai martaba ya samu nutsuwa ganin komai ya lafawa Sultan, Gimbiya Ummi kuwa yanzu ta mayar da hankali wajan tanadar kayayyakin tarar haihuwar Aymana.

Haka daga gidan su Aymana sun kawo kayan tarar jariri na kalar al'adunsu, wanda mutanen gidan suka sha mamaki, sai dai sun ganin ita kanta Aymana tana wasa da dukiya ashe ta samo hakanne daga Izzar gidan su.

Ƙawarta Ruƙayya ta kawo masu ziyara saboda ta zo Najeriya daga Saudiyya, Aymana ta s an karramata fiye da yadda ta karramasu a Madina.


Ruƙayya ta kalleta tace "Wai baki ji a jikin ko kina gab haihuwa, Ni fa kallon da nake maki ba zaki kai wani lokaci ba."

Aymana ta ɗan cije leɓo ta zata miƙe Sultan ya shigo, da sauri yazo yana kamata, ya kalli Ruƙayya "Ki na kallon ta sai ta faɗi kum..."

Dariya Rukkya tayi "Allah ya taimake ka, ai hakan ma motsa jini ne."

Ɗan guntun tsaki Sultan yayi "Likitocin nan kuna da naku matsalar, yanzu idan ta ji ciwo zaku koma kuna faɗan me yasa aka barta."

Zata kuma yin Magana, Aymana ta ƙabta mata ido, tana saka hannu abaki alamar tayi shiru, tasan cewar Sultan indai akan kula da ita ne ba zai yadda da zancen da zata kawo mashi ba.

Sai da yaga ta koma kan kujera, kafin ya sakar mata hannu, Aymana ta yi murmushi.

Ruƙayya ta ce "Ni kam bari na bar masu waje, Allah ya taimakeka."

Zama yayi ya jawo Aymana ya ɗorata a kafaɗar shi, yana shafa bayanta, Aymana ta ce "Ka shiga ka watsa ruwa naga lokacin salla ya kusa."

Sultan ya mata sumba a kumatu, ya miƙe ya nufi ciki, Ruƙayya ta ruƙe baki "Wallahi ni a tunani na matan sarakuna haƙuri kawai suke, tab! Musamman Sultan yadda yake faɗi yana cika yana batsewa a waje."

Dariya Aymana tayi bata ce komai ba, Ruƙayya tace "Allah ya fi duk sauran sarakuna Nuna Izza."

Aymana ta kalli Ruƙayya zatayi magana, Ruƙayya ta katseta "Wai kuwa yana ma barinki hutawa."

Harara Aymana tayi mata "Yaushe zaki koma?"

"Na gaya maki, shi ga ya tafi Ni ce nace gaskiya sai na ƙara hutawa a ƙasa ta."

Daɗi Aymana ta ji tace "Yauwa Ruƙayya Kinga sai kiyi zaman ki nan abin ki, har ki tashi komawa."

Zaro ido Rukkayya tayi "don me, Allah ya rufamin Asiri, Ni ban saba zaman ƙasaita ba."

Shiru Aymana tayi, Wannan itace kawai damar da take da ita wajan gujewa mutanan gidan, domin kuwa sam bata so ace sune zasu karɓi haihuwata.

Nan Aymana ta yiwa Rukkayya bayanin komai, akan ta zauna idan ta haihu sai ta tafi, Rukkayya ta ji tausayin Aymana tace "Shi kenan zance gida in ɗauki kaya zuwa gobe sai in dawo."

"Duk abin buƙatar ki akwai, kawai kiyi waya ki sanar."

Ajiyar zuciya Ruƙayya tayi "Shi kenan ba damuwa."

Aymana ta fara mata godiya, Rukkayya ta yi mamaki sosai, lallai Aymana tayi hankali ta kuma ƙara sanin rayuwa, saɓanin lokacin da suna makaranta Izza tana bibiyar jinin ta.

Cikin ɗakunan ɓangarenta ta aje ya, bayan ta gama gayawa Sultan ƙudirinta, ya amince sosai, haka ya zauna shida Rukkaya suka shirya duk abin buƙata na karɓar haihuwa.

***

Aymana a tsaitsaye ta fara ciwo, da kanta ta gane naƙuda ce take yi, ta samu Rukkayya zaune tana kallo  tace "Likita ina jin ba daɗi fa."

Dariya Rukkayya tayi tace "muje ciki."

Sai lokacin ma kula da yadda aka gyara wani ɗaki kamar asibiti harda gadon amsar haihuwa suka haɗa a ciki, Aymana ta zauna Rukkayya ta dubata ta ce "Dalla malama da saura."

Aymana ta ta shi zaune tana komawa kan kujera "bani so in sha wahala ne."

Wata irin Dariya ta ba Rukkayya, saboda Ruƙayya haihuwarta biyu "Ah! Hajiya ba wahala fa, kawai daga nan zuwa gobe inshaallah kina riƙe da jaririya."

Tayi maganar yana duba Agogo lokacin ƙarfe bakwai na yamma, Haka suka fito suka koma zaman su, wajan goma na dare Aymana ta fara cije-cijen leɓo.

Hakan yasa ta sanar da Farida kar wanda ya kuma shigowa, Farida ta ɗan fahimci wani abu sai dai tana gudun ta yi tambaya hakan ya zama laifi.

Sultan ya shigo yi masu bankwana zai tafi turakarshi, ya sameta ta rufe ido tana cije loɓo, hakan ya ɗaga hankalin shi.

Sai dai Aymana tana ganin shi ta kawar da komai tare da daurewa, da kanshi ya kira Ruƙayya yana tambayarta ko akwai wata matsala.

Aymana ta mata nuni akan tace babu "Kin tabbatar Ruƙayya?"

Rukkayya ta juya ta bar wajan ganin yana niyar haɗe fuskar shi da ta Aymana, Aymana ta yi murmushi, Sultan ya sumbashi hannunta ya kuma yi mata Sumba akan bakinta.

Cikin Sauri ta riƙo leɓonshi tana ɗan cizawa, ƙam yabarta, ta ci gaba da tsotse leɓon, ta ciza da ƙarfi kafin ta saki Sultan ya kalle ta "Shi ke nan har kin gama?"

Dariya tayi "Allah ya taimake ka."

Ya kalli inda Rukkayya take tsaye zai yi magana yaga bata nan, ya kuma kiranta tare da miƙewa tsaye ya na tattaki "Wa ya baki izinin tafiya?"

Aymana ta zaro ido, jin zai gudanar da Mulki akan ƙawarta, bayan kuma taimakonta tazo yi.

Rukkayya ta ɗan yi shiru, tana kallon shi, ta fahimci Izza ta ziyarci jinin shi.

Ya juyo Aymana ta ce "Allah ya huci zuciyar Sultan, Allah ya saka sanyi a zuciyar Sarkin sarakuna."

Murmushi ya yi ya kalli Ruƙayya, sai yaga ta sunkuyar da kai, sai lokacin yaga rashin dacewar abinda zai aikata, wata zuciyar ta shi ta bawa Ruƙayya laifi tunda har bai bata izinin tafiya ba, haka kuma ita ma bata nemi izinin ba.

Dariya yayi ya ce "Rukkayya!"

"Ina tuba." Ta faɗa.

Da 'yar dariya ya ce "waya ce maki ana gudanar da komai ba tare da izinin ba, an yafe maki darajar abinda kawarki take ɗauke."

Itama dariya tayi, Aymana tace "Kar ka ja ta gudu ta bar mu."

"Ai bata fara ba, in kuma ta aikata zata karɓi hukuncinta."

"Yau na shiga Ukku!" Cewar Rukkaya, Sultan ya saka dariya "Zan barku, zuwa safe zan dawo, Akwai wata likita dana tuntuɓa na sanar da ita, zaki samu taimakonta idan buƙatar hakan ta taso."

Yayi maganar yana shigewa wata ƙofa.

Rukkayya ta riƙe baki, tana kallon Aymana wadda lokacin ta ƙara cije leɓo, saboda daurewa kawai take dama, ta ce "A'a wallahi bani iyawa, haka kawai, Kiji yadda ya rikiɗe zai nuna Izza akaina, tafiyata zan yi, ƙara da ya tuntuɓi wata likitar ƙila ita ta ɗaure."

Dariya Ruƙayya ta bawa Aymana, ta kalleta ta ce "Haba! haba! Idan kin barni me ki ka yi kenan, ki jira ki ida ladar ki."

Tayi maganar tana miƙewa suka nufi ɗaki don kwantawa sai dai Ruƙayya bata barta ita ɗaya ba gudun wata matsala.

Ƙarfe biyu da 'yan daƙiƙu, Sultan yayi saurin farkawa daga baccin, yasa hannu ya dafe kanshi tare da karanto Addu'o'in kariya, ya miƙe yana kallon Ayda da ta ke gefen shi, Khairat tana cikin gadon jarirai.

Ya faɗa banɗaki yayi alwala, ya fito, ya canza jallabiya yanayin shigar larabawa, ya ɗauki wayar shi, ya buɗe ƙofa, yana son ganin Aymana ko don tabbatar da lafiyarta, hakan ya sa yabi ta ƙofofin baya ya shiga sashenta.

Ɗakinta ya duba bai sameta ba, ya ɗan kwankwasa ɗakin da Rukkayya ta sauka, ganin bata nan hakan yasa hankalinshi ya tashi ya nufi ɗakin da suka shirya don haihuwar Aymana.

Har zai kwankwasa sai yaga kamar hakan zai ɓata lokacin shi, da sauri Ruƙayya ta kalli ƙofa, Sultan ya nufi bakin gadon wajan da Aymana take nishi.

Tana ganin shi ta kawar da kanta gefe, Sultan ya kalli Ruƙayya "Me ke faruwa?"

"Allah shi taimakeka, ta na gab haihuwa da yardar Allah."

Ta yi maganar tana mayar da safar hannu ta likitoci, Sultan ya kamo hannun Aymana, lokacin tana dafe mararta, Ruƙayya tayi saurin gyarata, Sultan ya kalli ta "Ah Rukkaya Kiyi a hankali fa.

Shiru tayi ta cigaba da aikin ta, Aymana ta fara jin ciwo ya canza mata, lokacin ta fara wata irin zufa, duk yadda ta daure kar tayi magana sai da ta saki cizon da takewa harshenta tare da fara salati da ƙarfin murya.

Bata ida ba Sultan ya daɗe mata baki "Ba zaki mutu ki barni ba insha All..."

"Yauwa Aymana ki ƙara."

Sultan ya kai idanuwanshi kan jikin Aymana, cikin sauri ya ɗauke idanuwanshi, ganin yadda yanayin wajan ya canza ga yaro yana niyar fitowa, neman kwace hannunshi yayi don yaga tashin hankali.

Sai lokacin ya tabbatar da jan riƙon da Aymana tayi mashi ba za ya iya ba.

Ƙasa-ƙasa Aymana ta ce "Rukkaya ki ƙarani ina jin bazan iya ba kar ba ji ciw woo." Ta ƙarashe maganar tare da Sako Addu'o'i a zuciyarta.

Innalillahi Wa inna ilaihi raji'un Sultan yake furtawa, Aymana ta ja dogon nishi, Rukkayya tayi saurin cigaba da aikin ta.

Idanuwan Sultan a rufe, ga gumi yana zubar mashi.

Rukkayya ta ida ɗago abinda Aymana ta haifa, Aymana ta yi laƙas tana jin yadda jikinta yake komawa.

"Alhamdulillah Alhamdulillah." take faɗi.

Rukkayya ta fara nemar abin buƙata wajan raba Aymana da abinda ta haifa, Ruƙayya ta yanke cibi, ta Kalli Aymana Sai lokacin ta ga Aymana hankalinta yana kan Sultan data riƙe shi kuma ya kifa kanshi da gadon yana sauraronta.

Hawaye kebin idanuwanta, ta gayara komai ta jijjiga jaririn tana kallon Namiji ne aka haifa, wani daɗi ta ji ta fara faɗin "Aymana! Aymana!"

"Kin haihu fa."

Da murmushi ta juyo, daidai lokacin Sultan ya ɗago sai lokacin yaji ya iya raba hannunshi da nata.

"Ko da ban taɓa ɗanɗana ciwon nan ba, Rukkaya ba sai kin sanar dani na Haihuwa ba."

Sai da ta kuma jijjigashi, har Sultan ya matso zai tureta ganin kamar bata tausayin yaron kawai sai yaji yaron ya kwalla kuka.

Murmushi ya farayi, Ruƙayya ta miƙa mashi ta ce "Ka san me muka samu kuwa?"

Aymana tana jin gabanta yana dukan tara-tara tayi ƙaƙarin miƙewa ta kasa saboda rashin ƙarfi, Sultan ya ce "Me aka samu Rukkayya."

"Na miji."

Cikin sauri ya ƙara manna yaron a jikinshi ya ce "Magajin gobe."

Aymana ta rufe idanuwanta, Tana Hamdala ga mahaliccinta, tare da Addu'a kana tsari ga yaron.

Rukkaya tace "Bari nazo na dubaki."

"A kibarni a kwance, kin barni a haka."

"Ina ta yaro na ne."

Ta kalleta tana kaɗa kai, yanzu tana so taga yaron, Rukkayya ta ce "Lafiya lau, babu matsala jikin ki, muje ban ɗaki na ida aikina.

Duk ire-iren farin ciki da na riska a rayuwata, bana jin akwai kwatankwacin wannan, tabbas ina godiya ga mahalinccinmu, Allah yayi muku Albarka, Allah ya kare man ku, ya kawar da idanuwan basu sharri akan ku."

"Ameen ya amsa."

Tsawon mintuna, talatin suka fito, Aymana ta ɗan samu sauƙi-Sauƙi ta samu gashin jiki sosai.

Sultan kuwa ya aje yaron a gadon jarirai yana haɗa shayi a kofi.

Dariya Ruƙayya tayi "Allah ya baka nasara, ba zaka jira na ida aiki na ba."

"Ya ga kamar zaki ci tukuici da yawa shiysa ya kama maki." Cewar Aymana.

Rukkayya ta je ta ɗauko shi ta kawowa Aymana don fara bashi ruwan madarar farko da ke jikinta.

Ruƙayya ta ce "Waye zai sanar da su?"

"Bar su gari ya kara haske, Jakadiyya zaki faɗawa."

Haka kuwa akayi sai da suka bari bakwai na safiya, kafin suka sanar da Haihuwar Aymana, hakan ya jawo hankalin duk mutanen gidan, aka nufi sashen da son ganin abinda aka samu.

Toapa anan fa duk hakalin mahassada ya tashi, Gimbiya Mai gado kamar zata yi hauka, duk yadda taso ɓoyewa abin ya faskareta, dai juye-juyen maganganu take, Mama kuwa harda rawarta ta ce "Ashe Magaji yana zuwa shi ya sa na kasa bacci yau."

Kuyangi da Bayi suka ringa tururuwa wajan shigowa kowa yana nuna murnarshi, Farida kuwa ta kasa zama murna kamar zata mayar da yaron jikinta.

Aymana bakinta ya mutu bata ma son kallon su saboda kunya, Ruƙayya ce kawai ta ce "Yauwa Mama ƙara ki gasa mana ita da kyau."

Mama ta na shirin miƙewa Jakadiyya ta turo ƙofa tana kirari ga Sultan, hakan ya tabbatar da Sultan ne zai shigo.

Sanye da alkebba da wani rawani launin tsanwa mai cizawa Ya ɗan tsaya tare da gaishe da su Gimbiya Mai gado da Mama, Barka sukayi mashi ya zauna kujerar nesa dasu, Jakadiyya ta yi gaggawar zuwa ta anshi jaririn don bawa Sultan, tana rawar jiki atunaninta ta zo ta ɗaya wajan sanar da shi.

Amsar yaron yayi ya kalli Aymana sai lokacin yaga kamar Yaron yafi kama da ita, musamman dogon hancin ta, murmushi yayi ba tare da yi magana ba, ya kuma yiwa yaron Addu'o'i.

Aymana ta kalli Mama ta ce "Har yanzu banga Mama ba?"

"Ta na hanyar zuwa ita na bari da kanta take nuna yadda za a haɗa maki kayan wankan."

Aymana zatayi magana Ayda ta shigo da saurinta, ganin Sultan riƙe da yaron hakan yasa ta ja ta tsaya,  Mama tace "Ga fa iyayen yaron nan."

Da son tabbatar da Namiji ne, ta isa gaban Sultan, bata san lokacin data jefa tambaya ba "Namiji ne?"

"Kwarai kuwa." Cewar Mama tana nazarinta.

Murmushi kawai Aymana ta yi Sultan ya kalli Ayda yana mata nuni ta zauna gefen shi, tana zama ya aza mata yaron, kasa tallabewa tayi, shi kuma bai saki ba, ji tayi yana ƙara aza mata, cikin sauri ta dawo hankalinta tana riƙewa, sam ta kasa koda murmushin munafunci ne.

Har Sultan zai fara tattaki zuwa ciki, Mama ta ce "Ina tunanin Gimbiya Ummi ce zata shigo naji muryar Aisha."

Aymana ta kalle su "Ku mayar da wannan zanin, don ɗaukar yaron."

Tana miƙa masu, Mama ta kalleta zata yi magana Aymana ta ce "Shi ne zanin da ta kawo don ɗaukar sabon mai gidan nata, bai kamata taga ba'a ɗauke shi da shi ba."

Sultan ya kalleta, yana ɗan nazarinta, Gimbiya Ummi ta shigo da murmushi Fuskarta, ta kalli Gimbiya mai gado da tunda Sultan ya shigo bata ce Uffan ba.

"Ah! Kaji manyan kakanni, ashe ana nan." Tayi maganar cikin salon wasa.

"Dolen mu, Magaji fa, ai ya fi ƙarfin wasa."

Sultan ta bi da kallo, ya ɗan matsa yana rusunawa ya bata hanya, zama tayi, Ayda ta yi saurin miƙa mata yaron dama can taso ta miƙa shi.

Gimbiya Ummi ta karɓa tayi Addu'a, kafin ta ce "Lallai Saratu tana can tana waya ga shi an kawo mata mai kama da ita."

Da sauri Ayda ta kalli Gimbiya Ummi, hakan yana nufin yaron yana kama da Sultan kenan, dariya Mama tayi "Ni ma na faɗa."

Jakadiyya ta fara dariya "Hakane kuwa an tsaka kara, don ba zance kamar an tsaga kara ba."

Sultan yana jin daɗi a zuciyar shi, ya fara tattaki tare da yin hanyar fita.

Jakaddiya ta fara magana "Allah ya taimaki Sultan."

Chak ya tsaya yana sauraronta, cikin salon kissa ta ce "Da girman kujerar ka uban gidan talakawa, takawar abin faharin mutanen gida, toron giwa kake, Namijin Zaki kafin ƙarfin...

Kafin ta ida Sultan ya juyo "Ki na da abin cewa ba kin ki?"

"Sarkin sarakuna adai duba, na tsugunne na jiran ungo."

Dariya taso kubcewa Rukkayya taga salon roƙo a wajan dakadiyya, amma sam sauran mutanen wajan ko a jikinsu, dama sun san a rina, wai an saci zanin mahaukaciya.

Baiyi magana ba ya harɗe hannuwa a ƙirji, yana kallon ta "Allah ya huci zuciyar Sultan. Idan ɗan kaciya bai ci kaza ba ai ba yayi bara ba! Allah ya taimake ka rana ai bata ƙarya!"

"Jakadiya!"

Ya kira sunan ta, hakan ya sa tayi shiru don ba shi izinin magana "Kina da Tukuicin gonaki guda biyu daga nahiyarmu, haka an baki ɓangare don zaman ki a cikin Masarautar Toro, akwai sulallar zinari zuwa gareki."

Kowa na wajen sai da ya ɗago ya kalli Sultan, Jakadiyya ta hau godiya, tana guda ya kalle ta "Shi ke nan?"

Kai ya sosa tare da faɗin "Allah shi baka nasara,  Kura ta san gidan mai babbar sanda! Tsuntsu duka tsuntsune! Abokin ɓarawo ɓarawo ne!"

Zama ya koma yayi yana kallonta, Gimbiya Maigado ta kalli jakadiyya ta ce  
 "samun waje..."

Mama tayi dariya, Sultan Ya ce "Jakadiyya ki ka ce Abokin ɓarawa ɓarawo ne?"

"Takawa! Dare mahutar bawa. Na ga akwai wanda ba su runtsa idanuwansu ba daren yau don tarar Magajin gobe."

Murmushi yayi ya kalli Rukkaya sam bata fahimci ita ake wa roƙon ba, ya ce "Ruƙayya kenan?"

Jakadiyya ta ce "Rankashi daɗe!"

"Kwaututtukan Ruƙayya zai ta'allaƙa a nasu yankin, hakan yana buƙatar shiri, amma akwai kayan ado zuwa gare ta, haka kuma akwai munduwar zinari, da tsabar kuɗaɗe a Hannu."

Dariya su ka kamayi, Rukkayya ta riƙe baki, Sultan ya miƙe jakadiyya ta ƙara tsayar dashi, ta hanyar sako maganar Aymana "Uwar Magajin gobe!" 

Shiru yayi ya fice, Aka saka dariya, Gimbiya Mai gado ta miƙe rai ɓace, Ayda ta bi bayanta, Mama ta saka dariya "Ayi can dai, zakaran da Allah ya nufa da cara sai yayi!"

Jakadiyya ta miƙe tana kakkaɓe hannuwanta data dafa ƙasa ta kalli Rukkayya "Na dawo kan ki, bani tukuici na."

Gimbiya Ummi tayi dariya "Ruwa ba ya tsami banza."

Aymana ta yi dariya, Ruƙayya tace "Ni da abin ya bani mamaki kasa godiya nayi."

Gimbiya Ummi ta miƙe "Na barku lafiya."

Wayar Aymana ta fara ruri, Bilkisu ta gani ƙanwarta, hakan ya tabbatar mata da har labari yajewa mutanen Bilyam.

***

Waziri ratayar babbar riga kawai yake, ya rasa sukuni Ayda kuwa ta sa kukan baƙin ciki, duk abinda Sultan ya yi mata tana ganin ya fi son Aymana ne, tunda har zai iya yiwa Jakadiyya kyautar gonaki.

Gimbiya mai gado ta kaɗa ta raya wajan kawar da baƙin cikin dake ƙumbiya-ƙumbiya a zuciyarta amma hakan ya gagara, wanann lokacin ta ɗauka lallai duniya tayi masu juyin waina.

***

Masarautar Bilyam kuwa farinciki baya musaltuwa a wajan su, domin har sun fara shirin zuwa duba jariri, wannan lokacin Bilkisu da kayanta ta taho don zama wajan Aymana.

Hakan yayiwa Aymana daɗi sosai.

An cigaba da gabatar da zaman jego, har tsayin kwanaki biyar, Aymana bata samun lokacin ganin Sultan, iya gisuwa ne kawai da ya shigo, shi kanshi yana son samun lokacin kula da yaron shi amma hakan baya samuwa.

Aymana an gyagije, kamar ba ita ba, tunda aka fara zaman jegon babu abinda take sai saka tsadaddun kaya, Farida kullum tana riƙe ko goye da yaron Aymana ce ma ta ke ce mata ya aje shi ya huta.

Ranar da safe Sultan ya shigo, ya same ta tana shiryawa a ɗaki hakan ya basu damar yin magana "Ko Sultan zai iya magana?"

Ta ida saka rigarta tana kallon shi "Ko yaushe kana da dama babu buƙatar izini daga wajan kowa a gidanka."

"Ko kina da ra'ayi akan sunan Jariri kuwa?"

Aymana tayi jim kafin ta ce "E na da shi, amma ina son Sultan ya faɗi na shi."

Murmushi yayi ya nufe ta "Na fara tunanin sakawa yaron Sunan Sarkin Bilyam."

Zaro ido Aymana tayi "A'a Sultan, Na ce fa ina da ra'ayi na?"

"Amma ai kin bani damar fara faɗin"

"Hmm ai bance idan ka faɗa hakan za ayi ba."

"Me na ki ra'ayin."

"Ina son sunan Tsohon Sarki ne don girmamawa gare shi."

Sultan ya kalleta, zai yi magana ta ce "Ka bani dama." Tayi maganar cikin alamar roƙo.

Kai ya ɗaga mata tace "Ka ga na manta ban nuna maka kayan da ya aiko da su ba."

Tana maganar ta gabatar da kayan gareshi, yawanci kayan yaron sunfi yawa.

Sultan ya riƙe ƙugunta yana haɗe cikin su tare da shaƙar ƙamshinta a hankali ya furta "Ko me Mai martaba yayi zuwa ga Matar Sultan ba zai bi ya ba."

Rungumeshi tayi "Babana ya biya ni, Ina mai godiya."

Sultan ya fara diriricewa, jin tana mashi susa a bayan kunnai, ya haɗe jikin su, yana zura harshenshi a bakinta, ya rufe idanuwanshi, wani shauƙi yana bin jijiyoyinshi, yana mai sha'awar kasancewa tare da ita sai dai babu damar hakan.

Ji tayi ya jefesu kan gadon yana fara tumurmusarta, ya zura hannuwanshi jikinta, yana labubar dukiyar fulaninta, ta sani sarai yayi kewarta hakan yasa ta barshi, sai da ya jima kafin ya fara zura hannuwanshi kan mararta, Aymana ta maƙarale jikinta "Allah shi taimake ka jego."

Ya ɗagota yana raɓata jikin shi, ya miƙa mata hannun shi yace "Na fi ki sanin jego, ga shi kin kusa jiwa Sultan ciwo ranar."

Dariya tayi "Laifinka aka ce mata ana riki mai jego, likitoki ma kana ganin gado muke saka su suna riƙewa."

Dariya ya yi "Shi ne don ƙeta ni ki ka matseni."

Ta miƙe tana faɗin shikenan "Yaro na Zan rinƙa kiranshi An-nur."

"Muhammad Abdurrashid." Ya faɗa, Aymana ta jinjina kai. Sun shima kafin ya fita.

***
Ana gobe suna da safe sai ga Mutanan Masarautar Bilyam, da tarin yawansu, mutanan masarautar Toro ba suyi mamaki ganin su ba, Sai lokacin Aymana ta zage ta shige cikin danginta akayita shirye-shiryen hidimar suna.

Da yamma lis aka gabatar da kayayyaki daga kowane ɓangare, yan uwan Aymana sun nuna iya tasu bajintar haka ma a wajan mutanen toro.

Tun ranar ake kiɗe-kiɗe da busa, masu wasannin gargajiya su na yi, da daddare Sultan ya sanar zai yi hawan Kijisa ranar suna da yamma, don murnar zuwan Magajin masarautar.

Toapa anan fa maƙiya ido ya raina fata, kowanne ya kasa nutsuwa, suka fara shige da fice, musamman Ayda da take ganin cewar haihuwarta biyu, babu wacce ta ce zai yi hawa sai akan Aymana.

***

Ranar Suna yaro a amsa sunan shi kamar yadda Aymana ta buƙata, wannan lokacin Mai martaba da kanshi ya shigo don ganin yaron, hakan ya ƙara ɗugunzuma zuciyoyin mutanen gida.

Musamman su Waziri da basu taɓa tunanin Aymana zata kuma samun martaba irin haka ba, laifin da ta Aikata a masarautar ta cancanci ko wanne hukunci, amma sai suka ga saɓanin hakan.

A iya tunanin Aymana bata taɓa hango kalar wannan ranar a tunaninta, kowa yana hidima don ita, ga tururuwar mutane.

Katagin kaya Sultan ya haɗa  don bawa Aymana da yaronta, Haka tsohin gidan suka kwashi kayan zuwa ɓangaren Aymana.

Jakadiyya Wannan lokacin harda fadawa da kuma wasu mutane biyu maza daga ɓangaren Maga yaƙi, sunyi shigar yaƙi da kuma makamai a hannuwanshi.

Matan ne suka fara shiga suna sassauke kayan gaban Iyaye da 'yan uwan Aymana.

Mama ce ta fara bayani "Wannan Saƙone daga Mai martaba Sultan. Kayan Magajin gobe da na Mahaifiyar sa."

Gimbiya Mai gado ta daɗe kunnuwanta, sam batason jin ana faɗin magajin gobe.

Mama ta cigaba da bayaninta , ta miƙa wasu kaya "Alkabba, 'yar ciki da babbar riga, takalmi, da rawanin su, Sultan ya ce a ajewa magajin shi."

Kowa yayi mamaki, kenan hakan yana nufin Sultan ya tsayar da An-nur a matsayin Magaji.

Ta ɗaga wata ma'ajiyar da akayi da yadin karan miski "Kuɗaɗe ne abawa Magaji, wannan kuma kayan sakawar shi ne na wannan lokacin."

Godiya suka kamayi, Ruƙayya ta riƙo Aymana cikin murna, Aymana ta yi murmushi.

Mama ta ce "Ga kaya nan na fitar sarakunan Nahiyar, su kuma na Aymana ne, Haka kuma Akwai Ingarman doki da kayan hawansa."

Ta garashe zancen tana miƙa wata mundurwa ta zinari. Ta kakkaɓe hannuwanta.

Nan aka kama godiya ana Allah sam Barka, Farinciki zak zuciyar Aymana, ta riga ta gama amincewa Sultan yana mata so mafi girma, haka kuma yana ɗaga darajarta a kowane lokaci.

Ayda ta zuro ƙafa cikin adon suna, Goggo tana take mata baya, da wasu kuyangi, zura kai take tana kallon kayan da aka gewaye, cikin zafin zuciya da baƙin cikin banbancin da Sultan yake nunawa, wannan lokacin ba zata taɓa barin shi ba, sai dai idan duk mutanen gidan zasu juya mata baya amma sai ta jewa Sultan da maganar rashin adalci da yake wanzarwa.

Ta ɗau alwashin in har ya nuna iko akan ta kamar ko wane lokaci wallahi sai dai manyan masarautar zasu shiga tsakani, don tayi niyar shaidawa fada abin da yake yi.

Ta yi hanyar fita da zummar komawa ɓangaren shi. Mama ta fara magana lokacin tana kallon Jakadiyya dake ɗauke da wani akwati.

"Jakadiyya na dawo gare ki." Ta sauke akwatin dai-dai lokacin da mazan mayaƙan suka shigo.

Akwatin zinari ne da yake ta walƙiya, ta ɗan fara magana "Wannan babbar kyautace mafi girman daraja daga Sultan, tare da karramawa, wannan shine kyauta mafi girma Tukuici mai tsoka zuwa ga Aymana."

Ɗaya daga cikin Mazan da suka zo ya matsa yana buɗe akwatin.

Kyallin TAKOBIN ne ya haske idanuwansu, Jakadiyya ta rangaɗa buɗa "TAKOBIN masarautar ne, Sultan ya mallakawa Aymana Kum..."

Kafin ta ida haka kama surutai, Aymana ta zaro ido tabbas Takobin ce, hayaniya ta kaure aka kama maganganu an ma hana Jakadiya ida maganarta.

Aymana ta kwasa tsawa "Ina!  Ba zai yiwu ba! Ta yaya! Me ya sa!"

"Wannan hukuncin Sultan ne." Cewar Jakadiya.

"Ban yarda ba Wallahi, Allah ba zan karɓa ba." Ta ƙarashe maganar cikin zafin zuciya, da baƙin ciki wannan ai kamar wani abin kunyane Sultan ya aikata mata, ya sata tuno abinda ya lafa mata, me dalilinshi na yin hakan, bayan mutanen gidan suna ɗauka tunda har tana son Takobin rabuwar auren su kenen.

Zata kuma magana, Bilkisu ta yiwa ƙanwar Umma raɗa, hakan ya sa ta ce wa "An gode Inshaallah za a aiko maku da tukuici zuwa anjima."

Suka miƙe suna godiya, jakadiya tace "Muna jira, amma uwar masu gida nata daban ne!"

Kasancewar suna cikin ruɗani babu wanda ya kulata, Aymana ta kwallawa Jakadiya kira "Ki zo ki mayar da wannan Takobin, Allah tafi karfina, mallakin Sultan ne, ba mallakina ba, ba ni da iko akan hakan." Tayi maganar hawaye na gangaro mata.

Ajiyar zuciya Ayda tayi ta riga jakadiyya ficewa ta fashe da dariyar jin daɗi "Na faɗa maku Sultan nawa ne, nawa ne, Ai ƙudidin takobin ne ya kawota gidan nan tunda ya bata babu sauran abun yi."

Jakadiyya ta rusuna gaban Aymana "Allah ya baki nasara, ba na da idon kallon Sultan na mayar da kyautar da yayi, ga dakarun tsaro nan a ƙofa, za su kula da ku." Tayi maganar suna ficewa.

Aymana ta zube kan kujara tana bin 'yan uwanta da kallo, ta fasa kuka "Kunga abinda aka jamin ko, yanzu ya ake so nayi, don Allah ku mayar masa da abin sa Wallahi..."

"Babu ruwana ni kuwa, ina zan je wajan Sarkin sarakuna Aymana? Kuma da zummar mayar da kyaut..." Cewar ƙanwar Umma.

Bilkisu ta dafe kanta tana salati "Amma me ya sa Sultan ya nuna cewar ya bar maganar bayan kuma bai haƙura ba."

Kuka Aymana ta ƙara yi ta miƙe "Ina tunanin ya haƙurane a lokacin don ganin cikin da nake ɗauke, yanzu yana ganin na haihu shige dalilin shi na yin wannan hukuncin."

Tayi hanyar fita Ruƙayya ta jawota "Kar ki fita a haka ki goge fuskarki."

Ajiyar zuciya ta fara saukewa, ta juya ta nufi ciki, watsawa fuskarta ruwa tayi ta mayar da alkabbarta ta ƙofar baya ta bi don zuwa wajan Sultan.

Ba ta yi tunanin samun shi ba amma tayi addu'a ta same shi ɗin, cikin sa'a kuwa yana tsaye shigowarshi kenan daga fada Aymana ta yi sallama tana nufar shi.

Sultan ya ɗago ya sauke idanuwan shi akanta, lokaci guda ya fahimci kuka da ta yi.

Saukar da zuciyarta tayi tana ƙoƙarin daidaita kanta ta "Barka da dawowa Allah shi taimakeka!"

Sultan ya yi wani irin murmushi, yanzu ya tabbatar saƙon shi ya isa, hakan yasa ya nemi kujera ya zauna, Aymana bata jira ba, ganin ba zai amsa ba "Na samu saƙonninka, Gimbiya da magajin gobe suna godiya."

Ta ƙara ɗan matsawa "Amma Allah shi taimakeka, ayi min Afuwa, daga cikin afuwar da kake da, ban san Sultan da riƙo ba, Na san na aikata babban laifi me yasa ba za a yafe min ba." Jim tayi ba tare da ta ƙara faɗar komai ba


"Ina jinki."

"Ko me manufar Sultan akan mayar da TaKOBI gare ni, har yaushe na sanar mallakin ka ne? Na tuba amma ba za a ƙarɓi tuba na ba, ina mai bada haƙuri zan mado Takobin zuw..."

Kafin ta ƙarasa  ya katse ta "Aymana! Kar ki kuskura, hakan wani babban laifin ne kike shirin ƙara aikatawa, Takobin burin ki ne, to me don an mallaka maki..."

Ta nufe shi da sauri "Amma Allah ya baka nasara ta ya zan..."

"Ba na son Magana, Sultan yana buƙatar hutu, shi ne dalilin dawowata, zaki iya tafiya."
 
Yayi maganar yana nuna mata ƙofa, jikin Aymana yayi sanyi ta san babu wata kalma da zata biyo bayan abinda ya faɗa, ƙoƙarin sunkuyawa tayi tace "Allah ya taimaka." Tana maganar tana share kwallar dake zubar mata ta fice.

Haka Aymana ta yi wannan rana cikin baƙin ciki, da tunane tunane kala-kala, Farida ce ta zo mata da labarin da ake yaɗawa cikin gidan na cewar Sultan zai yanke alaƙa da ita.

Tun kafin Farida ta gama Aymana ta miƙe duk taron mutanen sun fahimceta.

A karo na biyu ta isa ɓangaren shi, lokacin ƙarfe biyar na marece, cikin sa'a ta samu yana shiri kayan hawan doki yake sakawa.

Aymana ta yi saurin nufarshi tana riƙe wani abun kwalliya da yake ƙoƙarin ɗaurawa a jikin shi.

Ta aza mashi, ta yi saurin nufar ma'ajiya tana fito da wasu rawani don ta zaɓa, Sultan ya ce "An fitar da Rawani."

Ta aje tana kallon gadon, ta ɗauka tana aza mashi akai, ya zauna bakin gado, ta ɗaga yadin da akayiwa kwalliya sama, ta durƙusa ta janye rawanin da ya rufe hancin shi da bakinshi.

Ta yi raurau da ido, Sultan ya ƙara gyara zama "Har kullun babu kalmar da ta kyau nuna kyawun abu, amma ina jin ƙanƙantar kalmar awajan faɗin ta ga Sultan.

Kamata yayi suka miƙe tsaye "Da taimakon ki hakan ya samu."

Sanyi taji a ranta, hakan ya sa ta ɗaga baki gare shi "Ina ƙara tuba! Sultan ka amshi tuba ta ina son maido maka Takobin nan kum..."

Kafin ta ida ya saki kafaɗunta, ya ƙura mata idanuwanshi dake fitar da wani tasiri a zuciyar ta, ya ɗugunguma, yana nufar mudubi don duba fuskar shi, Aymana ta ce "Sultan!"

 Ta cikin Mudubin yake kallon ta, ya ce "Kar na kuma jin wata kalma daga bakin ki, idan hakan ya faru sai na hukunta ki."

Ta durƙushe tana kuka, ya fesa turare yana kai kawo, yana son tashinta amma kuma baya son raini don yana ganin hakan shi zai sa ta shigo kashi da wani zance.

Ganin zai wuce ta kiƙe yana biyo bayan shi, da kukanta, sai dai bai saurareta ba ya fita aka ja ƙofa.

Anan fa Aymana ta gama rikicewa wannan lokacin dole taje don samun wanda zai shawo mata kan Sultan, tun da har ta yi wa 'yan uwanta magana sun ƙi, tana ta tunanin mafita, haka ta miƙe don zuwa wajan Gimbiya Ummi, tasan Sultan yana bin umarnin mahaifiyar shi, kuma ta tabbatar zata goya mata baya.

Ta samu Gimbiya Ummi da baƙi, ta gaishesu tana shiga ƙuryar ɗakin, ta kwallawa Kuyanga kira ta bata izinin sanar da ita Tana son ganawa da ita.

Gimbiya Ummi ta shigo tana faɗin "Lafiya kuwa Uwar Magaji, ana taro kin baro baƙi."

Aymana ta fashe da kuka ta faɗa jikinta "Don Allah Gimbiya ki yi min rai, Sultan yana son rabuwa dani, don Allah ki taimake ni."

"Subhanallah! Wani abu ya faru bani da labari? " Ta yi maganar tana ɗagota ta zaunar da ita "sanar da ni." 

Aymana ta share hawayen ta "Sultan ne ya aika min da Takobi, akan tukuici na, wallahi ba na so, Yanzu gaya nan kowa ya san cewar Sultan rabuwa zai yi dani, naje na bashi haƙuri ya ƙi saurare na."

Ta kai ƙarshen maganar da shiɗewar kuka Gimbiya Ummi ta kuma wani salatin "Abinda naji da gaske ne Aymana?"

Aymana ta ɗaya kai tana riƙe hannunta "Don Allah ki min rai, ki taimake ni ki bawa Sultan haƙuri in mayar mashi da ..."

Kafin ta ƙarasa Gimbiya Ummi ta ce "Haba ai mana, ina ruwana a wannan maganar ta ku, ai ya riga ya aiwatar zam bazan saka baki na ba."

Aymana ta fara roƙon Gimbiya Ummi "Aymana! Sarki fa? Ta yaya? Taya zan nufi Sultan, sam hakan ba zai yiwu ba, maza ki tashi ki tafi wajan baƙin ki, tsakanin ku ne ke da shi, Ni kam babu ruwana a ciki."

Gimbiya Ummi ta ƙarashe maganar tana yin hanyar fita, hankalin Aymana ya ida ta shi ainun, lallai wannan wani babban Al'amari ne yake shirin faruwa da ita.

Ta bar ɓangaren jiki babu kwari, tayi Sa'a duk mutanen gidan suna filin hawa, hakan yasa babu wanda ya ganta balle a tantance tashin hankalin da take ciki.

Ayda kuwa ado ta ci, ta saka ɗaya daga cikin kayan da ya bata lokacin haihuwarta, don yanzu ta gama da kwantar da hankalinta, tunda har Sultan ya bawa Aymana takobi shi kenan zance ya ƙare, har ta fara tunanin irin yadda zata ja ragamar mutanen gidan.

Aymana ta isa falon tana kallon Ruƙayya dake rurruga An-nur yana kuka. Ta zauna ta cikin damuwa Bilkisu tace "Wai ya ake ciki ne?"

"Zanje ma samu mai martaba, naga abin mai girma ne, ban taɓa tunanin Sultan zai min hakan ba, ga shi Gimbiya Ummi ta ce ba zata saka baki ba."

Ruƙayya ta ce "Ni dai ba shi Madarar shi ya sha, in ya so sai ki yi duk yadda zaki yi."

Aymana ta amshi yaron, su ka cigaba da fira, sai dai banda ita don ba hakanne gabanta ba.

Ta aje yaron ta miƙewarta ta fice, babban ɓangaren gidan ta nufa, ta na zuwa ta ga Mai martaba ya fito da fadawa shi.

Aymana ta zube tana gaisuwa, cikin Mamaki ya ce "Lafiya kuwa, Me ya hana ki halartar hawan Sultan?"

Shiru ta ɗan yi kafin ta ce "Allah shi taimake ka, dama na zo don ganawa da kai ne."

Baya ya koma yana faɗin "To fa, zo muje ciki."

Ayman ta miƙe ta bi bayanshi, suka shiga falon, ya zauna kan kujera ita kuma ta zube ƙasa, Saida ya nemi ta faɗa mashi dalilin zuwanta.

Aymana ta duƙar dakai jikin jin nauyi ta faɗa mashi komai har zuwanta wajan gimbiya Ummi.

Mai martaba ya sauke ajiyar zuciya tare da yin dariyar manya, ya miƙe ya nufi tebur da ke tsakiyar falon ya tsiyaya ruwa a kofi, yana kai kawo, kafin ya ce "To ni miye nawa anan, dole a bi hukuncin Sultan a gidan nan, shi ne shugaban kowa."

"Don Allah Baba ka taimaka min."

"Aymana na riga na saka araina Sultan ba zai yi wani abu babu hujja ba, saboda haka a bi duk abinda ya hukunta shi ne girmamawa."

Yayi  maganar yana yin hanyar fita ya juyo ya kalli kwalla a idanuwanta "Zanje filin hawane."

Ganin zai fice ta yi sauri miƙewa tare da faɗin "Sauka lafiya."


Ta fito tana tunanin ko dai ya gayawa iyayen shi, tunda har gashi sun goyi bayanshi, ta shiga tana kwallawa Bilkisu kira, sai ta samu bata nan.

Ta jawo wayarta, layin mahaifinta take kira, Sarkin Bilyam ya ɗauka yana tambayarta lafiya jin ta fashe da kuka.

"Wallahi baba Sultan so yake ya rabu dani, nasan saki na zai yi, kuma duk iyayen shi sun goyi bayanshi don Allah Baba ka taimaka min, na mayar da takobin nan."

Sai lokacin ya tambayeta akan me take zance, Aymana tana sanar da shi ya ce "Aymana! Ba ki da hankali ko? Ni zan wa Sultan magana, atunaninki ina da bakin ƙara magana da shi akan takobi, shi ya san manufar shi akan hakan, lokacin da ake jan kunannanki ai maishe damu mutanen banza kikayi, idan ma zai rabu da ke ai hukuncin shine, ikon shi ne, Ni ba ruwa na."

Kuka ta ƙara fasawa, Mai martaba ya kashe wayar yana wurgi da ita.

Aymana ta dafe kai, dai-dai lokacin ƙanwar Umma ta shigo tana faɗin "Ke dai ba zaki sawa zuciyarki ruwan sanyi ba ko?"

"Haba baba ni wallahi ba zan iyaba, Allah zan kai takobin nan in aje mashi kayan shi."

"Kin raina shi kenan ko."

Aymana ta kaɗa kai, zata miƙe Baba ta ce "Ki kira Farida ta zo ta kikkimtsa maki kayayyakin ki, mun gama magana da kowa sun bada izinin tafiya da ke Darul-Bilyam don wankan jego."

Wata irin razana Aymana tayi tare da dafe ƙirjinta "Wanka kuma, Ni wallahi ba zan je ba."

"Yau naga ikon Allah, kamar ya ba za ki je ba, kin manta al'adar Kaka ce a kai mata mai jego ta gyarata."

Aymana ya kalleta cikin tuhuma, ta miƙe ta kama hannunta tana hawaye "Don Allah Baba ku sanar dani, Sultan saki na yayi shi ne kuke ɓoyewa."

"Ba..."

"Idan ba haka bane ku barni anan mana, Allah ya gani ba zan iya daurewa ba."

Ta miƙe tana tunanin wanda zata kira ya haɗata da Kaka, Layin Umma ta kira, ta ce ta bada akai ma Kaka wayar.

Taso tambayarta yadda taji muryarata, amma ta ƙyaleta.

Tana jin sallamar Kaka ta saka kuka tana gaya mata, kaka ta rabka sallallami tare da faɗin "Yau naga ja'irar yarinya, idan ya sake ki shi ne za ki rikice haka, ni ya yi man Daidai Allah ya danƙara mashi Albarka, Na ƙi na ba shi haƙurin, Kiji mutuniyar kawai, lokacin da kika toshe kunnuwanki ida ina tausar ki  ai baki tunanin zan..."

"Ni dai Kaka na roƙe ki, ki ba shi haƙur."

"Ni jikar mutum huɗu, Allah ya kawo ki lafiya zan ce maki, amma babu ni a maganar tunkarar Sultan."

Tayi maganar tana miƙa wayar, ta na sake wani sabon kwankwamin.

***

Ana shirin Magriba Sultan ya dawo ya watsa ruwa ya tafi masallacin, bai jira sallar isha'i ba, ya dawo falon shi.

Yana zaune Bilal ya shigo da Bilkisu a bayanshi, Sultan ya kalli Billal ya ce "Ni fa ban fahimce ka ba."

Bilkisu ta zauna kujerar can nesa, Billal ya zauna kusa da ita, Sultan ya riƙe baki "Akwai alamar tambaya a nan."

Dariya Su ka yi Sultan ya ce "Dama an bani labarin kaine ka kawo ta."

Billal ya ce "Waye ya faɗi maka, abinda ko shigowa ban yi ba."

Dariya Sultan ya yi "Ko me ake a masarauta ta da sani na."


Ya maida hankalinshi kan Bilkisu "Yanzu ke wanann tuzurun kike so."

Rufe fuskarta tayi, Sultan ya buga kujera "Shi kenan ai ka yaudarar min ƙanwa."

"Kar ka ɓatamin wasa kana kirana tuzuru, kai ma mulki ne ya saka aure cikin lokacin da kayi."

Sultan yayi dariya "Wai a hakan ma na kife ciki na ƙi."

Billal yayi dariya "Shi kenan Bilkisu, tunda kina so zan tsara muku komai, Allah ya tabbatar da Alkhairi a tsakanin ku."

Za su yi magana Jakadiyya ta turo ƙofa tare da gaisuwa tana nemar wa Aymana izinin ganawa dashi.

Sultan baiyi magana ba, Jakaddiya ta daɗe a wajan Billal yana bin Sultan da kallo, kamar ba shi ne suka gama barkwanci ba.

Sai lokacin ya ɗaga kai, Jakaddiya ta ce "Allah ya ja zamaninka."

Aymana ta shigo, tana kallon su Bilkisu, tana ganin Bilkisu tayi rashin kunya har tana iya zuwa gaban Sultan da saurayi duk da yana abokin shi, ta so yin magana sai dai ba hakan ne gaban ta ba.

Za su bar masu wajan Sultan yace "Ku zauna."

Bilkisu ta san ba a yiwa sarki gardama, hakan ya sa ta zauna, Billan ya ce "Mu baku waje don..."

Cikin kaushin murya Sultan yace "Ka zauna!"

Aymana ta sunkuya tare da faɗin "Barka da hu..."

Bata ida ba Sultan ya ce "Ko me ya dakatar da ke wajan halartar hawa na?"

"Allah ya bak..."

"So nawa na sanar dake kar ki kuma bari na gabatar da wani taro ba tare da kin halarci wajan ba."


Zata kuma magana, Sultan ya miƙe tsake ya fara kai kawo "Kin aikata babban laifi Aymana, Magajin gobe kan shi, Ni ne na bada umarnin a kawo shi filin ina hankalinki yake?"

"Allah ya huci zuciyar Sultan."

Sultan ya juyo ya kalleta, ya daɗe yana bin fuskarta da kallo, ya ga kumburin da ta yi Ya ce "Na ce kar ki ƙara, kar ki ƙara, kar ki ƙara aikata kalar wannan kuskuren."

Aymana ta duƙar daki, ta na jin kamar zata yi kuka, sai dai batason yin hakan gaban Billal, zatayi magana  Sultan ya ce "Zan fita."

"Allah shi taimakeka, ina son magana da kai..."

"Lokacin salla yayi." Ya faɗa yana yin hanyar fita, Aymana ta bishi da kallo, Bilkisu ko a jikinta, Billal ne ma ya bawa Aymana haƙuri, Aymana tayi murmushi tana barin wajan.

***

Washe gari kamar wasa Aymana taga an gama haɗa masu komai na tafiyarsu, abin mamaki Sultan kamar ba a Ɓangaren shi ya kwana ba, tunda safe ya fice fada.

Hakan ya ƙara ɗaga hankalin ta, duk yadda taso ganawa da shi bata samu ba, sai mutanen gidan dake ta tururuwa wajan yi mata bankwana.

Kaya aka haɗa rigi-rigi harda akwatin Takobi, sai lokacin ta kula da masu tsaron Takobin ne suke riƙe da akwatin suna jiran fitowar su.

Ƙarfe sha biyu suka fito, wannan lokacin motoci Sultan ya tanadar musu, da ita da 'yan uwanta.

Mota biyu aka cika da barade da kayan yaƙinsu, don rakiyar Aymana da kuma tsoron takobin saboda gudun kota kwana, saboda tunda aka kai TAKOBIN a masarautar Toro ba a taɓa fitar da ita ba sai yau kuma ya dalilin Aymana.

Sauran masarautun nahiyar labari da ya kai masu sunyi mamaki, haka kuma sun ƙara jinjina lamarin Aymana da masarautar ta, yayin da wasu suke ɗauka kamar Sultan yayi amfani da ikon da yake dashi wajan  zartar da abinda yaga dama.

Sarakuna Dattawa da suka daɗe a nahiyar, suna ɗauka Sultan yaro ne, akwai ƙananun shekaru a tare da shi hakan ya sa ya ke barin Izza tana tasiri akan shi.

Fita da TAKOBIN daga masarautar Toro wani babban al'amari ne da firgita mutanen masarautar, hatta Mai martaba  ya shiga tashin hankali da bai taɓa shiga ba.

Sultan kuwa yana kallon fitar su ta fada, yana tunanin tun kaka da kakanni shi, yake ganin yadda ake killace takobin tare da tsoron ranar da za a fita da ita amma gashi yau da kanshi ya bada ta an fitar da ita.

Waziri da Yarima Saifu kuwa, son mulkinsu dama can ya ta'allaƙa da son takobin, tun lokacin da suka fara tunanin Aymana ta zo ballakar takobin basu taɓa yarda da kan ba sai yanzu.

***

Lokacin da Aymana ta isa Darul-Bilyam mutanen masarautar sun yi murnar ganinta da takobin, darajarta ta ɗaukaka, irin girmammawar da taga ana mata ya sha banban da sauran lokacin baya.

Sun tabbatar Aymana ta sha banban da duk 'ya'yan sarakunan nahiyar, kowa ya ji daɗin dawowar Aymana da takobin.

Sarkin Bilyam babu wani farin ciki a tare da shi, sai dai yana jin wani sanyi yana ratsa shi ko ba komai ya ji kusanci da takobin.

Lokacin ya sa a yanaji ɗakin da za a ajiye Takobin tare da masu tsaron dakin kamar yadda ake tsaronta a masarautar Toro.


Aymana ta kasa sakin jikinta, babu nutsuwa a tare da ita, kowa ya fahimci hakan.

Sultan ya shiga kewar matarsa, kowa na gidan ya kasa gane kan shi, Gimbiya Ummi ta fara damuwa amma tunda ta fahimta hakan ya kwantar mata da hankali tasan idan Aymana ta dawo komi zai dai-daita.

Yau yana fada zaune, Baba Waziri ya shigo, yana son magana da shi akan Aymana don ya ga tunda ta tafi babu wanda ya ƙara magana mai muhimmanci akan takobin.

Sultan ya sa hanki da ke hannun shi ya ɗan goge fuskarshi, Waziri ya rusuna da gaisuwar munafunci, fadawa ne suka amsa da "Sultan ya gaishe ka."

Waziri ya jinjina kai ya zauna dirshen a ƙasa, tsawon lokaci kafin ya fara magana "Allah ya taimakeka, akan maganar Aymana da takobi da ta tafi dashi..."

Cikin sauki Sultan ya ɗago yana kallon shi, Waziri ya ci gaba "Ya kamata ayi wani abu akai, ga ya za'a barta ta tafi da takobin ba tare da an ɗau mata ki ba, ya kamata ta maido ta sabod..."

Kafin ya ida Wani bafade cikin fadawan da gefen Sultan ya ce "Hattara dai Waziri, Sarki ba ya kyauta ya amsa."

Waziri ya ɗago yana kallon Bafaden ya na cije leɓo, cikin jin haushin shi, Shi kuwa Sultan ko da bafaden bai yi magana ba, ba zai ce komai ba ganin waziri yana neman mayar da shi ƙaramin mutum.

Tsawan daƙiƙu goma sha biyar babu wanda yayi magana, Sultan ya miƙe zai shiga gida, hakanne ya tabbatar masa da ba zai yi magana ba.

Ɓangaren Gimbiya Ummi ya shiga, yanzu nan yake zaman shi, yayi ta fira da ita. Zaune ya sameta ya gaisheta yana kallon yadda take huci, ya ƙara matsawa gaban ta "Allah ya la'anci abinda ya ɓata zuciyar mahaifiyar Sultan."

Gimbiya Ummi ta jinjina kai "To mi ye ruwana don ka bada Takobi, Gimbiya Mai gado zata zo ta yi min tsaye da maganganun rashin hankali."

Dariya yayi yace "Haba Kamar yau ki ka fara ji, ai wannan ba sabon abu bane."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi, ganin ranta ya ɓaci hakan yasa bai sanar da ita Waziri ya je mashi ba.

Gimbiya Ummi ta ce "Ko yaushe za ka je duba su? kar Magajin gobe yayi fushi da Sultan."

Dariya yayi yana miƙawa, don baya so ta ce zai je, yana son ƙara rikita Aymana ne, yana kaiwa ƙofa ya juyo "Au Kinga na manta, Ina saratu? wannan mutanen sun zo da maganar a saka ranar Auren, na basu zaɓi sunce wata ɗaya."

"Shi kenan Sultan, Allah ya tabbatar da Alkhairi."

"Ameen."
 Yana ɗaga labule Abul ya na shigowa da gudu, Sultan yayi saurin riƙe shi yana dariya "Daga ina kake?"

"Waje." Ya ce yana fizgewa tare da saka ɗan yatsanshi daya saba tsotsa a baki, Sultan ya cire yana jan hannun shi suka wuce cikin gida.

***

Aymana tana zaune a ɗakin Kaka, waya take ta dannawa sai ta kai kan layin Sultan zata kira shi, wata zuciyar take hana ta, sam ta kasa samun sauki, Allah ya gani tana kewar mijinta, musamman rashin nemanta ko da a wayane.

Dagewa tayi ta kira, cikin sa a ta shiga, ta fara tunanin yanke kiran amma ta daure, tunda ta riga ta shigar da kiran.

Har ta tsinke babu amsa, Aymana ta dafe kai, tunanin ta ya ƙara canzawa, ta kalli Kaka da ke mata wani kallo "Wai ni Kaka laifin me na miki ne?"

"Maganin da kika rage, waye kika bar mawa?"

"Wai Kaka abinda ba kuyi ba lokacin Aure sai yanzu ki takur..."

"Sai dai idan ba ki sha ba, amma na kai maki har ɗaki a kwarya." Sai lokacin Aymana ta tuna, Kaka zata yi magana Aka aiko kiran Aymana Sarki yana son ganawa da ita.

Yanzu a gidan idan tana tafiya girmamata ake sosai, saboda sarautarta da kuma takobi da ya zama mallakinta.

Sarki yana zaune Aymana ta durƙusa tana gaida shi, Mai martaba ya ce "Kin san da zuwan 'yan uwan Sultan ne, an ce za su zo duba An-nur."

Aymana ta kama Kame kame, tana saurin faɗin "Eh zuwa gobe ne zuwan ko?"

"Eh haka Sultan ya sanar dani."

Ajiyar zuciya tayi, wato itace dai ba zai kira ba, anan hankalinta ya ɗan kwanta. Suka cigaba da tattaunawa akan zuwan. lokacin da ta koma ciki, ta fara saka a kimtsa mata ɓangaren baƙi, da bada umarnin abubuwan da za a girka masu zuwa safen.

***

Ƙarfe biyar Sultan daga Masallaci ɓangaren Mama ya shiga, fadawanshi suka tsaya ƙofa don jiran shi.

Cikin Mamaki ta san yanzu ba ya shiga gidan ta ce "Ranka shi daɗe da kanka?" Tana magana tana jan tabarma, ta shimfiɗa tare da aza kafet, ta yi saurin zuwa don ɗauko mashi tuntun.

Sultan yayi dariya "Mama kar ki wahalar da kan ki."

Zama tayi tana gaisuwa, Sultan bai amsa ba ya ce "To Mama ƙarfe nawa ne tafiyarku?"

Dariya tayi "Ai tunda na ganka nasan akwai wani abu."

Murmushi yayi yaɗan kame fuska kaɗan "Yanzu dai ya isa sun dawo, lokaci ya ja fa."

Hararar shi tayi "Ni da ta sanar da ni ba zata dawo ba."

Zaro ido ya yi "Ta ɗauki maganganun mutanen gidannan kenan?"

"Haba Sultan, sam abinda ka zartar ya rikitamu wallahi, me sa zaka yiwa Aymana haka, ni Inshallah zan..."

"Ni fa ban aikata komai ba, me ya sa aka kasa fahimta na."

"Taya za a fahimceka, ka saka Aymana a ruɗani wallahi."

Ya yi Murmushi "Mama idan kunje ku shirya dawowarta, nifa ina kewar yaro na."

"Zuwan mu kaɗai ba zai wadatar ba, kai ma sai ka ziyarce su, Allah ya taimake ka."

"Ba damuwa,  Zan yi ƙoƙarin hakan."

Tunda Sultan ya koma yake jin daɗin jin Aimana ta damu akan rashin shi, ya ji babu daɗi, har zai kira sai kuma ya fasa kiran, ya barshi akan zai masu zuwan bazata.

Tunani ya farayi, ya sadaukar da takobin ga Aymana, duk da ya jima yana jin raɗaɗin hakan, to amma hakan shine daidai, hakan shine zaɓi da yake da ganin zai kwatar mata da hankali.

****

Mama, Hajiya Maigado, Goggo, Jakadiyya, Saratu, da wasu kuyangin gidan sune zasu tafi ganin Aymana da An-nur.

Farko Sultan ya so hana jakadiya tafiyar amma ta taushe shi da daɗin bakin tana son zuwa ta gano magajin gobe hakan ya sa ya amince mata don baya wasa akan An-nur, har ya kai baya iya ɓoyewa.

Yana shirin fitowa don sallamar mutanen da zasu tafi, Ayda ta turo ƙofar falon Sultan yana gyara maɓallin rigar shi.

"Barka da safiya."

Shiru bai amsa ba, ya na kallon yana yin shigarta, ya jima kafin ya ce "Da wani abu ne?"

"Dama mun shirya tafiya Darul-Bilyam ne."

Da sauri ya kuma kallonta, wato ita tafi ƙarfin sanar da shi zata je, sai ta shirya sannan zata zo mashi, ya fara tattaki "Sultan bai san da zuwan ki ba."

"Amma ai kasan da tafiyar ko."

Juyowa yayi da sauri, zuciyarshi ta fara tafasa da maganganun rashin girmamawarta, ya sauke ajiyar zuciya yana nemarwa kanshi nutsuwa "Muje za ki iya tafiya."

Bin shi ta yi baya tana watsa mashi wani irin kallo, ta yi niyar ko da ya hana sai taje ɗin ko don ta gano gidan da Aymana take taƙama da shi da kuma yi mata gori akan sarauta.

Ya samu duk sun shiga Mota,  da kayayyakin da zasu kaiwa Aymana, Mama da Gimbiya Ummi suna can nesa kaɗan suna magana, Mama ta amshi kudin da ta bata, tana faɗin na miye "Akai wa Aymana ta yi kitso da gyaran jiki na dawowarta."

"Amma wannan aikin Sultan ne."

"Na ga bashi da niyya."

Mama tayi dariya, ta lura Gimbiya Ummi ta so ta tafi Sultan salƙi akan Aymana ɗin.

Sai lokacin suka san tare da Ayda zasu tafi, Sultan ya masu Allah ya tsare ya wuce fada, su kuma suka ɗauki hanyar Masarautar Bilyam.


Sai da Aymana ta tabbatar an kimtsa ko ina, ɓangaren da za a dauke baƙin an haɗa shi da kayan sarauta na gargajiya, An baza kuyangi a wajen.

Ta koma ciki ta yi wanka, ta fara neman Farida don tayata kimtsawa sai da ta aika, Farida ta shigo da sauri ta na fadin "Ayi min Afuwa na je..."

"Yi min shiru, tun da kik zo gidannan shiriritar ki tafi yawa."

"Allah ya huci zuciyar Uwar ɗakina."

"Kin fitarmin da kayan kuwa."

"Eh." Ta faɗa tana tafiya don kwaso kayan, ta shigo dasu, Aymana ta shirya, doguwar rigar Atamface an mata adon buwatsu da aikin hannu, ɗinkin ya amshi jikinta, sai da ta ɗaura ɗankwali, kafin Farida ta fara saka mata awarwaraye, sarƙa da kuma sarƙir gafa.

Ta miƙe tsaye tana kallon kanta, Farida ta aza mata alkabba  ta jan yadin karan-miski, an yi mata aiki sak irin na jikin Atamfar, ta koma bakin gado ta zauna, Farida tana ɗaura mata takalmi kalar alkabbar, Aymana ta ce "Ba za a bar takalmi idan zan fita ba, zuwa su ƙaraso?"

Kafin ta ida suka fara jiyo hayaniya, Farida ta ce "Ina tunanin su ne ma."

"Za ki iya zuwa ki gano."

Farida ta miƙe don bin umarnin Aymana, sai da ta je har wajansu da gaisuwa tayi masu sannu, tayi hakanne don tabbatar da su waye su ka zo.

Tayi mamaki matuƙa ganin Ayda, lokacin da take gaida ita tana can tana kallon wani gini da aka yiwa tsini a sama.

Farida ta ce "Sannu da zuwa Gimbiya."

Ayda ta waigo tana bin Farida da kallo dai ta ganta sanye da kalar kayan Kuyangin gidan.

Bata amsa ba ta juya, tana bin hanyar da akayi dasu don rakasu masauki.

Ta koma yana durƙusawa ta fara karanto mata mutanen da suka zo.

"Allah sarki, ina da tabbacin Mama ba zata taɓa bari a barta ba."

"Allah shi taimakeki, Wannan zuwan fa da abin kallo, domin kuwa hadda Gimbiya Ayda."

"Me ki ka ce?"

"Kwarai harda ita."

Aymana tayi saurin miƙewa "Da abinda ya kawota kum..."

"Kwantar da hankalin ki, ganin kwam ne kawai, kuma zata tafi da dubun kunyarta."

Aymana ta yi murnushi "Bari zan saka takalmin, ina so nan da mintuna koma, masu rakiyata su na waje."

Farida ta miƙe ta fice cikin sauri ta yi hanyar ɓangaren Kuyangin gidan ta na bada umarni kamar yadda Aymana ta buƙata.

Sai da Aymana ta gama shiri, ta na miƙewa ta ji hayaniyar kuyangin a waje, hakan ya sa ta fita, cikin sauri suka yi shiru suna gaida ita, bata amsa ba, ta yi ta tsakiyarsu tana tafiya cikin isa, haka suka jera suna maye mata baya.

A bakin ƙofa ta tsaya, sai lokacin ta hango Bilkisu dake tahowa saɓe da An-nur a kafaɗa.

Shiga tayi har ciki Kuyangin suka shiga, sai dai sun jera kansu jikin bango, Aymana daga tsaye ta rusuna, tana gaishe da su Gimbiya Mai gado.

Amsawa sukayi suna washe baki, ya kalli yadda aka cika masu gabansu da kayan motsa maki da abinciccika iri-iri.

Ta koma saman wata kujera, ta zauna kuyanga Farida ta zauna gefenta daga ƙasan kafen, Aymana yi tayi kamar ma bata san cewar da Ayda a tafiyar ba, ta kalli Bilkisu da ke miƙa masu yaron.

Mama ta ce "MashaAllah Magajin gobe ya cika hannu, lallai..."

Wata irin harara Ayda ta yiwa Mama, Aymana ta ɗan taɓe baki "Aikuwa gashi nan Sai kukan da babu gaira babu dalili."

Gimbiya Mai gado ta yi dariya "Wato ya ɗauko kukan nan kenan, ai haka Sultan yayi idan ya fara ihu duk mutanan gidan nan sai sun taro."

Aymana ta ɗaure fuska tana ganin kamar raini ne take yi ga Sultan, ta kallo kuyangin dake zagaye da su tace "Za ku iya tafiya."

Gaba ɗaya suka rusuna da gaisuwa suka fice, Goggo ta ce "Yau gamu a masarautar Bilyam."

Aymana tayi murmushi tasan da biyu tayi maganar, sai lokacin Ayda ta ce "Ba haka nayi tunanin samun ..."

Da sauri Aymana ta kalleta, sai ta ga goggo tana taɓota akan ta yi shiru, Aymana ta yi murmushi "ikon Allah, wai da harda Gimbiya Ayda, Aini ban kula da ke ba, Sannunku da zuwa Lallai yau masarautarmu tana da manyan baƙi."

Mama tayi dariya, ta ji daɗin yadda Aymana ta basar, duk da acikin maganarta akwai nuna halin ko in kula, amma Ayda bata gane ba.

"Don Allah ku ci abinci ku gama, a kaiku cikin gida ku gaisa da mutanen gidan."

Ta yi maganar tana kallon Mama dakewa An-nur tawai, suka cigaba da zuba abinci.

Aymana ta miƙe zata ɗan fita waje, Ayda ta bita da ido ganin shirgar Alfarma dake jikinta, ga kyau da tayi, sam ba zaka ce ta haihuba, idan ba yaron ne kaga ta amsa ba.

Sai da ta nasu mintuna talatin, tana dawowa ta samu suna gabatar da sallar azahur, ta jira suka kammala, kafin ta ce zasu shiga ɓangaren Gimbiyoyin gidan.

Haka suka bi ɓangare ɓangare, da mamakin yadda itama masarautar tana da girma sosai kamar ta Toro, a ɗakin Kaka suka fi daɗewa, Kaka ta zage fira da Mama, yayin da kowa yayi shiru, Aymana ta ce "Mama ki tashi muje zaku gaishe da Mai martaba, idan kika biye Kaka ba zata bar ki ba."

"To Sarkin bayanau, ku kutafi Ni zan rakota wajan Sarkin."

Dariya tayi "Wai kin yadda Mama, in zaku tafi sai ta tsaya hutawa so tamanin da biyar."

Dariya suka saka, Mama ta ce "Ku tafiyarku."

Haka suka bar Mama da kaka, dama Kaka tayi hakanne don ta samu zantawa da Mama akan Aymana da Sultan, nan kuwa Mama ta warwarewa Kaka komai.

"Kenan ya sadaukar da takobin ne kawai ba don wani dalili ba."

"Ni a gani na, soyayya ce ta rinjaye shi, sannan kuma yana son ɗaga darajarta fiye da kowa a gidan."

Sun koma suna tattaunawa, ganin lokaci na tafiya Kaka ta ce "Shi kenan Mama, muje na raka ki."

Sun samu har sun bar fada, Mai martaba ya amshi Mama hannu bibbiyu, don Kaka ta sanar da shi itace wacce ta tagazawa Aymana akan komai, ya ji daɗi sosai har yayi mata godiya.

Ita dai sunkuyawa kawai tayi, ya kalli Kaka ya ce "Na bada komai da zasu tafi da shi har an saka musu a motocinsu, Amma dole na girmama Mama girmammawa ta musamman."

Mama tayi murmushi tana duƙar da kai, Mai martaba ya miƙe tsaye yana faɗin "Nasan idan nace na bata zaɓi ba zata zaɓa ba, amma Kaka me kike ganin za a bawa Mama."

Kaka ta kalle shi "To ko sillar Zinari ko munduwar zinarin, shine ba zasu zamar mata kayan da kowa zai fahimta ba."

Mama ta rusuna "Ina mai tuba ayi afuwa gareni, ba zani iya karɓa ba, Aymana tamkar 'ya na ɗauketa, bana jin..."

Kaka ta daɗe mata baki, Mai martaba yayi dariyar manya, ya shiga ciki, babu jimawa ya fito da wata 'yar jikkar yadi, ya bawa kaka "ga shi nan a bata, Mai martaba ya ji daɗin kulawarta ga Aymana."

Mama ta matsa tana godiya, Kaka ta ɗauko suka fito, a ƙofa ta bata "Kin ga saka abinki a zaka."

Mama tayi godiya, ta adana abinta, suka wuce ciki, sai dai an sanar dasu Aymana tana zagayawa da bakinne a cikin gidan, da ɗakunan tarihi.

Mama ta ƙaraso tana ganinsu, Gimbiya Mai gado ta bita da harara, don ta san ba a rasa yin wani gulmar, Mama ta basar tana faɗin "Wai ina saratu ne?"

Dariya Farida tayi "Saurayin Bilkisu ya zo ya tafi da su cikin gari."

Aymana tayi gaba suna binta baya, ta kai su wajan wani gini ta zauna a wani farfajiya ta ce "Wanann wani sabon ginine, duk girmanshi a cikin wuni ɗaya aka kammalashi."

Da mamaki suke kallon wajan da kuma yanayin ginin da aka yi shi da duwarwatsu manya.

"Washe garin da na dawo aka yi ginin, don killace takobin da ya zama mallaki na."

Nan fa aka fara muzurai, Ayda ta ɗan rausayar da kai, Gimbiya kai gado ta ce "Ginin ya yi kyau." Tana miƙewa. 

Haka suka miƙe banda Ayda da jikinta yayi sanyi, ta kasa ko motsa ƙafarta, har suka fara nisa, Aymana tana tsaye tana jiran ta miƙe su bar wajan.

Amma hankalin Ayda baya jikinta, mamaki take, kenan hankalin Aymana a kwance harma ta yiwa takobin ma'ajiya a masarautar su, kenan Sultan ba sakintan zai yi ba.

Aymana ta ce "Za mu iya tafiya?"

Ayda ta miƙe "Samun wani abun rasa wani abun yakan jawo, mai tunani yakan zurfafa tunani yayin da wasu sukan gajarta tunanin su."

Aymana ta yi saurin matsowa "Tabbas! Masu gajarta tunani suna ganin abinda zai yiwu kamar ba zai yiwu ba, amma da lokaci komai ya ke baiyyana."

Ayda ta kalleta "Sai me don an baki takobi? A ganinki ɗaukaka ki ne komai? Sultan zuciyar shi har kullum akan jinin shi ne, Magajin gobe kuwa ba..."

"Kul! Kar ki kurkura, Nan fadata ce, zan iya hukuntaki hukuncin da ba zaki iya ɗauka ba, na baki azabtarwa mafi girman azabtarwa, Magajin gobe ba abin rainawa bane."

Ta ida maganar tana yin gaba, Ayda ta kasa ida zancen, ta yi sororo, kafin ta bi bayan Aymana dake tafiya cikin zafin zuciya da cikar Izza.

Da Mamakin su aka rinƙa gabatar masu da abubuwa kyaututtuka daga kowane ɓangare na gidan.

Mama da ke tsaye a bakin ƙofa ita da Aymana ta miƙa ma Aymana takardar da aka zuba kudi a ciki tace "Wannan saƙon Gimbiya Ummi ne, ta ce kiyi shirin komawa kitso da gyaran jiki."

"Allah sarki Ina kewarta sosai." Ta amsa da godiya.

Sai da suka fito farfajiya don tafiya kafin su Bilkisu suka iso, sai lokacin ta kula har da An-nur suka tafi, Gimbiya Mai gado ta hau faɗan munafunci wai ba a kula dashi an yafi da shi nesa, yunwa zata kama shi.

Saratu tace "Kin ga fa jakar kayan abincin shi, mun ba shi madara."

Ayda ta kaɗakai tana cije loleɓo a zuciyarta tace dama yunwa ta kama shi ya mace kowa ma ya huta, sai muga yadda za a rinƙa mana tunƙaho kuma.

Haka suka tafi, kowa yana kewar junan su, hankalin Aymana ya kwanta koba komai ta san sun firgita da ganin irin nasu tsarin masarautar.

***

Daga Sallar i'sha Sultan ya isa ɓangaren Mama, Mama da murna ta baje mashi abinda aka bata, ya ji daɗi sosai, dama yayi tunanin hakan, anan yayita tambayarta An-nur, tace "komai lafiya lau, ba ka ga yadda yake son wasa ba, ina tunanin Kaka tana mashi rawa, da ga an fara sai ya kama dariya."

"Ah Mama dariya fa."

"Allah kuwa, ya fara wayo, ya kusa wata biyu fa yanzu."

"Eh Hakane, amma naga wasu yaran sai sukai wata nawa ma basa sanin ana masu wasa."

"Yara halittane, ko wanne da kalar wayon shi."

Sun yi fira kafin ya miƙe ya shiga ciki, abin Mamaki a falon shi ya samu Ayda, ya kalleta lokacin da take faɗin. "sannu da dawowa."

"Yauwa ya hanya?" Ya faɗa yana cire alkebbarshi.

"Lafiya lau." Ya kuma kallonta "Da wani abu ne?"

"Babu, mun gano Annur amma gaskiya banji dadin rashin kulawar da ake wa yaron ba."

Cikin sauri ya kalle ta, tare da tunanin ko mama ta boye wani abu ne "Me ya faru."

"Ta ya za ace ayi wuni guda ba'a ba yaro madarar uwa ba, wai sai madarar kwankwani ake ɗirka mashi."

Ko da babu ladabi a maganar Ayda, ba shi ne damuwar Sultan ba, ya ɗan shiga kaɗuwa, baya so wani abu ya samu yaron shi, ganin kamar ya yarda da maganar ta hakan ya sa ta ci gaba "Shi kenan kuma har an gina wa Takobin gidanmu ɗaki a wata masarautar, Haba Sultan."

"Ayda!" Ya kirata, yana nuna ta, kar ki kuma zo min da wannan zancen."

"Amma Sultan, gaskiya ce na faɗa, kai kanka ka san takobin nan yana da girma da daraja a gidan nan, amma ka ɗauka ka bata, bayan..."

"Kee?" 

Ya faɗa yana rufe idanuwanshi, ya nuna mata koma, Ayda ta ga ranshi ya ɓaci ba saurarenta zai yi ba, ta san idan ta kuma magana ranshi zai ida ɓaci, ta fice sumi-sumi.

Yana jin ta rufe ƙofa ya fara sauke ajiyar zuciya, tare da tunanin me ya sa Aymana zata kasa bawa yaron kulawa, bayan tasan shine rayuwar shi, shine abinda yafi so duk duniya.

Ya jawo wayarshi yana miƙewa tsaye, yayi tunanin kiranta, maganar Ayda ta kuma dawo mashi, ya sa hannu ya dafe kai a fili ya furta "Hukuncin da kika yi kenan Aymana, kin ginawa takobi gini, don killaceta."

Ya girgiza kanshi, tabbas yasan burin mutanen gidansu ya cika, sun kuma mallakar babban burin su a cikin mulki, ya danna wayar, lokacin Aymana har tayi shirin bacci sai dai Farida tana gefenta, An-nur kuwa yana ta zabga uban kuka.

Farida ta ce "Ko dai wani abu ya same shi?"

"Ba wani ko jiya haka yayi."

Farida zata kuma magana, wayar Aymana ta hau ruri, ta ɗauka zata miƙa mata "Waye?"

"Mai martaba Sultan."

Amsa ta yi ta aje harta tsinke, tana rurruga An-nur, kira ya kuma shigowa, Aymana ta ɗauka yana dubawa, sam bata yi tunanin zai ƙara kiraba, amma miye dalilin shi.

Tana ɗauka Sultan ya fara sallama ya jin kukan An-nur cikin sauri yake faɗin "Me ki ka mashi."

"Na yi mashi kuma Allah ya taimakeka?" Don maganar ta shigeta, ta kalli Farida dake niyar ficewa tana mata nuni akan taje da yaron falo, Farida ta amshe ki ta fice tare da jan ƙofa.

Aymana ta mayar da hankalinta kan waya "Zai yi kuka ne ba tare da an mashi komai ba."

"Zai yiwu akwai kewa tare da yaron, ganin ba shi da wayo ko bakin haɗar hakan, ya kan yi amfani da kuka domin isar da saƙon shi."

Sultan ya gane nufinta "To shi ne na ce idan kin tafi ki doke shi, ko ki hana shi abincin shi."

"Allah ya baka nasara, ina ganin kamar..."

"Kamar me! Kar ki ida Aymana, Abin da na maki zaki mayar akan yaro na, ba fa zan lamunta ba, ba za ki mayarmin da yaro mai rikiciba."

"Rikici kuma na yaushe, sai yayi ta min kuka akai, shi ya sa nake kyale shi nayi bacci na."

"Kee! Me ki ka ce? abin da aka faɗa min gaskiya ne kenan, taya yarona yana kuka ke kina bacci, kenan ba kya bashi Madarar shi."

"Sayar da ita na ke Sultan!"

"Aymana!" Ya faɗa yana ɗaukar rawanin shi don shiga ciki.

"Allah shi taimake ka."
"Kin san abinda kike faɗa."

"Na ce sayarwa nake."

Ya daka mata tsawa "Ba na son wasa, ta ya zaki rinƙa bawa yarona madarar kwankwani wallahi..."

Da mamaki yadda har an faɗin mashi zancen, wata zuciyar ta sanar da ita ba mamaki tunda anyi gaban mutanen da zasu sanar da shi.

"Allah ya ja kwananka, idan na sayar da tashi madarar nake siyo mashi da kuɗ..."

"Aymana wai kuwa ko kinsan da Sultan kike magana, Magajin nawa kike ba madarar kwankwani, bayan na ji kukanku likitoci kunfi bada koyan bayan shayar da yaro madarar uwa, Na rantse da tsarkin Mulkina, idan kika kuma hana yarona Madara sai na hukuntaki, Na sa a killaceki kamar baiwar da ba..."

"Sultan!"

Ta faɗa a hankali "Matar Sultan, diyar Sarkin Bilyam, Mahaifiyar magajin gobe a masarautar Toro, Mamallakiyar takobi, Sarauniyar matan duk nahiyar, kamanta, Sultan ka manta, ina ganin hukunci akai na ba ƙaramin abu bane."

Shiru Sultan yayi ya fara sauke ajiyar zuciya, sai lokacin ya ke tuno matsayinta, to amma yana samanta don dole ya sanar da ita kuskurenta.

"Aymana! Shi ke nan komai ya wuce, Amma ki kularmin da yarona."

Murmushi ta yi jin yadda yake magana ya kwantar da muryar shi "Dama kiran kenan?" Ta tambaya.

"Hmmm! Me kuma kike buƙata?"

"Ba na buƙatar komai, ina mamakin dalilin kiranne. Ganin ko kaɗan Sultan bai yi kewar Gimbiyarsa ba."

Ya zauna bakin gado "Kewar tana nufin na faɗa kom? mutanen da suke tare da ni sune suke gane ina kewar Gimbiya."

"Uhmm!"

"Me Uhm kuma, ki na so na nuna maki nayi kewar ne?"

"Eh mana ina son ganin haka."

"Yaushe za ki dawo, ranar na ke son nuna miki kalar kewar da nayi."

Ta gane nufin shi ta ce "ba ka nuna min a wayaba, hakanne ma idan na dawo."

"Haka ki ka ce?"

"Hakan ne ma, Allah ya baka nasara."

"Idan kika zado za ki na ihu ne, kina fadar kin tabbatar Sultan yayi kewar Gimbiya, in faɗa maki har sai kince kin tuba, da kika kwashi kaya kika barni."

Dariya tayi "Haba dai wane ihu, ko da can banyi ..."

"Rufe min baki, ke ɗince ba ki ihu?"

Dariya tayi, jin yadda yake mata maganganun barkwanci, ta kwanta tana janyo filo "Ya Magajin gobe? fatan yana lafiya?"

"Lafiya kalau yake."

"MashaAllah. Fatan an sanar dake dawowar ki."

"Waya faɗa maka yanzu zan dawo An-nur ko tafiya bai faraba."

Zaro ido yayi "sai ya iya Zama, iya rarrafe, ya iya tafiya sannan duk ina nan."

"Eh mana."

"Tom ni dai ina jin kunyar Mai martaba, amma nasan ke zaki iya sanar da shi ya waremin sashena da zan dawo."

Dariya tayi tana faɗin "Ni ma bana iya faɗa."

Haka firar su ta koma salon wasa da tsokana, fira mai tsawo har saida Aymana bacci ya fara fizgarta kafin ya barta.

Washe gari Aymana tasa aka fara shirya mata komai na tafiyarta, duk da dai bata wani fidda ranar tafiyar ba.

Daddare tana ɗakin Kaka sai ga kiran Sultan, yauma kamar jiya, sun sha fira sosai kamar ba su ba, Sultan ya gama da mantar da ita komai na damuwarta, ta kuma ƙarajin kewarshi fiye da ko yaushe.

Da safe Umma ta aika kiranta, ta zauna tana gaida ita "Yaushe ki ka fidda ranar tafiyar ki?"

"Nifa Umma ban saka rana ba."

"Ya kamata dai ki saka, zai yiwu Sultan kawaici yayi fa."

Aymana ta jinjina kai "Inshaallah Umma zan fidda."

"Idan kin fidda ki sanar dani."

Aymana sai da ta kwashi kwanaki Ukku ba tare da ta kuma tuntuɓar Umma da maganar ba, Sultan kuwa kira na bin kira suna fira da kalamai na sanyaya zuciya.

Yana jin daɗin fira da ita, musamman salon girmamawa da kalaman aika saƙo da take amfani dasu.

Yau ta dawo daga gidan su Rukkayya saboda Ruƙayya tana shirin komawarta Saudiya washegari, sunyi bankwana sosai kamar kar su rabu.

Farida ta shigo tana kwantar da An-nur akan gado, Aymana ta ce "kin ida haɗa kayan An-nur kuwa?"

"Allah ya taimakeki, yaushe ne tafiyar mu nag..."

"Nan da sati ɗaya ko sati biyu masu zuwa."

"Allah ya kaimu lafiya" Farida ta faɗa tana barin wajan cikin mamakin uwar ɗakin ta, ita bata damu da takoma ba, a zuciyarta ta fara tunanin Gimbiya Ayda tana can tana nata salon.

Dariya tayi tana barin ƙofar dakin.

Washegari Aymana tana kwance wayarta ta fara ƙara, ta duba agogo, ta ga ƙarfe goma tasan lokacin fita fadar shi ne.

Ta ɗauka tana faɗin "Allah ya baka nasara, Sarkin sarakuna, toron Giwa kake, takawa abin tunƙahon Aymana."

Sultan ya ƙara jin wata izza na fizgarshi, ya zauna saman kujerar falon, ya na sauke numfashi, hakan ya tabbatar mata da kirarinta ya karɓu.

"Ya ku ka tashi? fatan uwar gidan Sultan ta tashi lafya?"

"Alhamdulillah."

"Yaushe ne dawowar ki." ya faɗa cikin kawar da duk wani wasa a tsakaninsu, daga yanayin kaushin Muryar shi ta fahimci babu wasa a tare da shi.

"Eh to! Ni fa na shedawa Sultan ina son An-nur ya fara tafiya kafin in dawo."

Sultan ya miƙe ya ɗauki sandar shi, ya riƙe yana haɗawa da hankici.

Ya riƙe wayar a hannu, Aymana tana jin ana gaishe shi hakan ya tabbatar mata da cewar ya fita waje ne.

Ta yi Mamakin hakan, shi kuwa Sultan ɗakin Umma ya nufa, sai da ya gama gaida ita kafin ya mayar da wayar akunnan shi "Ba damuwa, Allah ya kaimu lokacin da zai fara tafiyar."

"Ameen." ta ce

Sultan ya dashe wayar, yana murmushi, Umma ta ce "Kai dawa?"

Cikin sauri ya ce "Sauri nake in shigo, yau na makara zuwa fada."

Ta bishi da ido, ya ƙara durƙusar da kanshi "Na bar ki lafiya."

Ta gane bayason sanar da ita ne.

Hakan ya sa ta gyale shi.

Sultan yana tashi daga fada karfe biyu ya shiga cikin gida, yayi wanka, ya kira Uzairu ya saka shi ya kimtsa mashi kaya a ƙaramin akwatin tafiya, ganin gaggawa a tare da Sultan hakan yasa shima Uzairu ya hanzarta yayi komai cikin lokaci.

Sai da Sultan ya gama shiri ya Aika a kira mashi Ayda, ya kalli Uzairu ya ce "Ka fitar da kayana cikin Sirri, sannan ka sanar da tafiyar gaggawa ta kama Sultan zai tafi, mintuna goma na ba abokan tafiyata su shirya."

Yayi maganar yana kallon agogon Hannunshi, Uzairu ya fice ta baya, Ayda ta turo ƙofa Sultan ya miƙe "Bana da isshen lokaci, zan yi tafiya yanzu."

Ayda ta ce "tafiya kuma? Shi ne sai yanzu zaka sanar dani?"

Matsawa yayi gabanta ya dafa kafaɗarta "Allah ya huci zuciyarki Gimbiya, Ayi min Afuwa."

Banbancin kirarin Ayda da Aymana, yakan kira Aymana da Gimbiyar Sultan ne, saɓanin Ayda da yake kiranta Ayda sai idan halin maza ya motsa ne yake kiranta da Gimbiya.

Ayda ta kawar da kanta "Haka kawai Ni ba zaka sanar dani ba."

Kafin ta ida ya haɗe jikinsu, yana saka hannu ya rufe mata baki, ya kai mata Sumba a wuya, Ayda ta riƙe shi tana yin lamo a jikinshi, Sultan ya ce "An yafe min ko?"

Ta janye kinkinta "Adawo lafiya."

Binta yayi da idanuwa, har ta juya sai kuma ta juyo "Wai ina ne  ka ce zaka je?"

Lokacin Sultan ya matse fuskarshi tamau, ya ƙura mata idanuwanshi, cikin sauri ta fice dariya yayi yana cije leɓo.

Uzairu ya kwankwasa ƙofar baya, ya jima kafin ya shigo, saboda ya ji Sultan ya aika kiran Ayda.

Ya shigo yana zubewa gaban shi "Ko mai ya kammala Allah shi taimakeka."

"Zamu iya tafiya a hanya munyi sallar la'asar."

Sultan ya yo gaba suka fito farfajiyar gidan, sai lokacin maganar tafiyar shi ta fara zuwa kunnuwan mutanen gidan.

Aka fara yi mashi fatan dawowa lafiya, ya kalli Jakadiyya tare da tsayawa, tana ganin haka ta matso gaban shi, Uzairu ya kalleta ya ce "Takarda daga Sultan kikaiwa Mama. Gidan Baba Galadima"

Jakadiyya ta karɓa tana binsu baya, ta wuce sashen Mama.

Sai lokacin ya hangi Mama tsaye sunyi karo da Jakadiya, ta fito ganin tafiyar shi.

Ya waiga yana nufa wajan Gimbiya Mai gado ya sunkuya alamar bankwana, ta ce "Adawo lafiya."

Ya miƙe yayi ƙofar ɗakin Gimbiya Ummi tana ɗaga labule taga yana nufowa, a ƙofa ta ida fitowa.

Sultan ya ɗan sunkuya, Cikin Mamakin da bata baiyyanar ba a fuskarta ta ce "Wannan wace irin tafiya ce Sultan?"

"Kiyi min Afuwa Allah ya taimake ki."

Ta dafa rawanin kanshi kamar tana saka mashi Albarka ta ce "Ina zuwa Sultan?"

Sai lokacin ya ji kunyar abinda yake shirin aikatawa, gashi ba zai yiwu ya faɗi wani abun ba, haka kuma baya buƙatar mutanan gidan su fahimci ya daɗe a wajan ta hakan yasa ya ce "Darul-Bilyam."

Gimbiya Ummi ta janye hannunta "Allah ya dawo mana da kai lafiya, ya tsare maka hanya Sultan."

A zuciyar shi yake amsawa ya na fara tattaki, sai ga Abul ya rugo da gudu ya faɗa jikinshi, Sultan ya riƙe shi, yana jan Hannunshi, suka nufi ɓangaren Mai martaba.

Yayi bankwana dashi, sai dai Mai martaba ya bashi girman shi bai tambayarshi ba ganin Sultan ɗin bai faɗi wajan da za shi ba.

Haka ya rakoshi waje, aka buɗe mota ya shiga ya zauna,  sai da aka fara tafiya Sultan ya cewa basu Umarni ta hanyar faɗa masu inda suka nufa.

Nan fa kowa yayi mamakin shi, hatta Uzairu da ke gaban mota bai kawowa ranshi hakan ba. shi kuwa Sultan waya ya jawo yana dannawa.

***

Aymana kuwa hidimarta kawai take a gidansu, ranar ta sha baccin rana sosai sai da aka fara kiran sallar la'asar ta tashi tayi wanka ta saka dogon rigar shadda.

Ta nufi ɗakin Kaka, ta samu Bilkisu zaune tana waya, ta zauna tana janye mata ƙafa ta zauna.

Kaka ta ce "Ki ka zo kina tureta."

"Ta haye kujera harda ƙafafuwanta."

"Sai ki hana ta tunda ɗakin ki ne, ki ta fi kibarmu musha iska kin ƙi."

Aymana ta ce "Ni dai ban san mi na tare ma Kaka ba, to ki kwantar da hankalin ki na kusa tafiya."

"Oho dai, marar sanin ciwon kai, in ba rashin sanin ciwon kai ba, sai ki baro miji, ayi ayi ki shirya komawa ki ƙi."

Bilkisu ta datse wayar ta na miƙewa "Bari ke dai Kaka, da fa harda kukanta ba inda zata."

Aymana ta harareta, Kaka ta ce "Ai lokacin gani take kamar rabasu za'ayi amma yanzu gashi ta ƙi komawa."

"Haba kaka ke fa kike cewa na ja ajina, na iya salon kissa."

Kaka ta riƙe baki "to sai nace ki zauna kiyi hali'an anan, ajin ya tsinke ai."

Aymana ta miƙe ta shige ƙuryar ɗakin kaka.

Ƙarfe Biyar da rabi Sultan ya isa masarautar, babu sanarwar zuwan shi, sai dai dirar su.

Kowa yayi mamaki, Sultan ya jima a mota kafin ya fito, lokacin an sanar cewar Sarki Sultan ne yazo.

Haka yasa fadawan masarautar suka shigo tararshi, fadar Mai martaba ya nufa, ya yi tattaki yana durƙushewa yana gaisuwa.

Mai martaba ya riƙe shi "Sultan kai ne tafe da wannan marecen?"

"Allah ya baka nasara."

"Sannunku da hanya, fatan kun iso lafiya."

"Alhamdulillah."

Mai martaba ya kuma kallon shi "Sannu sannu Sultan." Ya faɗa yana miƙewa.

Ya kalli wani bafaden ya ce "a kawo wa Sultan abin buƙata."

Ya kalli Sultan yana ɗan fita daga fadar.

Farida ce ke gudu-gudu tana neman Aymana a ɓangarorin gidan, tana da tabbacin Aymana bata san da zuwa Sultan ba, ganin bata bada wani umarnin shirya wani abu don shi ba.

A ɗakin Kaka ta leƙa har xata juya sai ta jiyo kukan An-nur da take ba Madara.

Cikin sauri ta shiga tana sallama a ƙofa.

"Lafiya kuwa Farida."

"Tun ɗazu nake bi ɓangare ɓangare ina neman ki."

Aymana ta ce "Ina nan zaune wannan yaron ne yake min kuka Wallahi."

Farida ta yi dariya "Ga dukkan alamu, ya shinshino ƙamshin turaren Sultan ne."

Da sauri Aymana ta ce "Me?"

"Sultan yana fadar Mai martaba, isowar shi kenan."

Mamaki far tare da Aymana, ta kalli Farida ta fara shu'umin murmushi "kin tabbatar?"

Farida ta ce "Ina da tabbaci Allah ya taimakeki."

Miƙewa tayi da sauri ta miƙa mata An-nur "Maza ki kai shi wajan Bilkisu, ta shirya mashi, Ni kuma ki haɗo min kayana zan shirya anan."

"Allah ya taimakeki, kamar ba ki buƙatar shiryawa, Alkebba ta wadatar."

"Na zama abokiyar tsokanar ki ko Farida?"

Tana dariya ta ce "Allah ya huci zuciyarki."

Ta fice abin ta.

Aymana tana ta tunani, kenan zuwa zai yi shi ya sa ya ce mata Allah ya kaimu lokacin tafiyar.

Aymana ta faɗa gado tana jin daɗi tare da ƙanƙame fulo.
